# cs.CV [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Projection-based coupling of infrared thermography and stereocorrelation-based digital image correlation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28905)
*Jendrik-Alexander Tröger,Lutz Müller-Lohse,Stefan Hartmann*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种基于外部投影的耦合方法，利用针孔相机模型（pinhole camera model）将红外热成像测量的二维温度数据与立体相关数字图像相关（stereocorrelation-based digital image correlation）获得的三维点坐标关联，实现弯曲表面上温度场与变形场在拉格朗日框架（Lagrangian frame）下的统一表达，并采用径向基函数（radial basis functions）进行时空插值以计算面内温度梯度与温度变化率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全场测量技术如数字图像相关（digital image correlation）和红外热成像（infrared thermography）在实验固体力学中广泛使用，但将两者数据表达在同一拉格朗日框架下需要复杂流程，尤其在分析非平坦表面时，现有方法难以高效且精确地实现这一耦合。

Method: 提出基于外部投影的耦合方法：采用两个独立校准的工业级系统，通过针孔相机模型将红外热成像的二维温度数据投影到立体数字图像相关获得的三维点坐标上；利用参考物体的单张图像校准投影矩阵（projection matrix）；保持现有图像配准（image registration）流程不变；同时采用径向基函数作为时空全局插值格式，计算弯曲表面上的面内温度梯度和温度变化率。

Result: 温度场被精确地表示在材料点（material points）上，该方法特别适用于弯曲表面且易于嵌入现有实验协议中，最终提供信息丰富且全面的全场数据集。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了一种将数字图像相关与红外热成像数据精确耦合的简化途径，尤其适用于弯曲表面，无需改变现有图像配准流程即可嵌入现有实验方案，并通过径向基函数插值获取温度梯度与温度率，扩展了全场数据的分析维度。

Abstract: Full-field measurement techniques such as digital image correlation and infrared thermography are prevalent in experimental solid mechanics. Digital image correlation is used to analyze surface deformation, while infrared thermography quantifies surface temperature fields. However, sophisticated procedures are necessary to express both datasets in the same Lagrangian frame, especially when analyzing non-flat surfaces. In this study, we propose an external projection-based coupling that uses the pinhole camera model to relate two-dimensional temperature data measured by infrared thermography to three-dimensional point coordinates from stereocorrelation-based digital image correlation. Unlike existing multiview approaches, we utilize two independently calibrated industrial-grade systems and augment the experimental evaluation with the pinhole camera model. The projection matrix of the camera model is calibrated using a single image of a reference object. Through this projection, temperature fields are accurately represented at material points. Our method is particularly suited for, but not restricted to, curved surfaces and straightforward to embed in existing experimental protocols, as the image registration is kept as is. Additionally, we propose using radial basis functions as a global interpolation ansatz in both space and time to compute in-plane temperature gradients and even temperature rates on curved surfaces, thereby providing an extensive and information-rich full-field dataset.

</details>


### [2] [Unlocking the Visual Record of Materials Science: A Large-Scale Multimodal Dataset from Scientific Literature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29667)
*Subham Ghosh,Shubham Tiwari,Mohammad Ibrahim,Abhishek Tewari*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出 MatMMExtract 端到端开源流水线，通过将复合科学图表分解为子面板并利用大语言模型生成结构化标注，构建了包含 391,606 个面板级图文对的大型数据集 MatSciFig；同时引入材料科学领域检测数据集 MaterialScope，在图文检索任务上实现了 4.4 倍的性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 材料科学文献中的图表蕴含数十年的实验知识，但当前 AI 难以规模化利用这些视觉记录。核心困难在于大多数科学图表是复合的（compound），单个标题同时描述多个子面板，导致直接的图文配对不可靠。

Method: 提出 MatMMExtract 端到端开源流水线，主要步骤包括：(1) 将复合图表分解为单个子面板；(2) 利用大语言模型（large language model, LLM）结合人工构建的材料科学分类体系（taxonomy），为每个子面板生成结构化的、有依据的标注。此外，引入 MaterialScope——一个包含 2,811 张人工标注的材料科学图表的领域专用检测数据集，并基于 YOLO12-m 微调以实现精确的面板定位。在生成标注时，对六种语言模型进行了基准测试，最终选用 Gemini 3.1 Flash Lite。

Result: 在 14,810 篇开放获取论文上运行 MatMMExtract，从 180,571 张图表中生成 391,606 个面板级图文对，每个标注包含子标题、涵盖 19 个大类和 100 多个子类型的双层可视化分类，以及科学摘要。微调后的 YOLO12-m 检测器在 MaterialScope 上达到 mAP_50 为 0.9227；Gemini 3.1 Flash Lite 的标注质量评分良好率达 82%，幻觉率（hallucination rate）为 4.8%。基于 MatSciFig 构建的双编码器检索基线在 R@1 上比零样本 CLIP 提升 4.4 倍。

Conclusion: MatMMExtract 流水线有效解锁了材料科学文献中视觉知识的可访问性，MatSciFig 数据集在视觉-语言学习（vision-language learning）中具有即时可用价值。所有资源均已开源发布。

Abstract: The materials science literature encodes decades of experimental knowledge in figures, yet this visual record remains locked away and inaccessible to AI at scale. The core difficulty is structural: most scientific figures are compound, with a single caption describing multiple sub-panels simultaneously, making direct image-text pairing unreliable. We present MatMMExtract, an end-to-end open-source pipeline that resolves this by decomposing compound figures into individual sub-panels and generating structured, grounded annotations using a large language model guided by a curated materials science taxonomy. Applied to 14,810 open-access articles, MatMMExtract produces MatSciFig; 391,606 panel-level image-text pairs from 180,571 figures, each annotated with a sub-caption, a two-level visualisation category spanning 19 classes and over 100 subtypes, and a scientific summary. To enable accurate panel localisation, we introduce MaterialScope, a domain-specific detection dataset of 2,811 manually annotated materials science figures, on which a fine-tuned YOLO12-m detector achieves mAP_50 of 0.9227. Among six benchmarked language models, Gemini 3.1 Flash Lite delivers the best cost-quality trade-off for annotation generation, with 82% of outputs rated good and a hallucination rate of 4.8%. A dual-encoder retrieval baseline on MatSciFig achieves a 4.4 times improvement in R@1 over zero-shot CLIP, demonstrating the dataset's immediate utility for vision-language learning. All resources are released openly to the community.

</details>

# hep-th [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [Quantum Black Hole Chemistry from Double Holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28408)
*Naman Kumar*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文指出扩展黑洞热力学（extended black hole thermodynamics）中全息字典（holographic dictionary）存在的颜色-体积简并（color-volume degeneracy）问题，并证明Karch-Randall双重全息（double holography）中的量子黑洞通过半经典机制自然消除了这一简并：物理膜（physical brane）上的反作用物质（backreacting matter）提供了独立于缺陷体积（defect volume）的颜色变量（color variable），无需引入非标准边界模量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩展黑洞热力学中，固定边界共形框架（conformal frame）下改变AdS半径会同时改变中心荷（central charge）和CFT的空间体积（spatial volume），导致第一定律（first law）的颜色和体积扇区被锁定，产生简并性。现有Weyl因子提议虽试图解决此问题，但引入了非标准边界模量。

Method: 采用Karch-Randall双重全息框架，将全息正则化表面替换为物理膜（physical brane），使经典体黑洞（classical bulk black hole）变为低维量子黑洞（lower-dimensional quantum black hole）。该几何包含所有阶反作用（backreaction）下的截断物质应力张量（cutoff-matter stress tensor），从而在无需引入非标准边界模量的情况下，自然解除颜色与缺陷体积的简并。

Result: 反作用的物质扇区（backreacting matter sector）提供了独立于缺陷体积的颜色变量，明确论证了这一机制在量子BTZ黑洞（quantum BTZ black hole）中的实现。量子反作用（quantum backreaction）成功解决了颜色-体积简并问题。

Conclusion: 双重全息框架中的量子反作用自然消除了扩展黑洞热力学中的颜色-体积简并，无需依赖非标准边界模量。缺失的热力学方向由双重全息量子黑洞的物理截断物质扇区提供。

Abstract: Extended black hole thermodynamics exposes a sharp tension in the usual holographic dictionary: at fixed boundary conformal frame, changing the AdS radius changes both the central charge and the spatial volume of the CFT, apparently locking the color and volume sectors of the first law. We show that this degeneracy is naturally removed for quantum black holes in Karch--Randall double holography. The mechanism is intrinsically semiclassical. Replacing the holographic regulator surface by a physical brane induces gravity coupled to a cutoff CFT, so classical bulk black holes become lower-dimensional quantum black holes whose geometry includes the cutoff-matter stress tensor to all orders in backreaction. This backreacting matter sector supplies a color variable distinct from the defect volume. We demonstrate the mechanism explicitly for the quantum BTZ black hole. Thus quantum backreaction resolves the same color-volume degeneracy addressed by the recent Weyl-factor proposal, but without introducing a non-standard boundary modulus. Instead, the missing thermodynamic direction is supplied by the physical cutoff-matter sector of the doubly holographic quantum black hole.

</details>


### [4] [Meson states in `t Hooft model: Hamiltonian approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28424)
*A. V. Smilga*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文指出，在无穷大N极限下的二维量子色动力学（QCD₂）中，高度激发束缚夸克-反夸克态的质量可以通过一个简单的量子力学模型（势能为V(x)=σ|x|）确定。在极端相对论情形下，质量平方遵循μ_n² = (g²N/2π)n，与't Hooft通过求解Bethe–Salpeter方程导出的规律一致；在非相对论情形下，能级渐近行为为ε_n = C n^{2/3}。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究无穷大N极限下二维QCD中高度激发束缚夸克-反夸克态的质量谱，并探索是否可以通过一个简单的量子力学模型（一维线性势）来重现't Hooft方程的结果。

Method: 采用一个量子力学模型，势能为V(x)=σ|x|，分别在极端相对论情形（ultrarelativistic case）和非相对论情形（nonrelativistic case）下求解束缚态能级。将结果与't Hooft通过求解Bethe–Salpeter方程（Bethe–Salpeter equation）得到的结果进行比较。

Result: 在极端相对论情形下，质量平方公式μ_n² = (g²N/2π)n与't Hooft方程的结果一致；但相对论哈密顿量（relativistic Hamiltonian）的能级具有有限宽度（finite widths），该宽度在大夸克质量下指数压低：Γ_n ∝ exp{-2πm²/σ}。在非相对论情形下，能级渐近行为为ε_n = C n^{2/3}。

Conclusion: 高度激发夸克-反夸克束缚态的质量谱可以在一维线性势量子力学模型框架下得到描述，其中极端相对论情形完全复现了't Hooft方程的结果，非相对论情形则给出了与薛定谔方程（Schrödinger equation）一致的n^{2/3}标度律。

Abstract: We point out that the masses of the highly excited bound quark-antiquark states in QCD$_2$ in the infinite $N$ limit may be determined in the framework of a simple quantum-mechanical model with the potential $V(x) = σ|x|$. In the ultrarelativistic case, the masses follow the pattern $$ μ_n^2 \ =\ \frac {g^2 N}{2π} n, $$ which coincides with the law derived by `t Hooft by solving the Bethe--Salpeter equation. In constrast to what follows from the exact analysis, the levels of the relativistic Hamiltonian have finite widths, but these widths are exponentially suppressed, $Γ_n \propto \exp\{-2πm^2/σ\}$ for large quark masses.
  In the nonrelativistic case, the levels follow the asymptotics $ε_n = μ_n - 2m = Cn^{2/3}$, where the constant $C$ can be determined by solving the `t Hooft equation or alternatively the nonrelativistic Schrödinger equation.

</details>


### [5] [Subregion observer rules from generalized entanglement wedges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28484)
*Lana Bozanic,Kenneth Higginbotham,Chris Waddell*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文发现两组独立提出的全息张量网络规则——科罗拉多（CO）组的观测者规则与Kaya-Rath-Ritchie（KRR）组的广义纠缠楔规则——恰好等价，进而利用这种等价关系在引力路径积分和JT引力中推广了相关方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 两组独立提出的全息张量网络（holographic tensor network）修改规则——CO组用于引入观测者，KRR组用于推导Bousso-Penington广义纠缠楔（generalized entanglement wedge）方案——被发现完全等价，提示AAIL启发的观测者规则与广义纠缠楔之间存在更普遍的关联。

Method: 首先利用KRR在固定几何态（fixed geometry states）下的引力路径积分（gravitational path integral）类比规则，将AAIL的路径积分规则推广至包含占据体院子区域（bulk subregion）的观测者；反过来，再利用AAIL规则在JT引力（JT gravity）中推导Bousso-Penington关于点状体区域（pointlike bulk regions）的方案。

Result: 证实了CO组与KRR组的两类张量网络规则完全等价；在引力路径积分框架下将AAIL规则推广至包含体院子区域观测者；在JT引力中从AAIL规则导出了Bousso-Penington方案。

Conclusion: 两组等价规则暗示了AAIL启发的观测者规则与广义纠缠楔之间存在更深层的联系，为全息映射中观测者与纠缠结构的关系提供了统一视角。

Abstract: We consider rules for modifying holographic tensor networks proposed in two independent contexts: by the Colorado (CO) group in 2503.09681 to incorporate observers in holographic maps, and by Kaya-Rath-Ritchie (KRR) in 2506.10064 to derive the Bousso-Penington generalized entanglement wedge proposal. Interestingly, these two sets of tensor network rules are exactly equivalent. This suggests a more general connection between these Abdalla-Antonini-Iliesiu-Levine (AAIL) inspired observer rules and generalized entanglement wedges. To pursue this connection, we first use KRR's analogous rules for the gravitational path integral (based on fixed geometry states) to generalize AAIL's path integral rules to include observers occupying a bulk subregion. Additionally, we leverage the connection in the opposite direction by using the AAIL rules to derive the Bousso-Penington proposal for pointlike bulk regions in JT gravity.

</details>


### [6] [Geometric pairing of Nambu--Goldstone modes in spacetime symmetry breaking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28485)
*Aleksander Głódkowski*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文识别了一种自发破缺时空对称性系统中的几何配对机制，导致成对的戈德斯通场（Goldstone fields）正则共轭并融合为单个B型南布-戈德斯通模（type-B Nambu–Goldstone mode, NGM）。该机制源于戈德斯通涨落对局部时空体积元的形变，使戈德斯通流形产生贝里曲率（Berry curvature）。结合现有约化方案，提出了多体系统无能隙NGM数量的一般计数公式，并在双分量玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚微观模型中验证了该机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在自发破缺时空对称性（spontaneously broken spacetime symmetries）的系统中，戈德斯通模的计数与分类问题尚未完全解决，特别是B型NGM的配对起源和物理机制仍不明确。本文旨在揭示一种普适的几何配对机制，为理解此类系统中无能隙模的数目提供统一框架。

Method: 首先从几何角度识别配对机制：戈德斯通涨落形变局部时空体积元，在戈德斯通流形（Goldstone manifold）上诱导出贝里曲率（Berry curvature），使成对戈德斯通场变为正则共轭并杂化形成单个B型NGM。随后将这种配对机制与现有的计数约化方案结合，提出一般性的计数公式。最后在双分量玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（Bose–Einstein condensate）的微观模型中展示该机制，具体分析了膨胀子（dilaton）与U(1)戈德斯通场融合为具有二次色散（quadratic dispersion）的单个NGM的过程。

Result: 建立了自发破缺时空对称性系统中戈德斯通场几何配对的一般机制，并提出了B型NGM的计数公式。在双分量BEC模型中，膨胀子与U(1)戈德斯通场成功配对融合为一个具有二次色散的单个NGM，验证了理论预测。

Conclusion: 该几何配对机制为自发破缺时空对称性系统中戈德斯通模的计数与分类提供了统一的理论基础。结合计数公式，可推广至更广泛的多体系统，用于预测和分析无能隙激发谱的结构。

Abstract: We identify a geometric pairing mechanism in systems with spontaneously broken spacetime symmetries, whereby pairs of Goldstone fields become canonically conjugate and hybridize into a single type-B Nambu--Goldstone mode (NGM). The mechanism originates from deformations of the local spacetime volume element induced by Goldstone fluctuations, which endow the Goldstone manifold with a Berry curvature. Integrating this pairing with existing reductions, we propose a general counting formula for the number of gapless NGMs in many-body systems. We demonstrate the mechanism in a microscopic model of a two-component Bose--Einstein condensate, where the dilaton and the $U(1)$ Goldstone field combine into a single NGM with quadratic dispersion.

</details>


### [7] [Calabi-Yau Metrics with Full Moduli Dependence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28487)
*Andrei Constantin,Seung-Joo Lee,Andre Lukas,Luca A. Nutricati*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本研究结合机器学习数值数据与符号回归（symbolic regression），构建了具有显式复结构（complex-structure）和凯勒模（Kähler moduli）依赖的近似Ricci平坦Calabi-Yau度量的解析表达式，并在双三次三维流形族上实现了与数值数据百分之几量级的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管数值与机器学习方法已能高精度构造紧致Calabi-Yau三维流形（Calabi-Yau three-folds）上的Ricci平坦度量（Ricci-flat metrics），但理解这些度量如何在模空间（moduli space）中变化对于现象学应用至关重要。现有方法缺乏对模依赖的显式解析表达。

Method: 提出一种显式的凯勒势（Kähler potential）Ansatz，其系数具有模依赖；将该Ansatz拟合至机器学习生成的数值数据，并利用符号回归从数据中重建系数的解析公式，从而获得具有显式模依赖的近似Ricci平坦度量。

Result: 将该构造应用于$\mathbb{P}^2 \times \mathbb{P}^2$中双三次三维流形（bi-cubic three-folds）的单参数族，所得近似解析度量与底层数值数据达到百分之几量级的一致性。

Conclusion: 符号回归与机器学习数值数据相结合，能够有效构建具有显式模依赖的近似Ricci平坦Calabi-Yau度量的解析表达式，为弦论现象学研究提供了实用的分析工具。

Abstract: Recent advances in numerical and machine-learning methods have enabled highly accurate constructions of Ricci-flat metrics on compact Calabi-Yau three-folds. For phenomenological applications it is crucial to understand how these metrics vary across moduli space. In this work, we construct approximate analytic expressions for Ricci-flat Calabi-Yau metrics with explicit complex-structure and Kähler moduli dependence by combining machine-learned numerical data with symbolic regression. Our approach is based on an explicit Ansatz for the Kähler potential with moduli-dependent coefficients. Fitting this Ansatz to numerical data and applying symbolic regression allows us to reconstruct analytic formulae for these coefficients, thereby obtaining approximate Ricci-flat metrics with explicit moduli dependence. We apply the construction to a one-parameter family of bi-cubic three-folds in $\mathbb{P}^2 \times \mathbb{P}^2$, achieving percent-level agreement with the underlying numerical data.

</details>

Method: 研究聚焦于Landau-Ginzburg/Gepner模型弦真空（string vacua），这类模型可能不包含Kähler模。作者对所有无Kähler模的Landau-Ginzburg定向折叠（orientifold）模型进行穷举列表，并计算每个模型的复结构模（complex structure moduli）数量与tadpole荷（tadpole charge）。

Conclusion: 基于复结构模数量与tadpole荷的计算结果，可以识别出哪些模型是真正有潜力用于构建具有现象学相关性的完全稳定化微扰弦真空（perturbative string vacua）的候选者。

Abstract: One of the main challenges in string theory Calabi-Yau compactifications to four dimensions is the stabilization of the massless complex structure and Kähler moduli. In type IIB string theory, complex structure moduli can be stabilized perturbatively by turning on fluxes on the internal space, while there is no perturbative mechanism for Kähler moduli stabilization. Since every Calabi-Yau manifold has at least one Kähler modulus (the overall volume), there is no hope to stabilize all moduli perturbatively. A way out is given by Landau-Ginzburg/Gepner models string vacua which can have no Kähler moduli. To identify the most promising candidates for fully stabilized perturbative string vacua, we provide an exhaustive list of Landau-Ginzburg orientifold models with no Kähler moduli, and compute for each model the number of complex structure moduli together with the tadpole charge. TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种通过自发对称性破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking）动态产生费米面失配（Fermi surface mismatch）的新机制，并在具有精确SU(2)味对称性的无质量双组分狄拉克理论（Dirac theory）中，通过自相互作用矢量玻色子凝聚（condensation）实现稳定相对论超流体（relativistic superfluid），将Chandrasekhar-Clogston线推广为耦合空间中的曲面。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究基于一个无质量双组分狄拉克理论（massless two-component Dirac theory），该理论具有精确的SU(2)味对称性（flavor symmetry）。关键机制是自相互作用矢量玻色子（self-interacting vector boson）的凝聚，这一过程在保持时间反演对称性（time reversal）的同时分裂费米面。

Result: 该机制产生了一个稳定的相对论超流体（relativistic superfluid），其费米面失配由对称性破缺耦合（symmetry-breaking coupling）自洽地（self-consistently）固定。Chandrasekhar-Clogston线（Chandrasekhar-Clogston line）被推广为耦合空间中的一个曲面（surface in coupling space）。

Conclusion: 研究表明，费米面失配可以源自系统内部的自发对称性破缺而非外部人为设定，这为理解非匹配条件下的配对超流/超导现象提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: When fermions pair across mismatched Fermi surfaces, the mismatch reflects a built-in inequivalence between the species. We show it can instead arise dynamically by spontaneous symmetry breaking. In a massless two component Dirac theory with exact SU(2) flavor symmetry, a self-interacting vector boson condenses, splitting the Fermi surfaces while preserving time reversal. Pairing then yields a stable relativistic superfluid, promoting the Chandrasekhar-Clogston line to a surface in coupling space, the mismatch fixed self-consistently by the symmetry-breaking coupling.

### [11] [CFT Dual for Timelike Geodesic in Lorentzian dS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28814)
*Xing Huang,Chen-Te Ma*

Main category: hep-th

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We construct the Euclidean CFT$_{d}$ dual of a generic massive scalar in Lorentzian dS$_{d+1}$ via analytic continuation. The resulting $PT$ defect defines a $PT$-invariant state that reproduces the Bunch-Davies Wightman function. However, the entanglement entropy captures only the real part of the central charge. This motivates a single-geodesic dual based on the timelike geodesic-integrated Wightman function, which yields the correlators between a bulk operator and a linear combination of an OPE block and its Casimir partner. We also derive the associated conformal defect and anomaly from an integral identity of the dS/CFT symmetry group.

### [12] [Axions on de Sitter space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28858)
*Vasileios A. Letsios,Stathis Vitouladitis*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了全局德西特空间（de Sitter space, dS_D）中无质量最小耦合紧致标量场（轴子）的量子化，发现其全希尔伯特空间为H=L²(S¹)⊗F，其中零模式提供了超越振荡福克空间（Fock space）的量子力学自由度，导致带电扇区中粒子数出现观察者依赖的效应，并通过欧几里得路径积分和三维德西特空间中的电磁对偶性拓展了分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准德西特空间量子场论（QFT）通常采用Bunch-Davies真空和振荡福克空间，但紧致标量场的零模式可能引入非平凡的量子力学因子，从而改变理论的希尔伯特空间结构及其物理后果，这一缺失需要被系统厘清。

Method: 作者采用正则量子化方法处理全局D维德西特空间中的无质量最小耦合紧致标量场（轴子），通过确定量子德西特荷将零模式与振荡模式分离，并借助Harish-Chandra特征标和欧几里得路径积分技术分析扇区结构，同时在dS₃中利用轴子-光子对偶性将结果映射至电磁学。

Result: 全希尔伯特空间为H=L²(S¹)⊗F，其中L²(S¹)上的整数量子力学动量对应守恒的U(1)平移荷；带电0粒子态是归一化的但仅具SO(D)不变性，导致不同德西特升维下的测地观察者对带电扇区中粒子数的判断不一致；带电扇区中的场强Wightman两点函数满足Hadamard条件，且在有限全局时间下非dS不变，但早期和晚期渐近恢复不变性；欧几里得路径积分中，标准D-球路径积分仅覆盖中性扇区，带电扇区需顶点算符插入，求和后给出包含整希尔伯特空间的装饰球路径积分；在dS₃中，轴子零模式对应电磁学中的磁单极子。

Conclusion: 轴子零模式在德西特空间中产生了超越标准Bunch-Davies真空框架的量子力学扇区，其带电态在全局时间上破坏德西特对称性但保持Hadamard性质，且通过路径积分和电磁对偶性展示了丰富的物理后果，对德西特空间量子场论的基础理解具有重要意义。

Abstract: We study a massless minimally coupled compact scalar, or axion, on global $D$-dimensional de Sitter space (dS$_D$). We quantise the theory canonically, determine the quantum dS charges, and find that the axion zero mode supplies a quantum-mechanical factor beyond the oscillator Fock space, $\mathcal{F}$. The full Hilbert space is $\mathcal{H}=L^2(S^1)\otimes\mathcal{F}$, with the integer quantum-mechanical momentum on $L^2(S^1)$ identified with the conserved $\mathrm{U}(1)$ shift charge. The 1-particle unitary irreducible representation (UIR) of the dS group, $\mathrm{SO}(D,1)$, captures the oscillator sector, but misses the zero mode. We find that the neutral 0-particle state is dS-invariant and normalisable. Charged 0-particle states are normalisable, but only $\mathrm{SO}(D)$ invariant. This implies that geodesic observers related by dS boosts do not agree on the particle number in a charged sector, an effect absent in QFTs equipped only with the standard Bunch-Davies vacuum. We compute field-strength Wightman 2-point functions in charged sectors and find that they are Hadamard. For non-zero charge they are not dS-invariant at finite global times, but they are asymptotically so at early and late times. We complement this analysis with a Euclidean perspective. The ordinary $D$-sphere path integral, $Z_{S^D}$, written in terms of Harish-Chandra characters, has access only to the neutral sector. Charged sectors require vertex-operator insertions, and summing over them gives a decorated sphere path integral, $\widehat{Z}_{S^D}=Z_\text{QM}\,Z_{S^D}$, that captures the entire Hilbert space, with $Z_\text{QM}$ denoting the partition function of a quantum rotor at a dimension-dependent effective temperature. Finally, in dS$_3$, we use the duality between an axion and a photon to translate our results to electromagnetism, where the axion zero mode gives rise to magnetic monopoles.

Abstract: We provide a field-theoretic construction of Padmanabhan's duality-invariant Feynman propagator for a massive point particle in Euclidean space $\mathbb{R}^D$. ### [14] [$BMS_3$-like algebras via the $Z_N$-graded $u(1)^2$ Kac-Moody algebra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29323)
*Armin Ghazi,Ahmad Moradpouri*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了从 u(1)^2 Kac-Moody 代数构造 Virasoro 代数的广义 Sugawara 构造所对应的非紧代数簇的紧化，发现无穷远点对应于 BMS_3 型代数的推广，并分析了其理想结构、幂零深度、因式分解性质以及中心扩张。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前研究表明，对于 u(1)^2 Kac-Moody 代数，存在具有 Z_N 分级的额外 Sugawara 构造，且这些构造构成一个非紧代数簇。本文旨在通过对该代数簇进行紧化（compactification），揭示无穷远点与 BMS_3 型代数之间的对应关系，从而统一并推广这类代数结构。

Method: 通过对非紧代数簇添加无穷远点进行紧化，分析紧化后无穷远点对应的代数结构。利用 Z_2 分级情况下的结果与标准 BMS_3 代数对比，并将 N > 2 的情形推广为 Vir 与幂零理想（nilpotent ideal）的半直积。进一步研究代数簇定义多项式的一次因式分解性质，以及相应代数的中心扩张（central extension）。

Result: 对于 Z_2 分级，紧化后的无穷远点对应的代数恰好是标准 BMS_3 代数，形式为 Vir ⋉ F，其中 F 是无穷维阿贝尔理想（abelian ideal）。对于 N > 2，存在标准 BMS_3 代数的推广，形式仍为 Vir ⋉ F，但此时 F 是非阿贝尔的幂零代数，其深度（depth）r < N。代数簇在该点的奇异性阶数（order of singularity）与幂零理想的深度相关。代数簇的定义多项式可分解为线性因子的乘积，若该性质成立，则可对所有 BMS_3 型代数进行分类。最后，这些代数的中心扩张与共形权重 h = 2 的原初场（primary field）对应的代数结构一致。

Conclusion: 通过紧化由广义 Sugawara 构造定义的代数簇，系统建立了从 u(1)^2 代数构造 BMS_3 型代数的框架，揭示了代数簇的几何性质（奇异性阶数）与代数结构（幂零理想深度）之间的深层联系，并提出了基于因式分解性质进行分类的可能性。

Abstract: The Sugawara construction provides a natural way to construct the Virasoro algebra from a current algebra. It was shown in Ref.~\cite{Ghazi:2025oin} that for the $u(1)^2$ Kac-Moody current algebra, there exist additional constructions that exhibit a $\mathbb{Z}_N$-graded structure. Indeed, the space of such constructions defines a non-compact algebraic variety whose dimension depends on $N$. In this paper, we consider the compactification of these algebraic varieties by adding points at infinity to the non-compact part, and show that these points correspond precisely to generalizations of $BMS_3$-like algebras. More explicitly, for a $\mathbb{Z}_2$ grading, the corresponding algebra coincides with the $BMS_3$ algebra, which takes the form $\mathrm{Vir} \rtimes F$, where $F$ is an infinite abelian ideal of the full algebra. For $N > 2$, we show that there exist generalizations of the standard $BMS_3$ algebra of the form $\mathrm{Vir} \rtimes F$, where $F$ is a nonabelian ideal that forms a nilpotent algebra of depth $r < N$. We further demonstrate that the depth of the algebra is related to the order of the singularity of the algebraic variety at that point. We also show that the polynomials defining the algebraic varieties exhibit a factorization property into linear factors, which, if true, classifies all $BMS_3$-like algebras. Finally, we study the central extensions of these algebras, which are consistent with the general structure of algebras corresponding to primary fields of conformal weight $h = 2$.

### [15] [Bounded Chaos in a Ghost-Coupled Hamiltonian System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29342)
*Zahra Molaee,Soleyman Fatholahzadeh*

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟研究了一个含“鬼魂自由度”（ghost degree of freedom，负动能贡献）的哈密顿系统，发现非线性相互作用项与饱和指数势能在特定参数范围内能够抑制相空间逃逸，并产生包含规则岛与混沌区的混合相空间结构，支持有界混沌（bounded chaos）运动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 负动能贡献（ghost自由度）会导致能量泛函（energy functional）无下界，从而引发相空间中的跑离行为（runaway behavior）。本文旨在探索非线性相互作用能否在经典层面抑制这种不稳定性。

Method: 采用哈密顿运动方程的直接数值积分、庞加莱截面（Poincaré surfaces of section）和轨迹投影（trajectory projections）分析相空间结构；通过最大李雅普诺夫指数（maximal Lyapunov exponent）表征混沌运动的边界性。

Result: 非线性相互作用与饱和指数势在研究的参数范围（ε, α）内能够抑制相空间逃逸；相空间呈现规则岛（regular islands）与混沌区（chaotic regions）共存的混合结构；最大李雅普诺夫指数表明临近轨迹指数分离但被限制在有界区域内，即存在有界混沌（bounded chaotic motion）。

Conclusion: 非线性约束（nonlinear confinement）能显著改变负能量扇区（negative-energy sectors）在经典层面的稳定性；在探索的参数域内，观察到了有界混沌机制，避免了由ghost自由度引发的发散行为。

Abstract: We study the dynamics of a Hamiltonian system with a ghost degree of freedom, characterized by a negative kinetic-energy contribution and the possibility of runaway behavior due to an indefinite energy functional. We present numerical evidence that a nonlinear interaction term, together with a saturating exponential potential $V_c$, can suppress phase-space escape over the parameter ranges explored in this work.
  Using direct numerical integration of the Hamiltonian equations of motion, Poincaré surfaces of section, and trajectory projections, we find that the ghost sector and nonlinear couplings generate a mixed phase-space structure with both regular islands and chaotic regions. The maximal Lyapunov exponent supports bounded chaotic motion: nearby trajectories separate exponentially while remaining confined to a finite region of phase space for the investigated initial conditions and parameters $(\varepsilon,α)$.
  These results suggest that nonlinear confinement can significantly alter the stability properties of negative-energy sectors at the classical level. They provide numerical evidence for a bounded-chaos regime in which ghost-induced divergences are avoided within the explored domain.

</details>

Method: 通过考察$\mathbb{RP}^{2}\times\mathbb{S}^{1}$上超对称理论配分函数的相等性，推导出一个新型beta型基本超几何积分恒等式。

Abstract: We derive a new beta-type basic hypergeometric integral identity from the equality of supersymmetric partition functions on $\mathbb{RP}^{2}\times\mathbb{S}^{1}$. Unlike previously known identities obtained from lens-space partition functions, this integral does not appear to arise as a degeneration of the lens elliptic beta integral. Our result enriches the collection of basic hypergeometric beta integrals arising from supersymmetric dualities and has applications to supersymmetric gauge theories, integrable models, and the theory of special functions.

### [17] [Gluon mass and small-x dynamics in hadrons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29455)
*Stanisław D. Głazek*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种通过引入胶子质量参数（gluon mass parameter）和辅助色八重态标量场（auxiliary color-octet scalar field）来正则化并消除量子色动力学（QCD）前形式哈密顿量中强于对数的发散（尤其是小x发散）的方法，并展示了该方法在散射振幅计算和重夸克束缚态本征值问题中的应用，以及对禁闭（confinement）概念和轻夸克动力学拓展的启示。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出使用胶子质量参数（gluon mass parameter）和一个对应于纵向极化胶子（longitudinally polarized gluons）的辅助色八重态标量场（auxiliary color-octet scalar field）来正则化并消除这些发散；当质量参数趋于零时，辅助场从强子组分动力学中退耦合，满足规范理论（gauge theory）要求。该方法同样适用于消除自相互作用中的二次紫外横向发散（quadratic ultraviolet transverse divergences）。

Result: 在重夸克（heavy quarks）有效哈密顿量的二阶弱耦合展开（second-order weak-coupling expansion）中已得到初步结果，包括在胶子质量参数趋于零的有效理论中禁闭（confinement）概念的建立，以及对将哈密顿量方法扩展到轻夸克（light quarks）动力学的启发性设想。

Conclusion: 该正则化方法有效解决了QCD前形式中强于对数的发散和小x发散问题，且能与规范理论的自洽性要求兼容；已为重夸克有效理论中的禁闭研究提供了基础，并为未来将哈密顿量方法推广至轻夸克体系指明了方向。

Abstract: Precise derivation of the logarithmically scale-dependent Hamiltonian eigenstate picture for hadrons in the space of virtual quark and gluon states of the canonical front form of QCD requires addressing first the problem of divergences stronger than logarithmic, and especially the small-x divergences in the dynamics of gluons. We propose to facilitate the regularization and cancellation of these divergences using a gluon mass parameter and an auxiliary color-octet scalar field corresponding to the longitudinally polarized gluons. The auxiliary field decouples from the hadronic constituent dynamics when the mass parameter tends to zero, as required in the gauge theory. The same method applies in the cancellation of the quadratic ultraviolet transverse divergences in the self-interactions. After explaining how the method works in computations of the scattering amplitudes, we describe its application to the bound-state eigenvalue problems. We focus on the results it leads to already in the second-order weak-coupling expansion for effective Hamiltonians of heavy quarks. They include the concept of confinement in an effective theory with the gluon mass parameter sent to zero and a heuristic scenario concerning extension of the Hamiltonian approach to the dynamics of light quarks.

### [18] [Observables in Schrödinger CFTs: How Aliens Built the Pyramids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29539)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在揭示薛定谔共形场论（Schrödinger CFT）中可观测量的代数结构，特别是零质量（或粒子数）算符所呈现的独特表示形式，从而深化对非相对论性共形场论（non-relativistic CFT）理论空间的理解。

Method: 作者利用双重态-算符对应（doubled state-operator correspondence）框架，系统分析了由“外来算符”（alien operators）构建的“金字塔表示”（pyramid representations）。此外，通过与洛伦兹CFT中的双重扭算符（double-twist operators）进行类比，并结合交叉通道（cross-channel）图像，处理了无质量粒子带来的系统性修正。

Result: 论文发现外来算符在代数结构上等价于洛伦兹CFT中的双重扭算符；当系统存在无质量粒子时，交叉通道会对这些算符产生系统性修正。此外，该结构还推广了Bekaert、Meunier和Moroz以及Golkar和Son提出的异常对称性守恒律。

Conclusion: 这项工作为理解非相对论性CFT的空间结构和热物理提供了新的视角，并建立了两类不同共形场论（相对论性与非相对论性）之间在算符代数上的深层联系。

Abstract: We discuss the algebraic structure of observables in Schrödinger CFTs. These operators have zero mass (or particle number) and generically transform in staggered ''pyramid representations'' built from ''alien operators,'' as we explain with the doubled state-operator correspondence. We comment on implications for the space of non-relativistic CFTs, thermal physics, and generalize the exceptional symmetry conservation laws of Bekaert, Meunier, and Moroz, and Golkar and Son. We show that alien operators are analogous to double-twist operators in Lorentzian CFT, with systematic cross-channel corrections from massless particles when they exist.

Method: 采用全息对偶方法，在AdS/CFT对应（AdS/CFT correspondence）框架下计算运动热规范理论中的全息纠缠熵，并系统分析化学势、温度及速度对纠缠熵的影响。

Result: 当化学势增大时，足够高的速度会增强全息纠缠熵；但在高温高速度条件下，化学势的依赖性几乎完全消失，热涨落占据主导；在极端相对论区域，纠缠熵随速度快速增长，速度成为压倒热贡献与化学贡献的主导参数。

Conclusion: 在运动热规范理论中，速度是调控全息纠缠熵的关键因素，极端相对论下热效应与化学势效应均被速度所压制。

Abstract: We have studied holographic entanglement entropy in a moving thermal gauge theory with a non-zero chemical potential. A sufficiently high velocity enhances the holographic entanglement entropy, particularly for larger values of the chemical potential. However, at high temperature and velocity, the chemical potential dependence is almost entirely washed out, indicating that thermal fluctuations dominate over charge-density effects. In the ultrarelativistic regime, the holographic entanglement entropy grows very rapidly with velocity, which emerges as the dominant parameter, largely suppressing both thermal and chemical contributions.

### [20] [Asymptotic boundary structure of Lagrangian gauge theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29587)
*Ivan Dneprov,Maxim Grigoriev,Mikhail Markov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究带边界规范理论（gauge theory）中预辛结构（presymplectic structure）的发散问题，提出通过Q-上循环（Q-cocycle）方法将体区域预辛结构重整化为边界规范PDE（gauge PDE）上的一对相容上循环——重整化上循环与反常上循环（anomaly cocycle），并将该形式体系应用于AdS和Minkowski时空中的标量场和麦克斯韦场（Maxwell field），表明AdS情形下的反常预辛结构自然导出全息外尔反常（holographic Weyl anomaly）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在带边界的局域规范理论中，边界自然定义另一规范理论，而体区域（bulk）的预辛结构是构造哈密顿形式的基础。然而在平空间全息（holography）框架下，无穷远（渐近）边界处的预辛结构发散，使得拉格朗日体系（Lagrangian system）向边界的延伸变得微妙，亟需系统化重整化方案。

Method: 利用规范PDE（gauge PDE）框架，证明体区域中的任意Q-上循环（尤其是预辛结构）在边界规范PDE上确定一对相容的Q-上循环：同鬼度（ghost-degree）的重整化上循环与低一度的反常上循环。反常上循环的构造类似于b-几何（b-geometry）中的留数映射（residue map）。

Result: 在AdS时空中，由反常预辛结构自然导出的作用量正是AdS/CFT语境下的全息外尔反常；在零无穷远（null infinity）情形中，该结果仅在少数特例中曾被认知。标量场和麦克斯韦场在AdS和Minkowski空间中的计算验证了一般形式体系的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文建立了带渐近边界规范理论的预辛结构重整化框架，统一处理了AdS和Minkowski时空中的边界反常，为全息对偶中的拉格朗日体系提供了一种系统的代数构造方法。

Abstract: Given a local gauge theory on spacetime with boundary, it naturally defines another gauge theory which can be regarded as a theory of the boundary values. For Lagrangian theories, it comes equipped with the presymplectic structure which can be used to define one or another version of Hamiltonian-like formulation of the initial model. This relation is especially manifest for AKSZ sigma models and more-generally gauge PDEs with compatible presymplectic structure in which case the boundary system is again a gauge PDE with presymplectic structure. In the context of (flat space) holography one is interested in boundaries at infinity, also known as asymptotic boundaries. The gauge PDE framework naturally extends to this setup, resulting in the notion of gauge PDE with asymptotic boundaries. Although this works perfectly well at the level of equations of motion, the extension to Lagrangian systems appears quite subtle because the presymplectic structure capturing the Lagrangian is divergent at the boundary. We show that any $Q$-cocycle in the bulk (and presymplectic structure in particular) determines a pair of compatible $Q$-cocycles of the boundary gauge PDE: the renormalized one of the same ghost-degree, and the anomaly cocycle of degree one lower. For the latter, the construction is somewhat analogous to the residue map known in the context of b-geometry. The general formalism is exemplified by scalar and Maxwell fields on AdS and Minkowski spaces. It turns out that in the AdS case the natural action determined by the anomaly presymplectic structure is precisely the one known as the holographic Weyl anomaly in the AdS/CFT context while its null-infinity counterpart was known in a few very particular cases only.

### [21] [Landau's Leviathans](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29612)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在确定多圈（multi-loop）多尺度费曼积分朗道奇点时面临消元（elimination）计算量过大的瓶颈，导致无法处理复杂的非平面图和全质量图。作者的核心动机是开发一种计算上可行、能够返回完整且真实奇点集的方法。

Method: 核心方法是通过在有限域（finite fields）上工作来实现必需的消元计算，从而解决多尺度积分在高圈前沿的计算瓶颈。具体而言，该方法通过检测与积分相关联的欧拉示数性（Euler characteristic）的下降点，直接读出朗道奇点。算法返回的奇点集在可检验条件约束下是真实且完整的。

Result: 该方法成功应用于超出当前方法能力范围的费恩曼积分：包括非平面六点两圈图和一个全质量三圈包络图。在这些例子中发现了多个新奇点，无论是在d维还是4维外部运动学（external kinematics）下，其复杂程度都超出此前已知的奇点结构。

Conclusion: 该算法为解析多圈费曼奇点提供了一种可行且系统化的技术方案，能够发现前所未有的复杂奇异结构，有望推动相关领域（如散射振幅分析）的进一步发展。

Abstract: We present a new method together with a proof-of-concept implementation for determining the Landau singularities of Feynman integrals, read off directly from where the Euler characteristic of the associated integral drops. Working over finite fields makes the requisite elimination tractable for multi-scale integrals at the multi-loop frontier. The algorithm returns the genuine and complete set of singularities, subject to a set of conditions which are practically testable. We apply these methods to classes of Feynman integrals beyond the reach of current methods, including non-planar six-point diagrams at two loops, as well as a fully massive three-loop envelope graph. Several of the newly found singularities, both in $d$- and 4-dimensional external kinematics, are of unexpected complexity when compared to previously known singularities for these examples.

Abstract: We derive parity-even transverse-traceless metric-like cubic vertices for massless bosonic higher-spin fields in AdS$_3$. ### [23] [Understanding Color Confinement through Quantum Reference Frames and Relational Observables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29668)
*Kei-Ichi Kondo*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于量子参考系（quantum reference frames, QRFs）和关系可观测量（relational observables）的色禁闭（color confinement）新表述。该方案认为色荷不是孤立的局域场，而是相对于色参考系或修整场（dressing field）的关系可观测量，从而解释了为何不存在孤立的带色渐近态（colored asymptotic sectors），并通过多个低维及降维模型提供了自洽性验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有色禁闭理论（如Kugo-Ojima图像）依赖于特定协变规范、未破缺的整体BRST对称性及具体的红外禁闭判据，缺乏一种不依赖于这些特定假设的普适性表述。本文基于量子参考系的视角，旨在提供一种关系性（relational）的色禁闭理解，统一现有的多种禁闭判据。

Method: 采用量子参考系（QRF）框架：将色荷视为相对于色参考系或修整场的关系可观测量，而非孤立局域场。通过高斯定律（Gauss law），局域色荷被排除在物理体代数（physical bulk algebra）之外，仅保留边界通量（boundary fluxes）和Wilson线（Wilson lines）等半局域数据。在(1+1)维杨-米尔斯理论、(1+1)维U(1)规范-希格斯模型，以及通过降维从四维SU(2)杨-米尔斯理论（限制在对称瞬子扇区）得到的二维U(1)规范-希格斯模型（在H²/AdS₂上）和三维SU(2)规范-希格斯模型（在H³/AdS₃上）中进行显式计算。

Result: QRF框架下的色禁闭特征在于：不存在全局良定义的远距离色参考系（long-distance color QRF）来支持孤立的非单态关系可观测量。该表述保留了Kugo-Ojima图像的洞察力，但避免了对特定协变规范、未破缺整体BRST对称性和特定红外禁闭判据的依赖。在多个低维和降维模型中的显式计算为表述的有效性提供了非平凡的一致性检验（nontrivial consistency checks）。

Conclusion: QRF框架下色禁闭提供了一种关系性表述，解释了为何孤立的带色渐近扇区（colored asymptotic sectors）不存在。该框架阐明了拓扑缺陷（topological defects）的作用，并表明其他禁闭判据——Wilson环面积律（Wilson-loop area law）、广义对称性（即中心一形式对称性，center one-form symmetry）的保持、以及剩余规范对称性（residual gauge symmetry）的恢复——均可组织为同一QRF结构的体现。论文还展望了该框架在四维杨-米尔斯理论和规范-希格斯理论中的应用前景。

Abstract: We present a formulation for understanding color confinement on the basis of quantum reference frames (QRFs) and relational observables. In the QRF approach to color confinement, colored quantities are not defined as isolated local fields, but rather as relational observables with respect to a color frame or a dressing field. By the Gauss law, local color charge is excluded from the physical bulk algebra, whereas semi-local data such as boundary fluxes and Wilson lines may remain. Color confinement is characterized by the absence of a globally well-defined long-distance color QRF capable of supporting isolated non-singlet relational observables. This formulation preserves the insight of the Kugo-Ojima type picture, while avoiding dependence on a particular covariant gauge, an unbroken global BRST symmetry, and a specific infrared confinement criterion. As concrete examples, we consider (1+1)-dim. Yang-Mills theory, (1+1)-dim. U(1) gauge-Higgs model, and the two-dim. U(1) gauge-Higgs model on $\mathbb{H}^2$ ($AdS_2$) and three-dim. SU(2) gauge-Higgs model on $\mathbb{H}^3$ ($AdS_3$) obtained by dimensional reduction of four-dim. SU(2) Yang-Mills theory restricted to symmetric-instanton sectors. Through explicit calculations in these examples and in controlled sectors, we provide nontrivial consistency checks for the validity of the present formulation. We also discuss prospects for four-dim. Yang-Mills theory and gauge-Higgs theories. QRF-based color confinement provides a relational formulation of why isolated colored asymptotic sectors are absent. At the same time, it clarifies the role played by topological defects and shows that other confinement criteria -- the Wilson-loop area law, the preservation of generalized symmetry, namely center one-form symmetry, and the restoration of residual gauge symmetry -- can be organized as manifestations of a common QRF structure.

</details>


### [24] [CFT Constraints on the Weak Gravity Conjecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29896)
*Saeed Noori Gashti,Behnam Pourhassan,İzzet Sakallı*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过AdS/CFT对偶中的边界计算，在dRGT有质量引力和爱因斯坦-ModMax非线性电动力学两类非Reissner–Nordström黑洞背景下证明了弱重力猜想（WGC），并进一步放松了dRGT推导中的简化假设，揭示了修正项对WGC界限的重整化影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弱重力猜想（Weak Gravity Conjecture, WGC）是量子引力自洽性的重要沼泽地判据，但其在非理想化黑洞背景下的普适性尚不明确。本文旨在利用AdS/CFT对应（AdS/CFT correspondence）的边界计算工具，检验WGC是否在更一般的引力与物质耦合体系中成立。

Method: 通过静态球对称dRGT有质量引力黑洞与爱因斯坦-ModMax非线性电动力学对偶黑洞的度规和规范场，构建带电Klein–Gordon方程，并在近视界（near-horizon）标度极限下将径向方程化为Whittaker形式，从边界推迟格林函数（retarded Green's function）的极点中提取体拟正则模（quasinormal modes）的虚部，从而导出阻尼时间不等式。

Result: 在dRGT黑洞中，所有有质量引力参数（α, β, m_g, h）均被消去，得到普适饱和界限 q/(m r_+) ≥ 1/√2 ≈ 0.707；在爱因斯坦-ModMax黑洞中，对偶对称非线性参数γ保留，得到界限 q/(m r_+) ≥ e^{-γ/2}，在Maxwell极限（γ→0）下退化为Reissner–Nordström界限1。放松dRGT推导中的精确极值性、最小耦合和高阶曲率项假设后，各修正项使界限重新依赖于m_g, α, β。

Conclusion: WGC在超出Reissner–Nordström理想化的两类黑洞体系中仍然成立，且界限量级为1。非线性效应（如ModMax参数γ）会单调削弱界限；dRGT中的简化假设一旦放松，修正项便以受控的函数形式重新进入界限，表明WGC的普适性依赖于理论的具体结构。

Abstract: The Weak Gravity Conjecture (WGC) is a swampland criterion of long standing: any consistent theory of quantum gravity must contain a charged particle whose charge-to-mass ratio exceeds that of an extremal black hole, so that gravity remains the weakest force. The AdS/CFT correspondence offers a calculable boundary handle on bulk gravity, and the imaginary parts of bulk quasinormal modes are read off the boundary as poles of a retarded Green's function. We show that the WGC follows from this boundary calculation in two settings that fall outside the Reissner--Nordström idealisation: static spherically symmetric black holes in dRGT massive gravity, and dyonic black holes in Einstein--ModMax non-linear electrodynamics. The chain runs from the metric and gauge field, through the charged Klein--Gordon equation, into a near-horizon scaling limit whose radial equation reduces to Whittaker form; the conformal weight $ν_0$ then enters a damping-time inequality. For the dRGT black hole every massive-gravity parameter ($α,β,m_g,h$) cancels out, leaving the universal saturation $q/(m r_+) \geq 1/\sqrt{2} \approx 0.707$. For the Einstein--ModMax black hole the duality-symmetric non-linearity parameter $γ$ survives, and yields $q/(m r_+) \geq e^{-γ/2}$, which reduces to the Reissner--Nordström bound $q/(m r_+) \geq 1$ in the Maxwell limit $γ\to 0$. Either result is of order unity, and the second weakens monotonically as the non-linearity grows. We then relax three of the simplifying assumptions of the dRGT derivation, namely exact extremality, minimal coupling, and the absence of higher-curvature terms. The cancellation breaks. Each correction reintroduces $m_g,α,β$ into the bound through a controlled functional dependence, and we tabulate and plot the relaxed forms across parameter space.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大质量 p 形式规范理论（gauge theories of massive p-forms）之间存在多种经典对偶性（dualities），但这些对偶性可能在量子层面被打破。本文旨在通过路径积分量子化，具体研究拓扑耦合的 BF 理论中对偶性的量子破坏机制。

Method: 采用路径积分量子化（path integral quantisation）方法，对 d 维拓扑耦合的 BF 理论进行量子化；通过积分掉其中一个形式，计算所得行列式，并引入反项（counterterms）来重整化（renormalise）其发散。行列式的计算依赖于时空拓扑数（topological numbers）。

Result: 在拓扑非平凡背景（topologically non-trivial backgrounds）上，大质量理论之间的量子对偶性被明确打破。该破坏与积分掉的规范形式与其纵向模式（longitudinal modes）之间无质量对偶性的量子破坏直接相关。特别地，反项之差与时空的欧拉示性数（Euler characteristic）成正比。

Conclusion: 引力瞬子（gravitational instantons）的存在表明，即使在闵可夫斯基时空（Minkowski space）中，当存在拓扑涨落（topological fluctuations）时，这些对偶性也可能被破坏。

Abstract: Gauge theories of massive $p$-forms are connected by various dualities, which hold classically but may be broken at the quantum level. One example is the $BF$ theory of topologically coupled $p$- and $(d-p-1)$-forms in $d$ dimensions, where the coupling between forms results in a manifestly gauge invariant mass term for either form when the other is integrated out classically. We perform the path integral quantisation of this theory; by integrating out one of the forms, the resulting determinants are sensitive to the topology of spacetime, and counterterms must be introduced to renormalise their divergences. We compute these determinants in terms of the topological numbers of spacetime, showing explicitly how the quantum duality of the massive theories is broken on topologically non-trivial backgrounds. This is directly related to the quantum breaking of the massless duality between the form that was integrated out and the longitudinal modes of its partner. In particular, the difference of counterterms is proportional to the Euler characteristic of spacetime. The existence of gravitational instantons suggests that these dualities may be broken even in Minkowski space in the presence of topological fluctuations.

### [26] [Nonlinear nature of near-equilibrium viscous fluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30043)
*Yan Liu,Hao-Tian Sun*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了d+1维中性相对论性粘性流体（neutral relativistic viscous fluid）的晚期弛豫行为，发现非线性分析预测声模（sound mode）的衰减律为$e^{-nω_I t}$，而非线性化流体动力学（linearized hydrodynamics）预测的$e^{-n^2ω_I t}$。作者推导出一个闭环渐近吸引子解（closed asymptotic attractor solution），其中第n次谐波的频率锁定为基模复数频率的n倍，能量流振幅满足级联关系$J_n=α_J^{\,n-1}J_1^n$。该吸引子的存在表明，即使在近平衡态，场幂次（field powers）与振幅阶数（amplitude order）也不等价。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究中性相对论性粘性流体在长时间尺度下的弛豫行为，特别是线性化流体动力学与非线性分析在声模衰减律上的预测分歧。

Method: 通过非线性分析推导出一个闭环渐近吸引子解，揭示第n次谐波频率锁定于基模复数频率的n倍，并导出能量流振幅之间的级联关系$J_n=α_J^{\,n-1}J_1^n$，其中系数$α_J$由状态方程（equation of state）、纵向粘性（longitudinal viscosity）和基波数决定。

Result: 线性化流体动力学预测声模按$e^{-n^2ω_I t}$衰减，而非线性分析给出衰减律为$e^{-nω_I t}$。对于共形流体（conformal fluids），$α_J=1/(8ηk)$，与arXiv:2512.07242的全息结果（holographic result）一致。

Conclusion: 吸引子的存在表明，即使在近平衡态，场幂次与振幅阶数并不等价，暗示非线性效应在流体弛豫过程中具有不可忽略的作用。

Abstract: We study the late-time relaxation of a neutral relativistic viscous fluid in $d+1$ dimensions. In the long-wavelength regime, linearized hydrodynamics predicts that the sound mode at momentum $nk$ decays as $e^{-n^2ω_I t}$. However, nonlinear analysis gives a decay of $e^{-nω_I t}$. We derive a closed asymptotic attractor solution in which the frequency of the $n$-th harmonic locks to $n$ times the complex frequency of the fundamental mode. The amplitude envelopes for energy current $J$ obey a simple cascading relation, $J_n=α_J^{\,n-1}J_1^n$, with $α_J$ fixed by the equation of state, the longitudinal viscosity, and the fundamental wavenumber. For conformal fluids, $α_J=1/(8ηk)$, in agreement with the holographic result of arXiv:2512.07242. The existence of the attractor shows that, even near equilibrium, field powers are not equivalent to amplitude order.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在规范/引力对偶（gauge/gravity duality）框架下，针对具有大能级层次和假真空特征的强耦合量子场论（strongly coupled quantum field theory），现有的PINNs全息逆问题方法尚无法处理这类涉及非平凡热力学行为和跳过重整化群流（skipping renormalization group flows）的新物理区域。

Method: 在已有PINNs方法基础上，发展了一套方法论改进，用于从边界热力学数据反向重建体标量势；该方法专门应对近简并态（near-degenerate states）、大能量层次（large hierarchies of energy scales）以及未被输入数据直接探测到的势能区域等挑战。

Abstract: We investigate the reconstruction of holographic duals for strongly coupled quantum field theories in regimes characterized by large hierarchies and the presence of false vacua. Within the gauge/gravity duality, these features translate into non-trivial thermodynamic behaviour and exotic renormalization group flows, including skipping flows between non-adjacent fixed points. Building on previous work based on Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs), we extend the holographic inverse problem of reconstructing the bulk scalar potential from boundary thermodynamic data into this new regime. This setting presents a variety of conceptual and numerical challenges, such as near-degenerate states, large hierarchies of energy scales, and regions of the potential that are not directly probed by the input data. We develop a set of methodological advances that overcome these obstacles, thereby improving the established PINNs-based methodology and extending it to new physical regimes of interest that were previously out of reach. Applying the developed framework, we demonstrate accurate reconstruction of scalar potentials deep into the false vacuum regime, achieving robust agreement with the physical features of the underlying thermodynamics despite significant numerical stiffness. Our results extend the bridge between holography and machine learning, and suggest that data-driven approaches can provide new insights into the structure of strongly coupled systems.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一种二次型无量纲规范变换（quadratic dimensionless gauge transformation），将其应用于复标量场、阿贝尔（Abelian）理论和非阿贝尔（Non-Abelian）理论，系统检验各理论的不变性；辅以显式图形分析（graphical analysis）来可视化不变性行为；详细研究协变导数（covariant derivative）在局域对称性操作下确保一致变换的必要性。

Conclusion: 协变导数（covariant derivative）是保证局域规范对称性下物理定律形式不变的关键工具，对协变性（covariance）的理解应落实为变换过程中物理定律形式得以保持。

Abstract: Symmetries plays a significant role in understanding the conservation laws in Quantum field theories. Here, we attempted a quadratic type dimensionless gauge transformation to achieve the invariance in QFTs. We have shown the extensive study of invariance of complex scalar, Abelian and Non- Abelian theories and established the conservation laws. We included an explicit graphical analysis to invoke the invariance. This is studied in a physical context, where different field configurations correspond to the same physical state. The necessity of the covariant derivative is studied in detail, highlighting how it ensures consistent transformation under local symmetry operations. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于高斯态（Gaussian states）的Kähler结构框架，计算了部分转置受限线性复结构（partially-transposed restricted linear complex structure）算符的对角化；通过将特征值问题重构为复平面上的边值问题（boundary value problem）实现了显式对角化；并提出了转置运算（transpose operation）的基无关定义以扩展该框架的方法。

Result: 完全刻画了(1+1)维无质量标量场真空态中两个任意紧致类空分离区域之间的纠缠负性（logarithmic negativity）及其携带模式（negativity cores）。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法可推广至更高维度和费米子场（fermionic fields），为进一步研究量子场的纠缠结构提供了可扩展的分析工具。

Abstract: Quantum fields exhibit a rich entanglement structure which is still not fully understood. In this work, we study the entanglement structure of the vacuum state of a massless scalar field in (1+1)-dimensions -- a paradigmatic case for both high energy and condensed matter physics. We fully characterize the entanglement negativity between two arbitrary compact spacelike-separated regions of the field by calculating the logarithmic negativity along with the modes carrying it, called negativity cores. We achieve this using a framework based on the Kähler structure of Gaussian states, wherein we calculate the diagonalization of the operator associated with the partially-transposed restricted linear complex structure. In doing so, we extend the methods of this framework by proposing a basis-independent definition of the transpose operation. The explicit diagonalization we perform is enabled by a reformulation of the eigenvalue problem as a boundary value problem in the complex plane. Our results also suggest extensions to higher dimensions and fermionic fields.

### [30] [Complex Phase Structure and Widom line for Euler Heisenberg black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30233)
*Mozib Bin Awal,Prabwal Phukon*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在Lee-Yang相变理论框架下研究欧拉-海森堡AdS黑洞的超临界热力学，发现该体系存在两个不同的临界点及一个合并后的退化高阶临界点，通过复分析揭示了李-杨奇点的分布和复相图结构，并在退化临界点处发现了无共存曲线情况下的Widom线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索欧拉-海森堡AdS黑洞在超临界区域的热力学相结构，并利用Lee-Yang相变理论（Lee-Yang phase transition theory）揭示复平面奇点结构与Widom线（Widom line）之间的深层联系，从而深化对超临界相变现象的理解。

Method: 将热力学描述延拓至复域（complex domain），通过分析Lee-Yang奇点（Lee-Yang singularities）的分布构建复相图（complex phase diagram）；重点关注双临界点体系以及退化高阶临界点（degenerate higher-order critical point）的奇点结构。

Result: 该体系存在两个不同的临界点（critical points），对应一个四相热力学结构；两个临界点合并后形成一个退化高阶临界点。在退化临界点处，尽管不存在传统的共存曲线（coexistence curve），仍然出现了一条明确的Widom线作为超临界区域的有效稳定性边界。在双临界点体系中，复相图显示出两条不同的Widom线，其中一条与共存曲线关联，另一条仅源于复奇点结构。Lee-Yang形式体系能够一致地再现单临界点体系和无临界性条件下的预期相结构。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了丰富的超临界相结构，为理解Widom线的起源和物理诠释提供了新的视角，并验证了Lee-Yang形式体系在处理多种临界点构型时的普适性和一致性。

Abstract: We investigate the supercritical thermodynamics of Euler-Heisenberg AdS black holes within the framework of Lee-Yang phase transition theory. We show that the system admits two distinct critical points associated with a four-phase thermodynamic structure and identify a degenerate higher-order critical point where the two criticalities merge. Extending the thermodynamic description into the complex domain, we determine the distribution of Lee-Yang singularities and construct the corresponding complex phase diagrams. At the degenerate critical point, we find that a well-defined Widom line emerges despite the absence of a conventional coexistence curve, acting as an effective stability boundary in the supercritical regime. In the two-critical-point regime, the complex phase diagram exhibits two distinct Widom lines, one associated with a coexistence curve and the other arising solely from the complex singularity structure. We further show that the Lee-Yang formalism consistently reproduces the expected phase structure for systems with a single critical point and in the absence of criticality. Our results reveal a rich supercritical phase structure and provide new insights into the origin and physical interpretation of Widom lines.

</details>

Conclusion: 基于上述结果，本文推测该抵消机制可能具有更广泛的普适性，而不仅限于当前检验的特定例子。

Abstract: Recent works have pointed out the existence of a holographic constraint on (extremal) three-point functions of scalar moduli in scale-separated AdS vacua. Moreover, it has been shown that this constraint is satisfied in the DGKT scenario in massive type IIA for the original $\mathbb{T}^6/(\mathbb{Z}_3 \times \mathbb{Z}_3)$ orbifold, as a result of a series of unexpected cancellations. ### [32] [Positivity properties of observables in planar maximally supersymmetric Yang-Mills theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30368)
*Maximilian Haensch*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究平面N=4超杨-米尔斯理论（planar N=4 super Yang-Mills）中精确可观测量作为't Hooft耦合函数的Stieltjes性质（正性谱测度上的单减色散表示），通过解析证明和数值证据展示了该性质对多种可观测量成立，并利用该性质从微扰输入推导出非微扰界和强耦合展开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受量子力学中类似结果的启发，探究平面N=4超杨-米尔斯理论中精确可观测量是否在't Hooft耦合上具有正谱测度（positive spectral measure）的单减色散表示（once-subtracted dispersion representation），即Stieltjes性质（Stieltjes property）。

Method: 通过积分表示（integral representations）对八边形反常维数（octagon anomalous dimension）、圆形威尔逊环对数（logarithm of the circular Wilson loop）、轫致辐射函数（Bremsstrahlung function）及BMN极限下的反常维数进行解析证明；对尖点反常维数（cusp anomalous dimension）和倾斜尖点反常维数（tilted cusp anomalous dimension）提供数值证据；利用Mellin-Barnes表示（Mellin-Barnes representation）从单减色散表示恢复强耦合展开及其非微扰修正。

Result: Stieltjes性质对多种精确可观测量成立（解析证明或数值证据支持），同时识别出该性质不成立的量并研究了较弱的完全单调性（complete monotonicity）。该性质可用于将微扰输入转化为严格的非微扰界（rigorous non-perturbative bounds），以及自举微扰系数（bootstrap perturbative coefficients）。

Conclusion: Stieltjes性质为平面N=4超杨-米尔斯理论中的可观测量提供了连接微扰与非微扰区域的强大分析工具，并可推广到从弱耦合数据估计强耦合展开的方法。

Abstract: We study positivity properties of exact observables in planar N=4 super Yang-Mills as functions of the 't Hooft coupling. Motivated by analogous results in quantum mechanics, we ask whether such observables admit a once-subtracted dispersion representation in the coupling over a positive spectral measure. Our main result is that this property, also known as the Stieltjes property, holds for a broad class of exact observables. We prove it analytically, through integral representations, for the octagon anomalous dimension, the logarithm of the circular Wilson loop, the Bremsstrahlung function, and anomalous dimensions in the BMN limit, and we provide numerical evidence for the cusp and tilted cusp anomalous dimensions. We also identify quantities for which the Stieltjes property does not hold, and study the weaker positivity property of complete monotonicity. The Stieltjes property yields two powerful consequences: it lets us turn perturbative input into rigorous non-perturbative bounds, and bootstrap perturbative coefficients. We also show how the strong-coupling expansion and its non-perturbative corrections can be recovered from the once-subtracted dispersion representation via a Mellin-Barnes representation and outline a method to estimate the strong-coupling expansion from weak-coupling data.

### [33] [Loop-level dipole currents and the renormalized hard celestial current algebra in QED](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30431)
*Ruiliang Li*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在红外减除的阿贝尔规范场论中，确定了归一化单圈对数软光子算符的有限能量作用，并通过Mellin差硬流之间的对易关系，建立了与长程天体OPE的有限能量联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在红外减除的阿贝尔规范理论中，理解单圈对数软光子算符的有限能量作用及其与硬流（hard current）之间的代数结构，是建立天体OPE（celestial OPE）与普通规范场论之间严格对应关系的关键。

Method: 利用归一化单圈对数软光子算符的有限能量作用，通过Mellin差硬流（Mellin-difference hard currents）的对易子提取出方案无关的硬-硬留数（hard-hard residue）；借助双粒子Plancherel变换（two-particle Plancherel transform）与亚纯延拓（meromorphic continuation）将该留数识别为解析双粒子初级模（analytic two-particle primary module），其系数映射构成硬流单上循环（hard-current one-cocycle），定义最小滤过阿贝尔扩张（minimal filtered abelian extension），并积分得到仿射作用（affine action）。

Result: 对于标量硬腿情形，固定腿算符与Choi-Kadhe-Puhm的对称性支配的长程对数塔系数一致；应用于树图标量QED光子交换块时，该构造从普通硬振幅和普适软核（universal soft kernel）确定了对数双粒子系数泛函，从而建立了偶极流Ward恒等式（dipole-current Ward identity）与指数化长程天体OPE之间的有限能量关系。

Conclusion: 本文的工作为红外减除规范理论中的软光子算符与天体OPE之间的代数对应提供了严格的构造性证明，并给出了有限能量下的可计算关系。

Abstract: We determine the finite-energy action of the normalized one-loop logarithmic soft-photon operator in an infrared-subtracted abelian gauge theory. Its commutator with Mellin-difference hard currents has a scheme-independent hard-hard residue that survives every one-particle redefinition. With the meromorphic continuation stated explicitly below, a two-particle Plancherel transform identifies this residue with an analytic two-particle primary module, and the coefficient map is a hard-current one-cocycle. The cocycle defines a minimal filtered abelian extension. It has a canonical two-particle primitive and integrates to an affine action. For scalar hard legs, the fixed-leg operator agrees coefficient by coefficient with the symmetry-governed long-range logarithmic tower of Choi, Kadhe, and Puhm. Applied to a tree-level scalar-QED photon-exchange block, the construction determines the logarithmic two-particle coefficient functional from the ordinary hard amplitude and the universal soft kernel. This gives a finite-energy relation between the dipole-current Ward identity and the exponentiated long-range celestial OPE.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: PEE线程（PEE threads）构成的网络可作为全息张量网络的几何基础，从而在引力子区域中实现表面-态对应和广义纠缠楔。

Abstract: It is well-known in integral geometry that a maximally symmetric Riemannian manifold, such as a static slice of vacuum AdS spacetime, can be perfectly covered by the geodesics in the Kinematic space, which we call the partial-entanglement-entropy (PEE) threads. In this context, the area of a codimension-one surface in the manifold can be computed by counting its intersections with the PEE threads, which is the celebrated Crofton formula. In this paper, we analyze the Kinematic space for a generic subregion in vacuum AdS space, and propose that the PEE threads emanate from a co-dimension one surface can perfectly cover a subregion in the manifold. Furthermore, we build holographic tensor network models on the network of the PEE threads confined in a subregion, thereby providing a concrete framework that realizes the surface-state correspondence and the generalized entanglement wedges for gravitational subregions.

Possible connections to the thermal bootstrap, multiloop calculations, integrability, AdS/CFT and string theory are briefly discussed. This is a proceedings contribution to the Athens Workshop in Theoretical Physics: 10th Anniversary, held at the National and Kapodistrian University of Athens on December 17--19 2025.

### [38] [Transition asymptotics for the real solutions of the sinh-Gordon Painlevé III equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28579)
*Kenta Miyahara,Maxim L. Yattselev*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文研究了定义在正半轴上的 sinh-Gordon Painlevé III 方程实值解的渐近行为，特别分析了当参数 $x$ 与 $p$ 同时趋于无穷时，由单值性参数（monodromy parameter）$p$ 和实参数 $s^{\mathbb{R}}$ 所参数化的解在不同标度区域之间发生的渐近过渡，揭示了从指数型到椭圆型再到三角型渐近行为的完整分类与转换条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前与 A. Its 的联合工作已刻画了当 $x\to\infty$ 时解的渐近行为，本文旨在进一步探索当 $x$ 与 $p$ 同时趋于无穷时（满足 $2\Im(p)=-s^{\mathbb R}$），奇异解（$|p|<\infty$）与光滑解（$p=\infty$）之间的过渡机制。

Method: 通过引入参数化关系 $|p|^2 = 1 + e^{2\varkappa x}$，将解的渐近行为按标度参数 $\varkappa$ 的不同取值区域进行分类分析，研究指数型、椭圆型（elliptic）与三角型（trigonometric）三种渐近形态之间的转换边界与条件。

Result: 发现光滑指数型渐近（smooth exponential asymptotics）在 $\varkappa>1$ 区域成立，且在 $\varkappa=2$ 处主导项阶数发生变化；在 $\varkappa=1$ 处指数型行为过渡为椭圆型渐近（elliptic asymptotics），后者在 $0<\varkappa<1$ 范围内均成立；当 $\varkappa$ 衰减至零时，椭圆型渐近退化为三角型渐近（trigonometric asymptotics），该三角型渐近对所有固定有界 $p$ 均成立。

Conclusion: 完整描述了 sinh-Gordon Painlevé III 方程实值解在 $(x,p)$ 联合大参数极限下的渐近相图（asymptotic phase diagram），明确了指数、椭圆、三角三种渐近区域及其转换边界，深化了对该可积系统（integrable system）解全局结构的理解。

Abstract: We consider solutions of the sinh-Gordon Painlevé III equation \[ u_{xx} + \frac{1}{x} u_x = \sinh u \] that are real on $(0,\infty)$. They are parametrized by the monodromy parameter $p\in\overline{\mathbb{C}}$, $|p|>1$, and an additional real parameter $s^{\mathbb{R}}$ when $p=\infty$. Our previous joint work with A. Its described the asymptotic behavior of these solutions as $x\to\infty$. Here, we describe the transition as $x, p\to \infty$, $2\Im(p)=-s^{\mathbb R}$, between singular solutions ($|p|<\infty$) and smooth solutions ($p=\infty$). In short, if we parametrize $|p|^2 = 1 + e^{2\varkappa x}$, then the smooth exponential asymptotics of the solutions extends to the region $\varkappa>1$, with a change of the leading order term at $\varkappa=2$; at $\varkappa=1$ the exponential behavior transitions into an elliptic asymptotics, which holds for all $0<\varkappa<1$; as $\varkappa$ decays to zero, elliptic asymptotics degenerates into trigonometric one, which holds for all $p$ fixed.

</details>


### [39] [Reduced Trilinear Reformulation of the Nakamura Conjecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29103)
*Takeshi Fukuyama*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本论文针对Tomimatsu-Sato时空族与Nakamura猜想中出现的混合导数结构，引入基于Z₃对称三线性Hirota算子的约化三线性表述，成功将Hirota双线性导数与普通一阶导数统一在该框架内，并展示了该表述自然继承Hirota型直接方法的结构特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Tomimatsu-Sato族是爱因斯坦方程的重要精确稳态轴对称真空解，其可积结构与Nakamura猜想中的n点Toda分子层次密切相关。然而，Nakamura猜想中的方程同时包含Hirota双线性导数（Hirota bilinear derivatives）与普通一阶导数项，无法完全在传统双线性代数框架内表述，这构成了理论整合的障碍。

Method: 引入基于Z₃对称三线性Hirota算子（Z₃-symmetric trilinear Hirota operators）约化扇区(a,b,c)→(a,b,1)的约化三线性表述（reduced trilinear formulation）。通过该框架，将Nakamura猜想中的Hirota双线性导数与普通导数项统一改写为约化三线性算子形式。

Result: 证明了约化三线性表述自然继承Hirota型直接方法（Hirota-type direct method）。传统双线性谱因子k_i−k_j被Z₃加权组合k_i+ωk_j和k_i+ω²k_j替代，形成了约化三线性层次特有的直接方法结构。

Conclusion: Tomimatsu-Sato层次的Toda分子描述可被视为更广泛三线性框架的约化扇区，这为稳态轴对称引力（stationary axisymmetric gravity）的可积结构提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: The Tomimatsu--Sato (TS) family, characterized by the rotation parameter $q$ and the TS index $δ=n,$ provides an important class of exact stationary axisymmetric vacuum solutions of Einstein's equations, whose integrable structure is known to be closely related to the $n$-point Toda molecule hierarchy through the Nakamura Conjecture. However, the set of equations appearing in the Nakamura Conjecture contains not only Hirota bilinear derivatives but also ordinary first-derivative terms, and therefore is not formulated entirely within the conventional bilinear algebra.
  In this paper we introduce a reduced trilinear formulation based on the reduced sector $(a,b,c)\rightarrow(a,b,1)$ of the $Z_3$-symmetric trilinear Hirota operators. We show that both the Hirota bilinear derivatives and the ordinary derivatives appearing in the Nakamura Conjecture can be rewritten completely within this reduced trilinear framework. Consequently, the set of equations admits a formulation in terms of reduced trilinear operators.
  We further show that the reduced trilinear formulation naturally inherits a Hirota-type direct method. The conventional bilinear spectral factor $k_i-k_j$ is replaced by the $Z_3$-weighted combinations $k_i+ωk_j$ and $k_i+ω^2k_j$, providing a direct-method structure characteristic of the reduced trilinear hierarchy.
  These results suggest that the Toda-molecule description of the Tomimatsu--Sato hierarchy may be viewed as a reduced sector of a broader trilinear framework, and provide a new perspective on the integrable structure of stationary axisymmetric gravity.

</details>

Method: 基于整数格点 $\mathbb{Z}^k$ 中可见点集的定义，采用衍射理论中的傅里叶分析方法，推导从有限个格点 $\{\mathbf{x}_1,\dots,\mathbf{x}_n\}$ 同时可见的点集的衍射谱系数显式公式，并将该程序推广至特定类别的切割投影集。

Conclusion: 从有限个格点同时可见的点集具有结构化的衍射特征，且该结果可通过推广程序适用于更一般的切割投影集，表明这类集合在衍射理论中具有良好的谱性质。

Abstract: Let $k\geq 2$ be a positive integer. It is known that the set of visible lattice points from the origin in $\mathbb{Z}^k$ has a translation bounded pure point diffraction spectrum. We investigate these properties for sets of points simultaneously visible from a finite set of lattice points $ \{\mathbf{x}_1,\dots,\mathbf{x}_n\} \subseteq \mathbb{Z}^k$. We provide explicit formulas for the coefficients of the diffraction spectrum. Additionally, we generalize our procedure to show that the set of visible points from the origin in certain classes of cut-and-project sets has a translation bounded pure point diffraction spectrum.

### [41] [Peculiarities Of High-Speed Dynamics Of Two-Photon Absorption In Si Nanowire Waveguides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29127)
*Vadym Zayets,Siim Heinsalu,Akihiro Noriki*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本研究通过三种独立的高速测量技术，揭示了硅纳米线波导中双光子吸收（TPA）的完整动力学路径，发现非线性光子吸收、电子激发和自由载流子生成三个阶段的速率存在显著差异，与经典TPA模型的预测不符，表明TPA过程存在多个竞争路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典双光子吸收（two-photon absorption, TPA）模型假设非线性光子吸收、电子从价带激发到导带以及自由载流子生成这三个过程以相同速率发生，但这一假设尚未经过完整实验验证。本文旨在通过多种高速测量手段，系统探究硅纳米线波导中TPA的完整动力学路径，以检验经典模型的准确性。

Method: 采用三种独立的高速测量技术（high-speed measurement techniques），分别探测TPA过程的不同阶段：非线性光子吸收（nonlinear photon absorption）、电子从价带（valence band）到导带（conduction band）的激发，以及自由载流子（free carrier）的生成。

Result: 测量发现三个阶段的速率存在显著差异：非线性光子吸收量超过解释TPA跃迁所需值的两倍；测量的TPA跃迁数量远超自由载流子密度，表明大部分被激发的电子在短于13皮秒（ps）的时间尺度内快速复合回价带；三个阶段的饱和行为在不同光子密度下表现出明显差异。

Conclusion: TPA在硅中的实际动力学过程比经典模型描述得更为复杂，存在多个竞争路径。理解TPA的完整机制面临的主要障碍是虚拟带隙中间能级（virtual midgap level）的物理起源尚不明确。研究结果可为高速硅基光子电路（silicon photonic circuits）中抑制非线性损耗以及利用TPA实现高速光开关和光子信号处理提供策略参考。

Abstract: We investigate the complete dynamical pathway of photon-electron interactions involved in two-photon absorption (TPA) in a silicon nanowire waveguide using three independent high-speed measurement techniques. These methods probe different stages of the process: nonlinear photon absorption, electron excitation from the valence to the conduction band, and free-carrier generation. According to the conventional model of TPA, these three processes should occur at identical rates. However, our measurements reveal significant discrepancies between them. The measured nonlinear photon absorption is more than twice the value required to account for the measured TPA transitions, indicating the presence of additional absorption pathways or nontrivial TPA dynamics. Furthermore, the number of measured TPA transitions substantially exceeds the measured free-carrier density, indicating that long-lifetime free carriers represent only a small fraction of the TPA-excited electrons, while the majority recombine rapidly back to the valence band on a timescale shorter than 13 ps. In addition, the three stages of the TPA pathway exhibit distinct saturation behaviors at different photon densities, further indicating that the TPA process in silicon is more complex than described by the conventional model. These findings provide new insight into the physical mechanisms governing TPA, suggesting the existence of multiple competing pathways for this optical transition. A major obstacle to a complete understanding of TPA is the unclear physical origin of the virtual midgap level. The potential strategies for minimizing unwanted nonlinear losses in high-speed silicon photonic circuits, as well as for exploiting TPA in high-speed optical switching and photonic signal processing are investigated.

</details>


### [42] [Dynamic Topological Light Control in Reconfigurable Non-Hermitian Metastacks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29996)
*Ryan Hogan,Zihan Lu,Han Peng,Jie Zhou,Yanling Xiao,Shining Zhu,Hui Liu*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无需光刻的非厄米（non-Hermitian）平面亚稳态堆栈（metastack），利用温度与热滞作为主动合成维度（synthetic dimension），在二氧化钒（VO2）薄膜中驱动绝缘体-金属相变（insulator-metal transition），实现了可调谐的拓扑界面态和极化敏感光谱控制；尤其发现路径依赖的奇异点（exceptional points, EPs）及其热滞诱导的连续演化和简并汇聚，实验上展示了近单位反射率调制与8%可逆光谱移动等宽幅动态光学控制能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统超表面（metasurfaces）实现动态光学控制通常依赖复杂光刻工艺，制造门槛高、可扩展性受限。本文旨在提出一种无需光刻、CMOS兼容的平面结构，通过非厄米设计与主动合成维度来克服上述局限性。

Method: 采用分布式布拉格反射器（distributed Bragg reflector）与VO2薄膜构成的非厄米平面亚稳态堆栈，利用温度与热滞作为主动合成维度，借助VO2的绝缘体-金属相变来主动调控拓扑界面态（topological interface states），从而实现极化敏感的光谱控制。

Result: 系统支持路径依赖的奇异点（exceptional points, EPs）；中间热滞态产生了连续的热、冷EP对，并最终汇聚为单一简并EP。实验上观测到宽范围动态光学控制，包括可逆8%光谱移动与近单位反射率调制，并具备超快动力学潜力。

Conclusion: 该CMOS兼容设计为主动光子学（active photonics）与拓扑光子学（topological photonics）提供了一种可规模化、结构简单的实现平台，无需复杂光刻工艺。

Abstract: Metasurfaces often require complex lithography for dynamic optical control. To overcome this, we utilize a lithography-free, non-Hermitian planar metastack comprising a distributed Bragg reflector and a vanadium dioxide (VO2) thin film. By virtue of temperature and thermal hysteresis as an active synthetic dimension and exploiting the VO2 insulator-to-metal transition, we actively tune topological interface states to achieve polarization-sensitive spectral control. Notably, our system hosts path-dependent exceptional points (EPs); the intermediate hysteretic states generate a continuum of hot and cold EP pairs that ultimately converge into a single, degenerate EP. Furthermore, we experimentally observe wide-range dynamic optical control, comprising reversible 8% spectral shifts with near-unity reflectance modulation, alongside potential for ultrafast dynamics. Ultimately, our CMOS-compatible design provides a scalable, simple platform for active and topological photonics.
