# quant-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [43] [The Schrödinger equation in the complex plane and quantum entanglement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28640)
*Vassiliy Lubchenko*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文将薛定谔方程（Schrödinger equation）的连续性方程（continuity equation）推广至复空间，通过定义复动量（complex momentum）揭示了量子流体的涡旋结构，并由此自然地导出了精确量子化条件（quantization condition），以及零点振动（zero-point vibration）与动量极点（momentum pole）之间的内在联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子力学框架中，薛定谔方程的流（current）和动量（momentum）通常定义在实空间。作者希望将这一描述拓展至复空间（complex space），从而揭示波函数（wavefunction）零点与奇异结构之间的深层几何关系，并为量子化条件提供一种新的、基于流体动力学的视角。

Method: 作者在复空间中为薛定谔方程构建了连续性方程，通过将复流（complex current）以粒子密度（particle density）归一化，定义了一个复动量。该动量是经典运动动量（kinematic momentum）解析延拓（analytic continuation）到复平面的量子类比。基于此，分析了相位梯度流（phase-gradient flow）和运动动量流的不可压缩性与转动特性。

Result: 波函数的零点（zeros）在复动量中产生简单极点（simple poles），这些极点在相位梯度流中表现为无旋涡旋（irrotational vortex）；波函数的临界点（critical points）则在运动动量流中呈现刚体式旋转流（rigid body-like rotational flows）。极点数量自动为整数，由此天然体现了基本激发的离散性。导出的精确量子化条件在半经典极限（semiclassical limit）下退化为玻尔-索末菲条件（Bohr-Sommerfeld condition）。动能可分解为运动动量的平均值与涨落两部分之和，束缚态中的零点振动仅源于动量涨落，并在无穷远处表现为刚体流。

Conclusion: 动量极点——即波函数的零点——可被视为涌现现象（emergent），这与薛定谔方程驻波解（standing wave solutions）所展现的量子纠缠（quantum entanglement）性质一致。该工作为量子化条件和量子流体的几何结构提供了统一的理论描述。

Abstract: We formulate a continuity equation for the Schrödinger equation in the complex space. We define a complex momentum by normalizing the complex current by the particle density. This momentum is a quantum analog of the classical, kinematic momentum analytically continued into the complex plane. The kinematic momentum and the gradient of the wavefunction's phase each represent a fluid-like flow in the complex plane; the phase-gradient flow is incompressible. The zeros of the wavefunction give rise to simple poles in the momentum. The poles manifest as irrotational vortexes in the phase-gradient flow, while critical points of the wavefunction present as rigid body-like rotational flows of the kinematic momentum. A discrete nature of elementary excitations comes about inherently because the quantity of the poles is automatically integer. An exact quantization condition is subsequently formulated, which reduces to the Bohr-Sommerfeld condition in the semiclassical limit. We establish a priori that the Bohr-Sommerfeld condition must be exact for the Harmonic Oscillator. We show that the kinetic energy is a sum of contributions of the average value and fluctuations, respectively, of the kinematic momentum. The zero-point vibrations within bound states are solely due to the fluctuations of the momentum and manifest as rigid-body flows at infinity. The momentum poles -- and hence the wavefunction's zeros -- can be viewed as emergent, consistent with the remarkable property of quantum entanglement exhibited by standing wave solutions of the Schrödinger equation.

</details>


### [44] [Volume Law and Universality of Entanglement Entropy in Random Graph Fermi Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29304)
*Saikat Sur*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用随机矩阵理论与渐近自由性，证明了 Erdős–Rényi 随机图上自由费米子的基态纠缠熵在热力学极限下服从精确的体积律，并发现其纠缠密度具有普适系数（约 0.386 nats），严格低于 Page 值。该体积律源于随机图缺乏几何局域性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究随机图上自由费米子系统的基态纠缠熵（ground-state entanglement entropy）行为，特别是其是否遵循面积律（area law）或体积律（volume law），以揭示非几何（non-geometric）图结构对纠缠特性的影响。

Method: 利用随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）和渐近自由性（asymptotic freeness）对 Erdős–Rényi 随机图上的自由费米子模型进行解析分析，并在热力学极限下计算基态纠缠熵。

Result: 基态纠缠熵在热力学极限下服从精确的体积律；纠缠密度具有普适系数，该系数不依赖于边概率和图的微观细节，数值结果约为 0.386 nats，严格低于 Page 值。

Conclusion: 随机图上纠缠熵的体积律反映了系统缺乏几何局域性（geometric locality），这与具有空间结构的晶格系统通常服从面积律形成鲜明对比。

Abstract: We study the ground-state entanglement entropy of free fermions on the Erdős--Rényi random graph, where each of the possible edges is present independently with some probability. Using random matrix theory and asymptotic freeness, we prove that the ground-state entanglement entropy obeys an exact volume law in the thermodynamic limit. The entanglement density, with a universal coefficient that is independent of the edge probability and the microscopic details of the graph. This coefficient is confirmed numerically to take the value approximately $0.386$ nats, strictly below the Page value. The volume law therefore reflects the absence of geometric locality in the random graph.

</details>


### [45] [Intrinsic Indistinguishability of Identical Particles and How Particle Labels Affect It](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29312)
*Valery Shchesnovich*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了全同玻色子（bosons）和费米子（fermions）在粒子数守恒演化下的不可区分性（indistinguishability），推导了投影不可区分性度量与动力学不变内部态之间的等价关系，并建立了任意部分可区分性下的多粒子可见态重构公式。此外，还揭示了引入额外粒子标签态可增加全同粒子多粒子不可区分性的反直觉效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有教科书框架仅处理玻色子和费米子的完全对称化/反对称化极限情况，缺乏对任意部分可区分性（partial distinguishability）的统一描述。本文旨在建立一种更一般的理论框架，能够刻画全同粒子在任意粒子数守恒演化下的不可区分性，并揭示其背后的动力学不变量（dynamical invariants）。

Method: 采用投影不可区分性度量（projective indistinguishability measure），将可见态（visible state）向对称/反对称子空间投影，并推导出该度量与动力学不变的内部态（dynamically invariant internal state）之间的等价表达式。进一步，通过编码动力学不变量的不可区分性函数（indistinguishability function），推导出多粒子可见态的重构公式（reconstruction formula），将对称化/反对称化框架推广到任意部分可区分性情形。最后，利用广义对称性上的投影度量（projective measures on generalized symmetries）对不可区分性的类函数（class-functions）进行完整刻画。

Result: 得到了投影不可区分性度量的等价表达式，建立了其与动力学不变内部态的联系。导出了适用于任意部分可区分性的多粒子可见态显式重构公式。给出了不可区分性类函数在广义对称性投影度量下的完整表征。发现了反直觉效应：增加额外粒子标签态（additional particle label states）可以提升全同粒子的多粒子不可区分性，该效应源于集体多粒子相位（collective multiparticle phases）的抵消。

Conclusion: 本文建立的不可区分性理论框架统一并推广了玻色子和费米子的教科书对称化方法，揭示了不可区分性度量与动力学不变量之间的深层联系。发现的反直觉效应表明，粒子标签态的增加并非总是降低可区分性，这对理解全同粒子的量子相干性和量子信息处理具有潜在意义。

Abstract: We investigate indistinguishability of identical bosons and fermions undergoing arbitrary particle-number-preserving evolutions of their visible degrees of freedom. For the projective indistinguishability measure, defined by the projection of the visible state onto the symmetric/anti-symmetric subspace, we derive an equivalent expression in terms of the dynamically invariant internal state. We further generalize the textbook symmetrization/anti-symmetrization framework for bosons and fermions to arbitrary partial distinguishability by deriving an explicit reconstruction formula for the multiparticle visible state in terms of the indistinguishability function encoding the dynamical invariants. We give complete characterization of the class-functions of indistinguishability by projective measures on generalized symmetries. Finally, we reveal a strikingly counterintuitive effect: introducing additional particle label states can increase the multiparticle indistinguishability of identical particles. The effect originates from the cancellation of collective multiparticle phases.

</details>


### [46] [Dissipative Effects in Transmission Line Analogues of Hawking Radiation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28505)
*Elián Urtubey,Fernando C. Lombardo,Paula I. Villar*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用电路量子电动力学（circuit quantum electrodynamics, cQED）平台，分析了两种超导电路类比黑洞模型（可调dc-SQUID传输线和基于SNAIL支持KdV孤子的传输线）在开放量子系统框架下产生可观测霍金辐射（Hawking radiation）的条件，并提出了基于希尔伯特-施密特距离（Hilbert-Schmidt distance）的观测判据。结果表明，可调传输线架构更可行，霍金温度约113 mK，而孤子模型需进一步优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 霍金辐射是弯曲时空量子场论（quantum field theory in curved spacetime）的核心预言，但直接观测远超当前实验能力。电路量子电动力学（circuit quantum electrodynamics, cQED）为在受控实验室条件下研究类比霍金辐射提供了可行的模拟平台。本文旨在分析两种超导电路类比黑洞架构产生可观测霍金温度的条件，并评估耗散和热噪声的影响。

Method: 研究了两种超导电路类比黑洞模型：可调dc-SQUID传输线（tunable dc-SQUID transmission line）和基于SNAIL（Superconducting Nonlinear Asymmetric Inductive Element）的传输线（后者支持KdV方程（Korteweg–de Vries equation）的孤子解（solitonic solutions））。采用开放量子系统方法（open quantum systems approach）分析了耗散（dissipation）和热噪声（thermal noise）的影响。除了粒子数测量（particle number measurements），还引入希尔伯特-施密特距离（Hilbert-Schmidt distance）来评估霍金信号相对于热浴的可区分性。

Result: 建立了实用的可探测性阈值（detectability thresholds），表明霍金温度（Hawking temperature）高于约73 mK时在现实实验条件下可被区分。可调传输线架构可达到约113 mK的霍金温度，因而更具可行性；而孤子模型需要进一步优化和更严苛的实验条件。

Conclusion: 可调dc-SQUID传输线架构在实现可观测类比霍金辐射方面比基于SNAIL孤子的方案更具优势，但两者在达到实验可探测性之前均需克服实际噪声与耗散的挑战。

Abstract: Hawking radiation is a fundamental result of quantum field theory in curved spacetime, yet its direct observation remains beyond current experimental capabilities. Circuit quantum electrodynamics provides a practical platform for realizing analogue systems where Hawking-like radiation may be studied under controlled laboratory conditions. In this work, we analyze two superconducting-circuit analogues of Schwarzschild black holes: a tunable dc-SQUID transmission line and a SNAIL-based transmission line supporting solitonic solutions of the KdV equation. We investigate the conditions under which these architectures can generate an observable Hawking temperature and study the impact of dissipation and thermal noise using an open quantum systems approach. To assess the observability of the Hawking signal, we propose complementing particle number measurements with estimates of the Hilbert-Schmidt distance to the thermal bath. Our analysis establishes practical detectability thresholds and shows that Hawking temperatures above approximately 73 mK remain distinguishable under realistic experimental conditions. While the tunable transmission line architecture can reach temperatures of about 113 mK and therefore appears more viable, the solitonic model requires further optimization and more demanding experimental conditions.

</details>


### [47] [Infrared Safety from ZX-Diagrams: A Categorical Proof of Soft-QED as Open Quantum System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29804)
*Soo-Jong Rey*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用丢弃ZX-演算（discard ZX-calculus）——一种用于混合态量子力学的图表语言——对QED中红外发散（infrared divergences）的Bloch-Nordsieck相消给出了非微扰的范畴论证明，并将软光子处理为开放量子系统，建立了从图表恒等到林德布拉德生成元（Lindblad generator）及非马尔可夫过程张量验证的完整框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为红外发散的Bloch-Nordsieck相消提供非微扰、范畴论的严格证明，验证伴随论文中基于开放量子系统处理软QED的物理推导在逻辑上的完备性与无隐藏假设性，并弥合范畴量子语义学、非平衡场论与开放量子系统编译之间的鸿沟。

Method: 采用丢弃ZX-演算这一图表语言作为核心工具；将软光子视为环境，被分辨的带电粒子与硬光子构成系统，建立完全正迹保持（completely positive trace-preserving, CPTP）映射；利用Feynman-Vernon影响泛函（influence functional）满足等历史归一化条件，在ZX-演算中将其表示为图表恒等式；构造CPTP Schur信道并取其无穷小极限导出精确的Lindblad生成元；开发用于非马尔可夫过程张量的局部CPTP认证流水线。

Result: 证明了双重位移图在幺正性（unitarity）、循环性（cyclicity）与丢弃（discard）规则下坍缩为裸线，实现了归一化条件的图表化验证；对非对角硬态元素，同一图表给出相干态重叠（coherent-state overlap），从第一性原理推导出软云退相干（soft-cloud decoherence）；构建了软壳粗粒化（soft-shell coarse graining）的CPTP Schur信道，其无穷小极限产生了由程函发射振幅（eikonal emission amplitudes）确定的Lindblad生成元；提出了适用于非马尔可夫过程张量的常数时间迹保持（trace preservation）验证方案。

Conclusion: 该工作从范畴论角度为软QED的开放系统处理提供了自洽性验证，确认了物理推导的逻辑完备性；所建立的框架将范畴量子语义学、非平衡场论与开放量子系统编译统一起来，为红外极限下的量子场论提供了新的形式化工具与数值验证手段。

Abstract: The discard ZX-calculus, a diagrammatic language for mixed-state quantum mechanics, is used to give a nonperturbative, categorical proof of the Bloch-Nordsieck cancellation of infrared divergences in QED. Soft photons are treated as an open quantum system: the resolved charged particles and hard photons form the system, while photons below a detector resolution form the environment. The reduced hard channel is a completely positive trace-preserving (CPTP) map, and the soft-photon theorem replaces the full S-matrix by a controlled displacement operator whose Feynman-Vernon influence functional satisfies the equal-history normalization ${\cal F}[J,J]=1 $. In the ZX-calculus, this normalization is a single diagrammatic identity: the doubled displacement diagram collapses to the bare wire under the unitarity, cyclicity, and discard rules. The proof therefore serves as a categorical consistency check on the open-system treatment of soft QED given in a companion paper; it confirms that the physical derivation is logically complete and free of hidden assumptions about the infrared limit. For off-diagonal hard-state elements, the same diagram yields the coherent-state overlap, giving a first-principles account of soft-cloud decoherence. The soft-shell coarse graining is then constructed as a CPTP Schur channel whose infinitesimal limit produces the exact Lindblad generator with jump operators determined by the eikonal emission amplitudes. Finally, a local CPTP-certification pipeline is developed for non-Markovian process tensors, enabling constant-time verification of trace preservation in open quantum simulations. The framework bridges categorical quantum semantics, non-equilibrium field theory, and practical open-system compilation.

</details>


### [48] [Quantum Eigenvalue Transformation via Linear Combination of Hamiltonian Simulation: A Weyl Calculus Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29848)
*Hongkang Ni,Lexing Ying*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出基于线性组合哈密顿量模拟（LCHS）的通用矩阵函数量子计算方法，利用外尔微积分（Weyl calculus）将非对易算子的LCHS公式构造转化为标量傅里叶逼近问题，实现了最优查询复杂度，并发展出无需先验假设的凸优化框架，能够直接生成离散LCHS公式，同时适用于含时耗散常微分方程（ODE）的模拟，成本相比先前最优方法降低2.1倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 核心工具是外尔微积分（Weyl calculus），它将非对易算子的LCHS公式构造转化为标量傅里叶逼近（scalar Fourier approximation）问题。基于此理论，进一步构建了一个无需先验假设（ansatz-free）的凸优化（convex optimization）框架，直接生成离散化的LCHS公式。

Result: 所提出的量子本征值变换（quantum eigenvalue transformation）算法达到了$\mathcal{O}(\log\frac{1}ε)$的最优查询复杂度（query complexity）缩放。含时耗散ODE模拟的成本相比先前最优方法降低了2.1倍。

Conclusion: 基于外尔微积分的LCHS理论为通用矩阵函数的量子计算提供了理论基础和高效优化框架，既适用于正规矩阵也适用于非正规矩阵，并显著提升了含时耗散系统的模拟效率。

Abstract: Linear combination of Hamiltonian simulation (LCHS) provides an efficient method for implementing matrix exponentials $e^{-tA}$ on quantum computers. In this paper, we develop LCHS formulas for computing general matrix functions $f(A)$ when $f$ is analytic on the numerical range of $A$, with $A$ possibly non-normal. The essential technical tool is Weyl calculus, which reduces the construction of LCHS formulas for noncommuting operators to scalar Fourier approximation problems. Our construction yields a quantum eigenvalue transformation algorithm with optimal $\mathcal{O}(\log\frac{1}ε)$ query complexity scaling. Furthermore, our Weyl-calculus-based theory gives rise to an ansatz-free convex optimization framework that directly produces discrete LCHS formulas. This circumvents the inefficiencies of traditional quadrature rules and yields formulas highly optimized for coherent implementation on quantum computers. In addition, both our theory and optimization framework apply to the simulation of time-dependent dissipative ODE $\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d} t} ψ(t) = -A(t)ψ(t)$, for which we achieve a $2.1\times$ cost reduction over prior art.

### [49] [Action on the Sphere: An Interfering Mean-Field Propagator for the Bose-Hubbard Dimer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30276)
*Elana F Todd-Miller,Eva-Maria Graefe*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于平均场（mean-field）近似，通过构建初值相干态传播子（coherent state propagator）并叠加平均场轨迹的相位，提出了一种能够再现玻色-哈伯德双模系统（Bose-Hubbard dimer）中击穿（breakdown）、复活（revival）及多粒子隧穿（tunnelling）效应的近似方法，该方法可推广至更一般的SU(2)及SU(M)哈密顿量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 玻色-哈伯德系统（Bose-Hubbard system）即使在双模情况下也展现出复杂的多粒子干涉效应，如复活、击穿和隧穿。最基本的平均场描述虽然简单，但无法完整捕捉这些量子动力学行为。因此需要构建一个超越平均场、能保留相位信息并准确描述多粒子动力学的近似方法。

Method: 从时间相关变分原理（time-dependent variational principle）出发，假设多粒子波函数为SU(2)相干态，从而导出平均场近似。在此基础上，构建初值相干态传播子，对平均场轨迹求和并保留其对应的平均场作用量（mean-field action）所决定的相位。进一步应用时间分片（time-slicing）程序，以准确捕捉多粒子隧穿效应。

Result: 该相干态传播子能够近似表达完整的时间依赖多粒子态，并成功再现击穿和复活动力学。结合时间分片程序后，能够准确捕获多粒子隧穿效应。

Conclusion: 该方法虽以玻色-哈伯德双模系统为分析对象，但可应用于更一般的SU(2)哈密顿量，并可扩展至SU(M)系统，表明其具有一定的普适性和推广潜力。

Abstract: The Bose-Hubbard system has been studied extensively both theoretically and experimentally, in particular in the context of ultracold atomic gases in optical lattices. Even in the two-mode case the many-particle dynamics display complex interference effects resulting in revival and breakdown phenomena as well as tunnelling. The most basic theoretical description is the mean-field approximation, which can be derived from a time-dependent variational principle assuming the many-particle wave function is an SU(2) coherent state. Here we build on this to construct a simple initial-value coherent state propagator, summing over mean-field trajectories and keeping track of their phases, given by the corresponding mean-field actions. This yields an approximation to the full time-dependent many-particle state, and is able to reproduce breakdown and revival dynamics. Applying a time-slicing procedure on top of this, we are able to accurately capture many-particle tunnelling effects. While in this paper we focus our analysis on the Bose-Hubbard dimer, the methods developed can be applied to more general SU(2) Hamiltonians, and can be extended to SU(M) systems.

Abstract: Quantum sensing promises enhanced precision, but the usual quantum Cramer Rao bound can be too optimistic for realistic linear sensors, where squeezing, filtering, and loss reshape quantum noise. We derive the tight Holevo Cramer Rao bound and show that realistic degradation yields a hierarchy with the usual bound and homodyne readout. This hierarchy already exists in gravitational-wave detectors. We propose a hardware-efficient readout that reaches the Holevo bound without extra signal loss, increasing compact-binary detection rates by up to 25% over the present LIGO homodyne readout.

### [51] [Krylov Complexity in Non-Inertial Quantum Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29770)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从Klein-Gordon辛形式（symplectic form）中直接提取SU(1,1)代数结构，利用该群结构化的哈密顿量推广Bogoliubov系数，进而构建Rindler对数目空间上的Krylov基，并导出Krylov复杂度的解析表达式。

Result: Krylov复杂度精确等于通过Bogoliubov混合产生的相关Rindler对平均数目；哈密顿量中失谐参数（detuning parameter）与对产生参数（pair-production parameter）的竞争将动力学分为双曲型Krylov扩散、临界增长与有界Krylov空间运动三个区域；在失谐主导区，对数目分布指数地局限于低Krylov能级，表现为Krylov复杂度的局域化。

Conclusion: 该工作为非惯性量子系统中Krylov复杂度的结构构建提供了新视角，揭示了加速观测者视角下量子复杂度与粒子对产生之间的内在联系。

Abstract: In this work, we formulate the Krylov complexity in non-In an inertial quantum system, the direct emergence of the $SU(1,1)$ sector from the Klein-Gordon symplectic form dictates that the Rindler pair-number sector naturally forms the Krylov basis for uniformly accelerating observers. Under this construction, we generalize the Bogoliubov coefficients by exploiting the $SU(1,1)$ group-structured Hamiltonian. Within this framework, we explicitly derive that the Krylov complexity is exactly equal to the mean number of correlated Rindler pairs generated via Bogoliubov mixing. Furthermore, the competition between the detuning parameter and the pair-production parameter in the Hamiltonian separates the dynamics into three distinct regimes: hyperbolic Krylov spreading, critical growth, and bounded Krylov-space motion. Notably, in the detuning-dominated regime, the pair-number distribution remains exponentially confined to low Krylov levels, implying that the wave packet becomes trapped at low levels, which manifests as the localization of Krylov complexity. Ultimately, our work sheds new light on the structural construction of Krylov complexity in non-inertial quantum systems.

### [52] [Imaginary pseudo entropy encodes temporal orientation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29235)
*Tatsuhiro Misumi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，虚部赝熵（imaginary pseudo entropy）虽通常为复数，但其虚部可通过校准复制干涉仪（calibrated replica interferometer）转化为可测量的时间定向记录，并给出Helstrom最优单发成功概率（Helstrom-optimal single-shot success probability）的精确上限；在量子信道下该信息仅递减，其可逆性由Petz恢复映射（Petz recovery）刻画。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 不同时间量子态之间的赝熵（pseudo entropy）通常为复数，但其虚部一直缺乏具有界定的操作意义（bounded operational meaning）。作者旨在为这一虚部赋予可测量的、有明确上下界的物理解释。

Method: 利用校准复制干涉仪将赝Rényi相位（pseudo-Rényi phase）转化为时间定向的记录，并结合复制可见度（replica visibility）来精确确定前向与反向辅助输出（ancilla outputs）之间的迹距离（trace distance），从而推导出Helstrom最优单发成功概率。

Result: 在短时间下，模哈密顿量（modular Hamiltonian）与物理哈密顿量（physical Hamiltonian）的对称化协方差（symmetrized covariance）决定初始可区分性响应；在任何公共量子信道（common quantum channel）下，对应的定向信息仅能递减，等号成立条件由Petz恢复映射刻画。

Conclusion: 虚部赝熵记录了一种时间定向之间的可逆区分性（reversible distinction），而粗粒化（coarse graining）可使该记录的丧失变为不可逆。

Abstract: Pseudo entropy between quantum states at different times is generally complex, yet its imaginary part has lacked a bounded operational meaning. We show that a calibrated replica interferometer converts the pseudo-Rényi phase into a directly measurable record of transition orientation. Together with replica visibility, it exactly determines the trace distance between forward and backward ancilla outputs and hence the Helstrom-optimal single-shot success probability. At short times, the symmetrized covariance of the modular and physical Hamiltonians sets the initial distinguishability response. Under any common quantum channel, the corresponding orientation information can only decrease, with equality characterized by Petz recovery. Imaginary pseudo entropy therefore records a reversible distinction between temporal orientations, while coarse graining can make the loss of that record irreversible.

### [53] [Provable random-matrix spectral ramp in a static, geometrically local Hamiltonian](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30635)
*Matteo Ippoliti*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本论文基于Bertini、Kos和Prosen（BKP）的 landmark 结果以及一种新提出的 Feynman-Kitaev 钟构造变体，首次在静态且几何局域的哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）中证明了谱型因子（spectral form factor, SFF）存在随机矩阵斜坡（ramp），即通过将 dual-unitary 电路的 Floquet 准能量谱嵌入静态局域哈密顿量的能谱，证明了后者在对称性扇区内的连通 SFF 继承了 BKP 斜坡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子混沌（quantum chaos）通常与量子系统能谱中随机矩阵统计（random-matrix statistics）的出现相关联，而谱型因子（SFF）的线性增长区（ramp）是随机矩阵系综的普适特征。此前，BKP 仅在周期驱动（Floquet）的 dual-unitary 电路中证明了该斜坡的存在；本文的目标是将这一结果推广到静态的、几何局域的多体系统。

Method: 采用一种新近提出的 Feynman-Kitaev 钟构造变体，将 dual-unitary 电路的 Floquet 准能量谱嵌入到一个静态局域哈密顿量的能谱中。通过这种方法，证明该静态哈密顿量的连通谱型因子（connected SFF）在特定对称性扇区内继承了 BKP 斜坡。

Result: 首次在时间无关的（time-independent）、几何局域的多体系统中，且具有有限局域希尔伯特空间维度（finite local Hilbert space dimension）的条件下，严格证明了谱型因子（SFF）中存在随机矩阵斜坡（ramp）。

Conclusion: 本文提供了首个在静态、几何局域多体系统中证明 SFF 斜坡的严格结果，将之前仅在 Floquet 系统中成立的 BKP 结果扩展至时间独立的哈密顿量体系。

Abstract: Quantum chaos is commonly associated with the emergence of random-matrix statistics in the spectra of quantum systems. A useful diagnostic is provided by the spectral form factor (SFF), which for random matrix ensembles displays a universal linear-growth regime (`ramp'). In the last decade, a landmark result by Bertini, Kos and Prosen (BKP) identified for the first time a class of geometrically local quantum dynamics of finite-dimensional particles where the SFF provably exhibits a random-matrix ramp: periodically driven (Floquet) qudit chains whose evolution is described by `dual-unitary' circuits. Here, building on the BKP result and on a recently proposed variant of the Feynman-Kitaev clock construction, we obtain a spectral ramp in a class of static, geometrically local Hamiltonians. Our strategy is to embed the Floquet quasienergy spectrum of a dual-unitary circuit into the energy spectrum of a static local Hamiltonian, and to prove that the latter's connected SFF inherits the BKP ramp within a symmetry sector. This is to our knowledge the first proof of a spectral ramp in a time-independent, geometrically local many-body system with finite local Hilbert space dimension.

*Jian Zeng,Xiangjun Tan,Hongzhang Wang,Yulei Zhang,Wendong Bian,Lingting Wu,Chenggang Yang,Zhengshan Guo,Jiankun Li,Yongfeng Wang,Jun Lu,Jun-Wei Luo,Tian Pei*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文报道了通过同位素纯化（isotopic purification）的70GeH4前驱体合成高质量二维空穴气（2DHG），有效抑制了73Ge核自旋涨落，使量子比特的T2*在甜点（sweet spot）处延长至超过20微秒，在非甜点处超过3微秒，实现了超过99.9%的单量子比特门保真度，并发现了与界面四极核动力学（quadrupolar nuclear dynamics）相关的新型噪声通道。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平面锗（planar Germanium）是构建自旋基大规模量子计算机的 promising 平台，但73Ge核自旋涨落限制了单量子比特性能，且量子比特甜点的位置差异阻碍了全晶圆范围内的高保真度操控。因此，有必要消除超精细噪声（hyperfine noise）的根本来源。

Method: 采用同位素纯化的70GeH4前驱体合成高质量二维空穴气（2DHG），通过抑制非零自旋原子核来降低超精细噪声；利用Hahn回波谱学（Hahn-echo spectroscopy）分析残余73Ge核的噪声特性及其动力学行为。

Result: 同位素纯化使量子比特在甜点处的T2*超过20微秒，非甜点处超过3微秒；在两种操作区域中单量子比特门保真度均超过99.9%；通过Hahn回波谱学发现一种有限频核噪声通道（finite-frequency nuclear-noise channel），其特性与Ge/SiGe界面附近残余73Ge核的四极修饰动力学（quadrupole-modified dynamics）一致。

Conclusion: 同位素纯化的平面锗是一种高相干性、可扩展的空穴自旋量子比特平台，并提供了界面四极核动力学的光谱探针。

Abstract: Planar Germanium has emerged as a promising platform to build spin-based large scale quantum computers. By exploiting the anisotropic hyperfine interaction of holes in Ge, qubits with long T2* have been recently realized. While the performance of single qubits is still more or less limited by 73Ge nuclear spin fluctuations, the site-to-site variation of qubit sweet spot becomes obstacles to maintaining high fidelity of each qubit across the whole wafer. To achieve high performance Ge-based quantum circuit, it is therefore essential to eliminate the origin source of hyperfine noise. In its Silicon counterparts, reduction of 29Si abundance enables exceptional high-fidelity operation. In contrast, hole qubits based on isotopically purified Ge have not been demonstrated. Here, we report the synthesis of high quality 2-dimensional hole gas (2DHG) with enriched 70GeH4 precursor. Due to the suppression of nonzero spin nucleus, the qubits' T2* on the sweet spot is moderately extended beyond 20 us, surpassing the previous best reported Ge hole qubits. More importantly, the qubits' T2* off the sweet spot is enhanced to above 3 us, enabling single qubit gate fidelity exceeding 99.9% in both operating regimes. Hahn-echo spectroscopy further resolves a finite-frequency nuclear-noise channel that is distinct from the conventional Larmor-linked hyperfine response. We associate this channel with quadrupole-modified dynamics of residual 73Ge nuclei sampling local electric-field gradients near the Ge/SiGe interface. Its field scaling and angle-dependent visibility are consistent with a qubit-visible quadrupolar nuclear-noise component transduced through the anisotropic hyperfine interaction of Ge holes. These results establish isotopically purified planar Ge as a high-coherence scalable platform for hole spin qubits and provide a spectroscopic probe of interfacial quadrupolar nuclear dynamics.

</details>


### [56] [Dissipative phase decision without ground-state preparation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28750)
*Hao-En Li,Yilun Yang,Lin Lin*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通过短时耗散冷却（dissipative cooling）来识别基态量子相（ground-state quantum phases）的动力学方法，无需制备高精度的基态近似态，而是通过监测候选相的代表态在冷却动力学下的早期响应来判断相变。该方法在多种自旋模型（包括受挫海森堡链、Kitaev蜂窝模型和XXZ链）中得到验证，并提供了理论保障。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法需要制备高精度的基态近似态来确定量子相，这在容错量子计算早期阶段难以实现。本文旨在开发一种更易于在近期待验证的量子设备上实现的相判定（phase decision）策略，仅需短时耗散动力学和粗粒度的滤波分辨率。

Method: 方法包括：(i) 制备候选相的代表态；(ii) 针对目标哈密顿量设计耗散冷却动力学，其中跳跃算子（jump operators）仅需短时哈密顿量模拟即可实现；(iii) 在系统混合至稳态之前，监控相敏感可观测量（phase-sensitive observables）的早期响应，快速抑制高能成分并进入低能流形（low-energy manifold），从而揭示基态相。

Result: 在受挫$J_1$--$J_2$海森堡链、Kitaev蜂窝模型和XXZ链上展示了策略的有效性，覆盖了Berezinskii--Kosterlitz--Thouless相变和拓扑相变。粗滤波分辨率和短演化时间即可恢复Luttinger参数和拓扑诊断量等相敏感量。此外，为自由费米子、自由玻色子系统以及相互作用费米子系统中的低能流形制备提供了理论依据。

Conclusion: 相判定有望成为早期容错量子设备（early fault-tolerant quantum devices）上实用性规模研究的可行目标。

Abstract: We propose a dynamical approach to identifying ground-state quantum phases through short-time dissipative cooling. Rather than determining the phase by preparing highly accurate approximations to ground states, we prepare a representative state of a candidate phase and monitor the early-time response of phase-sensitive observables under cooling dynamics tailored to the target Hamiltonian. For a class of phase-decision problems in which the relevant observables can be inferred from the low-energy manifold, and with jump operators implementable using only short-time Hamiltonian simulation, the dissipative evolution rapidly suppresses high-energy components and drives the system into a low-energy manifold whose observables already reveal the underlying ground-state phase, well before mixing to the steady state. We demonstrate this strategy for the frustrated $J_1$--$J_2$ Heisenberg chain, the Kitaev honeycomb model, and the XXZ chain, including Berezinskii--Kosterlitz--Thouless and topological phase transitions. In particular, coarse filter resolutions and short evolution times suffice to recover phase-sensitive quantities such as the Luttinger parameter and topological diagnostics. We further provide theoretical justification that cooling dynamics with such jump operators can rigorously prepare low-energy manifolds for free-fermionic and free-bosonic systems, and investigate this mechanism for interacting fermionic systems. Our results suggest that phase decision is a plausible target for future utility-scale studies on early fault-tolerant quantum devices.

</details>


### [57] [Properties of 2D Electron or Hole Gases at Tailored s-Si/SiGe Interfaces: A First-Principles Investigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28776)
*Garima Ahuja,Farha S,Tanuja Shridhar Joshi,Anil Shaji,Shobhana Narasimhan*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理杂化密度泛函理论计算，研究了拉伸应变硅/硅锗（s-Si/SiGe）界面处二维电子气或二维空穴气（2DEG或2DHG）的形成与性质。发现当锗浓度x<0.25时出现新型能带对齐，无法形成2DEG但可形成2DHG；当x>0.25时两者均可形成。计算得到的有效质量各向异性且与实验高度一致，相关结果对量子计算中的半导体自旋量子比特具有重要意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究s-Si/SiGe界面处二维载流子气（2DEG/2DHG）的形成条件与性质，为基于该体系的半导体自旋量子比特在量子计算中的应用提供理论基础。

Method: 采用第一性原理杂化密度泛函理论（hybrid density functional theory）进行计算，通过分析界面处能带对齐、电子能带结构、电荷密度分布及有效质量各向异性来表征二维载流子气。

Result: 发现了依赖于锗浓度x的能带对齐转变：x<0.25时导带无偏移，无法形成2DEG但可形成2DHG；x>0.25时两者均可形成。界面处出现两个近简并的2DEG态和两个2DHG态，载流子被限制在界面附近2-3原子层内。有效质量呈现显著的各向异性，尤其以2DHG态最为明显，且与实验结果高度吻合。

Conclusion: 通过适当掺杂和加栅极电压（gating）可调控界面载流子态，有效质量的各向异性可用于构建一维载流子气（1D carrier gas）。该研究对基于s-Si/SiGe的半导体自旋量子比特在量子计算中的应用尤为重要。

Abstract: We have performed first-principles hybrid density functional theory calculations to study the formation and properties of two-dimensional electron or hole gases (2DEG or 2DHG) at s-Si/SiGe interfaces. For small Ge concentrations $x < 0.25$, we find a novel type of band alignment with no offset in the conduction bands, implying that a 2DEG cannot be formed, though a 2DHG can. In contrast, for $x > 0.25$ the band alignment suggests that either a 2DEG or 2DHG can be formed. The electronic band structure features two nearly degenerate 2DEG states at the bottom of the conduction bands, and two 2DHG states at the top of the valence band. These states can be accessed by appropriate doping and gating. Charge density plots of these states show that they feature carriers confined to the near vicinity (2--3 atomic layers) of the interface. Calculated effective masses are anisotropic, being markedly so for the 2DHG states, and in excellent agreement with experiment. This property can be exploited to create a 1D carrier gas. Our results are especially important for s-Si/SiGe-based semiconducting spin qubits for quantum computing applications.

Method: 开发了一个直接从系综光谱（ensemble spectroscopy）重构自旋1/2固态缺陷中电跃迁偶极极化的框架，该方法结合了光致发光光谱（photoluminescence spectra）对磁场、光偏振和应变的响应。应用于包含多个晶学子位（crystallographic subsites）的硅中铒离子这一具有挑战性的体系。

Abstract: Spin-photon interfaces based on solid-state defects are key building blocks for scalable quantum networks and hybrid quantum platforms. Optimizing light-matter coupling in these systems requires precise knowledge of the optical transition dipole polarization, yet for many promising quantum emitters this quantity is hard to determine and therefore remains poorly characterized. Here, we develop a framework for reconstructing electric transition dipole polarization in spin-1/2 solid-state defects directly from ensemble spectroscopy. The approach combines the response of photoluminescence spectra to magnetic field, optical polarization, and strain. Applied to erbium ions in silicon, a particularly challenging system containing multiple crystallographic subsites, the framework identifies strain-induced shifts as the origin of asymmetric ensemble spectra and enables simultaneous determination of the optical dipole polarization and strain-orbital coupling tensor. The resulting model predicts how cavity-ion coupling depends on crystallographic orientation and magnetic-field direction, which we verify using single erbium ions coupled to a nanophotonic cavity. Together, these results establish a broadly applicable route for extracting microscopic properties of solid-state quantum emitters from ensemble spectroscopy and for engineering optimized spin-photon and spin-phonon interfaces.

### [59] [Kinetics of electron-phonon scattering in silicon resolved by Rydberg transitions of donors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28893)
*Nils Dessmann,Aidan G. McConnell,Sergey G. Pavlov,Guy Matmon,Gabriel Aeppli,Nikolay V. Abrosimov,Hari Paudyal,Michael E. Flatté,Benedict N. Murdin*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过结合Rydberg态形状因子和全布里渊区声子形变势，建立了施主-声子动力学的定量理论，并利用时间分辨自由电子激光实验验证。实验与理论的严格对比表明，硅导带底位置k0的公认值需要修正，并将施主弛豫确立为导带参数和散射过程的精密测量工具。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半导体中的施主（donor）Rydberg态具有类似真空原子Rydberg态的量子技术应用潜力，但电子-晶格耦合导致激发态寿命远短于真空中性原子，现有理论缺乏对施主-声子动力学的定量描述，制约了在真实材料堆栈中工程化施主系统以构建量子器件。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 理论方面，构建了包含Rydberg态形状因子（form factor）——利用其在实空间的大尺度在动量空间产生强选择性——以及全布里渊区（Brillouin zone）六个声子支（phonon branches）形变势（deformation potentials）的施主-声子动力学定量框架。实验方面，采用时间分辨自由电子激光（time-resolved free electron laser）测量进行严格对比验证。

Result: 广泛引用的硅导带底位置k0与观测到的施主弛豫速率（donor relaxation rates）不一致；当采用一个比通常假设更远离X点的k0值时，理论与实验取得定量一致。该严格的实验-理论对比将施主弛豫确立为导带参数和散射过程的精密计量学（precision metrology）方法。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了施主-声子动力学的定量基础，可用于在真实材料堆栈中工程化施主系统以构建量子器件。同时，硅导带底位置k0的修正对从量子器件到经典电子学的诸多领域均具有重要影响。

Abstract: Rydberg states of atoms in vacuum are now well recognized as a resource for quantum technologies. Donors in semiconductors also display analogous states, which have been proposed for similar applications. While they benefit from permanent locations in their host crystals, electron-lattice coupling leads to much shorter excited-state lifetimes than for neutral atoms in vacuum. Here we provide a quantitative description of donor-phonon kinetics, creating a basis for engineering donor systems in realistic material stacks for quantum devices. Our theory incorporates both form factors for the Rydberg states, which given their large extents in real space provide strong selectivity in momentum space, and tabulated deformation potentials for all six phonon branches throughout the Brillouin zone. By confronting this framework with carefully controlled time-resolved free electron laser measurements, we show that the widely quoted position of the silicon conduction band minimum, $k_0$, is inconsistent with observed donor relaxation rates and that quantitative agreement is obtained for a value further from the X-point than commonly assumed. This stringent experiment-theory comparison establishes donor relaxation as a precision metrology for conduction band parameters and scattering processes in silicon, with consequences spanning from quantum devices to classical electronics.

### [60] [Exact Hilbert-space ergodicity from continuous monitoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29042)
*Yue Wu,Yuzhi Tong,Liang Mao,Pengfei Zhang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明在连续监测的量子多体系统中，希尔伯特空间遍历性（Hilbert-space ergodicity）可以严格涌现，其平衡态分布由目标密度矩阵σ的Scrooge系综（Scrooge ensemble）唯一决定，且所需条件仅为跳算符（jump operators）形成一个形变酉1-设计（deformed unitary 1-design），远弱于完全遍历性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子多体系统通常被认为会在动力学驱动下趋于平衡，这一预期基于希尔伯特空间遍历性——即纯态演化在物理约束下均匀遍历希尔伯特空间。然而，如何严格建立这一遍历性的涌现机制，并明确其所需的最小条件，仍是一个待解决的核心问题。

Method: 作者针对任意目标密度矩阵σ，构造了一个连续监测的量子系统，并严格证明了在该系统中，σ对应的Scrooge系综是量子轨迹（quantum trajectories）在晚时（late-time）唯一的平衡分布。证明所需的核心条件是监测过程中的跳算符构成一个形变酉1-设计，这是一个比完全遍历性弱得多的条件。

Result: 数值模拟以热态（thermal states）作为平衡态，验证了理论预测。结果表明，在远弱于完全遍历性的条件下，连续监测系统中的希尔伯特空间遍历性可以严格实现。

Conclusion: 该工作为希尔伯特空间遍历性的涌现建立了一个严格的机制，并为在量子器件上对遍历性进行实验研究提供了一条实用路径。

Abstract: Quantum evolution is generally expected to drive a quantum many-body system toward equilibrium. This expectation is often justified by the Hilbert-space ergodicity of generic quantum dynamics, namely, the idea that pure-state evolution explores Hilbert space uniformly up to physical constraints. Such a statement can be made rigorous by requiring the associated state ensemble to form the Haar-random ensemble, or its more structured generalization, the Scrooge ensemble. In this Letter, we report the emergence of exact Hilbert-space ergodicity in a continuously monitored quantum many-body system. For any target density matrix $σ$, we construct a continuously monitored system for which we rigorously prove that the Scrooge ensemble of $σ$ is the unique late-time equilibrium distribution of quantum trajectories. Remarkably, this requires only that the jump operators in the monitoring form a deformed unitary 1-design, a seemingly much weaker condition than full ergodicity. We numerically demonstrate our predictions by simulating continuously monitored systems whose equilibrium states are thermal states. Our results establish a rigorous mechanism for the emergence of Hilbert-space ergodicity and provide a practical route for its investigation on quantum devices.

### [61] [Shadow tomography for classical tensor network simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29133)
*Jiace Sun,Garnet Kin-Lic Chan*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，受影子层析（shadow tomography）启发的思路在经过适当适配后，能在经典计算机上以更优的样本复杂度估计张量网络态（tensor network states）的可观测量。对于自旋（玻色）和费米子系统，该方法在特定任务和系统类型下可实现O(N)到O(N³)的缩放改进；对于长程相互作用的哈密顿量期望值估计，可达到最优的O(1)全局缩放（仅含对数因子）。此外，影子估计器（shadow estimator）在变分优化中能提供比标准蒙特卡洛估计器更稳定的梯度，并在长程海森堡模型和量子化学哈密顿量模拟中展示了实际优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 影子层析已被证明是量子计算机上从少量样本估计可观测量（observable）的高效工具，其样本复杂度优势显著。本文旨在探索这一思想是否能被移植到经典张量网络计算中，以改善对张量网络态上可观测量进行估计时的样本缩放（sample scaling）。

Method: 提出了影子估计器（shadow estimator），将影子层析思想适配到经典张量网络（tensor network）的收缩（contraction）需求上。针对自旋（玻色）与费米子两类系统分别设计了策略，并结合蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）框架实现。

Result: 在特定任务和系统类型下，样本复杂度可实现O(N)至O(N³)的缩放改进。对于长程相互作用哈密顿量期望值估计，达到了最优的O(1)全局缩放（仅含对数因子）。在变分优化（variational optimization）中，影子估计器提供的梯度比标准蒙特卡洛估计器更稳定。在2D长程海森堡模型和从头算量子化学哈密顿量（ab-initio quantum chemistry Hamiltonian）模拟中展示出实际优势。

Conclusion: 影子层析启发的样本估计方法可以有效推广到经典张量网络计算中，在多种任务上实现显著的样本复杂度改进，尤其对长程相互作用系统达到理论最优缩放，并在变分优化中提供更稳定的梯度。

Abstract: Shadow tomography has appeared as a powerful tool for estimating observables on quantum computers from a small number of samples. We show that shadow-tomography-inspired ideas can offer similarly improved sample scaling for estimating observables on tensor network states on classical computers after proper adaptation. We develop strategies for both spin (bosonic) and fermionic systems, tailored to the contraction requirements of tensor networks, and generate scaling improvements of factors of $O(N)$ to $O(N^{3})$ (where $N$ is system size), depending on the specific task and system type. For the important and difficult task of evaluating the expectation value of long-range interacting Hamiltonians, we achieve the optimal $O(1)$ overall scaling (up to logarithmic factors) for an arbitrarily fixed relative Monte Carlo error in both spin and fermionic systems. Additionally, we show that shadow estimators offer more stable gradients of observables in variational optimization tasks than standard Monte Carlo estimators. We demonstrate practical advantage by simulating systems with long-range interactions, including the 2D long-range Heisenberg model and an ab-initio quantum chemistry Hamiltonian.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 退相干是所有量子技术中最大的瓶颈。针对金刚石NV中心，退相干主要由金刚石晶格中的电子和核自旋浴引起，理解并利用这一机制是克服退相干的关键。

Method: 实验上对NV ensemble（NV色心系综）进行电子自旋回波（electron spin-echo）测量；同时结合数值模拟（numerical simulations）分析自旋浴与NV中心的耦合作用。

Result: 在垂直于NV轴的外加磁场方向的能级反交叉处，自旋浴与NV电子及宿主¹⁴N核的多体相互作用使回波包络以¹⁴N核自旋跃迁频率调制；数值模拟表明自旋浴耦合对观察到该调制必不可少。该振荡在反交叉处因零一级塞曼效应（zero first-order Zeeman effect）而具有2–3倍于平行磁场方向的长自旋回波相干时间，且频率高度稳定、对环境波动具有鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 该发现为多体物理学（many-body physics）的基础研究和量子传感（quantum sensing）提供了新的机遇。

Abstract: Decoherence is the biggest bottleneck in all quantum technologies. For nitrogen-vacancy (NV) centers in diamond, the loss of coherence is caused by the electron and nuclear spin bath of the diamond lattice. Here, we demonstrate that the spin bath - that typically causes decoherence - entangles the spin states of the NV electron and the host $^{14}$N nucleus. The many-body interaction between the $^{14}$N nucleus - electron - bath spins at an energy level anti-crossing occurring for an applied magnetic field orientation perpendicular to the NV axis is responsible for this effect. This is observed experimentally on NV ensembles via electron spin-echo measurements, where the echo envelope is modulated at the frequency of a $^{14}$N nuclear spin transition. Using numerical simulations, we show that the spin bath coupling to the NV centers is essential for observing this modulation. Due to the zero first-order Zeeman effect at the anti-crossing, the observed oscillations have long spin-echo coherence times, 2--3 times those at the parallel magnetic field orientation. The oscillation frequency is highly stable and robust against environmental fluctuations. These findings provide new opportunities for fundamental studies of many-body physics and quantum sensing.

</details>


### [63] [All-optical switching of continuous-variable entanglement in an absorption-suppressed plasmonic nanodimer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30315)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 亚波长量子光子电路元件需要同时满足三个要求：产生非经典光、抑制等离激元损耗以及保持动态可调谐能力，目前尚缺乏能同时实现这三点的有效方案。

Method: 采用正交等离激元纳米棒二聚体结构，通过相位锁定（phase-locked）的控制偏振来诱导等离激元折射率增强（plasmonic refractive-index enhancement），使探针响应进入近零消光区域，同时调谐局域二次谐波（second-harmonic）参量相互作用。

Result: 该非线性等离激元光源在吸收抑制（absorption-suppressed）区域工作，实现了量子关联的全光调控（all-optical control），展示了可切换的对数负性和单模非经典性。

Conclusion: 该工作为在衍射极限（diffraction limit）以下工作的主动可调谐量子等离激元电路元件（quantum-plasmonic circuit elements）开辟了可行的技术路线。

Abstract: A subwavelength quantum-photonic circuit element should simultaneously generate nonclassical light, suppress plasmonic loss, and remain dynamically tunable. We show that an orthogonal plasmonic nanorod dimer can satisfy all three requirements. A phase-locked control polarization induces plasmonic refractive-index enhancement, driving the probe response toward a near-zero-extinction regime while simultaneously tuning the local second-harmonic parametric interaction. The resulting nonlinear plasmonic source operates in an absorption-suppressed regime and enables all-optical control of quantum correlations. We demonstrate switchable logarithmic negativity and single-mode nonclassicality, establishing a route toward actively tunable quantum-plasmonic circuit elements operating well below the diffraction limit.

### [64] [Connecting Density Matrix Spectroscopy to Biexciton Entanglement Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30424)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验技术密度矩阵光谱学（DMS）可重构双激子发出的光子对密度矩阵，但该矩阵与双激子态及其纠缠动力学之间的精确联系尚不清楚。

Method: 首先推导 DMS 所得密度矩阵与双激子态之间的解析关系；然后基于扩展离子 Hubbard 模型（extended ionic Hubbard model），对二维电子-空穴体系进行数值模拟，比较 DMS 测量的纠缠动力学与双激子的实际纠缠动力学。

Result: DMS 能够部分捕获双激子的纠缠，尤其是双激子纠缠熵 $S_{\mathrm{bi}}$ 与构成双激子的激子波矢纠缠 $S_k$ 之差 $S_{\mathrm{bi}} - S_k$ 的动力学行为。

Conclusion: 结果证明了 DMS 在获取双激子纠缠动力学信息方面的有效性。

Abstract: Quantum entanglement is one of the most intriguing features of quantum mechanics. To investigate the entanglement between two excitons in a biexciton, an experimental technique called density matrix spectroscopy (DMS) has recently been developed. DMS combines stimulated emission tomography and pump-probe techniques to obtain a time-resolved density matrix of the polarization state of a photon pair emitted from the biexciton. The reconstructed density matrix is expected to encode information about the biexciton state and its entanglement dynamics, but the precise nature of this connection has remained unclear. In this paper, we derive an analytical relationship between the density matrix obtained by DMS and the biexciton state. In addition, we perform numerical simulations to compare the entanglement dynamics obtained by DMS with the biexciton's entanglement dynamics in a two-dimensional electron-hole system using an extended ionic Hubbard model. We find that DMS can partially capture the entanglement in the biexciton, in particular, the dynamics of the difference $S_{\mathrm{bi}} - S_k$, where $S_{\mathrm{bi}}$ is the entanglement entropy of the biexciton and $S_k$ is the entanglement in terms of the wavevectors of the excitons that constitute the biexciton. These results demonstrate the validity of DMS for obtaining information about the entanglement dynamics of the biexciton.

### [65] [Cavity-mediated probabilistic magic $T$-gate injection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30628)
*Sofia Cocciaretto,Roberto Menta,Vittorio Giovannetti*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 提出一种基于腔量子电动力学（cavity QED）的概率型幻态注入协议，通过可控原子-腔相互作用和条件测量，在腔模的前两个福克子空间（Fock subspace）中概率制备幻态（magic state），成功率达0.74，并利用隐形传态（teleportation）协议将幻态注入计算原子，所有操作均可基于里德伯原子-腔（Rydberg atom-cavity）平台实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非克利福德门（non-Clifford gates）是通用量子计算（universal quantum computation）的必要资源，但其容错实现通常依赖幻态蒸馏（magic-state distillation），导致量子比特数目和电路深度显著增加，亟需更高效的幻态制备与注入方案。

Method: 利用可控原子-腔相互作用和条件测量（conditional measurements），在单腔模的前两个福克子空间中概率制备有效幻态；随后通过缀饰态跃迁（dressed-state transitions）介导的隐形传态协议，仅需克利福德操作（Clifford operations）和一个辅助原子进行读出，即可将腔编码幻态注入计算原子。

Result: 每次尝试的成功概率为0.74，且与目标幻态相位（target magic phase）无关；所有所需操作——包括态制备、两量子比特交换门（two-qubit exchange gates）和投影测量（projective measurement）——均可在里德伯原子-腔平台上基于现有实验技术实现。

Conclusion: 该方案在原理上可进一步推广至逻辑层（logical level），借助集体里德伯相互作用（collective Rydberg interactions）和光学非线性（optical nonlinearities），实现腔介导的T门注入（cavity-mediated T-gate injection）直接作用于编码量子比特。

Abstract: Non-Clifford gates are a necessary resource for universal quantum computation, yet their fault-tolerant implementation typically relies on magic-state distillation, which incurs significant overhead in qubit count and circuit depth. In this work, we propose a probabilistic cavity-based magic-state injection protocol. Our scheme exploits controlled atom-cavity interactions and conditional measurements to probabilistically prepare an effective magic state encoded in the first two level Fock subspace of a single cavity mode, achieving a success probability of $0.74$ per attempt, independent of the target magic phase. The cavity-encoded magic state is subsequently injected into a computational atom via a teleportation-based protocol mediated by dressed-state transitions, requiring only Clifford operations and a single auxiliary atom for readout. We show that all required operations -- state preparation, two-qubit exchange gates, and projective measurement -- can be implemented with experimentally available techniques in Rydberg atom-cavity platforms. We further discuss how the scheme can in principle be adapted to operate at the logical level, where collective Rydberg interactions and optical nonlinearities provide a route toward cavity-mediated $T$-gate injection directly into code-encoded qubits.

### [66] [The BEG model at the FAD triple point on the square lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28821)

Method: 采用一种构型依赖簇权值的随机簇型表示（random-cluster type representation with configuration-dependent cluster weights），并将其与参数为1/2的伯努利点位渗流（Bernoulli site percolation）进行耦合分析。

Result: 证明了二维Blume-Emery-Griffiths模型在FAD三相点处，任意温度下均具有唯一的吉布斯测度（Gibbs measure），即该点处不存在相变（absence of phase transitions）。

Conclusion: 该结果严格确认了FAD奇异点处无相变的结论，为理解该模型在多重基态共存情形下的热力学行为提供了理论依据。

Abstract: In this note, we prove that the two-dimensional Blume-Emery-Griffiths model at the triple point Ferromagnetic-Antiquadrupolar-Disordered (FAD) has a unique Gibbs measure at any temperature, thereby establishing the absence of phase transitions. The FAD point lies at the intersection of lines separating three regions of the phase diagram, and it is a singular point where the model exhibits infinitely many ground states. Our proof is based on a random-cluster type representation with configuration-dependent cluster weights and a coupling with Bernoulli site percolation with parameter $1/2$.

### [67] [Metric Congruence in Finite-Dimensional Non-Hermitian Quantum Mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28868)
*Ramirez Romina,Reboiro Marta*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究有限维非厄米量子力学中的度量表示（metric representation），强调非厄米系统的物理描述可以在不同但同构的希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）中表述，并通过 Krein 空间形式主义（Krein-space formalism）建立与标准希尔伯特空间的明确联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强调非厄米哈密顿量（non-Hermitian Hamiltonian）的物理描述可以在不同但同构的希尔伯特空间中形式化，从而为一致描述非厄米系统提供理论框架。

Method: 采用 Krein 空间形式主义，展示赋予不定 Krein 度量（indefinite Krein metric）的向量空间如何通过合适的同构（isomorphism）与标准希尔伯特空间相关联；物理态、度量和算符需通过相应的希尔伯特空间同构进行迁移。

Result: 通过一个两能级非厄米自旋模型（two-level non-Hermitian spin model）进行数值验证，并使用 Robertson 不确定关系（Robertson uncertainty relation）作为一致性检验。结果表明，当算符和态固定而度量改变时出现的不确定关系表观违反（apparent violation），实质是表示不匹配（mismatch of representations），而非不确定性原理的失效。

Conclusion: 非厄米系统存在多种等价的表示，通过同构切换表示不会改变理论的物理内容；度量的不当变更会导致对不确定性原理的表面违反，需要在同构框架下正确迁移算符和态以保证物理自洽性。

Abstract: We study metric representations in finite-dimensional non-Hermitian quantum mechanics. The main purpose of this work is to emphasize that the physical description of a non-Hermitian system may be formulated in different, but isomorphic, Hilbert spaces. In particular, within the Krein-space formalism, we show that the vector space endowed with an indefinite Krein metric can be explicitly related to the standard Hilbert space through a suitable isomorphism. This observation is essential for a consistent description of non-Hermitian Hamiltonians. Physical states, metrics, and operators must be transported through the corresponding Hilbert-space isomorphism. In this way, equivalent representations of the same system can be used without changing the physical content of the theory. We illustrate these theoretical aspects by studying a two-level non-Hermitian spin model. We use the Robertson uncertainty relation as a consistency test. Apparent violations can arise when operators and states are kept fixed while the metric is changed, and therefore reflect a mismatch of representations rather than a failure of the uncertainty principle.

### [68] [How to Untwist Twisted Gauge Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28888)
*Serge Lazzarini,Thierry Masson,Louis Usala*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在扭曲规范场（twisted gauge fields）与标准规范场（standard gauge fields）之间建立了一个同构（isomorphism），该同构通过一个更大的主丛（principal bundle）$\mathcal{S}$ 实现，并允许在标准规范理论（如杨-米尔斯理论）中使用局部扭曲场，同时为 dressing fields 提供了新的主丛截面（section）解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有规范理论中，扭曲规范场与标准规范场分属不同的数学结构，缺乏统一的处理框架，限制了扭曲场在标准规范理论（如杨-米尔斯（Yang-Mills）理论）中的应用。同时，dressing fields 的几何意义尚未被充分阐明。

Method: 作者构造了一个更大的主丛 $\mathcal{S}$，使得 $\mathcal{P}$ 和 $\mathcal{Q}$ 成为其商丛（quotient bundles）。基于这一结构，建立了 $\mathcal{P}$ 上扭曲规范场空间与另一不同主丛 $\mathcal{Q}$ 上标准规范场空间之间的同构，该同构可延拓至底流形（base manifold）上的局部场（local fields）。此外，$\mathcal{S}$ 的同构类（isomorphism classes）与上循环（cocycle）的等价类（equivalence classes）之间存在一一对应。

Result: 实现了扭曲规范场与标准规范场的统一数学表述，使得局部扭曲场可直接用于标准规范理论中，从而同时处理来自 $\mathcal{P}$ 和 $\mathcal{Q}$ 的两个对称群（symmetry groups）。对 dressing fields 给出了新的解释，即将其视为主丛的动态（dynamic）或主动（active）截面。

Conclusion: 该同构为扭曲规范理论提供了一个统一的几何框架，拓展了标准规范理论的应用范围，并为 dressing fields 的几何本质提供了新的视角。

Abstract: This paper provides an isomorphism between the space of twisted gauge fields on a principal bundle $\mathcal{P}$ and the space of standard gauge fields on a different principal bundle $\mathcal{Q}$ associated to $\mathcal{P}$. This isomorphism extends to local fields on the base manifold, which enables the use of local twisted fields in standard gauge theories (e.g. Yang-Mills-like theories). This allows one to deal with two symmetry groups, coming from $\mathcal{P}$ and $\mathcal{Q}$, respectively. The construction makes use of a larger principal bundle $\mathcal{S}$ which has $\mathcal{P}$ and $\mathcal{Q}$ as quotient bundles. The gauge structure on $\mathcal{S}$ encodes both standard and twisted gauge structures on $\mathcal{P}$. In addition, the isomorphism classes of bundles $\mathcal{S}$ are in 1:1 correspondence with the equivalence classes of cocycles (up to a coboundary). This paper also provides a new interpretation of (full) dressing fields as dynamic (or active) sections of a principal bundle.

### [69] [The heat-kernel master field on $\mathbb{Z}^d$ at strong coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28945)
*Thibaut Lemoine*

Main category: math-ph

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究大 $N$ 杨-米尔斯理论在强耦合和热核作用下的精确行为，特别是 Wilson 圈期望的大 $N$ 极限、因子化性质以及主场（master field）的特征。

Method: 提出根热核主圈方程（rooted heat-kernel master loop equation），该方程在扩展的圈观测量空间上封闭；结合伴论文中的通用有限 $N$ 对偶公式（universal finite-$N$ duality formulas）和大 $N$ 热核估计，证明强耦合、阶数截断的根轨迹展开（strong-coupling, order-truncated rooted trajectory expansion），并识别其领头项为主场。

Result: 归一化 Wilson 圈期望存在无限体积大 $N$ 极限，在领头阶因子化，并具有全阶 $1/N$ 展开，系数指数局域；主场的领头项满足面积律上界，且具有更强的系数版本。

More precisely, we prove that normalized Wilson loop expectations have infinite-volume large-$N$ limits, factorize at leading order, and admit an all-order $1/N$-expansion with exponentially local coefficients, whose leading order characterizes the master field. We also prove an area-law upper bound for the heat-kernel master field, with a stronger coefficientwise version.
  The proof is based on a rooted heat-kernel master loop equation. Unlike the Wilson-action equation or the two-dimensional Makeenko--Migdal equation, this equation does not close on Wilson loop observables alone; it closes on an extended space of loop observables coupled to compactly supported plaquette decorations. We prove a strong-coupling, order-truncated rooted trajectory expansion and then identify its leading term with the master field. The main inputs are the universal finite-$N$ duality formulas developed in the companion paper \cite{Lem26a} and large-$N$ heat-kernel estimates from \cite{LemMai25,LM2}.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 所提出的上同调方法不仅为共形反常提供了新的概念性理解，还被预期能够成为高效计算微扰贝塔函数高阶系数的工具。

Abstract: We propose a cohomological approach to computing the conformal anomaly. Using the example of current-current deformations of two-dimensional conformal field theories, we reproduce the well-known Cardy formula for the leading contribution to the perturbative beta function as the coefficient of the cocycle that realizes the obstruction to deforming the Virasoro module structure on the state space. In addition to offering a novel conceptual perspective on the conformal anomaly, the proposed approach is anticipated to provide an efficient tool for computing higher-order coefficients of perturbative beta functions.

### [71] [A Unified Geometric Framework for BPS Flows: Split Attractor, Hessian, and Spectral Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29190)
*Qiang Wang*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个统一的几何框架，系统关联了$\mathcal{N}=2$超对称规范理论中BPS中心荷的三种结构：分裂吸引子流（SAF）、Hessian流（HF）和谱网络（SN），并基于此框架得到了新的BPS谱与盘计数生成函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: $\mathcal{N}=2$超对称规范理论中，与BPS中心荷相关的三种几何结构——分裂吸引子流（split attractor flow）、Hessian流（Hessian flow）和谱网络（spectral network）——各自独立发展，缺乏统一的几何框架来揭示它们之间的深层关联。

Method: 利用Kähler结构证明SAF与梯度Hessian流之间的正交性；通过提升-投影对偶性（lift-projection duality）建立谱网络与特征Hessian流（characteristic Hessian flow）的联系；采用基于SAF树深度的归纳法证明Kontsevich-Soibelman（KS）等变性。

Result: 给出了纯$SU(2)$和$N_f=4$（含更高味荷的新BPS指标）、纯$SU(3)$（完整BPS谱重构）、$SU(4)$、Kronecker $3$-quiver等详细例子；通过归纳法推导了Argyres-Douglas $H_1$理论的闭式BPS谱$\Omega(n\alpha_1+m\alpha_2)=\binom{n+m}{n}$；在热带极限（tropical limit）下推导了$SU(N)$规范理论的盘计数显式生成函数$Z_{\mathrm{disk}}^{SU(N)}$。

Conclusion: 该统一框架展现了强大的计算能力，为$\mathcal{N}=2$超对称规范理论提供了可验证的新预言。

Abstract: We provide a systematic and rigorous geometric framework that relates three structures naturally associated to BPS central charges in $\mathcal{N}=2$ supersymmetric gauge theories: the split attractor flow (SAF) of $|Z|$, the Hessian flow (HF) of $\operatorname{Im}(e^{-i\vartheta}Z)$, and the spectral network (SN) on the base curve of the Hitchin fibration. Our main contributions are: (i) a concise proof of orthogonality between SAF and gradient Hessian flow using only the Kahler structure; (ii) a precise lift-projection duality showing that the spectral network projects to the *characteristic Hessian flow* (the Hamiltonian flow of $\operatorname{Im}(e^{-i\vartheta}Z)$) on the Hitchin base, clarifying a crucial distinction; (iii) a complete proof of the Kontsevich-Soibelman (KS) equivariance by induction on the SAF tree depth, with the geometric ordering provided by the characteristic Hessian flow. We illustrate the framework with detailed and nontrivial examples: $SU(2)$ pure and $N_f=4$ (including new BPS indices for higher flavour charges), $SU(3)$ pure (full BPS spectrum reconstruction), $SU(4)$, the Kronecker $3$-quiver, and we apply the induction to derive a closed-form BPS spectrum for the Argyres-Douglas $H_1$ theory, $Ω(nα_1+mα_2)=\binom{n+m}{n}$, which is a new result. In the tropical limit we obtain an explicit generating function for disk counts in $SU(N)$ gauge theories, $Z_{\mathrm{disk}}^{SU(N)} = \prod_{α\inΦ_+}\prod_{k\ge1}(1-e^{-k\langleα,y\rangle})^{-\binom{k+\mathrm{ht}(α)-1}{\mathrm{ht}(α)-1}}$, which follows directly from our recursion. These results demonstrate the computational power of the unified framework and provide new, verifiable predictions.

</details>


### [72] [Probability density functions as solutions of heterogeneous Cattaneo-Vernotte diffusion equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29234)
*K. Górska,Ž. Tomovski,A. Horzela,M. Magdziarz*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文考虑具有指数型扩散系数的非齐次Cattaneo-Vernotte方程，在解在正负无穷处消失的初始边界条件下，利用拉普拉斯变换法（Laplace transform method）获得以修正贝塞尔函数（modified Bessel functions）之比表示的精确解析解，并通过完全单调函数（complete monotone functions）理论证明所得解为概率密度函数（probability density functions）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究具有指数型扩散系数的非齐次Cattaneo-Vernotte方程，以拓展该方程在异质介质中的解析求解能力，并揭示其解的数学性质。

Method: 采用拉普拉斯变换法（Laplace transform method）求解非齐次Cattaneo-Vernotte方程，得到两类由修正贝塞尔函数（modified Bessel functions）之比表示的精确解析解，并运用完全单调函数（complete monotone functions）理论验证解的概率密度函数性质。

Result: 获得了两种形式的精确解析解，均以修正贝塞尔函数之比表达；进一步证明这些解为概率密度函数（probability density functions）。

Conclusion: 所获得的精确解析解具有概率密度函数的数学结构，为理解异质Cattaneo-Vernotte方程在热传导或扩散问题中的物理解释提供了理论基础。

Abstract: In this paper, we considered a heterogeneous Cattaneo-Vernotte equation with an exponential type of diffusion coefficient under the fundamental initial and boundary conditions stating that the solution vanishes at $+/-$ infinity. Owing to the Laplace transform method we obtain two forms of exact analytical solutions which are presented in terms of the ratio of modified Bessel functions. Using the theory of complete monotone functions, we show that the obtained solutions are probability density functions.

### [73] [PDE-constrained optimization for virtual sensing in structural dynamics: Full-field displacement and force recovery from sparse sensors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29349)
*Minjae Kim,Jaehwan Jeong,Jaemin Kim*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文将虚拟传感问题建模为偏微分方程约束优化（PDE-constrained optimization, PDE-CO）问题，通过联合恢复全场位移和施加力分布，在结构健康监测的三个算例上显著优于传统模态展开方法，位移误差降低2至17倍，精度达到亚百分比水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虚拟传感（virtual sensing）——即从稀疏传感器测量恢复全场结构响应——是结构健康监测（structural health monitoring）中的一项基本挑战，现有方法如模态展开（modal expansion）在恢复精度和力与位移的联合优化方面存在局限。

Method: 将虚拟传感形式化为偏微分方程约束优化（PDE-constrained optimization, PDE-CO）问题，以弹性动力学方程作为等式约束，施加力分布为优化变量，联合恢复全场位移和力；通过反向模式自动微分（reverse-mode automatic differentiation）计算Tikhonov正则化目标函数的梯度，并采用L-BFGS迭代求解最优状态；框架结合离线FEniCSx有限元装配阶段与在线GPU加速JAX阶段。

Result: 在悬臂板、90°弯管和代表300 MW压水核反应堆的反应堆压力容器（reactor pressure vessel, RPV）三个复杂度递增的算例中，PDE-CO方法在所有情况下均优于模态展开，位移误差降低2至17倍，每个算例精度均达到亚百分比水平；GPU加速相比CPU实现高达64.8倍的加速比。

Conclusion: PDE-CO通过偏微分方程约束同时恢复位移和力，克服了模态展开中力需要从截断模态坐标反算且未参与联合优化的缺点；尽管计算成本增加，但GPU加速有效抵消了这一代价。

Abstract: Virtual sensing -- recovering full-field structural response from sparse sensor measurements -- is a fundamental challenge in structural health monitoring. This study formulates virtual sensing as a PDE-constrained optimization (PDE-CO) problem, where the governing elastodynamic equation serves as an equality constraint, the applied force distribution is the optimization variable, and the full-field displacement and force are jointly recovered. Gradients of the Tikhonov-regularized objective are computed via reverse-mode automatic differentiation through the forward PDE solver, and L-BFGS iteratively finds the optimal state. The framework couples an offline FEniCSx stage for finite element assembly with an online GPU-accelerated JAX stage, and is verified on three examples of increasing complexity: a cantilever plate, a $90^\circ$ elbow pipe, and a reactor pressure vessel (RPV) representative of a 300~MW pressurized nuclear reactor. PDE-CO consistently outperforms modal expansion across all three cases, reducing displacement errors by factors of $2$ to $17\times$ with sub-percent accuracy on every example. Unlike modal expansion, where force is derived by back-calculation from truncated modal coordinates and is not jointly optimized, PDE-CO recovers displacement and force simultaneously through the PDE constraint; the increased computational cost is offset by GPU acceleration delivering up to $64.8\times$ speedup over CPU.

</details>


### [74] [A Multi-Body Dobrushin-Sokal Criterion -- Part II](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29404)
*Jan Philipp Neumann*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了适用于具有复数值多体相互作用晶格气体的梅耶簇展开绝对收敛的充分条件，利用超图划分方案处理强多体相互作用，并与Gruber-Kunz条件结合扩展了聚合物展开的收敛结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典梅耶簇展开（Mayer cluster expansion）的收敛性主要针对成对相互作用，对多体相互作用（尤其是含复数值、高阶硬核排斥）的适用性有限，需要更一般的收敛条件。

Method: 通过提出一个绝对收敛的充分条件，并引入基于生成超图（spanning hypergraphs）的划分方案（partition scheme），将经典结果作为特例统一处理；同时将该条件与Gruber-Kunz条件结合，扩展聚合物展开（polymer expansion）的收敛范围。

Result: 该条件不仅涵盖多项经典收敛结果，还能处理超图独立多项式（hypergraph independence polynomials）背景下的高阶硬核排斥。与Gruber-Kunz条件结合后的收敛结果可与Nguyen & Fernández (2024)的最新成果相媲美。

Conclusion: 提出的充分条件为具有复数值多体相互作用的晶格气体提供了统一的收敛性框架，并在处理强多体相互作用及聚合物展开方面展现出优越性和竞争力。

Abstract: We prove a sufficient condition for the absolute convergence of Mayer cluster expansions of log-partition and correlation functions applicable to lattice gases with possibly complex-valued multi-body interactions. Not only are several classical results subsumed but a partition scheme for spanning hypergraphs also makes our methods well-suited for treating stronger multi-body interactions, including higher-order hard-core repulsion in the context of hypergraph independence polynomials. Furthermore, our approach is easily combined with the Gruber--Kunz condition to produce extended convergence results for the polymer expansion of lattice gases, rivalling those obtained not too long ago by Nguyen and Fernández (2024).

### [75] [Existence and absence of Bose-Einstein condensation in the interacting random Kac-Luttinger model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30277)
*C. Boccato,J. Kerner,M. Pechmann,W. Spitzer*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究Kac-Luttinger随机连续介质模型中零温下相互作用玻色子的凝聚类型转变。弱相互作用下证明了单粒子哈密顿量最低本征态中的凝聚（I型BEC），强相互作用下证明局域化状态中不可能发生凝聚，并证明了广义凝聚（多个本征态作为整体被宏观占据），从而展示了III型BEC的形成。这是该方向在高维随机连续模型上的首个严格结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有的关于随机系统中玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（Bose-Einstein condensation, BEC）的严格结果主要局限于一维或离散格点模型；该研究旨在将严格分析推广到高维随机连续介质模型，研究相互作用强度导致的凝聚类型的转变。

Method: 采用Kac-Luttinger引入的高维随机连续介质模型，在零温下对弱相互作用和强相互作用两种情形分别进行理论分析，利用单粒子哈密顿量的本征态性质来刻画不同类型的凝聚。

Result: 弱相互作用时，证明了单粒子哈密顿量最低本征态中的凝聚（type-I BEC）；强相互作用时，证明了局域化状态中无法发生凝聚，但存在多个单粒子哈密顿量本征态作为一个整体被宏观占据的广义凝聚（generalized condensation），且其中没有任何一个本征态单独被宏观占据（type-III BEC），从而证明了凝聚类型的转变。

Conclusion: 该工作首次在高维随机连续介质模型中严格证明了由相互作用强度驱动的凝聚类型转变，填补了该方向上的理论空白。

Abstract: In this paper, we study interacting bosons at zero temperature in a random and higher-dimensional continuum model introduced by Kac and Luttinger. For weak interactions we prove that there is condensation in the lowest eigenstate of the one-particle Hamiltonian (type-I BEC). For strong interactions, however, we show that condensation in a localized state cannot occur. We also prove generalized condensation, where a family of eigenstates of the one-particle Hamiltonian is macroscopically occupied as a whole. Combining these results yields a scenario where there is generalized condensation into a family of eigenstates of the one-particle Hamiltonian, but none of them is macroscopically occupied itself (type-III BEC). This proves a transition in the type of condensation. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first rigorous result in this direction for a random continuum model in higher dimensions.

</details>


### [76] [Generalized Hermite Polynomials and Spectral Degeneracies of a Singular Sextic Oscillator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30357)
*Davide Guzzetti,Dmitrii Rachenkov*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究准精确可解奇异六次振子及其代数谱，证明其特征多项式判别式可分解为三个因子，其中之一是广义埃尔米特多项式 $H_{mn}$ 的平方，其零点对应于第四潘勒韦方程有理解的极点。谱简并点（能级交叉点）与广义埃尔米特多项式的零点精确对应，提供了四阶潘勒韦方程版本的 Shapiro–Tater 渐近对应。此外，六次振子同时存在两个指数行为相反的拟多项式本征函数的参数条件也由广义埃尔米特多项式刻画，并给出了 $H_{mn}$ 的新行列式表示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究准精确可解奇异六次振子的代数谱结构，特别是谱简并（level crossing）现象的判据，并建立与第四潘勒韦方程（Painlevé IV）和广义埃尔米特多项式（generalized Hermite polynomial）之间的精确联系，从而推广最初针对四次振子与第二潘勒韦方程（Painlevé II）提出的 Shapiro–Tater 渐近对应。

Method: 通过分析确定代数谱的矩阵的特征多项式（characteristic polynomial），证明其判别式（discriminant）在特定参数范围内可自然分解为三个因子。利用广义埃尔米特多项式 $H_{mn}$ 的零点与第四潘勒韦方程有理解的极点之间的对应关系，刻画判别式轨迹（discriminant locus）的一个分量的谱简并点。同时研究六次振子同时存在两个指数行为相反的拟多项式（quasi-polynomial）本征函数的参数条件。

Result: 判别式的一个因子是广义埃尔米特多项式 $H_{mn}$ 的平方，其零点对应第四潘勒韦方程有理解的极点。谱简并点与 $H_{mn}$ 的零点精确对应，建立了 Painlevé IV 版本的 Shapiro–Tater 渐近对应。六次振子同时存在两个指数行为相反的拟多项式本征函数的参数条件也由 $H_{mn}$ 控制。此外给出了 $H_{mn}$ 的新行列式表示：即为代数谱矩阵的两个互补块的特征多项式的结式（resultant）。

Conclusion: 建立了准精确可解奇异六次振子的代数谱与第四潘勒韦方程及广义埃尔米特多项式之间的精确数学对应，推广了 Shapiro–Tater 渐近对应的适用范围，并为广义埃尔米特多项式提供了新的行列式表示。

Abstract: We study a quasi-exactly solvable singular sextic oscillator and its algebraic spectrum. For a distinguished range of parameters, we prove that the discriminant of the characteristic polynomial of the matrix determining the algebraic spectrum admits a natural factorization into three factors. One of these factors is the square of a generalized Hermite polynomial $H_{mn}$, whose zeros are poles of a rational solution of the fourth Painlevé equation. Hence, the spectral degeneracies (level crossing points) corresponding to a component of the discriminant locus are in exact correspondence with the zeros of generalized Hermite polynomials, providing an exact Painlevé IV analogue of the Shapiro--Tater asymptotic correspondence originally conjectured for the quartic oscillator and Painlevé II. We also characterize the values of the parameters for which the sextic oscillator admits simultaneously two quasi-polynomial eigenfunctions with opposite exponential behaviour at infinity, and show that this phenomenon is also governed by generalized Hermite polynomials. Our result also yields a new determinantal representation of $H_{mn}$ as the resultant of the characteristic polynomials of two complementary blocks of the matrix determining the algebraic spectrum.

</details>


### [77] [A Kac system interacting with two heat reservoirs: the shearing case](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30529)
*Federico Bonetto,Matthew Powell*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究一个由 M 个粒子组成的系统与两个大粒子库（各含 N ≫ M 个粒子）通过随机碰撞相互作用的动力学过程。该过程由 Kac 型主方程（Kac-type master equation）描述。证明在时间短于 √N / M 的尺度下，系统与有限库的相互作用可被近似为与两个剪切动态麦克斯韦热浴（shearing dynamic Maxwellian thermostats）的相互作用；当两个库的温度和平均速度相等时，还能得到一致的时间均匀近似。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解有限大小的热库（heat reservoirs）如何近似于理想化的无穷大热库（即热浴，thermostats），是统计力学（statistical mechanics）中的一个基础性问题。本文旨在严格证明，在特定时间尺度内，两个有限的大粒子库可以对一个小子系统的动力学产生与无穷大热浴等效的效应。

Method: 系统与热库之间的相互作用通过随机碰撞实现，整体演化由 Kac 型主方程（Kac-type master equation）描述。两个库的初始状态为非中心麦克斯韦分布（non-centered Maxwellian distributions），分别具有不同的温度（T_+ 和 T_-）和平均速度（p_+ 和 p_-）。通过数学分析证明，在时间尺度 τ < √N / M 内，有限库的效应可被剪切动态麦克斯韦热浴（shearing dynamic Maxwellian thermostats）所近似。

Result: 严格证明了当时间 t < √N / M 时，系统与两个有限粒子库的相互作用等价于与两个无穷大剪切动态麦克斯韦热浴的相互作用。作为副产品，当 T_+ = T_- 且 p_+ = p_- 时，得到了一个一致的时间均匀近似（uniform in time approximation）。

Conclusion: 有限大粒子库在足够短的时间尺度内能够被无穷大动态热浴有效近似，这一结果为使用理想化热浴模型（thermostat models）描述有限库相互作用提供了严格的理论依据。在对称条件下，这种近似甚至可以在整个时间轴上一致成立。

Abstract: We study a system formed by $M$ particles moving in 3 dimensions and interacting with two heat reservoirs, each with $N\gg M$ particles. The system and the reservoirs interact via random collisions and thus evolve via a Kac-type master equation. The initial state of the reservoirs is given by two non-centered Maxwellian distributions; they have temperature $T_+$ and $T_-$ and have average velocity $\vec p_+$ and $\vec p_-$, respectively. We prove that, for times shorter than $\sqrt{N}/M$, the interaction with the two reservoirs is well-approximated by the interaction with two shearing {\it dynamic} Maxwellian thermostats (i.e. heat reservoirs with $N=\infty$). As a byproduct of our analysis, we obtain a uniform in time approximation when $T_+=T_-$ and $\vec p_+=\vec p_-$.

</details>

### [78] [Deformed W-algebras and chiralized cluster seeds: subregular W-algebras and Inverse Quantum Hamiltonian Reduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30032)
*Mikhail Bershtein,Jean-Emile Bourgine,Ethan Fursman*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 本文引入手性簇种子（chiral cluster seeds）形式主义，用量子变形顶点算子取代量子簇变量，并将其应用于多种(q,t)-变形W-代数（包括超代数情形）。论文还构造了次正则（subregular）(q,t)-变形W-代数，建立了其与自由场实现及逆量子哈密顿约化的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 发展一种统一的形式主义，用以描述和关联多种(q,t)-变形W-代数的自由场实现，并填补次正则W-代数在(q,t)-变形框架下的研究空白。

Method: 引入手性簇种子（chiral cluster seeds）形式主义，用量子变形顶点算子（deformed vertex operators）替代量子簇变量（quantum cluster variables），通过关联的装饰箭图（decorated quiver）编码顶点算子乘积展开（operator product expansions）。对于次正则情形，构造了将其嵌入到秩二海森堡代数（rank-two Heisenberg algebra）张量积自由场实现中。

Result: 证明了不同自由场实现之间可通过关联手性簇种子的突变（mutations）相互联系。构造了次正则(q,t)-变形W-代数$\mathcal{W}_{\mathfrak{q},\mathfrak{t}}^{\text{sub}}(\mathfrak{sl}(N))$，并描述了所有可通过种子突变获得的自由场实现。建立了该代数与$\mathcal{W}_{\mathfrak{q},\mathfrak{t}}(\mathfrak{gl}(1|N))$的关系。

Conclusion: 所提出的手性簇种子形式主义为理解(q,t)-变形W-代数的结构提供了统一框架，且次正则代数的嵌入构造可视为逆量子哈密顿约化（inverse quantum Hamiltonian reduction）的变形类比。

Abstract: The recently introduced formalism of chiral cluster seeds replaces quantum cluster variables with deformed vertex operators. In this framework, a decorated quiver associated with a seed encodes the operator product expansions of the corresponding vertex operators. This formalism is applied to several $(q,t)$-deformed W-algebras, including $\mathcal{W}_{\mathfrak{q},\mathfrak{t}}(\mathfrak{gl}(N|M))$, $U_q(\widehat{\mathfrak{sl}}_2)$, and the deformed Bershadsky--Polyakov algebra. In particular, it is shown that different free field realizations of the currents are related by mutations of the associated chiral cluster seed.
  The second part of the paper introduces a $(q,t)$-deformation of the subregular W-algebras, denoted by $\mathcal{W}_{\mathfrak{q},\mathfrak{t}}^{\text{sub}}(\mathfrak{sl}(N))$. All free field realizations obtainable through seed mutations are described. An embedding of $\mathcal{W}_{\mathfrak{q},\mathfrak{t}}^{\text{sub}}(\mathfrak{sl}(N))$ into the free field realization of $\mathcal{W}_{\mathfrak{q},\mathfrak{t}}(\mathfrak{sl}(N))$ tensored with a rank-two Heisenberg algebra is constructed. This embedding may be viewed as a deformed analogue of inverse quantum Hamiltonian reduction. The relation between the subregular algebras and $\mathcal{W}_{\mathfrak{q},\mathfrak{t}}(\mathfrak{gl}(1|N))$ is also discussed.

</details>

### [79] [McMg: A Learned Phase-Space Multi-channel Multigrid Preconditioner for Helmholtz Equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30495)
*Jiwei Jia,Xinliang Liu,Juntao Wang,Jinchao Xu*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出多通道多重网格（Multi-channel Multigrid, McMg），一种面向高波数异质亥姆霍兹方程（heterogeneous Helmholtz equations）的学习型相空间多重网格预处理器，通过在粗化物理空间时保留通道维度中的局部波动信息，实现了比经典方法与现有神经预处理器更优的迭代收敛效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高波数异质亥姆霍兹方程的数值求解面临三大挑战：离散算子不定（indefinite）、污染效应（pollution）降低相位精度、标量粗网格校正（scalar coarse-grid correction）会丢失振荡误差所携带的局部相位与传播方向信息。现有方法在这些问题上表现不足。

Method: McMg 在迭代框架中将残差映射为校正量，核心思想是在粗化物理空间时，通过通道维度保留未解析的局部波动信息：每个粗网格节点携带一组经学习的振幅、相位、方向与散射系数包（packet），而非单个标量未知量。架构结合线性多通道转移算子、局部自适应模板（locally adaptive stencils）、神经 PDE 算子及由波速生成的介质相关光滑子（medium-dependent smoothers）。对于固定介质，V-cycle 对残差是线性的；非线性物理特征在设置阶段一次性计算并缓存，在线迭代仅执行固定系数的卷积运算。

Result: 实验表明，在小域上训练的模型可直接迁移至更大域与更高有效波数。Layer-by-Layer Progressive Finetuning (LLPF) 策略通过仅添加与微调新的粗层来扩展学习型格林算子（Green's operator）的支撑范围。在高频、高对比度及大规模三维问题上的数值实验显示，McMg 在迭代次数与墙钟时间上均显著少于强经典基线，并持续优于现有神经预处理器。

Conclusion: McMg 通过多通道相空间粗化策略有效解决了高波数亥姆霍兹方程求解中的信息丢失难题，兼具线性计算效率与跨尺度泛化能力，为波传播问题的神经求解器提供了新的设计范式。

Abstract: Solving heterogeneous Helmholtz equations at high wavenumbers remains challenging because the discretized operator is indefinite, pollution degrades phase accuracy, and scalar coarse-grid correction can discard the local phase and propagation-direction information carried by oscillatory errors. We propose Multi-channel Multigrid (McMg), a learned phase-space multigrid preconditioner for heterogeneous Helmholtz equations. Rather than predicting the solution directly, McMg maps residuals to corrections within an iterative framework. Its central idea is to coarsen physical space while retaining unresolved local wave information in the channel dimension: each coarse node carries a learned packet of amplitude, phase, direction, and scattering coefficients rather than a single scalar unknown. The architecture combines linear multi-channel transfer operators with locally adaptive stencils, neural PDE operators, and medium-dependent smoothers whose coefficients are generated from the wave speed. For a fixed medium, the V-cycle is linear in the residual; nonlinear physical features are computed once in a setup phase and cached, so each online iteration reduces to convolutions with fixed coefficients. We further study generalization across scales. Models trained on small domains transfer directly to larger domains and higher effective wavenumbers, and a Layer-by-Layer Progressive Finetuning (LLPF) strategy extends the support of the learned Green's operator by adding and finetuning only new coarse levels. Numerical experiments on high-frequency, high-contrast, and large-scale three-dimensional problems demonstrate that McMg requires substantially fewer iterations and less wall-clock time than strong classical baselines, while consistently outperforming existing neural preconditioners.

</details>
