### [80] [The cost rate of nonlinear remote stabilization on the Aubry--André lattice: a reflected off-spectral exponent and the sharp identity for almost every phase](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28650)
*Nassim Athmouni,Nejib Brahmia,Ahmed Hachani*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 本文研究Aubry–André链通过边界执行器（boundary actuator）控制远端站点所需能量的指数速率 $r(α,λ)$，证明该速率等于转移余循环（transfer cocycle）在反射带边（reflected band edge）$z^\star$ 处的谱外Lyapunov指数 $\gamma_\lambda(z^\star)$。在金属–临界区间 $0<λ\le2$ 上无条件成立，在局域化区间 $λ>2$ 上对几乎所有相位和Diophantine频率成立，并给出误差阶估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解Aubry–André链（quasiperiodic tight-binding model）中边界驱动控制远处量子态所需能量随系统尺寸的指数增长行为，揭示其与系统谱性质、Lyapunov指数及局域化–临界–金属相变的内在联系。

Method: 通过精确本征基约化将能量 $\mathcal{E}_N$ 表示为边界振幅比（boundary-amplitude ratios）的Cauchy二次型 $\tilde b^\top C^{-1}\tilde b$；利用反射带边 $z^\star=2E_{\min}-2α-E_{\max}$ 处的转移余循环谱外Lyapunov指数给出指数速率；在 $λ<2$ 时依赖于次临界几乎可约性（subcritical almost reducibility），在 $λ=2$ 时利用Green函数等于Lyapunov指数；在 $λ>2$ 时通过无逆余循环形式及Christoffel–Darboux恒等式化简系数，结合三距离引理（three-distance lemma）完成下界估计。

Result: 指数速率恒等于 $r(α,λ)=\gamma_λ(z^\star)$；该速率落在一个宽度为 $\log_+(λ/2)$ 的区间内，当 $λ\le2$ 时区间两端重合（谱的对数容量为 $\max(1,λ/2)$）。在 $λ>2$ 时上界无条件成立，下界对每个Diophantine频率和几乎所有相位成立，误差 $O(N^{-2/(2+τ)})$（有界类型下为 $N^{-2/3}$）。相对 gap $1-r/\gamma_λ(z^\star)$ 在局域化相两端趋于零，$λ\to\infty$ 时 $g_{\mathbb{C}\setminusΣ_λ}(z^\star)\to\operatorname{arccosh}3$。

Conclusion: 边界驱动Aubry–André链的能量指数速率完全由谱外Lyapunov指数在反射带边的取值刻画，在金属–临界区无条件成立，在局域化区在几乎必然意义下成立，建立了控制论（control theory）与准周期算子谱理论（spectral theory of quasiperiodic operators）之间的精确联系。

Abstract: We study the exponential rate $r(α,λ)$ of the energy $\mathcal{E}_N$ needed to steer a far site, at distance $N$, of an Aubry--André chain $H_λ$ via one boundary actuator with closed-loop margin $α$. An exact eigenbasis reduction writes $\mathcal{E}_N$ as a Cauchy quadratic form $\tilde b^\top C^{-1}\tilde b$ in the boundary-amplitude ratios, whose rate is the off-spectral Lyapunov exponent of the transfer cocycle at the reflected band edge $z^\star=2E_{\min}-2α-E_{\max}$, giving $r(α,λ)=γ_λ(z^\star)$. The rate lies in a bracket of width $\log_+(λ/2)$ whose ends coincide for $λ\le2$, the spectrum having logarithmic capacity $\max(1,λ/2)$.
  We prove the identity unconditionally, for every phase, on the whole metallic--critical range $0<λ\le2$: for $λ<2$ through subcritical almost reducibility as the sole external input, and at $λ=2$ because the Green's function there equals the Lyapunov exponent. For $λ>2$ the upper bound is unconditional, and the lower bound takes localization as its only external input: an inverse-free cocycle form makes $\mathcal{E}_N$ a cancellation-free positive sum, and a Christoffel--Darboux identity collapses its coefficients to $|c_k|=Q(δ_k)(\hatψ^{(k)}_N)^2$, where band-edge near-degeneracies cancel. With a three-distance lemma this yields $r=γ_λ(z^\star)$ at every Diophantine frequency and almost every phase, with gap $O(N^{-2/(2+τ)})$ for type $τ$ ($N^{-2/3}$ at bounded type), unconditionally for $λ\geλ_1$ and under a polynomial-prefactor localization hypothesis for $2<λ<λ_1$. The relative gap $1-r/γ_λ(z^\star)$ vanishes at both ends of the localized phase, with $g_{\mathbb{C}\setminusΣ_λ}(z^\star)\to\operatorname{arccosh}3$ as $λ\to\infty$.

</details>


### [81] [Transfer Operators, Canonical Center Dynamics, and Spectral Applications for Long-Range Operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29154)
*Xianzhe Li,Zhenfu Wang,Jiangong You,Qi Zhou*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 本文提出一个关于一般动力系统上长程算子（long-range operators）的算子理论框架，通过建立纤维化解丛上的部分双曲分裂（partially hyperbolic splitting）定义了规范中心丛（Canonical Center Bundle, CCB），并证明该中心丛可经由转移算子（transfer operator）的Riesz谱投影表示。框架将谱问题约化至中心丛，进而得到谱的Johnson型刻画。应用于拟周期薛定谔算子（quasi-periodic Schrödinger operators），推导出中心Thouless公式（Center Thouless formula），并依此证明了态密度的绝对连续性、定量Hölder连续性以及Anderson局域化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长程算子在动力系统与数学物理中具有重要地位，但缺乏统一的算子理论框架。具体地，Eliasson提出的态密度绝对连续性问题及You提出的定量Hölder连续性问题尚未解决，需要新的分析工具。

Method: 建立纤维化解丛上的部分双曲分裂，定义规范中心丛（CCB）；利用转移算子的Riesz谱投影表示中心丛；证明该中心丛在局部区域与有限近似内在中心丛（ICB）在间隙收敛（gap convergence）意义上一致；通过部分双曲结构将谱问题约化至中心丛，获得Johnson型谱刻画；针对拟周期薛定谔算子，证明中心余环（center cocycle）的解析性并建立中心Thouless公式。

Result: 在拟周期薛定谔算子（解析跳跃项、大解析势能、丢番图频率）设定下：1) 建立了态密度积分（IDS）的绝对连续性，解决了Eliasson问题；2) 证明了IDS的定量Hölder连续性，部分回答了You的提问；3) 获得了原薛定谔算子的Anderson局域化。

Conclusion: 所提出的算子理论框架为长程算子的谱分析提供了统一途径，部分双曲结构有效约化谱问题，中心Thouless公式成为推导态密度正则性与局域化现象的关键工具。

Abstract: We introduce an operator-theoretic framework for long-range operators over general dynamical systems with analytic hopping and small potential. By establishing a partially hyperbolic splitting on the fibered solution bundle, we define the Canonical Center Bundle (CCB) as the center subbundle of this splitting, which is shown to be globally trivial. The center bundle admits a representation via Riesz spectral projections of the transfer operator. Furthermore, we show that, in the local regime, the center bundle arising in this framework essentially coincides, in the sense of gap convergence, with the Intrinsic Center Bundles (ICB) obtained from finite-range approximations in \cite{GJ}.
  The partially hyperbolic structure thereby reduces the spectral problem to the center bundle, leading to a Johnson-type characterization of the spectrum in terms of the associated center cocycle. We then apply this framework to quasi-periodic Schrödinger operators with analytic hopping, large analytic potentials and Diophantine frequency. In this setting, the center cocycle is analytic and satisfies a Center Thouless formula. As consequences, we establish the absolute continuity of the integrated density of states (IDS), resolving a problem of Eliasson; prove quantitative Hölder continuity of the IDS, partially answering a question of You; and obtain Anderson localization for the original Schrödinger operators.

### [82] [Global smooth solutions by high mode Lie-Transport noise for Logarithmically Hyperdissipative Navier-Stokes equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28575)
*Antonio Agresti,Federico Butori,Eliseo Luongo*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文证明，在三维环面上带李传输噪声（Lie-transport noise）的对数超黏性纳维-斯托克斯模型（Navier-Stokes model），当噪声强度足够大且频率足够高时，系统以接近1的概率存在唯一全局光滑解。该机制通过缩放极限（scaling limit）产生有效耗散（effective dissipation），从而规避了守恒量缺失与随机拉伸奇异性的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有工作未能处理具有物理动机的噪声——该噪声不守恒能量（energy）或涡度（enstrophy），而是守恒环量（circulation）。因此，亟需建立这类系统的全局适定性（global well-posedness）。

Method: 采用对数超黏性（logarithmically hyperviscous）模型与李传输噪声相结合，包含输运（transport）与拉伸（stretching）两种效应；通过缩放极限产生有效耗散的概率机制来进行分析。

Result: 在噪声强度足够大且频率足够高的条件下，系统以任意接近1的概率存在唯一全局光滑解。

Conclusion: 该概率机制成功绕开了守恒量缺失的困难，并驯服了随机拉伸的奇异性，从而建立了全局适定性。

Abstract: We study a logarithmically hyperviscous Navier-Stokes model on the three-dimensional torus with Lie-transport noise, which includes both transport and stretching. We prove that, for noise of sufficiently large intensity and high frequency, the system admits a unique global smooth solution with probability arbitrarily close to one. Unlike previous works, this physically motivated noise does not preserve energy or enstrophy, but rather circulation. Global well-posedness is established through a probabilistic mechanism that produces effective dissipation via a scaling limit. Crucially, this approach bypasses the lack of conserved quantities and tames the singular nature of stochastic stretching.

### [83] [Random homomorphisms and Lipschitz functions on trees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29426)
*Alon Heller,Yinon Spinka*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究一般有限树上均匀随机图同态（graph homomorphism）的根节点值分布，通过与离散高斯型随机变量的随机比较，建立了上下尾界、方差界，并揭示了该模型在无限树上的局域化/去局域化转变，结论依赖于根与叶之间的有效电阻（effective resistance）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 图同态和整数值Lipschitz函数（Lipschitz functions）是统计力学、概率论与组合学中的重要模型。已有结果主要针对正则树或最小度至少为3的树，而一般树（尤其是包含叶节点的树）上的行为尚未被充分理解。本文旨在填补这一空白，建立适用于任意有限树的一般性结果。

Method: 本文采用随机比较（stochastic comparison）方法，将根节点同态值的绝对值与某些离散高斯型随机变量进行上下双向比较。分析工具包括与树关联的电路网络中的有效电阻（effective resistance）。研究在树上定义整数值函数，满足相邻顶点值相差恰好为1的约束，并在所有叶节点取值为0的条件下均匀随机采样。

Result: 主要结果包括：(1) 对所有偏差均成立的次高斯型（subgaussian）尾上界；(2) 在某个阈值之前成立的下界；(3) 方差的上界和下界，相差常数因子。对于无限局部有限树，该模型在暂留树（transient trees）上局域化（localized），在常返树（recurrent trees）上去局域化（delocalized）。类似结论对随机整数值Lipschitz函数也成立。

Conclusion: 本文将Benjamini–Häggström–Mossel关于正则树同态、Peled–Samotij–Yehudayoff关于正则树Lipschitz函数以及Lammers–Toninelli关于最小度≥3树上同态的结果推广到了一般有限树，建立了统一的随机比较框架。树上的局域化–去局域化转变由网络有效电阻完全刻画。

Abstract: A graph homomorphism is an integer-valued function on the vertex set of a graph that assigns values differing by exactly one to adjacent vertices. We consider uniformly random homomorphisms on general finite trees, conditioned to take the value zero at all leaves, and study the distribution of the value at the root. Our main result is a stochastic comparison, both from above and below, between the absolute values of the homomorphism value at the root and certain discrete Gaussian-like random variables. In particular, we obtain a subgaussian tail bound valid for all deviations, a matching lower bound that holds up to a certain threshold, and upper and lower variance bounds that differ by a constant factor. These bounds depend solely on the effective resistance between the root and the leaves in the associated electrical network. As a consequence, in the setting of infinite locally finite trees, we obtain that the homomorphism model is localized on transient trees and delocalized on recurrent trees. Analogous results are obtained for random integer-valued Lipschitz functions.
  Our results extend previous results of Benjamini--Häggström--Mossel on homomorphisms on regular trees, of Peled--Samotij--Yehudayoff on Lipschitz functions on regular trees, and of Lammers--Toninelli on homomorphisms on trees of minimum degree at least three.

### [85] [Propagation of chaos for Belavkin equations beyond pure states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29557)
*Gaoyue Guo*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文证明了一个由N个相互作用的密度矩阵值扩散过程组成的有限维系统的混沌传播（propagation of chaos）。在平均场哈密顿量（mean-field Hamiltonian）和独立布朗噪声驱动下，系统收敛到非线性矩阵值McKean-Vlasov扩散，并给出了显式迹范数（trace-norm）误差界。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究有限维相互作用量子系统在大N极限下的平均场行为，特别是混沌传播性质的严格数学证明，以理解从微观多体量子动力学到非线性平均场极限的过渡。

Method: 第一个结果结合了纯化论证（purification argument）、完全观测膨胀（fully observed dilation）、条件期望（conditional expectation）、相对熵估计（relative-entropy estimate）以及关联线性Zakai方程的稳定性估计。第二个结果在弱假设下利用随机BBGKY层级（stochastic BBGKY hierarchy）与紧致性加唯一性论证。结果给出了依赖于初始张量化误差和N的显式迹范数界。

Result: 第一个结果：针对任意混合初始态和所有测量效率，证明了每个固定边际在紧时间区间上一致收敛到非线性极限粒子的张量积，并给出了显式迹范数界。第二个结果：针对斜伴测量算符（skew-adjoint measurement operators），在混沌初始数据的较弱假设下，证明了每个固定边际的收敛性（不含显式速率）。

Conclusion: 建立了有限维相互作用密度矩阵扩散系统的混沌传播定理，为量子平均场动力学提供了严格的数学基础，覆盖了一般混合初始态和不同测量算符类型。

Abstract: We prove propagation of chaos for a finite-dimensional system of N interacting density matrix-valued diffusions. The interaction enters through a mean-field Hamiltonian, and each particle is driven by independent Brownian noises. The limiting equation is a nonlinear matrix-valued McKean-Vlasov diffusion whose coefficients depend on the averaged one-particle state.
  Our first result treats arbitrary mixed initial states and all measurement efficiencies. We prove convergence, uniformly on compact time intervals, of every fixed marginal toward the corresponding tensor product of nonlinear limiting particles, with an explicit trace-norm bound depending on the initial tensorization error and on N. The proof combines a purification argument, a fully observed dilation, conditional expectation, a relative-entropy estimate, and a stability estimate for the associated linear Zakai equations. Our second result considers skew-adjoint measurement operators. In this case the evolution preserves permutation symmetry and admits a stochastic BBGKY hierarchy. Under the weaker assumption of chaotic initial data, we prove convergence of each fixed marginal, without an explicit rate, by compactness and uniqueness for the limiting hierarchy.

### [86] [Single-point statistical moments of the nonhomogeneous stochastic advection equation in the small correlation length limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29479)
*Keiko Kircher,Cristian Proistosescu,Ryan L. Sriver*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文推导了非齐次随机平流方程（advection equation）单点统计矩（single-point statistical moments）的闭式表达式，利用特征线法（method of characteristics）获得解的显式形式，并给出了前四阶矩作为随机速度场特征长度尺度和时间平均场空间导数的函数；通过与数值模拟的对比验证了理论结果的准确性，提出了一个类似“状态方程”的广义框架，可用于直接从宏观平均态预测非高斯统计行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非齐次随机平流方程在自然界广泛存在（如地质、水文、大气科学），但其统计特性的解析求解长期受限于齐次系统的假设；非齐次情形传统上依赖高成本数值模拟，缺乏解析框架，因此亟需发展无需大规模数值计算的闭式表达理论。

Method: 首先采用特征线法获得非齐次随机平流方程（含线性松弛项）的解；然后基于该解推导单点统计矩的闭式表达式；将前四阶矩显式表达为随机速度场特征长度尺度与时间平均剖面空间导数的函数；最后通过数值模拟在多个物理参数下验证解析结果。

Result: 成功推导了前四阶单点统计矩的闭式解析表达式；数值模拟验证表明，解析结果与模拟结果在不同物理参数范围内高度吻合，证明了理论的可靠性。

Conclusion: 所发展的理论提供了一种广义“状态方程”式方法，能够直接从宏观平均状态预测系统的变异性与非高斯统计行为，适用于涵盖地质学、水文学和大气科学等跨时间与空间尺度的输运系统（transport systems）。

Abstract: This paper presents the derivation of closed-form expressions of the single-point statistical moments of a solution to a nonhomogeneous stochastic advection equation with a linear relaxation. While analytical solutions exist for homogeneous systems, nonhomogeneous cases have traditionally relied on intensive numerical simulations. Here, we provide an analytical framework for calculating single-point statistical moments by first obtaining the solution to the stochastic advection equation via the method of characteristics, from which the moments are derived. Explicit, closed-form expressions for the first four moments are derived as functions of the characteristic length scale of the stochastic velocity field and the spatial derivatives of time-mean profile of the field. The analytical results are validated against numerical simulations, demonstrating excellent agreement across a range of physical parameters. The resulting theory acts as a generalized ``equation-of-state" style approach for predicting variability and non-Gaussian statistical behavior directly from the macroscopic mean state, providing applicability across transport systems with a wide range of time and length scales, including geology, hydrology, and atmospheric sciences.

</details>


### [87] [Gappy Reconstruction of Bubbly Flows by Guided Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29843)
*Hridey Narula,Tianyi Li,Michele Buzzicotti,Luca Biferale,Prasad Perlekar*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本研究采用引导扩散模型（guided diffusion model）解决多相流中相受限测量下的速度场重建问题，利用二维切片训练，成功生成气泡相物理真实的速度场并重建三维流动，证明了扩散模型作为湍流多相流生成先验（generative priors）的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多相流实验难以同时获取不同相的速度测量数据，而基于相受限测量进行流场重建由于各相速度统计特性差异显著而极具挑战性。

Method: 使用引导扩散模型，从完全解析的三维直接数值模拟（direct numerical simulations）中提取二维速度场切片进行训练；模型可无条件生成速度场，也可在周围液相流动条件下进行条件生成；对相邻二维切片采用简单的拼接（patching）程序以重建气泡内部三维流场。

Result: 重建的气泡相速度场准确再现了流动的关键统计特征；相邻二维切片的拼接方法能够合理重建气泡内部的三维流场。

Conclusion: 扩散模型有潜力作为湍流多相流的三维生成先验，为从稀疏、部分或相受限测量中重建未观测或实验不可达的速度场开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Experiments in multiphase flows are often limited in their ability to simultaneously obtain velocity measurements in different phases. At the same time, flow reconstruction from phase-limited measurements is a challenging problem due to the substantially different velocity statistics across the phases. We address this problem for buoyancy-driven bubbly flows in the pseudo-turbulence regime by using a guided diffusion model. We train the model using two-dimensional slices of the velocity field extracted from fully resolved three-dimensional direct numerical simulations. The model generates physically realistic velocity fields both unconditionally and when conditioned on the surrounding liquid flow. The reconstructed bubble-phase velocity field accurately reproduces key statistical features of the flow. We further show that a simple patching procedure for adjacent two-dimensional slices enables a reasonable reconstruction of the three-dimensional flow inside a bubble. These results establish the potential of diffusion models to serve as generative priors for three-dimensional turbulent multiphase flows, opening a route toward the reconstruction of unobserved or experimentally inaccessible velocity fields from sparse, partial, or phase-limited measurements.

</details>

### [88] [Geometry-mediated shear softening in dense ordered granular packings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29051)
*Liuchi Li,Konstantinos Karapiperis*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过有限元模拟表明，在恒定体积分数下剪切致密有序颗粒堆积时，颗粒内部嵌入空隙所诱导的表观弹性各向异性与软化，可显著降低堆积体的表观剪切模量（最高降幅达90%），且该效应不依赖于颗粒的拉胀性（auxeticity），为软颗粒超材料（soft granular metamaterials）的集体力学性质设计提供了最小化机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高体积分数、强边界约束下的固体颗粒堆积体难以剪切。近期研究发现，在颗粒中嵌入空隙使其具有拉胀性（auxeticity）可改善剪切性；本文旨在检验拉胀性是否为必要条件，并探索在更受限的恒定体积分数条件下，颗粒几何如何调控堆积体的宏观弹性响应。

Method: 采用有限元模拟（finite element simulation），在恒定体积分数下对致密有序的颗粒堆积体施加剪切；通过控制颗粒内部嵌入空隙的几何形状，改变颗粒的表观弹性各向异性（apparent elastic anisotropy）与软化程度。

Result: 嵌入空隙的几何调控可使堆积体的表观剪切模量最多降低90%；该降低与接触力各向异性（contact-force anisotropy）的减小高度相关，且对系统尺寸和接触摩擦变化不敏感。

Conclusion: 拉胀性并非实现颗粒堆积体剪切软化的必要条件；颗粒尺度的几何设计，经由多体接触力学（multi-body contact mechanics）传递，能有效调控宏观系统尺度的弹性性质，为软颗粒超材料的靶向力学性能设计提供了最小化实现机制。

Abstract: Shearing a packing of solid granular grains can be difficult, especially when the solid fraction is high and the boundary confinement is strong. It was recently shown that embedding voids in grains can make a packing easier to shear when such voids make the grains auxetic. Here, we use finite element simulation to show that auxeticity is not a necessary condition even in a seemingly very constrained setting: shearing dense and ordered granular packings under a constant solid fraction. More specifically, by controlling the geometry of a void embedded in a grain, we induce an apparent elastic anisotropy and softening of the grain under shear, which collectively leads to a significant reduction -- up to 90\% -- of the apparent shear modulus of a packing of these grains. Complementary analysis shows that this reduction correlates well with a decrease in contact-force anisotropy, and is insensitive to system size and contact friction variation. Our results highlight how grain-scale geometry, mediated by multi-body contact mechanics, modulates macroscopic system-scale elasticity, providing a minimal design mechanism towards targeted collective mechanical properties of soft granular metamaterials.

</details>


### [89] [Emergence of beating in a magnetic flagellum consisting of active bots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29499)
*Francisca Guzmán-Lastra,Daniel Hernández,Nicolás Quintriqueo,Enkeleida Lushi,Erick Burgos*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过厘米级振动机器人（Hexbugs）构建磁性自推进粒子（MSPPs）链，研究了鞭毛拍动的涌现机制。实验与数值模拟结合，揭示了直链、稳定鞭毛拍动和裂变三种动力学 regime，其转变由主动力、链长和磁弯曲刚度竞争决定。拍动触发对应于超临界霍普夫分岔（supercritical Hopf bifurcation），磁弯曲刚度可通过偶极强度和链长独立调控，为主动细丝的力致屈曲与自振荡研究提供了宏观平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解主动细丝（active filaments）中鞭毛拍动（flagellar beating）的涌现机制及其力致屈曲不稳定性（buckling instability）的物理原理，并建立可独立调控活性和刚度的宏观实验平台。

Method: 使用厘米级振动机器人（Hexbugs）嵌入钕磁偶极子构建磁性自推进粒子（MSPPs）链；结合实验观测与数值模拟；引入运动学模型（kinematic model）复现取向动力学。

Result: 识别出三种动力学 regime：直链（straight chain）、稳定鞭毛拍动（stable flagellar beating）和裂变（fission）；拍动触发需要种子错位（seed misalignment），其由磁转矩（magnetic torques）与旋转噪声（rotational noise）平衡决定；该转变对应超临界霍普夫分岔（supercritical Hopf bifurcation）；运动学模型与实验观测高度吻合。

Conclusion: 磁弯曲刚度（magnetic bending stiffness）源于偶极-偶极相互作用（dipole-dipole interactions），可通过偶极强度和链长完全调谐，从而实现对活性和刚度的独立实验控制。该结果建立了一个用于研究主动细丝中力致屈曲与自振荡的宏观平台，与生物及合成微泳器（microswimmers）中的鞭毛运动直接相关。

Abstract: We investigate the emergence of flagellar beating in chains of magnetic self--propelled particles (MSPPs) built from centimeter--scale vibrating robots (Hexbugs) with embedded neodymium dipoles. When one end of the chain is anchored and self--propulsion is activated, longitudinal stress accumulates along the chain until it overcomes the magnetic bending stiffness, triggering a buckling instability that drives sustained flagellar beating. Using a combination of experiments and numerical simulations, we identify three distinct dynamical regimes straight chain, stable flagellar beating, and fission governed by the competition between active force, chain length, and magnetic bending stiffness. The onset of beating requires a seed misalignment set by the balance between magnetic torques and rotational noise, and we show that the transition corresponds to a supercritical Hopf bifurcation. A kinematic model reproduces the observed orientation dynamics with excellent agreement. The magnetic bending stiffness, which arises directly from dipole--dipole interactions, is fully tunable via dipole strength and chain length, offering independent experimental control over both activity and rigidity. Our results establish a macroscopic platform for studying force-induced buckling and self--oscillations in active filaments, with direct connections to flagellar motion in biological and synthetic microswimmers.

</details>


### [90] [A phase-field model for viscoelastic compressible tumor growth](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30041)
*Luise Zieger,Min Wu,Chaozhen Wei,John Lowengrub,Sebastian Aland*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过相场模型（phase-field model）耦合黏弹性力学与营养物质扩散，模拟实体瘤在周围介质中的生长。模型在径向对称构型下收敛于尖锐界面模型（sharp interface model），并揭示了二维和三维中由弹性屈曲和凋亡体积损失驱动的对称性破缺不稳定性（symmetry-breaking instabilities），以及组织流动性和可压缩性导致的拓扑变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 肿瘤生长过程中会产生并响应局部微环境中的机械应力，组织重排可松弛这些应力并使组织更类流体。机械转导（mechanotransduction）与生化信号之间的复杂耦合导致复杂的生长模式。为预测这些非线性相互作用的结果，需要建立能够同时考虑弹性、黏性、可压缩性以及营养物质扩散的数值模型。

Method: 发展了一个相场模型（phase-field model），将黏弹性力学的连续介质模型与生长促进营养物（growth-promoting nutrient）的扩散过程以质量守恒（mass conservative）方式耦合。该模型能够稳定而灵活地描述任意形状肿瘤的动力学行为。

Result: 模型在径向对称几何下收敛于尖锐界面模型（sharp interface model），可观察到稳态肿瘤的演化。二维和三维中的对称性破缺不稳定性由两种机制驱动：（i）营养物质梯度导致的差异生长引起的弹性屈曲不稳定性（elastic buckling instability）；（ii）凋亡相关体积损失（apoptosis-related volumetric loss）引发的不稳定性。组织流动性和可压缩性可导致肿瘤拓扑结构（tumor topologies）变化。

Conclusion: 该建模框架为研究组织力学（tissue mechanics）与生长因子信号（growth factor signaling）如何影响实体瘤的进展和侵袭潜力提供了一种稳健的方法。

Abstract: It is well known that growing tumors generate and respond to stress in their local microenvironment. Tissue re-arrangements can relax these mechanical stresses and make the tissue more fluid-like. Further, intricate coupling between mechanotransduction and biochemical signaling leads to complex patterns of growth. To predict the outcomes of these nonlinear interactions, we develop a phase-field model to simulate tumors growing into a surrounding medium taking into account their elastic and viscous properties as well as their compressibilities. We couple continuum modeling of the viscoelastic mechanics to the concentration of a diffusible growth-promoting nutrient in a mass conservative way. The phase-field method is a stable and flexible way to describe the dynamics of arbitrarily shaped tumors. We demonstrate convergence of the phase-field model to a sharp interface model in radially symmetric geometries and can observe progression to stationary tumors. However, our results show that these stationary symmetric tumors are subject to symmetry-breaking instabilities in 2D and 3D driven by two primary mechanisms: (i) elastic buckling instabiliies due to differential growth induced by the nutrient gradient and (ii) instabilities generated by apoptosis-related volumetric loss. Further, tissue fluidity and compressibility can lead to changes in tumor topologies. Our modeling framework provides a robust methodology for investigating how tissue mechanics and growth factor signaling influence the progression and invasive potential of solid tumors.

</details>


### [91] [Stress tensor field and mesoscopic stresses in the vertex model for tissues](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30401)
*Paulo C. Godolphim,Leonardo G. Brunnet,Rodrigo Soto*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该论文为顶点模型（vertex model, VM）提供了应力张量（stress tensor）的微观推导，建立了介观应力与VM力之间的联系，并指出应力场在张力跨细胞分布上具有自由度，这使得先前的表达式可视为该场的一种特例，同时暗示了介观应力与真实细胞中细胞骨架力传递结构之间的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文对VM中的应力张量进行了微观推导（microscopic derivation），将介观应力（mesoscopic stresses）与VM中的力（VM forces）联系起来。

Result: 推导得到的应力场在张力（tensions）如何跨细胞分布上具有自由度（freedom），这使以往提出的不同应力表达式可被视为该应力场的特定实现（particular realizations）。

Conclusion: 该发现暗示了介观应力与真实细胞中细胞骨架力传递结构（cytoskeletal force-transmission architectures）之间存在联系。

Abstract: Mechanical stresses are fundamental regulators in biological tissues, where the vertex model (VM) is pivotal for theoretical and force-inference studies. Yet, no uniform expression for the stress tensor exists for the VM. Here we provide a microscopic derivation of it, linking mesoscopic stresses to the VM forces. The stress field presents a freedom on how tensions are distributed across cells, which allows previous expressions to emerge as particular realizations of the field and suggests a link between mesoscopic stresses and cytoskeletal force-transmission architectures in real cells.

### [92] [Scale-coupling from kirigami cuts controls emergent mechanics in liquid crystal elastomers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30501)
*M. Strugaru,M. Ly,Q. Martinet,B. Bickel,J. Palacci*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过将液晶弹性体（LCE）与剪纸（kirigami）图案相结合，展示了一种利用宏观几何切割来调控微观分子自由度、进而编程宏观力学功能的多尺度力学超材料（multiscale metamaterial）新范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统材料的性质由微观组成与排列决定，而力学超材料（mechanical metamaterial）则依赖于介观结构而非构成材料。如何通过宏观几何改变来调控微观自由度以编程力学行为，是连接这两种范式的一个核心挑战。

Method: 在各向异性响应固体（anisotropic responsive solid）中引入切割（cuts），具体采用液晶弹性体（liquid crystal elastomer, LCE）薄片并结合剪纸（kirigami）图案，利用切割带来的工程应变来驾驭分子各向异性从而控制涌现力学行为。

Result: LCE剪纸结构实现了传统剪纸或纯LCE薄片无法实现的功能，如具有远程驱动能力的超软夹具（supersoft gripper），以及可在温度变化下可逆变形的结构。

Conclusion: LCE剪纸建立了一类新的多尺度超材料，其中几何结构控制着对微观自由度的访问，从而实现对宏观功能的编程。

Abstract: Conventional materials derive their properties from microscopic composition and arrangement, whereas mechanical metamaterials are defined by mesoscopic structure rather than constituent material. Bridging these paradigms, using macroscopic geometric alterations to orchestrate microscopic degrees of freedom and program mechanics, remains a central challenge. Here, we demonstrate that cuts in anisotropic, responsive solids provide such a connection. Using liquid crystal elastomer (LCE) sheets with kirigami patterns, we reveal that engineering strain through cuts harnesses molecular anisotropy to control emergent mechanics. Similarly, the interplay between cut patterns and the molecular phase transition of LCEs enables soft robotics functionalities such as supersoft grippers with remote actuation and architectures that reversibly morph under temperature variations, behaviors inaccessible to conventional kirigami or LCE sheets alone. LCE kirigami thus establish a new class of multiscale metamaterials in which geometry governs access to microscopic degrees of freedom, to program macroscopic function.

</details>


### [93] [Role of Single Chemical Heterogeneities in Generating Anisotropic Tactile Sensitivity and Soft Sliding Friction Phenomena](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30535)
*Kayla A. Hepler,Leanne Ton,Charles B. Dhong*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文实验研究了软弹性探针在单一化学异质性（由硅片上两种硅烷界面形成）上的滑动摩擦行为，发现摩擦现象的方向不对称性与化学材料差异程度相关，并通过人体触觉实验（n=36）表明摩擦力斜率（friction force slope）对触觉特征的清晰感知至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然物理异质性（physical heterogeneities）在滑动摩擦研究中已被广泛探索，但介观尺度（mesoscale）软滑动中化学异质性（chemical heterogeneities）的行为仍缺乏研究。本文旨在填补这一空白，系统表征化学异质性对摩擦行为的影响。

Method: 实验采用平面软弹性探针在硅片表面两种硅烷（silanes）形成的单一化学异质性界面上滑动，通过构建多载荷和多速度下的相图（phase maps），量化了化学边缘处及附近的多种摩擦现象，包括黏着尖峰形成（stiction spike formation）、边缘斜率方向（edge slope direction）、基线偏移（baseline shifts）和基线漂移（baseline drift），并分析了这些现象的滑动方向依赖性。

Result: 化学材料差异更大的异质性（丁基与氨丙基封端）表现出更多方向无关的现象，而材料差异较小的异质性（丁基与己基封端）则表现出方向依赖性。人体实验（n=36）中，受试者在后者上表现出方向依赖的准确率差异（66.7% vs 38.9%），而前者则不明显（77.8% vs 75%）。

Conclusion: 化学异质性引起的方向不对称性可归因于弹性体效应（elastic body effects）。结合相图分析，结果表明滑动经过化学边缘时摩擦力的斜率对生成清晰的触觉特征边缘至关重要，而非简单的材料特性差异或其他摩擦现象。

Abstract: Physical heterogeneities in the context of sliding friction, such as a human finger exploring an object, have been well studied, yet the behavior of chemical heterogeneities in mesoscale soft sliding remains underexplored, despite the similar prevalence of chemical and physical variations in real systems. Here, we experimentally characterized the friction of a planar soft elastic probe sliding across a single chemical heterogeneity that was formed at the interface of two silanes on silicon wafers. By constructing phase maps across multiple loads and velocities, we quantified the occurrence of several frictional phenomena at and around the chemical edge, including stiction spike formation, edge slope direction, baseline shifts, and baseline drift, and quantified their sliding direction-dependent formation. We found that chemical heterogeneities made by more disparate materials (butyl- and aminopropyl-terminated) exhibited several phenomena that were more often direction-independent compared to chemical heterogeneities formed from more similar materials (butyl- and hexyl-terminated). We attributed this directional asymmetry to elastic body effects. In subsequent human testing (n=36), we observed that humans also exhibited directional-dependent accuracy (66.7% versus 38.9%) on one pair (butyl- and hexyl-terminated) but not the other (77.8% versus 75%), which in the context of our phase maps, suggests that the slope of the friction force when sliding over a chemical edge is important for generating a clear edge of a tactile feature, rather than the differences in simple material properties or other friction phenomena.

</details>

### [94] [Breathing mode of quantum droplets in dipolar quantum gases: A sum-rule analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29370)
*Xinran Zhang,Junli Liu,Huiyun Xiao,Xiao-Long Chen,Yunbo Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文基于高斯变分方法与求和规则分析，推导了三维偶极玻色气体在各向异性谐振阱中的呼吸模式频率解析表达式，揭示了从稀薄玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚到稠密量子液滴相的相变与交叉行为，并与$^{166}$Er和$^{162}$Dy气体的实验数据吻合良好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解三维偶极玻色气体（dipolar Bose gases）在各向异性谐振阱中的基态性质和集体激发行为，特别是量子涨落（quantum fluctuations）对呼吸模式（breathing-mode）频率的影响，以及系统从稀薄玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（Bose-Einstein condensate, BEC）相到稠密量子液滴（quantum droplet）相的转变机制。

Method: 采用高斯变分拟设（Gaussian variational ansatz）结合非微扰求和规则分析（non-perturbative sum-rule analysis），推导轴向和径向呼吸模式频率的显式解析表达式，并通过数值求解含时扩展Gross-Pitaevskii方程（extended Gross-Pitaevskii equation）进行验证。

Result: 理论预测与$^{166}$Er和$^{162}$Dy气体的现有实验数据高度一致。在s波散射长度（$s$-wave scattering length）、原子数和阱纵横比（trap aspect ratio）的参数空间中构建了完整相图，揭示了稀薄BEC相与稠密量子液滴相之间的一阶不连续相变（first-order phase transition）和平滑交叉（crossover）。在准二维和准一维约束下，系统随散射长度发生相变和交叉，分别表现为峰值密度和原子云尺寸的不连续跳跃和连续交叉。量子涨落增强的不可压缩性显著提高了液滴相的呼吸模式频率。

Conclusion: 该工作为表征偶极量子气体（dipolar quantum gases）中的集体激发提供了一个严格且高精度的理论框架，为未来涉及镧系原子和极性分子（polar molecules）的超冷原子实验提供了定量见解。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate the ground-state properties and breathing-mode collective excitations of three-dimensional dipolar Bose gases in anisotropic harmonic traps incorporating quantum fluctuations. Combining a Gaussian variational ansatz with a non-perturbative sum-rule analysis, we derive explicit analytical expressions for both axial and radial breathing-mode frequencies, which are validated by numerical solutions of the time-dependent extended Gross-Pitaevskii equation. Our theoretical predictions show excellent agreement with existing experimental data for $^{166}$Er and $^{162}$Dy gases. By constructing comprehensive phase diagrams across the parameter space of the $s$-wave scattering length, atom number, and trap aspect ratio, we reveal both discontinuous first-order phase transitions and smooth crossovers between the dilute Bose-Einstein condensate and dense quantum droplet phases. We confirm that the enhanced incompressibility induced by quantum fluctuations significantly elevates the breathing-mode frequencies in the droplet phase compared to conventional weakly interacting Bose gases. Furthermore, the system undergoes a phase transition and a crossover over the scattering length under the quasi-two-dimensional and quasi-one-dimensional confinements, characterized by discontinuous jumps and continuous crossovers in peak density and atomic cloud sizes, respectively. Our work offers a rigorous and highly accurate framework to characterize collective excitations in dipolar quantum gases, providing quantitative insights for forthcoming ultracold atom experiments in lanthanide atoms and polar molecules.

</details>


### [95] [Vortex NOON states for rotation sensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29509)
*Simon Dengis,Nathan Dupont,Peter Schlagheck,Nathan Goldman*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在弱各向异性二维谐振势阱中利用冷原子生成少体玻色子涡旋NOON态的方案，并通过测地线非绝热驱动和共振/混沌辅助隧穿两种加速策略克服其生成时间过长的瓶颈，最终证明了该涡旋NOON态在旋转传感中可达到海森堡极限（Heisenberg limit）的测量精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成高度纠缠的少体玻色子涡旋NOON态（vortex NOON states）并实现其在高精度旋转传感（rotation sensing）中的应用，同时解决NOON态生成时间过长这一关键瓶颈。

Method: 基于冷原子在弱各向异性二维谐振势阱中的单粒子p轨道构建有效两模Bose-Hubbard模型（two-mode Bose-Hubbard model），其中涡旋模式（vortex modes）p_x±i p_y携带相反环量；在自陷（self-trapping）区域使NOON流形（NOON manifold）光谱分离，利用集体隧穿过程生成纠缠NOON态；针对小粒子数采用测地线反非绝热驱动（geodesic counterdiabatic driving），针对大粒子数在半经典区域采用共振与混沌辅助隧穿（resonance- and chaos-assisted tunneling）加速生成。

Result: 两种加速策略均能在实验相关时间尺度（experimentally relevant timescales）上生成近单位保真度（near-unit fidelities）的涡旋NOON态；所设计的干涉测量协议（interferometric protocol）利用涡旋NOON态对旋转的本征敏感性，可实现海森堡极限级别的极小外旋转检测。

Conclusion: 该工作为基于原子NOON态的旋转传感器（rotation sensors）开辟了道路，此类方案可泛化实现于具有涡旋型轨道（vortex-type orbitals）的玻色子约瑟夫森结（bosonic Josephson junctions）中。

Abstract: We introduce a scheme to generate NOON states of few-body bosonic vortices and demonstrate their application as high-precision rotation sensors. Our approach is based on cold atoms in a weakly anisotropic two-dimensional harmonic trap, where the single-particle p orbitals define an effective two-mode Bose-Hubbard model with vortex modes $(\mathrm{p}_x\pm\mathrm{i}\mathrm{p}_y)$ carrying opposite circulation. In the self-trapping regime, we show that the NOON manifold becomes spectrally isolated, and collective tunneling processes give rise to highly entangled vortex NOON states. However, these states emerge on prohibitively long timescales. To overcome this limitation, we develop two complementary acceleration strategies: geodesic counterdiabatic driving for small particle numbers, and resonance- and chaos-assisted tunneling in the semiclassical regime at larger particle numbers. Both approaches enable the generation of NOON states on experimentally relevant timescales while preserving near-unit fidelities. Finally, we quantify the metrological advantage of vortex NOON states by introducing an interferometric protocol that exploits their intrinsic sensitivity to rotation, enabling the detection of infinitesimal external rotations at the Heisenberg limit. Our work opens the door to rotation sensors based on atomic NOON states, generically realizable in bosonic Josephson junctions with vortex-type orbitals.

</details>


### [96] [Spin-orbit coupling induced geometric squeezing in rotating Bose-Einstein condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30187)
*Fei Zhu,Chunxia Guo,Rui Zhang,Lianghui Huang,Ren Zhang,Li Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出在赝自旋-1/2玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BEC）中通过自旋-轨道耦合（SOC）实现几何压缩的新方案，展示了最低朗道能级内的双声子跃迁导致的指数级压缩动力学，并探讨了原子间相互作用的影响，为自旋量子气体中的几何压缩提供了可行路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的几何压缩态（geometrically squeezed state）通过各向异性囚禁势生成，本文旨在探索利用自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling, SOC）作为替代途径来产生几何压缩，以拓展量子气体中压缩态的实现与调控手段。

Method: 基于赝自旋-1/2 BEC体系中的自旋-轨道耦合机制，通过虚自旋翻转过程（virtual spin-flip processes）在最低朗道能级（lowest Landau level）内实现有效的双声子跃迁（two-phonon transitions），从而在两个自旋分量中驱动指数级压缩动力学。进一步施加π/2自旋旋转以相干耦合两个自旋通道，产生双模几何压缩（two-mode geometric squeezing）。

Result: 自旋-轨道耦合可有效诱导最低朗道能级内的双声子跃迁，实现两个自旋分量的指数级压缩动力学；通过π/2自旋旋转可产生双模几何压缩；原子间相互作用对压缩性能存在影响，但存在可实现稳健压缩的参数区间。

Conclusion: 该工作为在自旋量子气体（spinor quantum gases）中实现和操控几何压缩提供了一条可行路径，拓展了压缩态制备的实验方案。

Abstract: Squeezed states play a key role in diverse frontiers of quantum physics. Geometrically squeezed states, a squeezed state in the orbital phase space of rotating Bose-Einstein condensates (BEC), have been conventionally generated by anisotropic trapping potentials. In this work, we propose a different route to generate geometric squeezing via spin-orbit coupling (SOC) in a pseudospin-1/2 BEC. We show that the SOC enables effective two-phonon transitions within the lowest Landau level via virtual spin-flip processes, leading to exponential squeezing dynamics in both spin components. Furthermore, by applying a $π/2$ spin rotation, the two spin channels can be coherently coupled to produce two-mode geometric squeezing. We also investigate the influence of interatomic interactions on squeezing performance and identify parameters where robust squeezing can be achieved. Our work provides a viable pathway to realize and manipulate geometric squeezing in spinor quantum gases.

### [97] [Finite-size effects in Schulz-Shastry-Luttinger models for determining anyonic signatures in 1d spin chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30539)
*B. Perković,M. Bonkhoff,T. Posske*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文研究了Schulz-Shastry-Luttinger液体的有限尺寸性质，揭示了任意子（anyon）特征，分析了周期边界和狄利克雷边界条件下的对角化、稳定性及边界特征量，并讨论了纵向自旋关联（longitudinal spin correlations）的体态与边界行为，包括次主导修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了揭示饱和自旋1/2锯齿链中螺旋基态低能激发所体现的任意子特征，需要对Schulz-Shastry-Luttinger液体的有限尺寸性质进行系统性研究。

Method: 研究了周期边界条件（periodic boundary conditions）和狄利克雷边界条件（Dirichlet boundary conditions）下的模型对角化与稳定性；推导了Friedel振荡（Friedel oscillations）和持续电流（persistent currents）等边界特征量；分析了纵向自旋关联在体态和边界的行为，包括次主导修正（subleading corrections）。

Result: 狄利克雷边界条件需要对耦合常数（coupling constants）和普适参数（universal parameters）进行精细调节，而在周期边界条件下仅限制其大小范围。

Conclusion: 该模型展现出密度和相位梯度的非对称及边缘耦合（asymmetric and marginal couplings），属于Schulz-Shastry类；边界条件的选择对系统参数的可调性有显著影响。

Abstract: We study finite-size properties of Schulz-Shastry-Luttinger liquids to reveal anyonic signatures, realized as low-energy excitations on top of the helical ground state in saturated spin-1/2 zigzag chains. The model features asymmetric and marginal couplings of density and phase gradients and belongs to the Schulz-Shastry class. We investigate periodic and Dirichlet boundary conditions and discuss its diagonalization as well as its stability. Although Dirichlet boundary conditions require a fine-tuning of coupling constants and universal parameters, only their magnitude is restricted for cyclic systems. We derive boundary characteristic quantities like Friedel oscillations and persistent currents. Finally, we discuss the bulk and boundary behavior of the longitudinal spin correlations including subleading corrections.

</details>


### [98] [Equilibrium and non-equilibrium phases of microwave-dressed polar molecules beyond rotational symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30589)
*Matteo Ciardi,Andreas Schindewolf,Tim Langen,Thomas Pohl*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过路径积分蒙特卡洛（path-integral Monte Carlo）模拟，揭示了微波修饰极性分子液滴阵列是气-液滴相变淬火下的亚稳态非平衡态，并指出相互作用各向异性（interaction anisotropy）是分子量子气体（molecular quantum gases）的关键特性，现有实验因旋转对称性完全破缺而无法实现反偶极相互作用下的分子晶体相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极性分子液滴实验为强偶极量子物质中的自组织现象开辟了新前沿，但液滴阵列的形成机制及其与理论预言的晶体相之间的关系尚不明确。需要第一性原理模拟（ab initio simulations）与实验直接对比，以澄清相关量子相图的本质。

Method: 采用路径积分蒙特卡洛（path-integral Monte Carlo）方法对大量分子系综进行模拟，分析微波修饰偶极相互作用（microwave-dressed dipole interaction）下气-液滴相变（gas-droplet phase transition）的淬火动力学。

Result: 实验观测到的液滴阵列是旋转对称性完全破缺条件下相变淬火产生的亚稳态非平衡态（metastable non-equilibrium state）。反偶极相互作用（antidipolar interactions）预言的分子晶体相在现有实验条件下缺失，原因在于当前微波修饰缺少角向对称性（angular symmetry），这重塑了多体能景（many-body energy landscape），无法用有效标量相互作用参数（effective scalar interaction parameters）描述。

Conclusion: 首次实现了第一性原理模拟与实验的直接对比，并确立相互作用各向异性（interaction anisotropy）是分子量子气体（molecular quantum gases）的关键特性。

Abstract: Recent experiments on molecular droplets have opened a new frontier of self-organization in strongly dipolar quantum matter. Microwave-dressing of polar molecules permits to tune both the strength and the angular structure of long-range interactions, potentially promoting a rich spectrum of quantum phases, from superfluid droplets with varying geometry and insulating or supersolid droplet arrays to strongly correlated crystals of individual molecules. Using path-integral Monte Carlo simulations of large molecular ensembles, we demonstrate that experimentally observed droplet arrays emerge as a metastable non-equilibrium state from the quenching of a gas-droplet phase transition under entirely broken rotational symmetry of the microwave-induced interaction potential. We moreover find that a crystalline phase of molecules, predicted for antidipolar interactions, is absent under conditions of recent experiments. This is traced back to the lack of angular symmetry in currently employed microwave-dressing, which qualitatively reshapes the many-body energy landscape and cannot be captured by effective scalar interaction parameters. Our results provide the first direct comparison of ab initio simulations and experiments and establish interaction anisotropy as a key aspect of molecular quantum gases.

</details>

### [99] [Distinct Roles of Hydrogen in Superconducting and Ferromagnetic Phases of CoZr$_{2}$H$_{x}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28726)
*Yuto Watanabe,Takayoshi Katase,Daisuke Takegami,Yoshikazu Mizuguchi*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究合成了不同氢含量的CoZr₂Hₓ，发现氢以两个浓度区间（低浓度超导相与高浓度铁磁相）嵌入，两者被宽组分间隙分隔。氢在低浓度下作为非磁性杂质抑制超导，在高浓度下通过Zr-H相互作用诱导铁磁性；超导转变温度的抑制可被Abrikosov-Gor'kov对破缺理论定量描述，暗示CoZr₂的超导能隙具有各向异性或多能隙特征，而非完全各向同性的s波对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氢气化（hydrogenation）为调控金属间化合物的物理性质提供了灵活途径，但氢在不同浓度区间如何影响超导性和磁性的微观机制尚不明确。

Method: 合成了不同氢含量的CoZr₂Hₓ样品，并对其超导转变温度、电子能带结构和磁性行为进行了实验表征与理论分析。

Result: 发现氢以两个浓度区间嵌入（低浓度超导相x=0-0.054与高浓度铁磁相x=2.786），二者被宽组分间隙分隔。高浓度下Zr-H相互作用显著调制跨越费米能级（Fermi level）的金属能带，引发铁磁性（ferromagnetism）；低浓度下氢作为非磁性杂质不改变电子能带结构。超导转变温度（T_c）随氢含量增加逐渐被抑制，且该抑制行为可由Abrikosov-Gor'kov对破缺理论（pair-breaking theory）定量描述。

Conclusion: 低浓度下氢作为非磁性杂质抑制超导，高浓度下通过Zr-H键合诱导铁磁序；CoZr₂的超导能隙为各向异性或多能隙结构，而非完全各向同性的s波对称性（s-wave symmetry）。

Abstract: Hydrogenation offers a versatile route to tuning the physical properties of intermetallic compounds. In this study, we synthesized CoZr$_{2}$H$_{x}$ with different hydrogen contents and found that hydrogen is incorporated in two distinct concentration regimes separated by a wide composition gap: a low-concentration hydrogenated superconducting phase ($x$ = 0-0.054) and a high-concentration hydrogenated ferromagnetic phase ($x$ = 2.786). Hydrogen plays fundamentally different roles in the two concentration regimes. In the high hydrogen concentration phase, the Zr-H interactions substantially modify the metallic bands crossing the Fermi level, leading to the emergence of ferromagnetism. In contrast, in the low hydrogen concentration phase, hydrogen behaves as a nonmagnetic impurity without altering the electronic band structure. Despite the nearly identical Debye temperatures across the low-concentration series, the superconducting transition temperature ($T_{\mathrm{c}}$) is progressively suppressed with increasing hydrogen content.The observed $T_{\mathrm{c}}$ suppression is quantitatively described by the Abrikosov-Gor'kov pair-breaking theory, indicating that the superconducting gap of CoZr$_{2}$ is anisotropic or multigap rather than a fully isotropic $s$-wave symmetry.

</details>


### [100] [Anomalous Behavior of the Ni$^{1+}$ moment and interstitial band in bi-infinite-layered La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_5$F](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28735)
*Young-Joon Song,W. E. Pickett,K. -W. Lee*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用第一性原理密度泛函理论（first principles density functional theory）计算，分析La₃Ni₂O₅F的电子结构与磁性倾向。重点关注层间间隙态形成的能带及自掺杂效应。

Result: 发现存在一个不与任何原子直接相关的层间间隙态衍生的单一能带E*，该能带分布在三个层中，对Ni离子提供自掺杂（self-doping），使Ni价态变为Ni^1.09+。阻断层La(O/F)La使NiO₂双层和间隙E*态密度严格局限在二维电子和磁系统中。磁性计算显示磁化率极低，直至强磁场下仍几乎为零，行为与以往镍酸盐（nickelates）不同。

Conclusion: 二维磁涨落（two dimensional fluctuations）和远离半填充（half-filling）的自掺杂效应可以解释实验上未观测到磁相变的原因。该结果为理解镍基超导体与铜基超导体的异同提供了新的电子结构视角。

Abstract: The discovery of superconductivity in hole-doped Ni$^{1+}$ systems with "infinite layer" NiO$_2$ square-lattices analogous to the Cu$^{2+}$ CaCuO$_2$ cuprate has renewed conflicting pictures of the Cu$^{2+}$$-$Ni$^{1+}$ similarity or distinction. Recent synthesis of formal Ni$^{1+}$ La$_3$Ni$_{2}$O$_{5}$F with two infinite NiO$_{2}$ layers per cell provides a novel member of this class. First principles density functional theory studies reveal an interstitial density derived single band $E^*$ in three layers unrelated to any atom, which provides self-doping to a Ni$^{1.09+}$ ion.The blocking La(O/F)La provides isolation of the NiO$_2$ bilayer and an interstitial $E^*$ density to strictly two-dimensional electronic and magnetic systems. Calculations of magnetic tendencies reveals behavior unlike previous nickelates, including vanishing susceptibility up to a large magnetic field. Two dimensional fluctuations and self-doping away from half-filling can account for the lack of observation of a magnetic transition.

</details>


### [101] [Hydrostatic pressure effect on the pseudogap in Y0.77Pr0.23Ba2Cu3O7-δsingle crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28794)
*A. L. Solovjov,L. V. Bludova,A. S. Kolesnik,E. V. Petrenko,M. V. Shytov,A. Sedda,E. Lähderanta,D. Sergeyev,R. V. Vovk*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究静水压（HP）对含Pr杂质的YPrBCO单晶超导及电子性质的影响机制，特别是磁性PrBCO缺陷在压力下的作用。

Method: 对Y_{1-x}Pr_xBa_2Cu_3O_{7-δ} (x=0.23)单晶施加最高约1.1 GPa的静水压（HP），测量电阻率ρ(T)、超导转变温度T_c、涨落电导率σ'(T)和赝能隙Δ*(T)随压力的变化。

Result: 电阻率在100 K处随压力的变化率为dlnρ(100 K)/dP = -(29 ± 0.2)%·GPa^{-1}；赝能隙Δ*(T)上的磁最大值在~0.5 GPa以下增强，0.6 GPa时消失，1.0 GPa以上重新出现且更显著。

Conclusion: 静水压（HP）对YPrBCO与纯YBa_2Cu_3O_{7-δ}单晶的ρ(T)和T_c的影响机制不同；压力通过三个阶段分别促进、中和和重新排列PrBCO磁性杂质对载流子的作用。

Abstract: We studied the changes of resistivity $ρ(T)$, superconducting transition temperature $T_c$, fluctuation conductivity $σ'(T)$, and pseudogap $Δ^*(T)$ of $Y_{1-x}Pr_xBa_2Cu_3O_{7-δ}$ (YPrBCO) ($x = 0.23$) single crystal under hydrostatic pressure (HP) up to $\sim 1.1$ GPa. Defects created by magnetic inclusions of $PrBa_2Cu_3O_{7-δ}$ (PrBCO) were found to play a significant role in the behavior of the sample. The largest decrease in $ρ(T)$ was found depending on HP at a rate of $d\lnρ(100~K)/dP = -(29 \pm 0.2) \% \cdot GPa^{-1}$. This indicates that the mechanisms of the influence of HP on the $ρ(T)$ and $T_c$ of YPrBCO and $YBa_2Cu_3O_{7-δ}$ single crystals are different. From the analysis of the pseudogap, it was revealed that the mechanism of the interaction of charge carriers with magnetic PrBCO impurities changes three times with increasing HP. Relatively low HP, up to $\sim 0.5$ GPa, promotes the formation of defects caused by PrBCO magnetic inclusions. Starting from 0.6 GPa, the HP neutralizes the influence of magnetic impurities, and the magnetic maximum on $Δ^*(T)$ disappears. Above $\sim 1.0$ GPa, HP aligns the magnetic moments of PrBCO, and the magnetic maximum reappears on $Δ^*(T)$, more pronounced than at $P = 0$.

</details>


### [102] [Theory of High-Tc Superconductivity in Cuprates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28906)
*E. C. Marino*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文回顾了铜氧化物高温超导（High-Tc superconductivity）的两种简化理论路径：t-J模型（基于Zhang-Rice单态）与Spin-Fermion-Hubbard模型（基于局域自旋与氧子晶格上掺杂空穴的Kondo相互作用），并论证后一条路径在解释空穴掺杂铜氧化物高温超导现象上取得了成功。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铜氧化物高温超导的核心物理过程发生在CuO₂面内，其有效电子动力学可由三带哈伯德模型（Three Bands Hubbard Model, 3BHM）描述，但该模型过于复杂，促使研究者寻找更简单且仍然相关的替代方案。

Method: 通过对比两种简化路径：一是将掺杂空穴与Cu²⁺电子束缚形成Zhang-Rice单态（Zhang-Rice singlets），导出t-J模型（t-J Model）；二是保留Cu²⁺电子的局域自旋方晶格，掺杂空穴沿氧子晶格运动，并经历类似近藤（Kondo）的磁相互作用与哈伯德型（Hubbard-like）电排斥，导出Spin-Fermion-Hubbard模型（Spin-Fermion-Hubbard Model）。

Result: 大多数研究者选择了t-J模型路径，而作者选择了Spin-Fermion-Hubbard模型路径，该选择最终发展出能够成功解释空穴掺杂铜氧化物高温超导的理论。

Conclusion: Spin-Fermion-Hubbard模型路径为高温超导理论提供了成功框架，作者以此回顾并论证其选择的合理性。

Abstract: The essential physical processes underlying the phenomenon of High-Tc superconductivity in cuprates occur in the $CuO_2$ planes, found in these materials. The dynamics of the active electrons belonging to such planes is well described by the Three Bands Hubbard Model (3BHM). The complexity of such model, however, led the researchers to look for simpler and yet relevant alternatives. In the attempts to circumvent the complexity of this model,two main simplified versions of the (3BHM) were considered. In the first alternative, one eliminates the doped holes and their respective sub-lattices by tying them to the $Cu^{++}$ electrons, thereby forming the so called Zhang-Rice singlets. The remaining dynamics consists in doping a Mott-Hubbard insulator and is described by the t-J Model. The second alternative
  maintains that the $Cu^{++}$ electrons form a square lattice of localized spins, while the doped holes move along the oxygen sub-lattices and undergo a Kondo like magnetic interaction with the localized spins, besides the Hubbard-like electric repulsion. This scenario is described by the Spin-Fermion-Hubbard Model. Most of the researchers in the field chose to follow the first road, while, I chose the second one. In this article I review in detail the reasons why that choice has led to a successful theory for High-Tc superconductivity in hole doped cuprates.

</details>


### [103] [40 years of cuprate high-Tc superconductors: a perspective on theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29249)
*Navinder Singh Bathinda*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文对铜氧化物高温超导体（cuprate high-Tc superconductors）超导机制的理论研究现状进行了简要而系统的综述，重点讨论了源自排斥相互作用的超导（superconductivity from repulsive interactions）这一自2015年以来逐渐成为主流的观点及其面临的挑战，并介绍了三种主要学派、2022年与安德森超交换机制（Anderson's super-exchange mechanism）相关的实验结果，以及更新后的安德森“教条”（dogmas），以纪念高温超导研究40周年。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铜氧化物高温超导体的超导机制至今仍是凝聚态物理（condensed matter physics）的核心未解难题。本文旨在提供一个条理清晰的理论概述，梳理不同学派的观点，特别是自2015年“共识”论文以来日益受到关注的源自排斥相互作用的超导这一思路，并总结普遍适用的实验事实（即安德森的“教条”），以纪念该领域研究40周年。

Method: 本文采用综述性论述方法，系统回顾了铜氧化物高温超导机制的理论想法；具体讨论了源自排斥相互作用的超导这一主流假设及其面临的挑战，呈现了三种主要学术流派（three main schools of thought），并分析了2022年一项与安德森超交换机制相关的实验结果；同时，基于2000年后发现的新普适实验事实，更新了安德森的“教条”列表。

Result: 本文呈现了三种主要学派的理论观点；指出了源自排斥相互作用的超导理论所面临的挑战；介绍了2022年一项支持或涉及安德森超交换机制的实验结果；并提供了一个更新版的安德森“教条”清单，这些教条是从复杂实验结果中提炼出的、对铜氧化物超导机制具有核心意义的普适事实。

Conclusion: 通过回顾理论进展与关键实验事实，本文为理解铜氧化物高温超导机制提供了一个系统性的理论快照。更新后的安德森“教条”突出了2000年后新发现的普适事实，为后续理论构建提供了重要的约束条件，并以此纪念高温超导领域40年来的研究成果。

Abstract: An attempt is made to give a brief but coherent account of the situation of the theoretical ideas in addressing the mechanism of superconductivity in cuprate high-Tc superconductors. Specifically, the idea of superconductivity from repulsive interactions is discussed as it is gaining ground since the `consensus' paper was written in 2015\cite{kei}. The challenges it faces is also discussed. Three main schools of thought are presented, and an experimental result of 2022 pertaining to Anderson's super-exchange mechanism is also discussed. An updated list of Anderson's ``dogmas" is also presented, as after year 2000, many other universally applicable experimental facts has been discovered. The ``dogmas" are universal facts which are distilled from a variety of complex experimental results, and highlights the key findings that seems to be central to the mechanism of superconductivity in cuprates. These are discussed as a commemoration of 40 years of high-Tc cuprate research.

### [104] [Time-local nonequilibrium Green's function method for real-time dynamics in quantum systems coupled to superconducting leads](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29266)
*Taira Kawamura*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种时间局域的非平衡格林函数（nonequilibrium Green's function）方法，通过将超导引线的自能（self-energy）在Nambu空间进行辅助模展开（auxiliary-mode expansion），将包含记忆积分的Kadanoff-Baym方程转化为常微分方程组，从而高效模拟超导引线耦合量子系统的实时动力学。以超导-量子点-超导结的电压淬火（voltage-quench）动力学为例，验证了该方法能捕捉瞬时过程并收敛到交流约瑟夫森（ac Josephson）周期性稳态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导引线自能在Nambu空间中呈现强频率依赖的矩阵结构，导致时间域中存在非局域的记忆核（nonlocal memory kernels），直接传播Kadanoff-Baym方程计算量极大，亟需发展高效的时间局域化方案。

Method: 将原本针对正常金属引线的辅助模扩展方法推广至Nambu空间自能，把超导引线自能分解为有限个指数模式，从而将含记忆积分的Kadanoff-Baym方程转化为一组封闭的常微分方程。

Result: 在超导-量子点-超导结的电压淬火动力学分析中，系统在施加直流偏压后经历瞬态过程并弛豫至交流约瑟夫森周期性稳态，所得周期性稳态电流与Floquet格林函数解一致。

Conclusion: 所提出的时间局域格林函数形式能够在保留超导引线记忆效应的前提下，实现一般时间依赖偏压、超导相位及中心系统单体哈密顿量下的高效实时模拟，并通过稳态验证了方法的正确性。

Abstract: We develop a time-local nonequilibrium Green's function formulation for real-time dynamics in quantum systems coupled to superconducting leads. The superconducting lead self-energy is a strongly frequency-dependent matrix in Nambu space, giving rise to nonlocal memory kernels in the time domain. This makes direct propagation of the Kadanoff-Baym (KB) equations computationally demanding. To overcome this difficulty, we extend the auxiliary-mode expansion, originally developed for normal-metal leads, to Nambu-space self-energies. This allows us to decompose the superconducting lead self-energy into a finite number of exponential modes and to transform the KB equations with memory integrals into a closed set of ordinary differential equations. The resulting time-local equations enable efficient real-time simulations under general time-dependent bias voltages, superconducting phases, and one-body Hamiltonians of the central system, while retaining the memory effects induced by superconducting leads. As an application, we analyze voltage-quench dynamics in a superconductor-quantum-dot-superconductor junction and show that, after a dc bias is suddenly applied, the system evolves through a transient regime and relaxes to an ac Josephson periodic steady state. The resulting periodic steady-state current agrees with the Floquet Green's function solution, validating the present real-time formulation.

</details>


### [105] [Superconductivity in Jellium Model Revisited](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29306)
*Michael V. Sadovskii*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文在KMK电介质形式体系下重新分析了啫喱模型（jellium model）中的超导电性，通过直接对角化方法数值求解线性化KMK积分方程，并首次系统性地在介电函数中引入静态哈伯德局域场修正（static Hubbard local-field corrections）作为超越随机相位近似（RPA）的扩展。结果表明，与以往分散的结果相比，该工作缩小了超导临界温度 $T_c$ 的可能取值范围；在金属氢情形下，$T_c(r_s)$ 呈现特征穹顶状，最大值出现在 $r_s\sim 9.0$ 处，仅约零点几开尔文，远低于基于高配对玻色子频率的朴素预期，原因是啫喱模型在所有密度下均处于弱耦合超导区间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前关于啫喱模型（jellium model）超导电性的研究结果散布范围较大，缺乏系统性的超越随机相位近似（RPA）的分析；此外，对于金属氢中基于高配对玻色子频率可能产生高温超导的朴素预期缺乏严谨检验。

Method: 采用Kirzhnits、Maksimov与Khomskii（KMK）发展的电介质形式体系（dielectric formalism），对线性化KMK积分方程进行解析分析，并通过直接对角化（direct diagonalization）进行数值求解，以获取超导临界温度 $T_c$ 随Wigner-Seitz半径 $r_s$ 的依赖关系。作为首次系统性扩展，在介电函数中引入静态哈伯德局域场修正（static Hubbard local-field corrections），以超越随机相位近似（RPA）。

Result: 结果整体上缩窄了 $T_c$ 的可能取值范围，相比之前分散的文献结果更为集中。对于金属氢（metallic hydrogen），$T_c(r_s)$ 呈现特征穹顶状（dome）依赖关系，最大值出现在 $r_s\sim 9.0$ 处，仅约零点几开尔文。在所有密度下，啫喱模型均处于弱耦合超导区间（weak-coupling regime）。

Conclusion: 金属氢中基于高配对玻色子频率（pairing Boson frequency）可能产生高温超导的朴素期待并不成立，原因是啫喱模型在所有密度下均表现为弱耦合超导机制，因此 $T_c$ 值仅处于亚开尔文量级。

Abstract: We reanalyze superconductivity in jellium model within the dielectric formalism developed by Kirzhnits, Maksimov, and Khomskii (KMK), which is probably the most reliable approach to this model. The linearized KMK integral equation for superconducting transition temperature is analyzed analytically and solved numerically by direct diagonalization to obtain $T_c$ dependence on Wigner - Seitz radius $r_s$. As a first systematic extension beyond random - phase approximation (RPA), static Hubbard local - field corrections are incorporated into the dielectric function. Our results in general narrow the interval of possible $T_c$ values in comparison with widely scattered results of some of the previous works. For the case of metallic hydrogen our calculations show $T_c(r_s)$ dependence with characteristic dome with maximum of $T_c$ at $r_s\sim$ 9.0 of the order of some fractions of Kelvin only, despite the naive expectations based on the high values of pairing Boson frequency. This is due to the weak - coupling regime of superconductivity in jellium model at all densities.

### [108] [Unconventional Superconductivity in the Chiral Topological Semimetal Ag2Pd3S](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29767)
*Roshan Kumar Kushwaha,Dibyendu Samanta,Sudarshan Sharma,Mathew Pula,Shashank Srivastava,Poulami Manna,Arushi,Sajilesh K. P.,Suhani Sharma,Priya Mishra,Prabin Kumar Naik,James Beare,Yipeng Cai,Kenji M. Kojima,Amit Kanigel,Graeme M. Luke,Sudeep Kumar Ghosh,Ravi Prakash Singh*

TL;DR: 本文报道在手性拓扑半金属Ag₂Pd₃S中发现非常规超导，该材料同时表现出超导态中自发时间反演对称性（TRS）破缺以及多种高拓扑荷的多重能带交叉费米子，为研究超导二极管效应和手性自旋选择性提供了平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性晶体（chiral crystals）为研究破缺反演对称性、强自旋-轨道耦合与电子拓扑的相互作用提供了独特环境，但内在手性材料中的超导现象极为罕见。本文旨在探索手性拓扑半金属Ag₂Pd₃S中是否存在非常规超导，并揭示其超导态与拓扑能带结构之间的关联。

Method: 采用电阻率（electrical resistivity）、磁化率（magnetization）和比热（specific-heat）测量确认体超导性；利用μ子自旋旋转与弛豫（muon spin rotation and relaxation, μSR）实验检测超导态中是否自发破缺时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry, TRS）；通过第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）分析费米面附近的能带拓扑结构；结合Ginzburg-Landau理论的对称性分析推测超导序参量形式。

Result: Ag₂Pd₃S在超导转变温度T_C = 1.1(2) K处呈现体超导；μSR实验表明超导态具有全能隙（fully gapped）且自发破缺时间反演对称性（TRS），使其成为首个具有本征TRS破缺的手性拓扑半金属超导体；第一性原理计算在费米能级附近发现多个多重能带交叉点（multifold band crossings），包括Kramers-Weyl费米子、双自旋-1（double spin-1）以及自旋-3/2（spin-3/2）准粒子，均具有大拓扑荷（topological charges）。Ginzburg-Landau对称性分析指出超导态为环超流有序（loop-supercurrent-ordered）态，兼具全能隙和自发TRS破缺。

Conclusion: Ag₂Pd₃S是同时实现TRS破缺超导与手性多重费米子（chiral multifold fermions）共存的材料平台，有望用于实现本征超导二极管效应（intrinsic superconducting diode effects）和手性诱导自旋选择性（chirality-induced spin selectivity），为开发无耗散拓扑量子技术提供了变革性途径。

Abstract: Chiral crystals provide a unique setting where broken inversion symmetry, strong spin-orbit coupling, and electronic topology intertwine, yet superconductivity in intrinsically chiral materials remains rare. Here, we report unconventional superconductivity in the chiral topological semimetal Ag$_2$Pd$_3$S, an enantiomorphic analog of natural mineral coldwellite, crystallizing in the right-handed space group $P4_132$. Bulk superconductivity with a transition temperature $T_C = 1.1(2)$ K is confirmed by electrical resistivity, magnetization, and specific-heat measurements. Muon spin rotation and relaxation ($μ$SR) experiments reveal a fully gapped superconducting state that spontaneously time-reversal symmetry (TRS) breaking establishing Ag$_2$Pd$_3$S as the first chiral topological semimetal superconductor exhibiting intrinsic TRS breaking. First-principles calculations uncover multiple multifold band crossings near the Fermi level, hosting Kramers-Weyl, double spin-1, and spin-3/2 quasiparticles with large topological charges. These unconventional fermions generate symmetry-protected topological surface states and underscore the nontrivial topology of the normal state. Symmetry analysis based on the Ginzburg-Landau theory suggests a loop-supercurrent-ordered superconducting state, yielding a full gap alongside spontaneous TRS breaking. The coexistence of TRS-breaking superconductivity and chiral multifold fermions identifies Ag$_2$Pd$_3$S as a platform for realizing intrinsic superconducting diode effects and chirality-induced spin selectivity, offering a transformative pathway toward dissipationless topological quantum technologies.

### [109] [Ultrasound Evidence for a Low-Temperature Anomaly Inside the Superconducting State of 4Hb-TaS$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30502)
*Yongwei Li,Dmitri V. Efremov,Paul Leask,Andreas Hauspurg,Irena Feldman,Jochen Wosnitza,Amit Kanigel,Sergei Zherlitsyn,Hans-Henning Klauss,Vadim Grinenko*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过极低温超声测量技术在层状范德瓦尔斯超导体 4Hb-TaS₂ 中，在超导转变温度 T_c≈2.9 K 之下约 1 K 处发现了一个新的异常信号。该异常表现为超声衰减（ultrasonic attenuation）在超导态中间区域保持较大值，直至 T*≈1 K 才急剧下降，同时伴随声速变化（sound velocity change）的显著异常。该异常可被磁场和 Se 替代迅速抑制，提示其可能起源于超导态内部的某种相变或 1T 层的诱导超导电性（induced superconductivity）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索层状范德瓦尔斯超导体 4Hb-TaS₂ 在超导态内部的低能激发和可能的额外相变，以理解该材料中 1T 与 1H 层之间复杂的超导耦合机制。

Method: 采用低温超声测量（low-temperature ultrasound measurements），结合比热（specific heat）和交流磁化率（ac magnetic susceptibility）测量，对高质量单晶 4Hb-TaS₂ 进行表征。

Result: 在 T_c≈2.9 K 处观测到尖锐的超导转变。在超导态内部靠近 T*≈1 K 处发现额外的异常信号：超声衰减 Δα 在超导中间区域保持较大值，直到 T* 附近才急剧下降；同时相对声速变化 Δv/v 呈现显著异常。该异常被外加磁场和 Se 替代迅速抑制。

Conclusion: 4Hb-TaS₂ 在超导态内部约 1 K 处存在一个额外的低温异常，可能与 1T 层中的诱导超导电性有关。

Abstract: We report low-temperature ultrasound measurements on single crystals of the layered van der Waals superconductor 4Hb-TaS$_2$. Specific heat and ac magnetic susceptibility show a sharp bulk superconducting transition at $T_{\rm c}\approx 2.9$~K. Ultrasound measurements reveal an additional anomaly deep inside the superconducting state near $T^{*}\approx 1$~K. The most direct signature is observed in the relative ultrasonic attenuation change $Δα$: instead of being rapidly suppressed at $T_{\rm c}$, $Δα$ remains large throughout the intermediate superconducting regime and drops strongly only near $T^{*}$. This loss of acoustic dissipation is accompanied by a pronounced anomaly in the relative sound velocity change $Δv/v$, indicating strong coupling to the lattice. The low-temperature anomaly is rapidly suppressed by magnetic field and by Se substitution, suggesting a possible superconducting origin of the anomaly. We speculate that this feature may be related to induced superconductivity in the 1T layers.

</details>

### [110] [Radiation Damage of TF-1 and PbWO$_4$ Crystals with 20 MeV Electrons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28440)
*Hamlet G. Mkrtchyan,Arthur H. Mkrtchyan,Vardan H. Tadevosyan,Hrachya H. Marukyan,Argine S. Hakobyan,Ashot S. Hakobyan,Arthur A. Hoghmrtsyan,Diana G. Khurshudyan,Nina N. Prazyan,Albert H. Shahinyan,Adelina S. Stepanyan,Lusine R. Vahradyan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文利用 20 MeV 电子束辐照研究了铅玻璃 TF-1 和钨酸铅（PbWO₄）两种晶体的抗辐射性能（radiation hardness），发现 PbWO₄ 的抗辐射能力比 TF-1 强数十倍，且热退火（thermal annealing）能有效恢复辐照后晶体的透射率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究两种不同类型晶体（铅玻璃 TF-1 与钨酸铅 PbWO₄）在电子束辐照下的光学性能退化程度，并评估其抗辐射能力差异，以探索更适合高辐射环境应用的晶体材料。

Method: 使用 AANL 的 LUE-75 直线加速器产生的 20 MeV 电子束对晶体进行两个阶段的辐照实验，并在辐照前后和热退火后测量 200–1000 nm 波长范围内的透射率（transmittance）。热退火采用等时退火（isochronal annealing），温度范围为 160–250°C，持续 10–12 小时。

Result: 第一阶段辐照（0.125 μA，720 s，吸收 5.6×10¹⁴ e⁻）后，TF-1 的光学性能出现严重退化，而 PbWO₄ 几乎未受影响。第二阶段仅对 PbWO₄ 辐照（0.28 μA，1200 s，额外吸收 2.1×10¹⁵ e⁻），仍未观察到显著退化，表明 PbWO₄ 的抗辐射能力比 TF-1 强数十倍。退火后晶体的透射率随退火温度和时间的增加而提高。

Conclusion: PbWO₄ 晶体相对于 TF-1 具有显著优越的抗辐射性能（radiation hardness），热退火可有效恢复辐照引起的光学损伤，这一发现对高能物理和辐射环境下的探测器材料选型具有参考价值。

Abstract: We studied the radiation hardness of two types of crystals, lead glass TF-1 and lead tungstate PbWO$_4$, using a 20 MeV electron beam from the LUE-75 linear accelerator at AANL. The transmittance of the crystals in the wavelength range of 200-1000 nm was measured before and after irradiation, and after thermal annealing. %
The irradiation was performed in two stages. First, both crystals were irradiated with beam current of 0.125 $μ$A, each for a total exposure time of 720 s and absorbing $5.6 \times 10^{14}~e^-$. %
Strong degradation of the optical properties of TF-1 caused by this amount of radiation was observed, while the effect on PbWO$_4$ was negligible (it is a few tens of times radiation harder than TF-1). %
In the second stage, only the PbWO$_4$ crystal was exposed to radiation, with a beam current of 0.28 $μ$A and an exposure time of 1200 s, absorbing an additional $2.1 \times 10^{15}e^-$, still no notable effect. %
Thermal annealing was performed in the temperature range of 160 to 250$^\circ$C (isochronal) for 10-12 hours. The transmittance of the annealed crystals increased with the annealing temperature and time.

</details>


### [111] [mCGCNN: A Dual-Stream Crystal Graph Convolutional Neural Network for the Efficient Prediction of Magnetic Properties of Crystalline Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28458)
*Sourav Mal,Satadeep Bhattacharjee*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 提出了一种磁性感知晶体图神经网络 mCGCNN，通过引入磁性子图、角度感知消息传递和金属-配体-金属交换路径描述符，显著提升了总磁矩预测精度（测试 MAE 从 2.54 μB 降至 2.02 μB，R² 从 0.644 提升至 0.776），并改善了铁磁/反铁磁分类性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准晶体图神经网络（crystal graph neural networks）将所有原子同质化处理，主要通过原子对距离编码化学键，忽视了晶体中磁序（magnetic order）依赖的矩承载子晶格和配体介导的交换路径。

Method: 基于 Goodenough-Kanamori-Anderson 物理的启发，提出 mCGCNN，在全结构图上附加专用磁性子图（magnetic subgraph）；磁性通道对磁性中心执行角度感知消息传递（angle-aware message passing），使用金属-配体-金属交换路径描述符，同时通过逐层交叉耦合传递结构信息和配体场信息；采用独立的磁性子晶格池化（magnetic-sublattice pooling）操作避免磁性相互作用被非磁性原子稀释。

Result: 在 Materials Project 的自旋极化 DFT 数据集上，mCGCNN 将总磁矩预测的测试 MAE 从标准 CGCNN 的 2.54 μB 降至 2.02 μB，测试 R² 从 0.644 提升至 0.776，并优于增强的 CGCNN 基线；磁矩回归预训练可进一步提升铁磁/反铁磁分类性能。

Conclusion: 将交换几何（exchange geometry）直接纳入图神经网络架构，为磁性材料的预测模型提供了一条物理基础扎实的改进路径。

Abstract: Magnetic order in crystals is governed by moment-carrying sublattices and ligand-mediated exchange pathways, yet standard crystal graph neural networks treat all atoms homogeneously and encode bonds primarily through pair distances. We propose mCGCNN, a magnetism-aware crystal graph network that augments the full structural graph with a dedicated magnetic subgraph. The magnetic stream performs angle-aware message passing over magnetic centers using metal-ligand-metal exchange-path descriptors motivated by Goodenough-Kanamori-Anderson physics, while layer-wise cross-coupling transfers structural and ligand-field information from the full crystal graph. A separate magnetic-sublattice pooling operation prevents the magnetic interaction from being diluted by nonmagnetic atoms. Benchmarked on a curated Materials Project spin-polarized DFT data, mCGCNN improves total magnetic moment prediction from a CGCNN test MAE of 2.54~$μ_B$ to 2.02~$μ_B$, outperforming a strengthened CGCNN readout baseline and raising the test $R^2$ from 0.644 to 0.776. When pretrained on moment regression, the same magnetic representation improves ferromagnetic/antiferromagnetic classification. The results demonstrate that incorporating exchange geometry directly into graph architectures provides a physically grounded route to predictive models of magnetic materials.

</details>


### [112] [Microscopic and macroscopic characterization: MBE-grown versus sputter-deposited Au/Co/Au thin films for CISS and MIPAC effect studies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28508)
*Lokesh Rasabathina,Thi Ngoc Ha Nguyen,Aleksandr Kazimir,Rico Ehrler,Julia Krone,Franziska Schölzel,Zihao Liu,Peter Heinig,Markus Gößler,Irene Coin,Christina Lamers,Georgeta Salvan,Lech Tomasz Baczewski,Christoph Tegenkamp,Olav Hellwig*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过比较分子束外延（MBE）与磁控溅射制备的Au/Co/Au铁磁薄膜吸附手性肽后的微观与宏观磁性变化，发现微观尺度的手性诱导自旋选择性（CISS）效应在两种样品中均稳健存在，而宏观的吸附手性分子诱导磁化（MIPAC）效应则对衬底微结构更敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性诱导自旋选择性（CISS）效应在自旋电子学中有重要应用，但衬底微结构（substrate microstructure）对CISS效应以及吸附手性分子诱导磁化（MIPAC）效应的影响尚不清楚，本研究旨在阐明这一关系。

Method: 对比研究了通过分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy, MBE）和磁控溅射（magnetron sputtering）制备的Au/Co/Au铁磁薄膜，在吸附L-手性α-螺旋富含丙氨酸肽后，利用X射线反射率、X射线衍射、原子力显微镜、扫描隧道显微镜、扫描隧道谱以及磁光克尔效应等手段进行表征。

Result: MBE制备的样品具有更尖锐的界面和更窄的Au(111)摇摆曲线宽度；两种样品在局部均具有平滑的Au(111)表面；微观扫描隧道谱显示两种样品均表现出相似的依赖于磁化方向的隧穿电流，证实了分子尺度的CISS效应大小相当；宏观磁光克尔效应显示仅溅射沉积样品在肽吸附后出现轻微的矫顽力增强和畴壁速度降低。

Conclusion: 微观CISS特征在两种样品中均稳健存在，而宏观MIPAC型磁响应则对衬底微结构更为敏感。

Abstract: Chirality-induced spin selectivity (CISS) enables spin-dependent transport at chiral molecule/Au(111) interfaces and is used in spintronics when combined with ferromagnetic thin films in spin-valve-type hybrids. However, the influence of substrate microstructure on CISS and the related magnetization induced by the proximity of adsorbed chiral molecules (MIPAC) effect is still not well understood. In this study, we compare the effects of the adsorption of L-chiral alpha-helical alanine-rich peptides on Au/Co/Au ferromagnetic thin films fabricated by molecular beam epitaxy (MBE) and magnetron sputtering. X-ray reflectivity and X-ray diffraction show sharper interfaces and a narrower Au(111) rocking-curve width for the MBE-grown sample. However, atomic force microscopy and scanning tunneling microscopy images reveal that both sample types have locally smooth Au(111) surface regions suitable for peptide adsorption, despite clear differences in larger-scale morphology. Microscopic scanning tunneling spectroscopy after peptide exposure yields similar magnetization-direction-dependent tunneling currents in both sample types, confirming a similar magnitude CISS effect on the molecular scale. In contrast, macroscopic magneto-optical Kerr effect hysteresis loops and effect microscopy reveals that only sputter-deposited samples show slight coercivity enhancements and a consistent reduction in domain wall velocity after peptide exposure. These results suggest that microscopic CISS signatures are robust for both sample types, whereas macroscopic MIPAC-type magnetic responses are more sensitive to the substrate microstructure.

</details>


### [113] [Surrogate-Gated Generation and Foundation-Model Embeddings for Bayesian Materials Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28578)
*Sk Md Ahnaf Akif Alvi,Jan Janssen,Danny Perez,Douglas Allaire,Raymundo Arroyave*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出在闭环材料发现流程中，通过插入高斯过程（Gaussian process）获取门（acquisition gate）作为廉价概率替代模型（probabilistic surrogate），对生成式扩散先验（diffusion prior）的输出进行排序筛选，从而在固定预算内显著降低属性评估（property evaluation）的调用成本，并保持与无门控微调（ungated fine-tuning）相当或更优的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在闭环材料发现（closed-loop materials discovery）中，属性评估（property evaluation）占据主要成本。生成式变体（generative variant）中，学习先验（learned prior）提出候选结构，属性预言机（property oracle）进行评分。研究动机是探究是否可以用一个廉价概率替代模型（probabilistic surrogate）对生成器的输出进行分类筛选（triage），以及该替代模型需要在哪些方面表现良好。

Method: 在三种架构不同的预训练扩散先验（MatterGen、CrystalFlow、ADiT）和两个目标属性（室温热容和体模量）上，于强化学习引导的生成工作流（RL-steered generative workflow）中，在结构生成与预言机之间插入一个高斯过程获取门（Gaussian process acquisition gate）。通过预算匹配消融（budget-matched ablation）隔离机制，并进行了跨因子基准测试（cross-factorial benchmark），覆盖力学、电子和振动属性。

Result: 该门控机制在固定每周期预算内，性能匹配或超过无门控的生成模型微调（ungated fine-tuning）。在相同的四调用预算下，基于排名的选择优于任意选择，确认收益来自替代模型的选择能力；门控机制在大约五分之一调用次数下达到接近穷尽预言机支出的约9%以内。密度泛函理论（DFT）验证显示，体模量发现中学习预言机平均误差在2.5%以内，替代模型对生成结构的排序达到Spearman ρ = 0.94。跨因子基准测试中，预训练ORB嵌入配合高斯过程是最可靠的组合。

Conclusion: 廉价概率替代模型能够有效对生成式材料发现流程中的候选结构进行排序筛选，在显著降低预言机调用成本的同时保持高精度。提出的完整流水线已作为开源软件发布。

Abstract: Closed-loop materials discovery iterates between proposing candidate structures and evaluating their properties, and property evaluation dominates the cost. In the generative variant, a learned prior proposes candidate crystals and a property oracle scores them; we ask whether a cheap probabilistic surrogate can triage the generator's output, and what such a surrogate must do well. Across three architecturally distinct pretrained diffusion priors (MatterGen, CrystalFlow, ADiT) and two targets (room-temperature heat capacity and bulk modulus), we insert a Gaussian process acquisition gate between structure generation and the oracle in an RL-steered generative workflow. The gate matches or exceeds ungated fine-tuning of the generative model while capping oracle calls at a fixed per-cycle budget. Budget-matched ablations isolate the mechanism. At an identical four-call budget, ranking-based selection outperforms arbitrary selection, confirming that the gain comes from the surrogate's choice; the gate comes within $\sim$9\% of exhaustive oracle spending at roughly one-fifth of the calls. A density-functional-theory check of the bulk-modulus discoveries confirms the learned oracle to within 2.5\% on average and the surrogate's ranking of the generated structures at Spearman $ρ= 0.94$. A cross-factorial benchmark of surrogate performance spanning mechanical, electronic, and vibrational properties identifies pretrained ORB embeddings with a Gaussian process as the most reliable combination, which we adopt as the building blocks of the proposed workflow. The complete pipeline is released as open-source software.

</details>


### [114] [Structural relaxation and stagnation of grain boundary during migration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28658)
*Tingting Yu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过模拟发现，晶界（grain boundary, GB）可通过空位、孪晶（twinning）和位错（dislocation）等缺陷发射实现弛豫（relaxation），从而降低晶界平均原子能量。研究进一步揭示了晶界迁移过程中的停滞（stagnation）现象及其与平均原子能量和体积的关联，为通过设计晶界微观结构提升材料强度奠定基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纳米材料中晶界（grain boundary, GB）在热或机械刺激下的不稳定性是主要瓶颈，而晶界弛豫（relaxation）可通过结构修饰使GB进入更低能量状态来稳定材料性能；然而，对弛豫机制理解的缺乏限制了其应用。

Method: 采用斜升能量守恒取向驱动力（ramped energy-conserving orientated driving force）进行模拟，研究晶界在特定驱动力下的迁移行为，并分析平均原子能量与平均原子体积的变化。

Result: 晶界可通过空位、孪晶和位错等缺陷发射实现弛豫，降低平均原子能量。在特定驱动力下晶界突然停止迁移，驱动力增至某值后恢复迁移；即使在固定驱动力下也可能出现停滞。停滞原因与晶界平均原子能量和平均原子体积的变化有关。

Conclusion: 停滞现象的发现有助于更深入理解晶界迁移特性，并为通过设计晶界微观结构（grain boundary microstructures）以提升材料强度提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Instability is a major bottleneck in nanomaterials due to grain boundary (GB) activities under thermal or mechanical stimuli. The relaxation of GB will stabilize the properties of materials by structure modification of GBs to lower energy states. However, lack of understanding of mechanisms limits the application of GB relaxation. In this study, we certify that GB can realize relaxation through defect emission including vacancy, twinning and dislocations, etc, which lower the average atomic energy of GB. In particular, we found stagnation and shear-coupling migration accompany the relaxation process, where a lower average atomic energy and lower average atomic volume of grain boundaries can be the reasons for stagnation. In this study, we found when simulated by ramped energy-conserving orientated driving force, under a specific driving force, the grain boundary suddenly stops migrating during the migration process, and as the driving force increases to a certain value, the grain boundary continues to migrate. Even at fixed driving forces, the grain boundary migration process can stall. This phenomenon has been found in many grain boundaries, and it has been found that the reason for the stagnation is the change of the average atomic energy of grain boundaries and the average atomic volume of grain boundaries. The discovery of this stagnation phenomenon is helpful to better understand the migration characteristics of grain boundaries and lays a foundation for improving the strength of materials by designing grain boundary microstructures.

</details>


### [115] [Strain engineering of ultrafast magnetism in the room-temperature vdW ferromagnet Fe3GaTe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28668)
*Fan Fei,Yangchen He,Wuzhang Fang,Jessica Kienbaum,Jacopo Simoni,Robert Boyd,Yuan Ping,Daniel A. Rhodes,Jun Xiao*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文展示了通过机械应变连续调控室温范德华铁磁体Fe₃GaTe₂的平衡磁响应和超快退磁动力学，发现拉伸应变可加速超快退磁过程，且这一加速机制无法通过单纯增加泵浦光通量实现。结合第一性原理计算，应变通过改变自旋-晶格能量转移来实现对退磁动力学的调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 控制超快磁动力学（ultrafast magnetic dynamics）对于理解非平衡自旋相互作用（nonequilibrium spin interactions）和推进高速自旋电子学（high-speed spintronics）至关重要，但现有研究缺乏高效的原位（in situ）调控策略，大多依赖于材料的本征性质。

Method: 实验上对室温范德华铁磁体Fe₃GaTe₂施加最高4.2%的单轴拉伸应变（uniaxial tensile strain），利用时间分辨磁光克尔效应（time-resolved magneto-optical Kerr effect）测量超快退磁动力学，并结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）分析应变对自旋-晶格能量转移的影响。

Result: 施加4.2%拉伸应变使矫顽场从接近零增至100 Oe，表明有效垂直磁各向异性（perpendicular magnetic anisotropy）增强。1.2%拉伸应变使特征退磁时间缩短约20%，且该加速退磁区域无法通过增加未应变样品的泵浦光通量达到。

Conclusion: 机械应变（mechanical strain）是一种按需调控超快磁动力学的有效途径，通过重构磁能量景观（magnetic energy landscape）和相关自旋弛豫路径（spin-relaxation pathways），可降低所需光学能量。

Abstract: Controlling ultrafast magnetic dynamics is critical to understanding nonequilibrium spin interactions and advancing high-speed spintronics. However, a lack of efficient in situ tuning strategies leaves most ultrafast studies largely dependent on the intrinsic properties of the individual materials. Here we demonstrate continuous strain tuning of both the equilibrium magnetic response and ultrafast demagnetization dynamics in the room-temperature van der Waals ferromagnet Fe3GaTe2. Applying up to 4.2% uniaxial tensile strain increases the coercive field from nearly zero to 100 Oe, consistent with an enhancement of the effective perpendicular magnetic anisotropy. Time-resolved magneto-optical Kerr effect measurements further reveal strain-accelerated ultrafast demagnetization, with 1.2% tensile strain reducing the characteristic demagnetization time by approximately 20%. Remarkably, strain accesses an accelerated demagnetization regime that cannot be reached simply by increasing pump fluence in the unstrained sample. Combined with first-principles calculations, our results resolve that the applied strain modifies the spin-lattice energy transfer, leading to the observed accelerated demagnetization. These findings establish mechanical strain as an effective route for on-demand control of ultrafast magnetic dynamics while reducing the required optical energy by reconfiguring the magnetic energy landscape and associated spin-relaxation pathways.

</details>


### [116] [Emergence of half-semiconductor behavior and tunable magnetism via carrier doping in Janus VXSe (X=Cl, Br, I) monolayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28713)
*Zhixiang Wang,Aining Wang,Zikui Ye,Yuqiao Qu,Qian Zheng,Yiding Liu,Qiang Fan,Gang Yao*

TL;DR: 基于第一性原理计算，本文预测了一类新型Janus VXSe（X=Cl, Br, I）单层材料，它们均为本征铁磁半导体，具有较高居里温度（最高128K）和磁各向异性能（最高910 μeV/V），且载流子掺杂可调控其自旋极化与磁易轴，为二维自旋电子学器件提供潜在平台。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）对Janus VXSe（X=Cl, Br, I）单层进行结构预测与电子性质、磁性质分析；通过载流子掺杂模拟其自旋极化状态与磁易轴（magnetic easy axis）的变化。

Abstract: Two-dimensional ferromagnetic semiconductors with high Curie temperature, large magnetic anisotropy, and electrically tunable properties are highly sought for nanoscale spintronics.
