### [118] [Structural properties of one-dimensional $\mathrm{Cs}_2\mathrm{CoCl}_4$ confined within single-walled carbon nanotubes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28983)
*Jaskaran S. Mangat,Yu Lei,Matthew Weyland,Yisong Han,Kiran Bal,Martin R. Lees,Craig I. Hiley,Piotr Dłużewski,Sławomir Kret,Peng Wang,Richard I. Walton,Jeremy Sloan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究发现，在一维（1D）限域条件下，金属卤化物Cs₂CoCl₄在单壁碳纳米管（single-walled carbon nanotubes, SWCNTs）中随管径减小依次结晶为四方晶系（tetragonal）和正交晶系（orthorhombic）的杆群（rod group）结构，且在1 nm直径附近表现出巨大的重入正交应变（re-entrant orthorhombic strain）。尽管结构发生显著变化，Co²⁺的有效磁矩和韦斯常数（Weiss constant）仅小幅增加，表明限域结构在拓扑上保留了块体（bulk）的核心磁性。所观察到的非常规多晶型（polymorphs）明显不同于高压压致变色多晶型，突显出一维限域作为一种独特结构调控工具的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 一维限域下晶体在金属性、磁性和化学状态上表现出剧烈变化，然而二元金属卤化物与三元金属卤化物钙钛矿（perovskites）之间的中间相空间在一维极限下的多晶型现象尚未被充分探索。

Method: 采用像差校正（扫描）透射电子显微镜（aberration-corrected (scanning) transmission electron microscopy）和多重片层模拟（multislice simulations），对Cs₂CoCl₄在单壁碳纳米管中的结构进行表征；通过直流磁化率（d.c. magnetization）拟合确定Co²⁺的磁性参数。

Result: Cs₂CoCl₄在径向压缩下依次结晶为四方晶系℗4/mcc和正交晶系℗mcm杆群，并在1 nm管径附近出现巨大的重入正交应变。限域后Co²⁺有效磁矩仅从4.607(3) μ_B/f.u.增至4.788(3) μ_B/f.u.，韦斯常数从-7.9(3) K变为-4.09(7) K。

Conclusion: 一维限域能够诱导出不同于高压压致变色相变的非常规多晶型，并在结构改变的同时拓扑地保留块体的核心磁性，表明一维限域是一种独特且有前景的结构调控手段。

Abstract: Crystals under one-dimensional (1D) confinement are well-known to exhibit drastic changes in metallicity, magnetic properties and chemical state, however, the intermediate phase space between binary metal halides and ternary metal halide perovskites remains poorly explored, especially in the context of the rich polymorphism exhibited by both families in the one-dimensional limit. Through aberration-corrected (scanning) transmission electron microscopy and multislice simulations, it is shown that the metal halide $\mathrm{Cs}_2\mathrm{CoCl}_4$ crystallizes in the tetragonal $\wp4/mcc$ and orthorhombic $\wp{mcm}$ rod groups under radial compression within single-walled carbon nanotubes (SWCNTs) of increasingly small diameter, with a massive re-entrant orthorhombic strain towards the $1$ $\mathrm{nm}$ extremum. The persistence of $\mathrm{Co}^{2+}$ is determined from fits to the d.c. magnetization, with a surprisingly small increase in the effective moment ($4.607(3)$ to $4.788(3) \mathit{μ}_\mathrm{B}/\mathrm{f.u.}$) and Weiss constant ($-7.9(3)$ to $-4.09(7) \mathrm{K}$) after confinement in the SWCNTs, suggesting that the confined structure topologically preserves the core magnetic properties of the bulk. Both unconventional polymorphs observed are noticeably different to the high-pressure piezochromic polymorph previously shown to undergo a tetrahedral-to-octahedral coordination transition, highlighting 1D confinement as a unique tool for structural manipulation.

### [119] [A Ginzburg-Landau theory of intrinsic dislocation-loop formation in diamond with machine-learned atomistic simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29055)
*Xiaoya Chang,Arsalan Hashemi,Nima Ghafari Cherati,Mikko Karttunen,Adam Gali,Tapio Ala-Nissila*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过构建金兹堡-朗道（Ginzburg-Landau）理论和量子力学精度的机器学习原子模拟，证明了金刚石中位错环的形成是一个一级相变（first-order phase transition），其驱动力主要来自键能重组（≈98%），而非弹性释放。该发现提供了一条无氮（nitrogen-free）缺陷形成路径，可补充传统Ia型金刚石中氮介导（nitrogen-mediated）的缺陷机制，并为辐照诱导环（irradiation-induced loops）的研究提供了一个可迁移的理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金刚石在电子学和量子技术中的应用受限于缺陷（defects），但缺陷从迁移点缺陷（migrating point defects）成核的过程很少被视为相变（phase transition）进行研究。本文旨在揭示该过程的相变本质并构建定量理论。

Method: 构建了以环面积（loop area）为序参量（order parameter）的金兹堡-朗道理论，其系数由量子力学精度（quantum-mechanically accurate）的机器学习原子模拟（machine-learned atomistic simulations）直接确定。通过纳米尺度和纳秒时间尺度的模拟，并结合克拉默斯速率理论（Kramers' rate theory）表征相变动力学。

Result: 碳自间隙原子（carbon self-interstitials）通过扩散-复合（diffusion-recombination）和晶格交换（lattice exchange）聚集形成线缺陷基序（line-defect motifs），进而孕育出棱柱型½⟨110⟩位错环（prismatic ½⟨110⟩ dislocation loop）和两种板状平面缺陷（platelet-like planar defects）。该相变为强一级相变（strongly first-order），驱动力约98%来自键能重组（bond-energy reorganisation），仅约2%来自弹性释放。

Conclusion: 这些缺陷由碳间隙原子内禀形成（intrinsically），无需氮参与，因此提供了一条无氮途径（nitrogen-free pathway），可补充长期争议的Ia型金刚石中氮介导（nitrogen-mediated）机制，并为辐照诱导环的研究提供了一个可迁移的理论框架（transferable framework）。

Abstract: Defects limit the performance of diamond in electronics and quantum technologies, yet how they nucleate from migrating point defects is rarely described as a phase transition. Here we show that dislocation-loop formation in diamond is a \emph{first-order phase transition}. We build a Ginzburg-Landau theory of it whose order parameter -- the loop area -- and coefficients are fixed directly from quantum-mechanically accurate machine-learned atomistic simulations. From simulations at nanometre and nanosecond scales, we find that carbon self-interstitials aggregate, by diffusion-recombination and lattice exchange, into line-defect motifs that seed a prismatic $\tfrac{1}{2}\langle110\rangle$ dislocation loop and two platelet-like planar defects. We also characterize the dynamics of the transition with Kramers' rate theory. The transition is strongly first-order, driven overwhelmingly ($\approx98\%$) by bond-energy reorganisation rather than elastic relief. Because these defects form \emph{intrinsically} -- from carbon interstitials alone, without nitrogen -- our results offer a nitrogen-free pathway complementary to the nitrogen-mediated routes long debated for type-Ia diamond, and a transferable framework for irradiation-induced loops.

</details>


### [120] [Oblate Spheroid Excitation Theory: A Unified, Lattice-Free Foundation for Plastic Deformation from Which Dislocations Emerge as Collective Excitations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29061)
*Albert Linda,K. A. Padmanabhan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文提出了扁球激发理论（Oblate Spheroid Excitation Theory, OSET），将塑性形变（plastic deformation）的基本载体定义为扁球转形区（oblate-spheroidal transformation zone, OSTZ），并证明经典位错理论（dislocation theory）是OSET在大N极限下的涌现结果，从而建立了一个无需晶格假定、适用于多种固体的塑性形变统一框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典位错理论（dislocation theory）依赖于周期性晶格（periodic lattice）的假设，因此无法描述晶界（grain boundaries）、玻璃、陶瓷或接近玻璃化转变的纳米晶体中没有周期晶格的塑性流动（plastic flow）。该研究试图构建一个不依赖晶格结构的、更根本的塑性形变基础理论。

Method: 提出扁球激发理论（OSET），将剪切本征应变（shear-eigenstrained）的扁球体——扁球转形区（OSTZ）——作为任意固体中塑性形变的基本载体，并基于Eshelby夹杂理论（Eshelby's inclusion theory）进行解析处理。OSTZ具有有限、非奇异（non-singular）、本质热激活（thermally activated）的能量场和应力场。通过解析推导，证明单个及链式OSTZ与经典位错结构之间的数学等价关系。

Result: 证明三个关键结果：单个OSTZ产生非奇异的弹性偶极子（elastic dipole），而非位错的奇异场；共面链式N个OSTZ在数学上与Peierls-Nabarro位错全同；真正的位错仅在链达到晶格设定的临界长度时才成核。由此无参数地推导出理论剪切强度（theoretical shear strength）、Peierls应力（Peierls stress）、芯区能量（core energy）、Frank-Read临界应力和堆垛层错能（stacking-fault energy）。实验验证方面，OSET再现了晶界滑移数据，并对文献中涵盖金属、陶瓷和块体金属玻璃的41个系统的拟合结果中，膨胀本征应变和剪切本征应变的精度分别达到2%和15%以内。

Conclusion: 经典位错理论是OSET在集体大N极限下的涌现现象（emergent phenomenon），而非预先假定的基本实体。OSET提供了一个比经典位错理论更根本、适用范围更广的塑性形变基础，可跨越不同材料类别。

Abstract: Dislocation theory has underpinned crystal plasticity for a century, yet its lattice-dependent definition cannot describe plastic flow in grain boundaries, glasses, ceramics, or nanocrystals near the glass transition, where no periodic lattice exists. We propose the Oblate Spheroid Excitation Theory (OSET): the elementary carrier of plastic deformation, in any solid, is a shear-eigenstrained oblate spheroid, the oblate-spheroidal transformation zone (OSTZ), treated within Eshelby's inclusion theory. The OSTZ requires no lattice and has a finite, non-singular, intrinsically thermally activated energy and stress fields. Three results are proved: a single OSTZ produces a non-singular elastic dipole, not a dislocation's singular field; a co-planar chain of N OSTZs is mathematically identical to a Peierls-Nabarro dislocation, core width and Burgers vector fixed by OSTZ geometry; and a genuine dislocation nucleates only once the chain reaches a host-lattice-set critical length. Dislocations emerge as a collective, large-$N$ limit of OSET rather than an assumed entity, and the theoretical shear strength, Peierls stress, core energy, Frank-Read critical stress, and stacking-fault energy follow as derived, parameter-free quantities. OSET is validated against grain-boundary-sliding data, independent literature spanning metals, ceramics, and bulk metallic glasses, and a recent 41-system compilation, reproducing the fitted dilatational and shear eigenstrains to within 2% and 15%, respectively. Because classical dislocation theory emerges from OSET but OSET does not require dislocations, it provides, in our view, a more fundamental, broadly applicable foundation for plastic deformation across material classes.

</details>


### [121] [Real-space identification of distinct magnetic configurations in a candidate d-wave altermagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29140)
*Jin-Cheng Gu,Mingzhe Hu,Ziyin Song,Lihan Wang,Lihong Wang,Junming Zhang,Jiali Zhao,Hang Li,Shifeng Jin,Xin-Ding Zhang,Genfu Chen,Hongming Weng,Zhongxu Wei,Tian Qian*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过自旋极化扫描隧道显微镜（spin-polarized scanning tunnelling microscopy）结合准粒子干涉成像，在原子尺度上确定了候选d波交错磁体（altermagnet）KV₂Se₂O的实空间磁构型，发现该材料中存在C型和G型两种磁构型，分别对应d波交错磁序和常规反铁磁序，从而建立了动量空间自旋劈裂与实空间磁序之间的直接联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已在多种材料中观测到与交错磁性（altermagnetism）一致的动量空间自旋劈裂电子结构，但其与实空间磁构型之间的关系尚不完全清楚，因为相似的自旋劈裂结构可能源于不同的磁序。在候选d波交错磁体KV₂Se₂O中，观测到的动量相关自旋劈裂的磁起源一直存在争议。

Method: 采用自旋极化扫描隧道显微镜（spin-polarized scanning tunnelling microscopy, SP-STM）结合磁场相关准粒子干涉成像（quasiparticle interference imaging），在原子尺度上确定KV₂Se₂O的磁构型。

Result: 自旋分辨准粒子干涉揭示了V₂O层内呈现棋盘状反平行自旋织构，并通过单胞台阶边缘确定了层间自旋排列。识别出C型和G型两种磁构型：两者在单层层面均产生相似的自旋劈裂电子结构，但分别对应d波交错磁序和常规反铁磁序（antiferromagnetic order）。

Conclusion: 这些观测揭示了由近简并磁态（nearly degenerate magnetic states）导致的复杂磁景观。研究结果建立了动量空间自旋劈裂与实空间磁序之间的直接联系，为识别交错磁体（altermagnetic materials）中自旋劈裂电子结构的微观起源提供了分析框架。

Abstract: Altermagnetism is an emerging class of magnetic order characterized by momentum-dependent spin-split electronic structures despite vanishing net magnetization. Although momentum-space signatures consistent with altermagnetism have been reported in a growing number of materials, their relationship to the underlying real-space magnetic configurations remains incompletely understood, because similar spin-split electronic structures can arise from distinct magnetic orders. In the candidate d-wave altermagnet KV2Se2O, the magnetic origin of the observed momentum-dependent spin splitting has remained controversial. Here, we employ spin-polarized scanning tunnelling microscopy combined with magnetic-field-dependent quasiparticle interference imaging to determine the magnetic configuration of KV2Se2O at the atomic scale. Spin-resolved quasiparticle interference reveals a checkerboard-like antiparallel spin texture within the V2O layer and determines its interlayer spin arrangement across unit-cell step edges. Remarkably, we identify both C-type and G-type magnetic configurations, both of which generate similar spin-split electronic structures at the single-layer level but correspond to d-wave altermagnetic and conventional antiferromagnetic orders, respectively. These observations reveal a complex magnetic landscape arising from nearly degenerate magnetic states. Our results establish a direct connection between momentum-space spin splitting and real-space magnetic order, providing a framework for identifying the microscopic origin of spin-split electronic structures in altermagnetic materials.

</details>


### [122] [Kinetically Controlled Condensation Boundary Governing Indium Incorporation in InGaN Metal Organic Vapor Phase Epitaxy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29163)
*Qihui Lin,Junlin Wu,Erqi Xu,Jiaqing Yue,Jiale Wang,Zihao Xu,Haixin Qi,Liyi Luo,Haitao Wang,Jia Wang,Hiroshi Amano,Bo Shen,Guangxu Ju*

TL;DR: 本文结合原位同步辐射X射线晶体截断杆（crystal truncation rod）测量与二元Burton-Cabrera-Frank模型，定量研究了金属有机气相外延（MOVPE）生长InGaN过程中铟（In）的掺入行为。模型通过区分In吸附原子（adatom）与凝聚液滴，并引入Ga-In耦合掺入动力学，精确描述了铟组分对前驱体通量和生长温度的非线性依赖关系，定量预测了动力学控制的冷凝边界，为高In组分InGaN生长提供预测框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高In组分InGaN材料在光电器件中具有重要应用，但In掺入过程中存在非线性依赖关系和液滴形成等复杂问题，缺乏定量预测模型。本文旨在发展一个能够描述In掺入动力学并预测冷凝边界的理论框架，以优化高In组分InGaN的生长工艺。

Method: 采用原位同步辐射X射线晶体截断杆（crystal truncation rod）测量技术，结合二元Burton-Cabrera-Frank模型。模型区分了In吸附原子（adatom）与凝聚液滴两种状态，并纳入耦合的Ga-In掺入动力学（coupled Ga-In incorporation kinetics）。

Result: 模型成功捕捉到铟组分对前驱体通量和生长温度的本质上非线性（intrinsically nonlinear）依赖关系。确定了在给定温度下对应最大可达到In组分的临界In覆盖度（critical In coverage），该覆盖度由In吸附原子供给与掺入容量之间的动力学平衡决定，定义了一个随温度和Ga通量变化的动力学控制冷凝边界（kinetically controlled condensation boundary）。模型定量预测了这一边界，与独立测量结果一致。

Conclusion: 该模型为高In组分InGaN生长提供了预测性框架（predictive framework），可有效优化生长条件并避免液滴形成。

Abstract: We combine in situ synchrotron X-ray crystal truncation rod measurements with a binary Burton-Cabrera-Frank model to quantify indium incorporation during InGaN growth by metal-organic vapor phase epitaxy (MOVPE) on GaN(0001). By distinguishing In adatoms from condensed droplets and incorporating coupled Ga-In incorporation kinetics, the model captures the intrinsically nonlinear dependence of indium composition on precursor flux and growth temperature. The critical In coverage corresponding to the maximum attainable In composition at a given temperature is determined by a kinetic balance between In adatom supply and incorporation capacity, defining a kinetically controlled condensation boundary that shifts with temperature and Ga flux. The model quantitatively predicts this boundary, in agreement with independent measurements, and provides a predictive framework for optimizing high-In-content InGaN growth while avoiding droplet formation.

### [123] [Silicon-compatible ideal antiferroelectricity with large digital electromechanical responses enabled by thermal-strain domain engineering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29219)

Result: 拉伸应变稳定了(004)o畴，实现直接一步切换；而压缩应变稳定的(240)o畴则通过中间铁电态（ferrielectric states）切换。所得薄膜展现出近零剩余极化（remanent polarization）、方形双电滞回线、~75ns的纳秒级开关速度、~0.6%的大可逆电致应变（reversible electrostrain）以及稳健的工作窗口。

Abstract: Antiferroelectrics exhibit reversible antipolar-polar transformations, offering a compelling platform for multiple functionalities in modern nanoelectronics, yet deterministic control of antiferroelectric domains and switching pathways remain elusive. The resulting films exhibit near-zero remanent polarization, square double hysteresis, nanosecond switching (~75ns), large reversible electrostrain (~0.6%) and robust operation windows. These findings provide key insights into domain-engineered ideal antiferroelectricity on silicon, opening a viable route toward high-performance antiferroelectric nano-electronic devices.

### [124] [Multiphysical impedance spectroscopy of porous electrodes based on linear irreversible thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29257)
*Junning Jiao,Juner Zhu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文从线性不可逆热力学出发，建立了多物理阻抗谱（multiphysical impedance spectroscopy）的一般理论框架，通过扰动一个物理场并测量另一共轭场响应，探测本构矩阵的非对角元（交叉耦合）。将理论特化至电-化-力学路径，导出了力-电化学阻抗谱（MEIS）的闭式表达式，并给出了微观结构化的孔隙度-容纳桥接函数和三相闭合关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多孔电极中电、化学、力学、流体、热场强耦合，但传统频域诊断（如电化学阻抗谱EIS和动态力学分析DMA）仅探测单一物理场响应（本构矩阵对角元），无法捕捉决定结构演化和退化的交叉耦合效应。

Method: 基于线性不可逆热力学（linear irreversible thermodynamics）构建多物理阻抗谱一般理论；对电-化-力学通路做特例化，推导力-电化学阻抗谱（mechano-electrochemical impedance spectroscopy, MEIS）闭式解；通过亥姆霍兹自由能（Helmholtz free energy）导出微结构刚度与黏度决定的孔隙度-容纳桥接函数，并建立三相（固-液-空）闭合关系以连续插值非饱和与Biot饱和极限。

Result: MEIS阻抗因子化为化学积累项乘以化学-力学与孔隙-力学核之和；无量纲化将谱简化为五组参数，识别出相位角为化学-力学参数的判别量，并定位到第二象限行为（second-quadrant behavior）的起始频率，该行为在全电池中源于膨胀电极与收缩电极的竞争。

Conclusion: MEIS是交叉耦合光谱族的一个成员，所建立的统一框架可推广至其他物理场的交叉耦合阻抗谱。

Abstract: Porous electrodes couple electrical, chemical, mechanical, hydraulic, and thermal fields, yet conventional frequency-domain diagnostics interrogate only one of them: electrochemical impedance spectroscopy (EIS) the electrical response and dynamic mechanical analysis (DMA) the mechanical. Each reads a diagonal entry of the multiphysical constitutive matrix and is blind to the cross-couplings that govern structural evolution and degradation. Starting from linear irreversible thermodynamics, we formulate a general theory of multiphysical impedance spectroscopy, in which perturbing one field and measuring the conjugate response of another probes an off-diagonal entry of the constitutive matrix, recovering the static coupling coefficient and resolving its relaxation dynamics across frequency. Specializing to the electro-chemo-mechanical pathway yields a closed-form theory of mechano-electrochemical impedance spectroscopy (MEIS), in which a small harmonic current is applied and the stack stress is measured; the impedance factorizes into a chemical-accumulation term multiplying the sum of a chemo-mechanical and a poro-mechanical kernel. The porosity-accommodation bridge function is derived from a Helmholtz free energy -- following from a microstructural stiffness and viscosity rather than a fitted form -- and a three-phase (solid-fluid-void) closure interpolates continuously between unsaturated and Biot-saturated limits through a void-accommodation fraction. Non-dimensionalization reduces the spectrum to five groups, identifies the phase angle as the discriminator of the chemo-mechanical parameters, and locates the onset of second-quadrant behavior, which in a full cell arises from the competition between an expanding and a contracting electrode. MEIS emerges as one member of a family of cross-coupled spectroscopies the same framework brings within reach.

*Diego De Gusem,Arnaud Nizet,Bartel Van Waeyenberge*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从理论推导出发，建立描述法向应变驱动下反铁磁畴壁运动的方程；随后将解析模型与基于mumax⁺的微磁学（micromagnetic）仿真结果进行比较，涵盖应变梯度、振荡应变及瑞利波（Rayleigh wave）等多种应变剖面。

Conclusion: 该解析模型可准确描述反铁磁畴壁在法向应变下的运动；驻表面声波（standing surface acoustic wave）有望作为赛道存储器中的纠错方法。

Abstract: We derive an equation describing domain wall motion in antiferromagnets under the influence of normal strain. From this equation, we find that the domain wall moves towards positions where $\varepsilon_{xx}$ is high and $\varepsilon_{zz}$ is low. Furthermore, each strain component leads to a different terminal velocity for the same strain profile. This difference arises because both strains affect the domain wall width in opposite ways: $\varepsilon_{xx}$ reduces the width, whereas $\varepsilon_{zz}$ increases it. The model is then compared with mumax$^+$ simulations for various strain profiles, including a strain gradient, an oscillating strain, and a Rayleigh wave. The comparison shows good agreement between the analytical and numerical results. Finally, we demonstrate the potential of standing surface acoustic waves as an error correction method in racetrack memory.

### [126] [Bilinear Flexo-Antiferrodistortive Coupling in Ferroelastics: Polar Twins, Antiphase Boundaries and Fingerprints of Alterelectricity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29456)
*Eugene A. Eliseev,Anna N. Morozovska,Venkatraman Gopalan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过Landau-Ginzburg-Devonshire方法证明了在反铁畸变铁弹体中存在一种称为“双线性挠性-反铁畸变耦合”（bilinear flexo-antiferrodistortive coupling）的Lifshitz不变量形式耦合，该耦合可在畴壁和反相边界诱导出子晶格敏感的极化，并可能对应于交替电（alterelectric）型四极电有序，但该效应在大多数纳米反铁畸变铁电/反铁电材料中被压电/线性挠电耦合掩盖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示反铁畸变铁弹体中电极化矢量与反铁畸变长程序参量之间的线性梯度型耦合——即双线性挠性-反铁畸变耦合——的存在性及其物理后果，并探讨其作为交替电型长程有序指纹特征的可能性。

Method: 采用Landau-Ginzburg-Devonshire方法进行对称性分析，并利用四子晶格模型揭示双线性挠性-反铁畸变耦合在畴壁和反相边界处诱导子晶格敏感极化的微观机制。

Result: 双线性挠性-反铁畸变耦合可在无反铁电或铁电有序的反铁畸变铁弹体中的孪晶壁和反相边界处诱导出子晶格敏感的极化；该极化垂直于反铁畸变长程序参量，且在相邻子晶格中方向相反，形成棋盘格型结构，可能对应交替电型四极电有序。然而，在大多数纳米反铁畸变铁电/反铁电材料中，该耦合的物理表现被压电耦合和/或线性挠电耦合所掩盖。

Conclusion: 双线性挠性-反铁畸变耦合是反铁畸变铁弹体中交替电型长程有序的一个指纹特征，因为普通的挠电耦合无法在反铁畸变铁弹体的畴界处诱导出交替电型极化。

Abstract: Using the Landau-Ginsburg-Devonshire approach we show that the linear gradient-type coupling between the electric polarization vector and antiferrodistortive long-range order parameter pseudovector, that has the form of Lifshitz invariant and named "bilinear flexo-antiferrodistortive coupling", can emerge in all antiferrodistortive ferroelastics, since it is symmetry-allowed. Using the four sublattices model we reveal that the bilinear flexo-antiferrodistortive coupling can induce the sublattice-sensitive polarization at the twin walls and antiphase boundaries in antiferrodistortive ferroelastics without any ferroelectric or antiferroelectric ordering. Since the induced polarization is perpendicular to the antiferrodistortive long-range order parameter and counter-directed in neighboring sublattices with checkerboard-type direction of antiferrodistortive long-range order parameter, such structure of polarization may correspond to the alterelectric-type quadrupolar electric order. However, physical manifestations of the bilinear flexo-antiferrodistortive coupling are invisible in most nanostructured antiferrodistortive ferroelectrics and antiferroelectrics due to the domination of piezoelectric and/or linear flexoelectric couplings. Since a common flexoelectric coupling cannot induce the alterelectric-type polarization at domain boundaries in antiferrodistortive ferroelastics, we believe that the bilinear flexo-antiferrodistortive coupling can be a fingerprint of recently discovered alterelectric long-range order in antiferrodistortive ferroelastics.

Abstract: Predicting a material's properties from its structure is a central, fast-advancing problem in computational materials science. Conclusion: ML-AC克服了现有介质易受离子扩散降解的弱点，可消除额外阻挡层（节约多达3 nm空间），对金属线宽接近10 nm的场景尤为关键。其综合性能可显著改善硅基半导体电子器件，并兼容未来二维电子学。

The challenge lies in achieving a dielectric constant less than 3, as traditional low-k dielectrics are inherently unstable at the 2D limit due to their amorphous or porous nature. The realisation of ultrathin dielectrics with low-k is also needed to address current bottlenecks in integrated circuits scaling. Specifically, low-k materials are necessary to minimise parasitic capacitances as the distance between conductive elements shrinks below 10 nm. Moreover, advanced architectures like gate-all-around field effect transistors (GAA FET) require even lower dielectric constants (k<2) at sub-3nm thickness. Here, we show that layer-by-layer grown multilayer amorphous carbon (ML-AC), as thin as 0.8 nm, is a mechanically robust 2D ULK dielectric with k of 1.35 and dielectric strength of 28-31 MV cm-1. The lack of any long-range order, its intrinsic 2D nature, sp2 carbon character and low density are all essential for minimising dielectric permittivity. Moreover, ML-AC overcomes the vulnerability of existing dielectrics to ion diffusion degradation with a record metal ion diffusion time to failure (TTF) of 10^10 s for even a single layer. Therefore, otherwise necessary additional layers occupying up to 3 nm can be eliminated, which is especially significant as metal line widths approach 10 nm. Combined with its low-temperature, direct and conformal growth even on a dielectric, these critical features enable substantial improvements in silicon-based semiconductor electronics and ensure compatibility with future 2D electronics.

### [130] [Ferron Hall effect: Transverse accumulation of polarization driven by thermal gradients in ferroelectrics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29765)
*Daniel A. Bustamante Lopez,Verena Brehm,Dominik M. Juraschek*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理（density functional theory）与原子晶格动力学模拟，理论证明了铁电材料中由霍尔效应（Hall effect）偏转的携带电偶极矩的晶格激发（称为ferrons）会产生横向电极化累积，即铁子霍尔效应（ferron Hall effect），并在BaTiO3中验证了该效应，指出ferrons是横向输运中与磁振子（magnons）对应的电极化类似物。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 声子霍尔效应（phonon Hall effect）已描述了磁场下纵向热梯度产生横向热流的现象，但该效应在铁电材料中是否会导致电极化累积尚不清楚。本文旨在从理论上揭示，当被霍尔效应偏转的晶格激发携带电偶极矩时，会在铁电体中产生横向电极化累积，从而建立一种新的热电耦合机制。

Method: 采用基于密度泛函理论（density functional theory）获得的参数进行原子尺度晶格动力学（atomistic lattice dynamics）计算，在原型铁电体钛酸钡（BaTiO3）中演示铁子霍尔效应。

Result: 成功在BaTiO3中证明了铁子霍尔效应的存在，即携带极化（polarization）的晶格激发——ferrons在横向输运中产生电极化累积。

Conclusion: Ferrons被确认为横向输运中与磁振子（magnons）对应的电极化（electric polarization）类似物，该发现为通过热和磁场手段调控铁性序（ferroic order）提供了新的路径。

Abstract: The phonon Hall effect describes the generation of a transverse heat current in response to a longitudinal thermal gradient in a magnetic field. Here, we theoretically demonstrate that, when the lattice excitations deflected by the Hall effect carry electric dipole moments, their transverse motion produces an accumulation of electric polarization in ferroelectric materials. This accumulation is driven by lattice excitations that carry polarization, known as ferrons, and we therefore call the mechanism the ferron Hall effect. Using atomistic lattice dynamics with parameters obtained from density functional theory, we illustrate the effect in the prototypical ferroelectric BaTiO3. Our results identify ferrons as the electric-polarization analogues of magnons in transverse transport and provide a route toward thermal and magnetic manipulation of ferroic order.

Here, we systematically investigate the magnetic and transport properties of antiferromagnet EuAuAs. Magnetic characterizations reveal antiferromagnetic transition at 5.7 K and 6.3 K for $H \parallel ab$ and $H \parallel c$, accompanied by metamagnetic transition and small hysteresis for $H \parallel ab$. Furthermore, the magnetoresistance exhibits butterfly-shaped hysteresis and strong angular dependence, which are likely associated with spin-dependent electron scattering, magnetic-domain evolution, and domain-wall pinning. *A. Ya. Maltsev*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先在主导紧束缚近似（tight-binding approximation）下尝试估算概率，发现由于简单立方或体心立方晶格谱的奇异性而无法估算。随后引入高阶修正（higher-order corrections），以获得更精确的电子谱（electron spectra）解析表达式，并由此估算该概率。

Result: 在主导紧束缚近似下，对于简单立方或体心立方晶格，无法估算超复杂电导率图出现的概率。通过使用高阶修正改进了电子谱的解析精度，从而实现了对该概率的有效估算。

Conclusion: 对于具有简单立方或体心立方晶格的导体，需超越主导紧束缚近似、采用高阶修正才能可靠估算超复杂电导率图出现的概率。该概率通常较低，但一旦出现，可在强磁场中观察到丰富的非平庸效应。

Abstract: We study the probability of the emergence of ultra-complex conductivity diagrams in conductors that satisfy the tight-binding approximation and have the simple or body-centered cubic lattice. The presence of ultra-complex conductivity diagrams allows us to observe a number of highly nontrivial effects in strong magnetic fields, however, the probability of their emergence in a given substance is quite low. In the case of the simple or body-centered cubic lattice, the leading tight-binding approximation does not allow us to estimate this probability due to the peculiarities of the spectra in this situation. To estimate this probability, we use higher-order corrections to the leading approximation, which yield more accurate analytical expressions for the electron spectra.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Floquet工程（Floquet engineering）依赖强光场操控电子结构，但光驱动Floquet-Bloch态寿命较短；相干声子被认为能实现更长寿命的Floquet-Bloch态，但缺乏实验验证。

Method: 采用时间分辨多光子光电子发射（time-resolved multiphoton photoemission）结合量子拍光谱学（quantum beat spectroscopy），在石墨烯覆盖的Ir(111)表面上追踪由相干声子修饰的镜像势态（image-potential states）的相干电子动力学。

Result: 量子拍信号显示边带结构（sideband structure）的基频周期与相干声子频率一致，符合Floquet理论（Floquet theory）预期；同时观测到同频率的独立强度振荡，证实相干声子模式被激发。声子驱动Floquet-Bloch态的寿命比传统光驱动态长1-2个数量级。

Conclusion: 这些结果建立了一种在时域上识别声子驱动Floquet-Bloch态的实验方法，并揭示了它们在超快时间尺度上的形成过程。

Abstract: Controlling material excitations offers access to novel fundamental and technological properties. The paradigm of Floquet engineering, the manipulation of the electronic structure using a coherent and time-periodic driving source, has attracted significant attention. While most realizations rely on strong optical fields, coherent phonons provide an alternative route to realizing Floquet-Bloch states, and are expected to enable substantially longer-lived Floquet-Bloch states. We show that laser-excited coherent phonons drive Floquet-Bloch states. Using time-resolved multiphoton photoemission combined with quantum beat spectroscopy on graphene-covered Ir(111), we track the coherent electronic dynamics of the image-potential states dressed by coherent phonons. The beat signal indicates the presence of sideband structure with the coherent-phonon frequency as its fundamental period, consistent with Floquet theory. Furthermore, an independent oscillation in intensity at the same frequency was observed, confirming excitation of the coherent phonon mode. Compared with conventional light-driven Floquet-Bloch states, the observed phonon-driven Floquet-Bloch states persist for one to two orders of magnitude longer. These results establish a time-domain route to identifying phonon-driven Floquet-Bloch states and reveal their formation on ultrafast timescales.

Abstract: A compact structure model for the icosahedral phase Cd5.7Yb is presented. The model is based on a higher-dimensional description and a cut-and-projection procedure to generate the atom distribution in three-dimensional physical space. It strictly employs only spherical or elliptical occupation domains, ensuring a low number of parameters and low calculation cost. In the presented form the model has seven adjustable parameters. Despite its minimalistic setting, the model reproduces available experimental data, such as chemical composition, mass density and electron density distribution, as well as the cluster structure in physical space very well. Nevertheless, the approximation of the occupation domains by spheres and ellipses evidently implies limitations in accuracy and universality. The model can be adapted for the description of other Tsai-type icosahedral phases.

### [136] [Ferroelastic domain wall motion and collective domain switching in RbSCN](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30125)

Method: 采用低频（0.05–40 Hz）动态弹性测量和共振超声谱学（resonant ultrasound spectroscopy）（100–600 kHz）两种技术，结合可压缩赝自旋模型计算畴壁宽度（twin boundary width）w、畴壁能（domain wall energy）F_w以及Peierls势（Peierls potential）V_0的温度依赖性，并基于该模型推导临界钉扎应力σ_c(T)的理论预测。

Conclusion: RbSCN在T*附近的弹性异常归因于集体畴切换事件，其触发条件是温度依赖的临界钉扎应力σ_c(T)降至外加应力σ以下，即T*对应σ=σ_c的状态；这一机制与KSCN的反常行为有本质区别。

Abstract: Low frequency (0.05 - 40 Hz) dynamic elastic measurements and resonant ultrasound spectroscopy measurements (100-600 kHz) of RbSCN have been performed in the temperature region of the order-disorder improper ferroelastic phase transition at T$_c \approx$ 435~K. Quite similar to KSCN, the low frequency data show - in addition to the intrinsic phase transition anomalies - superelastic softening in a- and b-directions, resulting from movements of ferroelastic domain walls under dynamic stress. However, in contrast to KSCN, a sudden discontinuous increase of Young's modulus appears in RbSCN at { T$^{\ast} < T_c $}, which is accompanied by a frequency dependent damping peak. This behaviour is reminiscent of a first order phase transition.\\ Heating RbSCN slightly above T$^{\ast}$, followed by subseqent cooling, removes all {signs of domain wall dynamics}. The results demonstrate, that the anomalies in RbSCN around $T^{\ast}$ result from collective domain switching events that are induced when the {temperature dependent critical pinning stress, $σ_c(T)$ falls below the applied external stress $σ$, implying that $T^{\ast}(σ=σ_c)$. This interpretation is supported by calculations of the temperature dependences of twin boundary widths $w$ and energies $F_w$, as well as the Peierls potential $V_0$ using a compressible pseudospin model, which leads to a critical pinning stress, $σ_c(T)$ that is in excellent agreement with experimental values of $T^{\ast}(σ_c)$. }

Abstract: This study systematically investigated the influence of boron incorporation in Cu-O thin films and the effect of oxygen partial pressure ($p_{\rm ox}$) on the phase evolution, chemical bonding, and electrical characteristics of the prepared films. A phase transition from Cu$_2$O to Cu$_2$O/Cu$_4$O$_3$ to CuO was observed as oxygen partial pressure increased. Boron incorporation significantly broadened the stability window of the Cu$_2$O and Cu$_4$O$_3$ phases and delayed the transition to CuO at higher oxygen partial pressure. In the highly B-doped Cu-O films, Cu$_4$O$_3$ was stabilized even under oxygen-rich conditions along with the CuO phase, suggesting that boron significantly altered the oxidation pathway. The formation of B-O and possible B-O-Cu configurations altered the local oxygen chemistry and promoted mixed-valence copper oxide phases. These findings demonstrate that boron doping is an effective approach for tailoring the phase stability, defect chemistry, and electrical characteristics of Cu-O thin films for optoelectronic and photovoltaic applications.

### [138] [Bayesian model comparison of type-I and type-II ultrafast demagnetization dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30334)
*Hiroki Wadati,Tetsuro Ueno*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过高斯卷积的唯象模型和基于贝叶斯信息准则的统计模型比较，系统研究了有限时间分辨率和噪声对超快退磁动力学类型分类（type-I vs type-II）的影响，发现仪器响应函数卷积会显著削弱两类动力学的可区分性，导致分类结果高度依赖于实验条件和分析方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验中有限的时间分辨率和噪声可能掩盖超快退磁动力学的内在特征，导致基于时间演化的类型-I（type-I）和类型-II（type-II）分类变得模糊甚至不可靠，因此需要定量评估这些实验因素对分类判别能力的影响。

Method: 采用高斯卷积（Gaussian convolution）的唯象模型（phenomenological models）生成合成数据集，结合基于贝叶斯信息准则（Bayesian information criterion, BIC）的统计模型比较方法，系统分析不同时间分辨率和噪声水平下两类退磁动力学的可区分性，并进一步对NiCo2O4薄膜的实验数据进行验证。

Result: 仪器响应函数的卷积显著缩小了type-I和type-II内在响应之间的可观测差异，因此在宽泛的参数区间内，模型判别在统计上变得不具结论性（statistically inconclusive）。对NiCo2O4薄膜实验数据的分析进一步验证了这一框架的适用性。

Conclusion: 超快退磁动力学的表观分类对实验分辨率、噪声水平和分析方法高度敏感，现有分类结果需要在考虑这些因素的前提下谨慎解释。

Abstract: Ultrafast demagnetization dynamics are often phenomenologically classified into type-I and type-II responses according to their temporal evolution following femtosecond laser excitation. However, finite experimental temporal resolution and noise can substantially obscure the intrinsic dynamics and complicate this classification. In this work, we investigate the distinguishability of type-I and type-II demagnetization dynamics using Gaussian-convolved phenomenological models and Bayesian information criterion-based statistical model comparison. Synthetic datasets with varying temporal resolution and noise levels are first analyzed to evaluate the conditions under which the two classes can be reliably discriminated. We show that convolution with the instrumental response function significantly reduces the observable differences between the intrinsic responses, thereby producing broad regimes in which model discrimination becomes statistically inconclusive. The applicability of the framework is further demonstrated through analysis of representative experimental ultrafast demagnetization data from NiCo2O4 thin films. These results suggest that the apparent classification of ultrafast demagnetization dynamics can be highly sensitive to experimental resolution, noise level, and analysis methodology.

</details>


### [139] [Hidden Defect Chemistry in Ion-Irradiated MoS$_2$ Field-Effect Transistors Revealed by Photocurrent Loss](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30361)
*L. Daniel,D. Sutarma,L. Klieve,O. Kharsah,U. Hagemann,O. Altenhoff,S. Sleziona,L. Breuer,P. Kratzer,M. Schleberger*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过低能 Ar⁺ 离子辐照在单层 MoS₂ 场效应晶体管（FET）中优先引入硫空位（V_S），结合电学表征、表面分析与第一性原理计算发现：暗态下器件表现稳健，但光照下的光电流与光致掺杂（photodoping）随辐照剂量增加而系统性降低；表面碳氢残留物可能通过钝化硫空位隐藏缺陷效应，密度泛函理论（DFT）计算证实了这一微观机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单层 MoS₂ 中的缺陷工程（defect engineering）是调控场效应晶体管（field-effect transistors, FETs）性能的重要途径，但器件中缺陷的电子响应常被接触效应、衬底效应、吸附物和化学钝化所掩盖，因此需要一种方法能够排除干扰、直接识别缺陷对电学特性的影响。

Method: 对 MoS₂ FET 进行低能 40 eV Ar⁺ 离子辐照，优先在沟道中产生硫空位（V_S）并最小化衬底损伤；对比暗态与光照下的电学表征结果，结合原子力显微镜（AFM）和 X 射线光电子能谱（XPS）进行表面分析，并采用密度泛函理论（density-functional theory, DFT）计算构建微观模型。

Result: 暗态转移特性（dark transfer characteristics）在中低辐照通量下表现稳健，仅在高通量下出现显著退化；而在 532 nm 光照下，光电流和光致掺杂（photodoping）随离子通量增加而系统性降低，揭示了暗态测量无法观测的辐照诱导变化。表面分析显示即便经过充分清洗，器件表面仍存在大量含碳残留物。DFT 计算表明：未饱和 V_S 引入带隙态（in-gap states），H–C_S 构型可抑制这些带隙态，而无氢碳取代则仍残留缺陷态。

Conclusion: 含碳表面污染（carbon-containing surface contamination）是解释 MoS₂ 及相关过渡金属二硫族化合物（TMDC）器件中缺陷工程实验的关键因素；碳氢残留物可能作为硫空位钝化的“储库”（reservoir），掩盖辐照引入的缺陷效应，需在实验设计与结果解读中加以重视。

Abstract: Defect engineering in monolayer MoS$_2$ is a promising route to tune field-effect transistors (FETs), but the electronic response of defects in processed devices can be masked by contacts, substrate effects, adsorbates, and chemical passivation. Here, we irradiate MoS$_2$ FETs with low-energy 40~eV Ar$^+$ ions to preferentially create sulfur vacancies (V$_S$) in the channel while minimizing substrate damage. We compare dark and illuminated electrical characterization with surface analysis and first-principles calculations. Dark transfer characteristics show an apparent robustness against irradiation up to moderate fluences, with pronounced degradation only at the highest fluence. Under 532~nm illumination, however, the photocurrent and light-induced photodoping decrease systematically with increasing ion fluence, revealing irradiation-induced changes that are hidden in standard dark measurements. Atomic force microscopy and X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy show substantial carbon-containing residues on processed devices even after extended cleaning. We propose that such residues may provide a reservoir for hydrocarbon-mediated passivation of sulfur vacancies. Density-functional-theory calculations provide a microscopic model consistent with this scenario: unsaturated V$_S$ introduce in-gap states, H-C$_S$ configurations suppress these states, and carbon substitution without hydrogen leaves defect states in the band gap. Our results highlight carbon-containing surface contamination as a key factor in interpreting defect engineering experiments on MoS$_2$ and related TMDC devices.

</details>

### [143] [Excitons in Large Disordered Boron-Nitride Layer using Linear-Scaling Bethe-Salpeter Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30585)
*Thomas Galvani,Lorenzo Sponza,Hakim Amara,Sylvain Latil,Stephan Roche*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种实空间线性标度贝特-沙尔普特框架（Bethe-Salpeter framework），通过亚晶格分辨的微扰解耦将局域电子-空穴对映射到稀疏紧束缚模型上，并结合核多项式方法（Kernel Polynomial Method）实现 O(N) 计算成本的吸收谱求解。应用于安德森无序的单层六方氮化硼（hBN）系统（含高达 10^5 个轨道），揭示了无序诱导的亮激子不对称展宽、主吸收峰从二次红移到线性红移的转变，以及激子质心的安德森局域化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的从头算格林函数方法（GW 近似的贝特-沙尔普特方程，GW approximation and Bethe-Salpeter equation）在计算激子光谱时计算成本高昂，难以应用于大尺度或无序体系。本文旨在开发一种线性标度方法，将激子光谱学拓展至常规 ab initio 方法无法企及的大规模、无序、莫尔超晶格（moiré）、准晶（quasicrystalline）及结构复杂的量子材料。

Method: 提出实空间线性标度贝特-沙尔普特框架，采用亚晶格分辨的微扰解耦（sublattice-resolved perturbative decoupling），将局域电子-空穴对映射到稀疏紧束缚模型（sparse tight-binding model）；进而应用核多项式方法以 O(N) 计算复杂度求解吸收光谱。

Result: 应用于安德森无序（Anderson disorder）的单层六方氮化硼（hexagonal boron nitride，hBN），轨道数高达 10^5。结果揭示：无序导致亮激子（bright exciton）的不对称展宽；主吸收峰从二次红移（quadratic redshift）转变为线性红移（linear redshift）；激子质心（center of mass）发生安德森局域化（Anderson localization）。

Conclusion: 该方法将激子计算扩展至传统 GW 近似与贝特-沙尔普特方程难以处理的大尺度、无序、莫尔、准晶及结构复杂量子材料，为光学光谱学在这些系统中的研究开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We introduce a real-space, linear-scaling Bethe-Salpeter framework that enables excitonic spectroscopy in large and possibly disordered boron-nitride-derived systems. Thanks to the use of a sublattice-resolved perturbative decoupling that maps localized electron-hole pairs onto a sparse tight-binding model, we implement the Kernel Polynomial Method to compute absorption spectra with O(N) cost. To illustrate the capabilities of our method, we apply it to Anderson-disordered monolayer hexagonal boron nitride with up to $10^{5}$ orbitals. The method reveals a disorder-induced asymmetric broadening of bright excitons, a crossover from quadratic to linear redshift of the main absorption peak, and Anderson localization of the exciton center of mass. This approach extends excitonic calculations beyond the reach of conventional ab initio Green's function methods (GW approximation and Bethe-Salpeter equation), opening optical spectroscopy to large-scale, disordered, moiré, quasicrystalline, and structurally complex quantum materials.

### [144] [Pathway variability, coat stiffening and mechanical adaptation during clathrin-mediated endocytosis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30267)

Conclusion: 网格蛋白涂层是一种具有预应力和记忆的适应性组装体，其命运和材料参数反映了其生长的环境。有效涂层弯曲刚度和偏好曲率在生长过程中涌现，而非预先指定的材料参数。

Abstract: Clathrin assemblies in cells can persist as flat plaques, abort after partial invagination, or close into clathrin-coated vesicles, but the determinants of these different fates remain unresolved. To investigate the stochastic and complex dynamics of clathrin assemblies, we have developed a kinetic Monte Carlo simulation framework that couples individual clathrin agents to an adaptive continuum membrane. In this hybrid discrete-continuum description, the effective coat bending rigidity and the preferred coat curvature emerge during growth, rather than being prescribed as material parameters. Once connected, curved lattices stiffen from molecular bending modes to coat-level rigidities, because curvature changes require increased stretching or compression, while newly incorporated triskelia hardcode a history-dependent preferred curvature. An analytical theory for non-Euclidean elasticity identifies the relevant internal variables and predicts growth laws that are validated by the simulations. The same microscopic assembly rules yield flat, stalled, and closed coats through two sequential gates in the effective membrane-coat energy landscape. Comparisons with experimentally observed coat geometries and nanodissection-induced curvature changes agree with our theoretical predictions without any fitting parameters. The clathrin coat thus emerges as an adaptive assembly with prestress and memory, whose fate and material parameters reflect the environment in which it has been growing.

### [145] [Entanglement and non-separability of momenta and coordinates at colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24468)
*Marco Fabbrichesi,Roberto Floreanini,Luca Marzola*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文探讨了在加速器实验中检验相空间变量是否可分离的可能性。通过EPR型关联研究相空间不可分离性，将原始EPR设置用坐标和动量在真实实验中实现，并利用半球投影将连续变量约化为双量子比特系统来量化动量纠缠。以电子对撞机中的τ轻子产生为例，通过蒙特卡洛模拟证明相空间不可分离性可在实验上得到评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验相空间变量（phase-space variables）在加速器实验中是否可分离，这是量子纠缠研究在粒子物理中的延伸。现有实验多关注自旋或极化，而原始EPR悖论（EPR paradox）涉及的是坐标与动量，这一原始设定尚未在实验中得到充分检验。

Method: 首先利用EPR型关联（EPR-like correlations）研究相空间不可分离性，将原始EPR设置以坐标和动量形式在真实实验中实现。然后通过半球投影（hemispherical projections）将连续变量（continuous variables）约化为双量子比特系统（two-qubit system），进而量化粒子对动量中的纠缠。最后以电子对撞机中τ轻子的产生为例，从τ衰变为π介子和中微子的过程中重建动量，并通过蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulation）验证实验可行性。

Result: 通过蒙特卡洛模拟表明，相空间不可分离性（phase-space non-separability）可以通过实验手段进行评估，具体在τ轻子对产生的场景中得到了验证。

Conclusion: 加速器实验具备检验相空间变量可分离性的能力，这为在高能物理中研究基于坐标-动量的量子纠缠提供了可行的实验路径。

Abstract: We explore the possibility of testing in collider experiments whether phase-space variables are separable. We first study phase-space non-separability by means of EPR-like correlations. The original EPR setting is realized in an actual experiment, specifically in terms of coordinates and momenta, as per the original formulation, rather than spins or polarizations. We then show how to quantify the entanglement in the momenta of particle pairs by reducing the continuous variables to a two-qubit system through hemispherical projections. We discuss in detail the production of $τ$-leptons at an electron collider, reconstructing the momenta of the former from their decays into pions and neutrinos, and demonstrate through a Monte Carlo simulation that phase-space non-separability can be experimentally assessed.

### [146] [Soft Contributions Stabilize NNLO QCD Corrections to Quarkonium Production and Decay](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28494)
*Luca Maxia,Hua-Sheng Shao,Lukas Simon,Guoxing Wang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究识别了非相对论量子色动力学（non-relativistic QCD）中NNLO级QCD修正出现微扰不稳定性的根源，并提出了一种简单的修正方案。将该方法应用于S波色单态夸克偶素过程后，显著改善了微扰收敛性及其与实验数据的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非相对论量子色动力学（non-relativistic QCD）框架下，夸克偶素（quarkonium）产生和衰变的次次领头阶（NNLO）QCD修正存在微扰不稳定性（perturbative instabilities），这一问题阻碍了理论预测与实验数据的精确比较。本文旨在识别该问题的起源并给出有效的解决方案。

Method: 通过分析微扰不稳定性（perturbative instabilities）在NNLO阶数上的结构特征，定位其根本成因，并据此提出一种简单的修正方法（remedy）。

Result: 将所提出的方法应用于S波色单态（S-wave color-singlet）夸克偶素（quarkonium）的产生与衰变过程后，微扰收敛性（perturbative convergence）得到了显著改善，理论结果与实验数据（experimental data）之间的一致性也大幅提升。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了NRQCD框架下NNLO级QCD修正不稳定的根源，并提供了一种轻便的修正策略，有效提升了理论预测的可靠性及其与实验的匹配度。

Abstract: Next-to-next-to-leading order (NNLO) QCD corrections to quarkonium production and decay are known to exhibit perturbative instabilities within non-relativistic QCD. We identify the origin of this problem and propose a simple remedy. Applying our approach to $S$-wave color-singlet quarkonium processes, we achieve substantially improved perturbative convergence and agreement with experimental data.

### [147] [Polarization interference in exclusive $V+$jets at all orders in $α_s$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28496)
*Trina Basu,Richard Ruiz*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用中间螺旋度极化规范玻色子的螺旋度振幅新计算方法，重新研究了质子-质子对撞中$pp\to V+{\rm jets}$过程（$V=γ^*,Z^{(*)},W^{(*)}$衰变为无质量轻子）的横纵向极化干涉现象。研究表明，在强耦合常数$α_s$的各阶及喷注运动学独占条件下，$γ^*\to\ell^+\ell^-$的极化干涉在轻子相空间积分后消失，将已知的包容过程结果加以推广；而由于宇称破缺，$W$和$Z$玻色子的干涉抵消被弱化。文中还给出了唯象截断效应的简单公式，并讨论了该结果对多玻色子过程、新物理中的手征规范玻色子以及重离子碰撞中弱玻色子极化测量的意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献已证明包容过程中$\gamma^*$的横纵向极化干涉在轻子相空间积分后消失，但该结论是否适用于更一般的、包含喷注（jet）的独占性（exclusive）过程尚不明确。本文旨在填补这一空白，系统研究$pp\to V+{\rm jets}$过程中极化干涉的相空间积分行为，并分析宇称破缺对$W$和$Z$玻色子的影响。

Method: 采用中间螺旋度极化（helicity-polarized）规范玻色子的螺旋度振幅（helicity amplitude）新计算方法，对$pp\to V+{\rm jets}$过程（$V=γ^*,Z^{(*)},W^{(*)}$）在强耦合常数$α_s$各阶及喷注运动学独占条件下进行解析分析。通过对轻子$\ell^\pm$的相空间积分，检验极化干涉项的消除情况，并针对$W$和$Z$玻色子的宇称破缺效应给出修正公式。

Result: 对于$\gamma^*\to\ell^+\ell^-$，极化干涉在轻子相空间积分后严格消失，将包容过程的已知结果推广到了独占性喷注过程；由于弱相互作用中的宇称破缺（parity violation），$W$和$Z$玻色子的干涉抵消被显著弱化。此外，给出了一个考虑唯象截断（fiducial cuts）影响的简单公式。

Conclusion: 本文结果对多玻色子过程的分析具有直接启示，并可应用于新物理场景中手征规范玻色子（chiral gauge bosons）的研究，以及重离子碰撞（heavy ion collisions）中弱玻色子极化测量的精确建模。

Abstract: Using new methods for computing helicity amplitudes with intermediate helicity-polarized gauge bosons, we revisit the transverse-longitudinal polarization interference in the $pp\to V+{\rm jets}$ process for $V=γ^*,Z^{(*)},W^{(*)}$ decaying to massless leptons. At each order of the strong coupling constant $α_s$ and remaining exclusive with respect to jet kinematics, we show that the polarization interference in $γ^*\to\ell^+\ell^-$ vanishes after phase-space integration over the kinematics of $\ell^\pm$, thereby extending well-known results for the inclusive process. Due to parity violation, cancellations are softened for the $W$ and $Z$ bosons. We give a simple formula to account for fiducial cuts. We comment on the implications for multiboson processes, and the applicability of our results to chiral gauge bosons in new physics scenarios and to polarization measurements of weak bosons in heavy ion collisions.

### [148] [Defining a Minimum Resolution for Unbinned Analyses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28498)
*Manuel Szewc*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出最小分辨率似然（Minimum Resolution Likelihood, MRL）方法，通过定义基准信号区（Fiducial Signal Region）将对撞机分析中机器学习模型估计背景似然时产生的系统效应转化为统计不确定性，从而消除或减小信号强度估计中的偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在对撞机分析中，前沿机器学习模型被直接用于估计背景的似然函数（likelihood function），但由此引入的系统效应（systematic effects）难以量化，可能导致相关信号参数估计出现偏差。

Method: MRL方法定义了一个基准信号区（Fiducial Signal Region），通过该区域的构造将原本难以处理的系统效应有效转化为统计不确定性（statistical uncertainties），从而修正似然估计。

Result: 在玩具示例和基于HI-SIGMA技术的双希格斯粒子（di-Higgs）搜索实际应用中，MRL方法得到的信号强度估计要么无偏，要么与零一致（即无虚假信号）。

Conclusion: MRL方法能够有效解决机器学习模型直接用于背景似然估计时由系统效应导致的偏差问题，兼具理论可靠性与实际应用可行性。

Abstract: Collider analyses combine rigorous statistical techniques with state-of-the-art Machine Learning models. However, when the latter are used directly to estimate the likelihood function of the background, hard to quantify systematic effects may bias the estimation of the relevant signal parameters. To address this problem, we present the Minimum Resolution Likelihood (MRL) method, which defines a Fiducial Signal Region that effectively turns the systematic effects into statistical uncertainties. We show with examples that the resulting signal strength estimation is either unbiased or consistent with zero. We consider both toy examples and a realistic application based on the HI-SIGMA technique applied to di-Higgs searches.

### [149] [Searching for the $G(3900)$ via the $K^- p \to D_s^- Λ_c^+ G(3900)^0$ reaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29359)
*Qing Lu,Cai Cheng,Yin Huang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出通过反应 K⁻ p → Dₛ⁻ Λ_c⁺ G(3900)⁰ 来研究 G(3900) 结构，采用有效拉格朗日方法（effective Lagrangian approach）并考虑中心产生机制（central production mechanism）及 t 道 D⁰ 和 D*⁰ 交换，预测了总截面和角分布，认为未来实验可作为探测 G(3900) 是否为真实共振态（genuine resonance）的有力手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用有效拉格朗日方法（effective Lagrangian approach），假设反应经由中心产生机制（central production mechanism）进行，主要贡献来自 t 道 D⁰ 和 D*⁰ 交换。基于 G(3900) 可能为 P 波 D̅* D 分子态（molecular state）的解读，其对 D̅* D 道的耦合常数由先前对 e⁺e⁻ → D̅* D 数据的拟合确定。同时引入由坡密子（Pomeron）和雷吉子（Reggeon）交换介导的 K̅ N 初态相互作用。

Result: 初态相互作用显著增强了产生截面（production cross section）。预测了总截面和角分布。

Conclusion: 未来实验若能测量所预测的总截面和角分布，将有望揭示 G(3900) 的本质，尤其是判断其是否为真实的共振态（genuine resonance）。

Abstract: The nature of the $G(3900)$ structure, observed in $e^{+}e^{-}\to D\bar{D}$, remains unclear and may stem either from a genuine resonance or from charmonium interference and threshold effects. We therefore propose searching for the $G(3900)$ signal in the reaction $K^- p \to D_s^- Λ_c^+ G(3900)^0$, where the interference effects present in $e^{+}e^{-}\to \bar{D}^{*}D$ are absent. We employ an effective Lagrangian approach, where the reaction proceeds via a central production mechanism dominated by $t$-channel $D^{0}$ and $D^{*0}$ exchanges, based on the possible interpretation of $G(3900)$ as a $P$-wave $\bar{D}^{*}D$ molecular state, whose coupling to the $\bar{D}^{*}D$ channel is fixed from our previous fit to the $e^{+}e^{-}\to \bar{D}^{*}D$ data. The $\bar{K}N$ initial-state interaction, mediated by Pomeron and Reggeon exchanges, is also included and leads to a significant enhancement of the production cross section. If measured in future experiments, the predicted total cross sections and angular distributions can provide a promising probe of the nature of the $G(3900)$, and in particular of its possible genuine resonance nature.

### [151] [Soft-Radiation-Induced Decoherence of Heavy-Quark Spin Entanglement at the Electron-Ion Collider](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29944)
*Sanskriti Agrawal,Muneeb Zahoor,Raktim Abir*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文利用软胶子定理（soft-gluon theorem）识别出一种“软反冲机制”（soft-recoil mechanism），证明未分辨的软胶子辐射会诱导重夸克-反夸克对（heavy quark-antiquark pair）自旋关联（spin correlations）的退相干（decoherence），并提出了可在电子-离子对撞机（EIC）上测量的辐射分箱观测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解深度非弹性散射（deep-inelastic scattering）中未分辨胶子辐射如何影响重夸克-反夸克对的自旋关联退相干，并寻找可在实验上探测该效应的可测观测量。

Method: 基于软胶子定理，将软辐射贡献分解为领头阶的eikonal项（保持Born自旋结构不变）和次领头阶的软项（引起自旋关联平面的随机反冲旋转），通过对未分辨胶子求迹（tracing over unresolved gluon）得到退相位（dephasing）有效动力学。

Result: 发现法向关联在次领头阶保持不变，而面内自旋相干（in-plane spin coherences）受到抑制。估算了Concurrence和Bell-CHSH不等式违背的降低量，并提出了基于面内与法向自旋关联比值的辐射分箱观测量。

Conclusion: 该观测量能够隔离软反冲机制所预言的特征性非各向同性自旋抑制，为在EIC上探测辐射诱导的纠缠夸克-反夸克对自旋退相干提供了可测量的实验手段。

Abstract: Using the soft-gluon theorem, we identify a soft-recoil mechanism by which unresolved gluon radiation induces decoherence in the spin correlations of heavy quark-antiquark pairs produced in deep-inelastic scattering. We show the eikonal soft contribution preserves the Born spin structure, whereas the subleading soft term generates stochastic recoil-induced rotations of the spin-correlation plane. Upon tracing over the unresolved gluon, these rotations produce an effective dephasing channel: the normal-axis correlation remains unchanged at this order, while the in-plane spin coherences are suppressed. We estimate the resulting reduction of concurrence and Bell-CHSH violation, and propose a radiation-binned EIC observable based on the ratio of in-plane to normal spin correlations. This observable isolates the characteristic anisotropic suppression predicted by the soft-recoil mechanism and provides a measurable handle on radiation-induced spin decoherence of an entangled quark-antiquark pair produced in a deep-inelastic scattering process.

### [152] [Feasibility study of light sterile neutrino searches with a future NINJA-like detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30135)
*Doris Barčot,Tsutomu Fukuda,Monojit Ghosh,Leon Halić,Mahesh Jakkapu,Teppei Katori,Budimir Kliček,Masahiro Komatsu,Tomokazu Matsuo,Osamu Sato,Atsumu Suzuki*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文对J-PARC未来NINJA类实验在3+1框架下探测eV尺度惰性中微子（sterile neutrino）的灵敏度进行了现象学可行性研究，分析了不同楼层探测器配置（B2、SS、GROUND）及多种分析条件对活性-惰性混合参数约束能力的影响，结果表明SS楼层配置提供最强的约束，NINJA类探测器有望在未来的运行中对轻惰性中微子场景给出有竞争力的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有中微子振荡实验存在超出标准三味框架的异常迹象，而eV尺度的惰性中微子（sterile neutrino）是可能的扩展解释之一。本文旨在评估未来NINJA类实验在J-PARC下对3+1框架中惰性中微子的探测灵敏度，为实验优化提供依据。

Method: 基于3+1框架，对NINJA类实验进行现象学可行性研究，使用ν_μ→ν_e出现通道（appearance channel）以及ν_μ→ν_μ和ν_e→ν_e消失通道（disappearance channel）。考虑探测器位于NM大楼不同楼层（B2、SS、GROUND）对应不同离轴角（off-axis angle）的未来配置，采用简化的有效探测器响应，将事件分类为电子类（electron-like）和缪子类（muon-like）拓扑并施加恒定基准选择效率。探索不同曝光场景，评估上界能量截断（upper energy cut）等分析选择的影响，纳入信号与背景率归一化的系统不确定性，检验能量分辨率变化和关键背景（如带电电流和中性电流相互作用的缪子误识别）效率变化的鲁棒性，并考察多探测器位置数据联合的效果。

Result: SS楼层配置对活性-惰性混合参数（active-sterile mixing parameters）提供最强的约束；B2和GROUND配置对于探测的质量平方差（mass-squared differences）提供与当前现有界限相当的约束。NINJA类探测器在优化的统计量和基准识别性能下，有望在未来运行中提供具有竞争力的轻惰性中微子约束。

Conclusion: NINJA类探测器具备探测eV尺度惰性中微子的潜力，其中SS楼层配置最为有利。通过优化统计量和识别性能，该实验能够在未来对3+1框架下的轻惰性中微子场景给出有竞争力的限制。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the sensitivity of future NINJA-like experiment at J-PARC to eV-scale sterile neutrinos within the 3+1 framework. We perform a phenomenological feasibility study using the $ν_μ\rightarrow ν_e$ appearance, $ν_μ\rightarrow ν_μ$ and $ν_e \rightarrow ν_e$ disappearance channels, focusing on possible future configurations of the detector located at different floors of the NM building (B2, SS, and GROUND), corresponding to different off-axis angles. Our analysis is based on a simplified and effective detector response, in which events are classified into electron-like and muon-like topologies and constant benchmark selection efficiencies are applied. We explore different exposure scenarios and assess the impact of analysis choices such as upper energy cuts. We include systematic uncertainties corresponding to normalization for signal and background rates and study the robustness of our results with respect to variations in the assumed energy resolution, and vary efficiencies for key backgrounds such as muon misidentification from charge current and neutral current interactions. Finally, we examine the effects of combining data from multiple detector locations. We find that the SS floor provides the strongest constraints on the active-sterile mixing parameters, while the B2 and GROUND configurations offer constraints comparable to the current bounds for probed mass-squared differences. Our results indicate that a NINJA-like detector, optimized for sufficient statistics and benchmark identification performance, has the potential to provide competitive constraints on light sterile neutrino scenarios in its future runs.

### [153] [A directional force template for quadratically coupled ultralight dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28491)
*Dawid Brzeminski,Aaron Pierce*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对超轻标量暗物质与标准模型粒子之间的二次耦合（quadratic coupling）在地球附近产生的非径向各向异性力，开发了适用于MICROSCOPE卫星的多极信号模板，并利用该模板重新分析了现有数据，发现如果利用非重叠信号分量，可将对该类暗物质的耦合灵敏度提升超过一个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将诱导力分解为径向（radial）多极系数和极向（polar）多极系数，并将该力投影到MICROSCOPE卫星的测量轴上，从而构建出适用于各向异性情形的信号模板。利用该模板，通过仅保留与径向力模板重叠的信号分量，重新解读（recast）已发表的MICROSCOPE约束。

Result: 估计了利用额外的非重叠信号分量所能获得的灵敏度增益。对于质量 $\gtrsim 10^{-9}$ eV 的暗物质，若采用包含非重叠信号的全部分析，可将对二次耦合标量暗物质的耦合灵敏度相比仅用径向力模板重新解读的结果提升一个数量级以上。

Conclusion: 本文提出的多极信号模板能够更充分地利用MICROSCOPE卫星的数据，从而显著提升对超轻标量暗物质二次耦合的探测灵敏度，表明现有空间实验数据中可能隐藏着更强的暗物质约束能力。

Abstract: Quadratic couplings between ultralight scalar dark matter and Standard Model fields can produce a distorted dark-matter field profile around the Earth. Gradients in the field induce a non-radial, composition-dependent force that can be suppressed at the Earth's surface while remaining accessible to space-based experiments. The MICROSCOPE satellite, which searched for violations of the equivalence principle, can constrain this force, but existing results assume a radial force, and they cannot be directly translated into an optimal bound in the anisotropic regime. We develop a signal template for this regime by organizing the force into radial and polar multipole coefficients and projecting the force onto the MICROSCOPE measurement axis. We use this template to recast the published MICROSCOPE constraint using the component of the signal that overlaps with the radial-force template. We estimate the sensitivity gain that would be provided by an analysis utilizing the additional non-overlapping signal. Such an analysis could improve sensitivity to the couplings of quadratically coupled scalar dark matter by more than an order of magnitude relative to the radial-force recast for dark matter masses $\gtrsim 10^{-9}$ eV.

### [154] [Analytic two-loop electroweak corrections at high energies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28880)
*Hantian Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文总结了标准模型（Standard Model）中双圈四点电弱振幅（two-loop four-point electroweak amplitudes）在解析高能计算方面的最新进展，并以希格斯玻色子对产生（Higgs boson pair production）为例，展示了电弱修正（electroweak corrections）中丰富的对数修正（logarithmic corrections）和幂次修正（power corrections）结构及其在高能区的重要效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电弱散射振幅（electroweak scattering amplitudes）的高能行为具有重要的理论价值与唯象学（phenomenological）意义，因此需要对其在高能区进行精确的解析计算。

Method: 采用解析高能计算方法，对标准模型下双圈四点电弱振幅进行理论计算与分析。

Result: 在希格斯玻色子对产生过程中，识别出丰富的对数修正和幂次修正结构，并在高能区发现显著的修正效应。

Conclusion: 双圈电弱振幅的高能解析计算取得了重要进展，这些修正对于理解高能区的电弱相互作用具有重要影响。

Abstract: The high-energy behaviour of electroweak scattering amplitudes is of theoretical and phenomenological interest. In these proceedings, we summarize recent progress in analytic high-energy calculations for two-loop four-point electroweak amplitudes in the full Standard Model. As a representative application, we discuss the electroweak corrections to Higgs boson pair production, where rich structures of logarithmic and power corrections appear and sizeable effects are found in the high-energy region.

### [155] [Equilibrium Statistics as Conditional Laws and Conservation-Induced Correlations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29050)
*Sunil Jaiswal,Amaresh Jaiswal*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 提出了一个用于相对论系统的统一条件概率框架，通过对加法守恒律（additive conservation laws）进行条件限制，同时导出平衡占据统计（equilibrium occupation statistics）与守恒诱导关联（conservation-induced correlations）。该框架将平衡态视为封闭系统的条件极限律，并通过鞍点展开得到麦克斯韦-玻尔兹曼、玻色-爱因斯坦和费米-狄拉克统计，利用高斯展开得到有限秩守恒协方差。进一步定义了与选定守恒量正交的投影可观测量（projected observables），可剔除守恒贡献，并通过PYTHIA8/Angantyr生成的p+Pb碰撞数据进行了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的相对论系统统计描述中，平衡统计与守恒律诱导的关联效应通常被分开处理，缺乏统一的理论框架。特别是在小碰撞系统（small collision systems）中，守恒效应对长程关联（long-range correlations）的贡献不可忽略，但缺少系统性的方法将其与其他来源（如非流效应）分离。

Method: 构建一个统一的相对论系统条件概率框架，基于对加法守恒律的条件限制，以鞍点展开（saddle order）获得单模边缘分布（one-mode marginal），以高斯展开（Gaussian order）获得双模边缘分布（two-mode marginal）的有限秩协方差。通过定义与选定守恒量正交的投影可观测量，构造保守量正交协方差，从而剔除守恒贡献。

Result: 在鞍点阶，单模边缘分布分别恢复麦克斯韦-玻尔兹曼、玻色-爱因斯坦和费米-狄拉克统计，其中守恒量决定指数倾斜（exponential tilt），微观占据测度（microscopic occupation measure）决定统计类型。双模边缘分布的高斯展开给出精确守恒诱导的有限秩协方差。投影可观测量构造的协方差在领头阶不含守恒贡献。在PYTHIA8/Angantyr生成的p+Pb事件中，投影操作去除了守恒对齐贡献，而守恒正交协方差基本不变。

Conclusion: 该框架为相对论系统中平衡统计与守恒诱导关联提供了统一的理论基础。在小碰撞系统中，投影可观测量方法能有效分离守恒对齐的长程关联贡献，为实验数据分析提供了新的工具。

Abstract: We present a novel unified conditional-probability framework for relativistic systems in which conditioning on additive conservation laws simultaneously yields equilibrium occupation statistics and conservation-induced correlations. In this formulation, equilibrium arises as a conditional limit law of a closed system. The one-mode marginal gives Maxwell--Boltzmann, Bose--Einstein, and Fermi--Dirac statistics at leading saddle order, with the conserved quantities fixing the exponential tilt and the microscopic occupation measure determining the statistics. Expanding the two-mode marginal to Gaussian order gives the leading finite-rank covariance between modes induced by exact conservation. When contracted with observables linear in mode occupations, this covariance gives their leading exact-conservation contribution. We use this structure to define projected observables orthogonal to selected conserved quantities. By construction, their covariance has no leading exact-conservation contribution. In small collision systems, where conservation effects are less suppressed by multiplicity and can survive standard nonflow suppressions, this provides a direct way to isolate conservation-aligned contributions to long-range correlations. We demonstrate this with PYTHIA8/Angantyr-generated p+Pb events at $\sqrt{s_{\mathrm{NN}}}=5.02~\mathrm{TeV}$ by comparing ordinary and projected covariances, showing that the projection removes the conservation-aligned contribution while leaving the conservation-orthogonal covariance essentially unchanged.

</details>


### [156] [Size Dependence of the Sommerfeld Enhancement for Puffy Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29710)
*Wu-Long Xu,Jin Min Yang,Wen-Na Yang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了膨胀暗物质（puffy dark matter）湮灭过程中索末菲增强因子（Sommerfeld enhancement factor）的尺度效应。通过分波法（partial-wave method）分析无内部结构的电荷密度分布情况，发现两个无量纲参数可表征共振结构；进一步以金块型暗物质（nugget-type dark matter）为例，展示了其索末菲增强的共振行为与点状粒子类似，并指出有限尺寸是除低速外影响增强的又一基本因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在传统点状暗物质模型中，索末菲增强已被广泛研究，但现实中暗物质可能具有有限空间延展（即“膨胀暗物质”），其有限尺寸对湮灭率的影响尚缺乏系统性分析。作者旨在厘清暗物质非点状结构如何改变索末菲增强的共振特性，并识别影响增强因子的关键参数。

Method: 采用分波法（partial-wave method）研究膨胀暗物质，仅给定电荷密度分布而无需指定内部具体结构。引入两个无量纲参数对索末菲增强的共振结构进行分类与表征。随后以具有非平凡内部结构的金块型暗物质（nugget-type dark matter）为例进行具体分析。

Result: 两个无量纲参数能够有效刻画索末菲增强的共振结构。暗物质粒子的有限尺寸是除低速度（low velocity）之外另一个影响索末菲增强的基本因素。金块型暗物质的索末菲增强因子表现出与点状粒子相似的共振行为。

Conclusion: 膨胀暗物质的有限尺寸会显著改变索末菲增强，因此在对暗物质湮灭进行精确建模时，必须将暗物质粒子的空间延展纳入考量。该工作为更广泛类型膨胀暗物质的增强因子计算提供了统一框架。

Abstract: We examine the size effects in the Sommerfeld enhancement factor for puffy dark matter annihilation. First, we use the partial-wave method to study the case of puffy dark matter for which only a charge density distribution is given without specifying its internal structure. We find that by using two dimensionless parameters, we can provide a characterization of the resonance structure of the Sommerfeld enhancement. Using this approach, we demonstrate that the finite size of dark matter particle is another fundamental factor, in addition to low velocity, that affects the Sommerfeld enhancement. Then, as an example of puffy dark matter with nontrivial internal structures, we perform the analysis for the nugget-type dark matter, whose Sommerfeld enhancement factor is found to exhibit a resonant behavior similar to that of point-like particles.

</details>
