### [157] [Comment on "Fundamental limit of phonon Tesla valve for heat rectification from first principles"](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28407)
*Samuel Huberman,Aleksei Sokolov*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文对一篇声称发现热整流（thermal rectification）现象的研究提出质疑，指出在固定背景的线性化玻尔兹曼输运方程（linearized phonon Boltzmann transport equation, BTE）框架下，任何满足平衡温度平移不变性和适定边值问题的被动两端储热器问题，其正向与反向电阻必然相等，从而否定了该工作中所报告的整流比（rectification ratio）作为双端热整流的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在批判性地审视参考文献中报告的热整流比γ = R_f / R_b是否能够代表真正的双端（two-terminal）热整流效应，纠正该研究在物理框架理解上的混淆。

Method: 作者基于线性化声子玻尔兹曼输运方程（linearized phonon BTE）的基本性质进行理论分析，考察散射算符（scattering operator）是否保持均匀平衡温度平移（uniform equilibrium temperature shift），以及边值问题（boundary-value problem）是否适定（well posed），从而推导正向和反向电阻的对称性。

Result: 在被动两端储热器（passive two-terminal reservoir）问题中，任何满足散射算符保持均匀平衡温度平移且边值问题适定的固定线性化BTE，都会给出相等的正向和反向电阻（forward and reverse resistance）。该工作报告的定向依赖性仅源于其所施加的梯度加权源-汇方案（gradient-weighted source–sink protocol），而非真正的双端热整流。

Conclusion: 参考文献中报告的整流比并非真正的双端热整流，而是源于特定边界协议下的人为响应；研究者应严格区分此类方向依赖性响应与真正的热整流效应。

Abstract: Thermal rectification is a two-terminal property: the same device must carry different heat-current magnitudes when two reservoir temperatures are interchanged. In this Comment on Ref.~\cite{WuHu2026}, we ask whether the reported ratio $γ=R_{\mathrm{f}}/R_{\mathrm{b}}$ can represent such a two-terminal rectification ratio within the fixed-background linearized phonon Boltzmann transport equation (BTE) used in that work. We show that, for a passive two-terminal reservoir problem, any fixed linearized BTE whose scattering operator preserves a uniform equilibrium temperature shift, and whose boundary-value problem is well posed, gives equal forward and reverse resistance magnitudes. A direction-dependent response can still occur under a prescribed gradient-weighted source--sink protocol, but such a response should be distinguished from two-terminal thermal rectification.

</details>


### [158] [Comparison of different exact generalized Langevin equations with a non-linear potential of mean force and an observable-dependent mass and friction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28426)
*Benjamin J. A. Héry,Lucas Tepper,Roland R. Netz*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文基于Mori-Zwanzig投影形式体系（Mori-Zwanzig projection formalism），系统分析了标量可观测量（scalar observable）的四种广义朗之万方程（generalized Langevin equations, GLEs）的性质，指出它们在记忆摩擦核（memory friction kernel）与势能项（potential）上的差异，并阐明了将有效动能纳入势能项的优势条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为任意可观测量推导出基于广义朗之万方程（GLEs）的运动方程，并分析不同GLE形式之间的结构差异与适用条件。

Method: 采用Mori-Zwanzig投影形式体系（Mori-Zwanzig projection formalism），利用演化算符（evolution operator）和投影算符（projection operator），对标量可观测量（scalar observable）推导出四种不同的广义朗之万方程（GLEs），并比较记忆摩擦核（memory friction kernel）和势能项（potential）的依赖关系。

Result: 四种GLE均精确成立，但在记忆摩擦核是否依赖于可观测量（observable-dependent）以及势能项是否包含可观测量有效动能（effective kinetic energy）上存在区别。

Conclusion: 当可观测量的速度满足Wick定理（Wick's theorem）时，将有效动能纳入势能项具有优势，因为即使忽略摩擦力项和正交力项（orthogonal force），也能正确重现可观测量及其速度的分布。

Abstract: The Mori-Zwanzig projection formalism constitutes a powerful and robust framework for deriving equations of motion in terms of generalized Langevin equations (GLEs) for an arbitrary observable using evolution and projection operators. Based on this framework, we analyze the properties of four distinct GLEs for a scalar observable including a Markovian force derived from a generally non-linear potential, a non-Markovian friction force, and an orthogonal force, commonly interpreted as a random force. While all four GLEs are exact, they differ in the memory friction kernel, which may either be dependent or independent of the observable, and by the potential, which may either include or exclude the effective kinetic energy of the observable. Inclusion of the kinetic energy in the potential is advantageous for observables whose velocity satisfies Wick's theorem, since this reproduces the correct distribution of the observable and its velocity even without contributions from the friction force and the orthogonal force.

</details>


### [159] [Ultrafast directed transport via energy recuperation in non-Markovian systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28567)
*Mateusz WIśniewski,Jakub Spiechowicz*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文证明能量回收（energy recuperation）是非马尔可夫系统（non-Markovian systems）的普遍特征，即使是无外力驱动的自由布朗粒子（free Brownian particle）或仅由惯性（inertia）引起的强阻尼体系也能实现。该机制是记忆诱导超快定向输运（memory-induced ultrafast directed transport）的根源，并可能从根本解释生物细胞内胞质溶胶（cytosol）的黏弹性（viscoelasticity）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于近期实验[Nat. Commun. 16, 10114 (2025)]证明黏弹性流体（viscoelastic fluid）中受驱过阻尼胶体粒子可回收耗散能量，本文旨在将这一预言大幅推广，探究能量回收现象是否具有普适性。

Method: 通过理论分析和/或数值模拟，从非马尔可夫动力学（non-Markovian dynamics）出发，考察无外力自由布朗粒子、纯惯性效应（即使处于强阻尼 regime）等更简单体系中的能量回收行为。

Result: 能量回收是非马尔可夫系统的通用特征，在平衡态（equilibrium）与非平衡态（out of equilibrium）下均成立；惯性本身（无需外驱）即可在强阻尼下产生该效应；该机制是周期势（periodic potential）中记忆诱导超快定向输运的根源，粒子速度几乎达到无势垒系统的极限速度。

Conclusion: 能量回收可能在自然界中普遍存在，可能是具有记忆（memory）的各种现象的基本运作方式；该结果可能从根本上回答为何生物细胞内的胞质溶胶（cytosol）是黏弹性的。

Abstract: A recent pioneering experiment [Nat. Commun. 16, 10114 (2025)] demonstrated that a driven overdamped colloidal particle in a harmonic trap immersed in a viscoelastic fluid can recuperate energy dissipated into the surrounding bath and convert it into useful work. In this article we considerably extend the original predictions. In particular, we show that energy recuperation is a generic feature of non-Markovian systems both in and out of equilibrium, even as simple as a free Brownian particle. Moreover, we demonstrate that inertia alone, even in the strong damping regime, can lead to this effect despite the absence of any external forcing. These results suggest that energy recuperation can be ubiquitous in nature and it may be the modus operandi of various phenomena in setups with memory. We show that this novel mechanism of energy recovery is the source of memory-induced ultrafast directed transport of a particle in a periodic potential in which it almost attains its top speed corresponding to the system with no energy barriers. Our results may answer from the fundamental point of view the question why the cytosol, the intracellular fluid in biological cells, is viscoelastic.

</details>


### [160] [Phase Time Crystals and Pairing in Binary Active Chiral Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28653)
*C. Reichhardt,C. J. O. Reichhardt*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一类称为“相位时间晶体（phase time crystal）”的动态系统，由两类具有中程或长程排斥相互作用的粒子构成，在均匀手性（uniform chirality）的圆形驱动下，两粒子种类相位相差180度。系统可自组织形成多种动态晶体态，包括三角晶格配对联、条纹相、重叠堆积晶体、无序相玻璃态等，且这些状态对热涨落具有鲁棒性。通过改变驱动手性，可实现包括动态方自旋冰几何结构在内的多种活性分子晶格。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索由两类受圆驱动粒子组成的非平衡动态系统中，粒子间排斥相互作用与手性驱动耦合所产生的新型自组织行为与动态结晶现象。

Method: 设计了一类由两种粒子种类组成的二元组装体系，粒子间存在中程或长程排斥相互作用，施加均匀手性的圆形驱动，且两粒子种类相位相差180度。通过改变粒子密度和轨道半径等参数，系统性地研究了其自组织行为。

Result: 发现系统可形成丰富的动态晶体态：包括配对联组成三角晶格的配对晶体、条纹相、重叠堆积晶体、无扩散的无序相或相玻璃态（phase glass state）、混合流体及多种相分离态。这些状态对热涨落具有鲁棒性，配对晶体可熔化为配对流体。改变驱动手性后，系统形成条纹和堆积晶格，但无配对晶体。通过调节手性驱动性质，可实现动态方自旋冰几何结构及更高阶复杂结构。

Conclusion: 系统在手性驱动和排斥相互作用下展现出丰富的动态自组织行为，且可通过调控驱动参数实现对多种活性分子晶格的灵活构建，为非平衡态物质组织提供了新途径。

Abstract: We introduce a class of dynamic systems we call phase time crystals consisting of a binary assembly of particles with intermediate or long-range repulsive interactions that are subjected to a circular drive of uniform chirality in which each particle species is out of phase from the other by 180 degrees. As a function of the particle density and orbit radius, this system can organize into a rich variety of dynamical crystalline states, including one in which the out of phase particles form bound pairs that assemble into a triangular lattice. We also find stripe phases, overlapping packed crystals, disordered or phase glass states with no diffusion, mixed fluids, and different types of phase-separated states. We show that these states are robust against the addition of thermal fluctuations, and that the paired crystal can melt into a paired fluid. If the drive on each particle species is of opposite chirality, the system forms stripes and packed lattices, but no paired crystal is present. We demonstrate that by modifying the nature of the chiral driving, it is possible to realize numerous kinds of active molecular lattices, including dynamic square spin ice geometries and higher-order complex structures.

</details>


### [161] [Forward-backward correspondence between stationary structure and splitting probabilities in active matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28709)
*Derek Frydel*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文揭示了受限活性物质中稳态分布与首次通过概率之间的精确对偶关系，具体表现为壁分裂概率（wall splitting probability）的空间导数生成稳态密度，这一关系在任意空间维度下对三类典型活性粒子模型（run-and-tumble、active Brownian、active Ornstein–Uhlenbeck）均成立，从而建立了稳态描述与首次通过描述之间的桥梁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 活性粒子在硬壁约束下会因方向持续性（directional persistence）在边界累积并发生动态吸附，但以往研究主要关注边界吸附本身，缺乏对壁分裂概率这一“粒子能否到达对侧边界”问题的理论理解，更忽略了稳态分布与首次通过（first-passage）描述之间的内在联系。

Method: 直接在位置-速度相空间（position-velocity phase space）中对比前向和后向演化方程，推导出稳态分布与分裂概率之间的精确关系；该方法对run-and-tumble、active Brownian、active Ornstein–Uhlenbeck三种活性粒子模型统一适用，且不限制空间维度。

Result: 稳态密度由分裂概率的空间导数生成；壁动态吸附粒子的分布由壁分裂概率编码；该对应关系在任意空间维度下均成立，揭示了稳态与首次通过描述是同一持续性驱动的动力学（persistence-driven dynamics）的互补表示。

Conclusion: 该工作为受限活性物质的稳态性质与首次通过性质之间建立了严格的解析桥梁，表明边界分裂概率及其空间导数可以完整地刻画系统的稳态结构，为理解和预测活性物质在受限环境中的输运行为提供了统一的理论框架。

Abstract: Active particles confined by hard walls accumulate at boundaries and may become dynamically adsorbed due to directional persistence. In this work, we show that the same persistence mechanism also gives rise to a finite wall splitting probability, meaning that a particle initialized at a wall can reach the opposite boundary before returning to its starting point. By comparing forward and backward evolution equations directly in position--velocity phase space, we derive exact relations linking stationary distributions and splitting probabilities for run-and-tumble, active Brownian, and active Ornstein--Uhlenbeck particles. In particular, we show that the stationary density is generated by the spatial derivative of the splitting probability, while the distribution of dynamically adsorbed particles at the walls is encoded in wall splitting probabilities. The correspondence is valid in arbitrary spatial dimension and establishes an exact bridge between stationary and first-passage descriptions of confined active matter, revealing them as complementary representations of the same persistence-driven dynamics.

</details>


### [162] [Finite-resolution exhaustive traversal of thermodynamic state spaces has divergent thermodynamic length](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29751)
*Satori Tsuzuki*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文将通过曲线在d维热力学状态空间（thermodynamic state-space）中实现ε-密集覆盖所需的代价，建立热力学覆盖的操作性资源律，并推导出摩擦张量（friction tensor）与覆盖度量（coverage metric）之间的关系，最终给出在固定耗散预算下所需热化时间或扫描速率的标度律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 连续空间填充映射可以满射到高维区域，但热力学协议（thermodynamic protocols）是可通过有限分辨率路径实现的。本文试图将经典几何估计转化为热力学覆盖的操作性资源律，以量化在有限精度下遍历高维状态空间所需的最小代价。

Method: 利用标准覆盖/管道估计给出曲线长度的下界；通过柯西-施瓦茨不等式（Cauchy--Schwarz inequality）将摩擦张量与度量张量关联，推导二次过功（quadratic excess work）的下界；对详细平衡三态马尔可夫跳变过程（Markov jump process）和过阻尼谐振阱（overdamped harmonic trap）推导微观摩擦度量；使用栅格扫描（raster scan）和Morton/Z-order曲线分析代价标度。

Result: 对于d>1的正则窗口，曲线长度下界为L_g≥C_g ε^{1-d}-O(ε)；固定二次过功预算下维持慢驱动需要τ=Ω(ε^{2(1-d)})；在过阻尼谐振阱中，栅格扫描给出L_ζ~Δ_g^{-1}和固定时间W_ex^{(2)}~Δ_g^{-2}；实验室或模拟截断消除了连续发散，有L_op=Θ(max{ε,Δ_g}^{1-d})。

Conclusion: Morton/Z-order保持标度指数但增加局域性依赖的振幅；受控的奇异性响应代理度量可诊断临界前因子和方向可积性，但除非从微观动力学导出，否则不是物理摩擦张量。

Abstract: Continuous space-filling maps can be surjective onto higher-dimensional regions, but thermodynamic protocols are rectifiable finite-resolution paths. We study exhaustive traversal of a compact $d$-dimensional thermodynamic state-space window $(\mathcal{M},g)$ by curves $H_\varepsilon$ whose images are $\varepsilon$-dense in intrinsic distance. A standard covering/tube estimate gives $L_g[H_\varepsilon]\ge C_g\varepsilon^{1-d}-O(\varepsilon)$ for every regular $d>1$ window. The geometry is classical; the contribution is to turn it into an operational resource law for thermodynamic coverage. When the physical friction tensor $ζ$ coincides with, or uniformly dominates, the coverage metric $g$, Cauchy--Schwarz for the quadratic slow-driving action gives $W_{\rm ex}^{(2)}\ge L_ζ^2/τ=Ω(\varepsilon^{2(1-d)}/τ)$. Equivalently, at fixed quadratic excess-work budget, maintaining slow driving requires $τ=Ω(\varepsilon^{2(1-d)})$. We derive microscopic friction metrics for a detailed-balance three-state Markov jump process, $ζ_{ij}=(β/γ)(π_iδ_{ij}-π_iπ_j)$, and for an overdamped harmonic trap, $\mathrm d\ell_ζ^2=μ^{-1}\mathrm da^2+(4βμk^3)^{-1}\mathrm dk^2$. In the trap, a raster scan gives $L_ζ\simΔ_g^{-1}$ and fixed-time $W_{\rm ex}^{(2)}\simΔ_g^{-2}$, while fixed dwell time shifts the cost to acquisition time. A laboratory or simulation floor cuts off the continuum divergence as $L_{\rm op}=Θ(\max\{\varepsilon,Δ_g\}^{1-d})$. Controlled singular response-proxy metrics diagnose critical prefactors and directional integrability, but are not physical friction tensors unless derived from microscopic dynamics. Morton/Z-order preserves the exponent while increasing locality-dependent amplitudes.

</details>


### [163] [Reply to Comment on "Scaling and universality at noisy quench dynamical quantum phase transitions"](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28892)
*S. Ansari,R. Jafari,A. Akbari,M. Abdi*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文是针对Sirker评论的回应，澄清了在噪声和混合态动力学中，两种不同的Loschmidt回波扩展方式（Uhlmann-Bures保真度 vs 操作定义的噪声平均激发概率协议）对应不同的物理可观测量，因此关于动力学量子相变（DQPT）的结论并不矛盾。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: J. Sirker的评论指出，在噪声和混合态动力学中，Loschmidt回波从纯态到混合态的扩展并非唯一，不同扩展方式保留了不同的物理性质。该论文旨在回应这一评论，澄清其原始工作中定义的可观测量与评论所讨论的混合态保真度（mixed-state fidelity）之间的本质区别，并表明两者之间不存在直接矛盾。

Method: 论文通过区分两种不同的Loschmidt回波扩展方式进行分析：其一是评论中使用的基于噪声平均密度矩阵的Uhlmann-Bures保真度（Uhlmann-Bures fidelity）；其二是原始工作中定义的操作量——先确定噪声斜坡过程中产生的噪声平均激发概率，再对这些噪声平均跃迁概率构造的纯态进行相干斜坡后演化，取对数得到Loschmidt回波。论文强调后者是基于操作假设（operational assumption）定义的，并非混合态保真度。

Result: 评论的结论——当通过Uhlmann-Bures保真度定义返回率时，任何非零噪声下DQPT均不会出现——对于其所讨论的混合态保真度可观测量是成立的，并与先前研究一致。而原始论文中报道的非解析性（nonanalyticities）涉及的是两阶段操作协议（two-stage operational protocol），不应等同于Uhlmann-Bures保真度的零点。

Conclusion: 为Uhlmann-Bures返回率建立的定理与原始论文中针对不同操作协议得出的结论之间不存在直接矛盾。两种扩展方式对应不同的物理可观测量，各自的结论在其适用范围内均有效。

Abstract: The Comment by J. Sirker [arXiv:2511.16509] raises an important issue concerning dynamical quantum phase transitions (DQPTs) in noisy and mixed-state dynamics, namely that the extension of the Loschmidt echo from pure to mixed states is not unique and different extensions preserve different physical properties. The Comment examines a noise-averaged mixed-state fidelity and shows that DQPTs cannot occur for any nonzero noise when the return rate is defined through the Uhlmann-Bures fidelity of the noise-averaged density matrix. This conclusion is valid for the mixed-state fidelity observable discussed in the Comment and is consistent with prior studies [https://doi.org/10.1103/PhysRevB.109.L180303, arXiv:2504.03005]. Our article [https://doi.org/10.1103/mkll-nd46] investigated a different operationally defined quantity: the logarithm of the Loschmidt echo obtained by first determining the noise-averaged excitation probabilities generated during the noisy ramp and then performing a coherent post-ramp evolution of a pure state constructed from these noise-averaged transition probabilities. As emphasized explicitly in our original publication, this observable is defined through an operational assumption and is not the same quantity as the mixed-state fidelity. The nonanalyticities reported in Ref. [https://doi.org/10.1103/mkll-nd46] therefore concern this two-stage operational protocol and should not be identified with zeros of the Uhlmann-Bures fidelity. There is therefore no direct contradiction between the theorem established for the Uhlmann-Bures return rate and the conclusions obtained for the different operational protocol studied in Ref. [https://doi.org/10.1103/mkll-nd46].

</details>


### [164] [Pseudo entropy and topological phases of matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29311)
*Pramod Kamal Kharel,Manghang Limbu,Nabaraj Khatri,Ashish Khanal,Kiran Adhikari*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文发现伪熵（pseudo entropy）可作为区分拓扑相（topological phases）的新型探针，以Su–Schrieffer–Heeger模型为例，通过分析平均过剩熵在拓扑相变中的行为，揭示了伪熵在相同相中的非正性以及虚部伪熵对临界时间的追踪能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）已被证实可有效探测量子混沌和相变等现象；伪熵（pseudo entropy）作为最近提出的类时间推广，其应用潜力尚待发掘。本文旨在探索伪熵是否也能作为区分拓扑物质相（topological phases of matter）的新型探针。

Method: 以Su–Schrieffer–Heeger模型为代表示例，定义并计算平均过剩熵ΔS₁₂（伪熵与平均纠缠熵之差），研究其在拓扑到平庸（topological-to-trivial）和平庸到拓扑（trivial-to-topological）相变中的行为。同时分析基态淬火（ground-state quench）协议下的拓扑穿越淬火（topology-crossing quenches）过程。

Result: 当两个态处于同一相时，在周期性边界条件下ΔS₁₂非正；在开边界条件下，仅当系统足够大时ΔS₁₂才非正。此外，拓扑穿越淬火中，虚部伪熵（imaginary pseudo entropy）能够追踪由Fisher零点（Fisher zeros）预测的临界时间。

Conclusion: 伪熵可以作为区分拓扑相的有效探针，其行为在边界条件与系统尺寸影响下呈现出清晰的相变特征，并为理解拓扑淬火动力学提供了新视角。

Abstract: Entanglement entropy has proven to be a powerful probe of phenomena such as quantum chaos and phase transitions. Pseudo entropy is a recently proposed time-like generalization of an entanglement measure, motivated by de Sitter holography. In this work, we find that pseudo entropy can also serve as a novel probe for distinguishing topological phases of matter. For this, we consider the Su--Schrieffer--Heeger model as a representative example and investigate the averaged excess entropy $ΔS_{12}$, defined as the difference between pseudo entropy and the average entanglement entropy, across the topological-to-trivial and trivial-to-topological phase transitions. When the two states are in the same phase, we find that $ ΔS_{12}$ is non-positive under periodic boundary conditions, while for open boundary conditions, it is non-positive only when the system is sufficiently large. Moreover, we analyze ground-state quench protocols for topology-crossing quenches and find that the imaginary pseudo entropy tracks the critical times predicted by the Fisher zeros.

</details>

Abstract: Room-temperature, unshielded recording of cardiac magnetic signals has remained a significant challenge since the inception of magnetocardiography (MCG). In this work, we present an MCG system based on optically pumped magnetometers (OPMs) designed to operate in ambient magnetic environments and acquire adult human cardiac magnetic fields, without the need for active or passive shielding. The system operates in a gradiometer configuration, achieving background-noise cancellation with a common-mode rejection ratio (CMRR) of 31 dB and a gradient sensitivity of 314 $\mathrm{fT/cm/\sqrt{Hz}}$. ### [166] [Poisson-shot-noise hybrid machines: efficiency and quasistatic divergence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29838)
*Rita Majumdar,Costantino Di Bello,Ralf Metzler,Rahul Marathe,Édgar Roldán*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了由过阻尼布朗粒子构成的微观主动热机模型，该粒子同时与热浴（被动）和非热浴（主动）接触，主动浴由泊松散粒噪声（PSN）建模。通过解析计算与数值模拟，分析了准静态循环协议下的热力学性能，发现机器可同时作为热机和制冷机运行（混合机器），并揭示了平均提取功与冷浴吸热之比可超越被动浴温度对应的卡诺效率。文章引入基于信息度量的准静态散度来定义真正的效率（受卡诺效率约束），并探讨了PSN shot率与非高斯性对效率的影响，发现了最优shot率以及效率与峰度之间的非一一对应关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微观主动热机（active heat engine）是统计力学与非平衡热力学的前沿课题，但以往研究较少同时考虑主动浴的shot噪声特征以及机器兼具热机与制冷机双重功能的混合行为，且对超越卡诺效率的宣称缺乏严谨的热力学第二定律约束下的效率定义。本文旨在建立包含泊松散粒噪声（Poisson shot-noise, PSN）的主动热机模型，并在准静态极限下引入信息理论度量来定义真实的效率边界。

Method: 采用过阻尼朗之万方程描述陷俘在谐振子势中的布朗粒子，主动浴效应由具有特定振幅分布的泊松散粒噪声（Poisson shot-noise, PSN）随机力模拟。通过解析计算与数值模拟，研究两冲程（two-stroke）和斯特林型（Stirling-like）准静态循环协议下的热力学性能，并引入信息论度量——准静态散度（quasistatic divergence）来定义受卡诺效率约束的真正效率。

Result: 在特定参数范围内，机器表现为混合机器（hybrid machine），同时以热机和制冷机模式分别相对于被动/主动浴运行。在总体表现为热机的参数区域，平均总提取功与冷浴总吸热之比可能超越被动浴温度对应的卡诺效率。存在最优PSN shot率使效率最大化，且效率与粒子位置分布的非高斯性（峰度，kurtosis）之间存在非一一对应关系（non-bijective relation）。

Conclusion: 本文为理解主动热机中shot噪声与非高斯统计对热力学性能的影响提供了理论框架。引入的准静态散度（quasistatic divergence）为主动热机提供了一个符合第二定律的、受卡诺效率约束的bona fide效率定义。最优shot率和效率-峰度非一一对应关系的发现，有助于设计基于主动浴的微观热机并理解其效率极限。

Abstract: We study stochastic models of a microscopic active heat engine, comprised of an overdamped Brownian particle trapped in a harmonic potential, and in simultaneous contact with thermal (passive) and athermal (active) baths. The interaction with the active bath is modeled as a stochastic force described by Poisson shot-noise (PSN) having a specified amplitude distribution. With analytical calculations and numerical simulations, we study the thermodynamic performance of the machine to quasistatic cyclic protocols analogous to those running two-stroke and Stirling-like engines. For specific parameter ranges, the thermodynamic behavior is that of a $\textit{hybrid machine}$, simultaneously operating as a heat engine with respect to the passive/active baths and as a refrigerator with respect to the passive/active baths. Focusing on the parameter region where the overall performance is such of an engine, we show that the average total extracted work per cycle divided by average total heat intake from the cold baths per cycle may surpass the Carnot efficiency associated with the temperature of the passive baths. Applying the second law for active heat engines, we focus on a bona fide efficiency (bounded by Carnot's efficiency) that incorporates an information-theoretic metric $\mathcal{I}-$ which we call $\textit{quasistatic divergence}-$ quantifying how distinguishable are the engine's statistics in the quasistatic limit with respect to a continually changing equilibrium distribution. We analyze, with theory and numerical simulations, how the PSN shot rate and the degree of non-Gaussianity in the particle position distribution influence the efficiency of the engine, and explore the correlation between non-Gaussianity and efficiency. Our findings reveal optimal PSN shot rates maximizing the engine's efficiency and an intriguing non-bijective relation between efficiency and kurtosis

### [167] [Surviving the Attack of the Clones](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30235)
*Denis S. Grebenkov*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个群体动力学（population dynamics）模型，其中每个扩散粒子在撞击催化表面时可分裂为两个独立克隆体。该群体并行搜索一个隐藏的部分反应性靶标，旨在触发反应事件（如病毒攻击）。论文建立了关于最快首次反应时间（fastest first-reaction time, FRT）的生存概率非线性积分方程，分析了其概率密度与矩，推导了平均FRT的上下界，并通过数值解揭示了自催化复制（autocatalytic replication）在加速扩散搜索方面的优势与局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解自催化复制机制对群体水平上最快首次反应时间统计特征的影响，量化加速扩散搜索的效果及其适用范围，为病毒攻击等生物搜索过程提供理论依据。

Method: 建立关于生存概率（survival probability）的非线性积分方程，通过分析推导最快首次反应时间的概率密度函数（probability density function）及其各阶矩；基于系统参数（靶标反应性、催化速率、扩散系数等）推导平均FRT的下界与上界；在基础几何设定下对非线性方程进行数值求解。

Result: 自催化复制能够显著加速扩散搜索过程，但该加速效果存在固有优势和局限性；数值解在基本几何设定下揭示了这些特征。

Conclusion: 自催化复制通过快速增加搜索者数量，可有效缩短群体搜索时间，但其加速效果受系统参数制约，并非无条件最优。

Abstract: We consider a population dynamics model in which each diffusing particle that hits a catalytic surface can split into two independent copies (clones). The particles of such a growing-in-size population search in parallel for a hidden partially reactive target to trigger a reaction event (e.g., a viral attack). We investigate the statistics of the fastest first-reaction time (FRT) among all the particles. We establish a nonlinear integral equation for the survival probability and then analyze the associated probability density of the FRT and its moments. Lower and upper bounds on the mean FRT are then deduced in terms of the system parameters (target reactivity, catalytic rate, diffusivity, etc.). Because autocatalytic replication can rapidly increase the number of searchers, it can substantially accelerate the diffusive search. We solve the nonlinear equations numerically in a basic geometric setting and reveal advantages and limitations on the autocatalytic search.

### [168] [Robust secret storage in networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30261)
*Vinko Zlatić*

TL;DR: 本文研究网络中的安全信息存储问题，提出分布式秘密存储的形式化框架，并将该问题表述为鲁棒性泛函（robustness functional）的优化，旨在平衡网络退化下的存活能力（survivability）与对抗性妥协（adversarial compromise）。通过最小信息承载子图（MICS）精确刻画存活能力，构造了无需全局网络信息的半局部优化方法，并在极限情形下将鲁棒性泛函映射为有效的自旋哈密顿量（spin Hamiltonian）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 建立分布式秘密存储（distributed secret storage）的形式化框架，将问题表述为鲁棒性泛函的优化。引入最小信息承载子图（minimal information-carrying subgraphs, MICS）给出存活能力的精确表示，并基于此构造半局部优化方法，其动力学不依赖全局网络结构。

Conclusion: 所提出的形式化框架和MICS表示为设计网络上的分布式秘密存储策略提供了理论基础，半局部方法允许在实际大规模网络中无需全局信息即可进行优化，而与自旋哈密顿量的映射则可能借助统计力学（statistical mechanics）工具进一步分析该问题。

Abstract: The problem of storing secure information on a network is studied. A formal framework for distributed secret storage is introduced, and possible applications in technological and social systems are discussed. The problem is formulated as the optimization of a robustness functional in which two competing requirements are balanced: survivability under network-degrading processes and resistance to adversarial compromise. An exact representation of survivability is derived in terms of minimal information-carrying subgraphs (MICS), which provide a reduced description of the reconstruction events relevant to the stored information. This representation is then used to construct semi-local optimization methods whose dynamics do not require global knowledge of the network structure. Finally, it is shown that, in a limiting case, the robustness functional can be mapped naturally to an effective spin Hamiltonian.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用功涨落定理（work fluctuation theorem）估计自由能差时，其收敛性往往较差，需要大量轨迹（trajectories）来计算平均值。该研究旨在改善这一收敛性问题。

Method: 借鉴护航自由能估计（escorted free energy estimation）和机器学习中的扩散模型（diffusion models）思想，引入一个不修改原始动力学的虚拟控制场（virtual control field）${\boldsymbol u}_θ$，构造出无穷多种满足功涨落定理形式的类功量$W_θ$，并通过优化参数$θ$来提升估计收敛性。

Result: 该方法能够为零方差估计（zero-variance estimator）自由能差提供条件，数值模拟表明其在收敛性方面有显著改进。

Conclusion: 提出的方法通过引入虚拟控制场构造多种类功量，可在不改变原始动力学的前提下优化自由能估计的收敛性，为高效计算非平衡自由能差提供了新途径。

Abstract: For a process in which a system is driven irreversibly from equilibrium state $A$ toward equilibrium state $B$, the free energy difference $ΔF = F_B-F_A$ can be estimated using the work fluctuation theorem $\langle e^{-W/T}\rangle = e^{-ΔF/T}$, where $W$ and $T$ denote work and temperature. The estimate often suffers from poor convergence with the number of trajectories used to calculate the average. Borrowing ideas from escorted free energy estimation, and from diffusion models of machine learning, we show how to construct infinitely many work-like quantities, $W_θ$, that satisfy $\langle e^{-W_θ/T}\rangle = e^{-ΔF/T}$, for the same underlying dynamics. Our method involves a virtual control field ${\boldsymbol u}_θ$ that does not modify these dynamics. We show how to choose parameter values $θ$ to optimize convergence of the free energy estimate, for a fixed set of trajectories. We identify conditions under which our method provides a zero-variance estimator of $ΔF$. We use numerical simulations of model systems to illustrate the gains in convergence that our method can achieve.

</details>


### [170] [A Field-Theoretic Framework for Work Statistics and Universal Scaling in Non-equilibrium Phase Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30503)
*Yanbo Qiao,Ruohan Xu,H. T. Quan*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个场论框架（field-theoretic framework），用于研究驱动通过临界点的 O(N) 模型中的功统计量（work statistics）。通过分析复合幂算子的动态重整化群（renormalization group）流，自然导出 Kibble-Zurek 标度律，并从第一性原理推导了拓扑缺陷的功累积量标度，跳过了启发式的冻结近似（freeze-out argument）。研究发现孤立量子系统的功累积量密度标度指数与开放量子及经典系统不同，后者经历维度坍缩（dimensional collapse）。理论通过精确高斯解和数值模拟验证，建立了远离平衡态功统计量的通用基础，桥接了随机热力学（stochastic thermodynamics）与重整化群理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究在描述驱动通过临界点的系统时，通常依赖启发式的冻结近似来推导 Kibble-Zurek 标度律，缺乏一个从第一性原理出发的统一框架。本文旨在建立一套场论方法，直接从重整化群流出发推导功统计量的普适标度行为，从而弥合随机热力学与重整化群理论之间的间隙。

Method: 采用场论框架分析 O(N) 模型在驱动通过临界点时的功统计量；通过研究复合幂算子（composite power operators）的动态重整化群流，推导功累积量的标度指数；分别处理孤立量子系统与开放/经典系统，并利用精确高斯解（exact Gaussian solutions）和数值模拟验证理论结果。

Result: 推导出第 n 阶功累积量密度（work cumulant density）的普适标度关系 $c_n \sim τ_Q^{-α_n}$。孤立量子系统的标度指数为 $α_n = p(d+nz)ν/(1+pzν)$，而开放量子系统和经典系统经历维度坍缩后指数变为 $α_n = pdν/(1+pzν)$。理论得到了精确高斯解和数值模拟的验证。

Conclusion: 该理论为远离平衡态的通用功统计量奠定了坚实基础，成功将随机热力学与重整化群理论联系起来，为研究临界动力学中的功统计量提供了一种系统化的第一性原理方法。

Abstract: We develop a field-theoretic framework for work statistics in $O(N)$ models driven through criticality. By analyzing the dynamic renormalization group flow of composite power operators, we find the Kibble-Zurek scaling laws as a natural consequence of the flow, and we derive the scaling of work cumulants relevant to Kibble-Zurek scaling of topological defects from first principles, bypassing heuristic freeze-out argument. This yields the universal scaling $c_n \sim τ_Q^{-α_n}$ for the $n$-th work cumulant density: isolated quantum systems exhibit a scaling of $α_n = p(d+nz)ν/(1+pzν)$, whereas open quantum and classical systems undergo a dimensional collapse to $α_n = pdν/(1+pzν)$. Validated by exact Gaussian solutions and numerical simulations, our theory establishes a foundation for general work statistics far from equilibrium, thereby bridging stochastic thermodynamics and the renormalization group theory.

</details>


### [171] [Why can genetic algorithms work in high-dimensional search spaces?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30619)
*Stephen Whitelam*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文证明，在变异率极小的极限下，精英主义 (1+M) 遗传算法（genetic algorithm）的等效动力学等价于在各项异性高斯白噪声（anisotropic Gaussian white noise）作用下的裁剪梯度下降（clipped gradient descent）。因此，简单的变异-选择遗传算法在期望意义上跟随损失函数的梯度，无需显式计算梯度或对损失评估进行平均。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解遗传算法能够有效扩展到高维和大规模搜索空间的内在机制，并澄清其与梯度下降（gradient descent）类优化方法之间的理论联系。

Method: 通过理论分析，研究精英主义 (1+M) 遗传算法在小变异极限下的有效动力学，将其等效为带各向异性高斯噪声的裁剪梯度下降过程，并利用损失函数黑塞矩阵（Hessian）的有效秩（effective rank）分析算法的收敛速度。

Result: 遗传算法比梯度下降更慢，原因是存在沿梯度横向方向的噪声。但这一减速并非由搜索空间的参数数量决定，而是由损失函数黑塞矩阵的有效秩控制。对于神经网络损失函数中常见的集中型黑塞谱（concentrated Hessian spectra），有效秩可以远小于参数数量。

Conclusion: 这一理论分析可能解释了遗传算法为何能够扩展到大型搜索空间：其实际性能瓶颈取决于损失函数黑塞矩阵的有效秩而非参数维度，在神经网络场景下有效秩通常远小于参数数量，从而缓解了维度诅咒（curse of dimensionality）的影响。

Abstract: We show that the effective dynamics of the elitist $(1+M)$ genetic algorithm is, in the limit of small mutations, clipped gradient descent on the loss in the presence of anisotropic Gaussian white noise. In expectation, therefore, a simple mutation-selection genetic algorithm follows the gradient of the loss, without explicit calculation of gradients and without averaging over loss evaluations. The genetic algorithm is slower than gradient descent because of the noise that acts in directions transverse to the gradient. However, this slowdown is controlled not by the number of parameters of the search space but by the effective rank of the Hessian of the loss function. For the concentrated Hessian spectra observed in neural-network loss functions the effective rank can be far smaller than the number of parameters, which may explain why genetic algorithms can scale to large search spaces.

</details>

### [172] [Latent Genetic Algorithm for Crystal Structure Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29220)
*Kaixin Zheng,Wanjian Yin,Hongyu Yu,Hongjun Xiang*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于潜在遗传算法（Latent Genetic Algorithm, LGA）的晶体结构预测新范式，通过预训练通用原子间势（universal interatomic potentials）的潜在表示（latent representation）作为连续进化坐标，有效解决了传统实空间交叉操作破坏有利局域模体的问题。LGA将HfO₂基态恢复率从20-35%提升至60-95%，在16种钙钛矿的统一变超胞搜索中降低近十倍成本，并揭示了PbTiO₃/PbZrO₃超晶格中此前未被报道的长周期基态结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统晶体结构预测方法在实空间（real-space）中进行交叉操作时，由于母体结构在几何上不匹配（如晶胞、密度、对称性不同），常常破坏有利的局域模体（local motifs）。亟需一种能够继承这些模体并跨越不同结构空间的连续进化坐标机制。

Method: LGA利用预训练通用原子间势学习到的潜在表示作为进化坐标；子代通过逆向优化（inverse optimization）原子位置和晶格向量以匹配目标潜在表示生成，该目标潜在表示由父代潜在向量的插值（interpolation）构建。

Result: LGA抑制了高能量和短接触的子代结构；将HfO₂的基态恢复率从20-35%提高到60-95%；在16种钙钛矿的统一变超胞搜索中实现了近十倍的搜索成本降低；在(PbTiO₃)ₙ/(PbZrO₃)ₙ超晶格中发现了具有面内有限-q调制（in-plane finite-q modulation）周期性的长周期基态结构。

Conclusion: LGA提供了一种表示引导（representation-guided）的基态结构预测新范式，并为无需解码器（decoder-free）的材料逆向设计（inverse design）提供了实用途径。

Abstract: Predicting crystal structures requires navigating rugged energy landscapes in which favorable local motifs must be inherited across candidates with incompatible cells, densities, and symmetries. Conventional real-space crossover often destroys these motifs when parent structures are geometrically mismatched. Here we show that latent representations learned by pretrained universal interatomic potentials can serve as continuous evolutionary coordinates for crystal structure prediction. In the Latent Genetic Algorithm (LGA), offspring are generated by inverse optimization of atomic positions and lattice vectors to match a target latent representation, which is constructed via interpolation of the parent latent vectors. LGA suppresses high-energy and short-contact offspring, increases the HfO$_2$ ground-state recovery rate from 20-35% to 60-95%, and enables a unified variable-supercell search over 16 perovskites with a nearly tenfold reduction in search cost. Applied to (PbTiO$_3$)$_n$/(PbZrO$_3$)$_n$ superlattices, LGA reveals $\sqrt{2} \times 3\sqrt{2} \times 1$ long-period ground-state structures characterized by a common in-plane finite-$q$ modulation $q{_\parallel} = (1/6,1/6)$ and layer-coupled sidebands. To our knowledge, this in-plane periodicity has not been reported in any related oxide perovskite superlattice studies. Altogether, LGA offers a powerful representation-guided paradigm for ground-state structure prediction and provides a practical, decoder-free route toward materials inverse design.

</details>

### [173] [Geometric Algebra Meets Cartesian Tensors: Higher-Order Equivariance for Interatomic Potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29584)
*Can Polat,Erchin Serpedin,Mustafa Kurban,Hasan Kurban*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出 CliffordSTF，通过对称无迹张量（symmetric-traceless tensor）轨道与克利福德多向量（Clifford multivector）的双线性交叉收缩，弥补 Cl(3,0) 原子间势在力的方向预测上的结构性缺陷，在 rMD17 和 OC22 基准上取得显著的力方向与能量精度提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 Cl(3,0) 原子间势（interatomic potentials）虽能准确预测力的大小，但在力的方向预测上表现极差：在十二个模型的基准研究中，所有 L ≤ 1 基线的聚合力余弦相似度（aggregate force-cosine similarity）均低于 0.25。问题的根源在于结构性的：ℝ³ 中两个向量的几何积（geometric product）只能实现其不可约表示（irreducible representation）中的 L=0 和 L=1 分量，而主宰每个消息传递层（message-passing layer）的逐边双线性（per-edge bilinear）中缺少对称无迹秩-2 分量。

Method: CliffordSTF 将克利福德多向量（Clifford multivector）与秩 2 和秩 3 的闭式对称无迹张量轨道（closed-form symmetric-traceless tensor tracks）通过双线性跨轨道收缩（bilinear cross-track contractions）耦合，仅使用单个可学习双线性（learned bilinear），无需 Clebsch–Gordan 表、Wigner-D 矩阵或 e3nn 调用。

Result: 在 rMD17 上，CliffordSTF 将聚合力余弦相似度从 0.055（基础 Clifford）提升至 0.551，实现了方向精度的量级提升；同时力平均绝对误差（MAE）降低 15.8%，能量 MAE 降低 10.9%。所提方法在所有无 CG（CG-free）或体序（body-ordered）基线中表现最优（所有对比方法 ≤ 0.17）。在催化基准 OC22 上，CliffordSTF 在 S2EF 任务中取得了最佳分布外（out-of-distribution）能量 MAE，在 IS2RE 任务中取得了 L ≥ 2 方法中最佳的分布内（in-distribution）能量 MAE。十一变体消融实验表明两个轨道具有互补性，单独使用任一轨道均无法达到组合模型的性能。

Conclusion: CliffordSTF 通过引入对称无迹张量轨道，有效解决了克利福德势在力方向预测上的结构性缺陷，在不依赖 Clebsch–Gordan 等复杂工具的前提下，显著提升了力的方向精度和整体能量/力预测性能，在分子动力学和催化基准上均优于多种基线方法。

Abstract: $\mathrm{Cl}(3,0)$ interatomic potentials, despite their algebraic elegance, predict force magnitudes accurately but force directions poorly. Across ten rMD17 molecules, every $L \leq 1$ baseline in our twelve-model study attains aggregate force-cosine similarity below $0.25$. The cause is structural. The geometric product of two vectors in $\mathbb{R}^3$ realises only the $L=0$ and $L=1$ components of its irreducible representation content, leaving the symmetric-traceless rank-2 component absent from the per-edge bilinear that drives each message-passing layer. We address this with CliffordSTF, which couples the Clifford multivector to closed-form symmetric-traceless tensor tracks at ranks two and three through bilinear cross-track contractions, using a single learned bilinear and no Clebsch--Gordan tables, Wigner-$D$ matrices, or e3nn calls. On rMD17, CliffordSTF raises aggregate force-cosine similarity from $0.055$ (base Clifford) to $0.551$, an order-of-magnitude relative directional gain, alongside improved magnitude accuracy (force MAE $15.8\%$ lower; energy MAE $10.9\%$ lower). It outperforms all CG-free or body-ordered baselines in our study (all $\leq 0.17$). On catalysis benchmarks, CliffordSTF achieves the best out-of-distribution S2EF energy MAE on OC22 in our experiments, and the best in-distribution energy MAE among $L \geq 2$ methods on OC22 IS2RE. An eleven-variant ablation shows the two tracks are complementary: neither alone matches the combined model.

</details>


### [174] [Thermal Fundamental Gap Predictions in DFT via Optimally Tuned Hybrids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29696)
*Tim Gould,Leeor Kronik,Gil Amoyal,Stefano Pittalis*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过三步理论构建，将杂化密度泛函理论（hybrid density functional theory）扩展至有限温度下的电子基元带隙（fundamental gap）预测，推导了热力学广义Kohn-Sham框架与热Janak定理，并证明最优调节（optimal tuning）从基态策略升级为有限温度带隙预测的必要原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有限温度下电子基元带隙的预测在概念和实践中一直具有挑战性，现有的理论框架难以准确描绘热力学系综（thermal ensemble）中的电子激发行为。

Method: 首先，将广义Kohn-Sham杂化密度泛函理论推广至热力学系综，从热单粒子辅助系统出发推导Mermin广义Kohn-Sham框架。其次，通过该框架下严格成立的Janak定理（Janak's theorem）的推广形式，将Hirata的热准粒子图像（thermal-quasiparticle picture）重新表述为热轨道带隙估计量，并推导出低温闭合形式，其误差由导数不连续性（derivative discontinuity）控制。最后，利用最优调节消除该误差，使辅助轨道带隙在低温下与相互作用带隙匹配。

Result: 推导出了由导数不连续性控制的低温闭合形式带隙估计量；证明最优调节可将辅助轨道带隙与相互作用带隙精确对齐；通过应用验证了理论的有效性及其推论。

Conclusion: 在杂化泛函框架内，最优调节不再是可选的基态策略，而是实现精确有限温度带隙预测的强制性原则（mandatory principle）。

Abstract: Predicting electronic fundamental gaps at finite temperature has remained conceptually and practically challenging. We address this in three connected steps. First, we extend generalized Kohn--Sham hybrid density functional theory to thermal ensembles, deriving a Mermin generalized Kohn--Sham framework from a thermal one-particle auxiliary system and an exact density-functional remainder. Second, via an extension of Janak's theorem that holds rigorously in this framework, we recast Hirata's thermal-quasiparticle picture as a thermal orbital gap estimator and derive a closed low-temperature form, the error of which is controlled by the derivative discontinuity. Third, because optimal tuning eliminates this error, the auxiliary orbital gap matches the interacting gap at low temperature, upgrading optimal tuning from a ground-state strategy to the governing principle -- mandatory, not optional -- for accurate finite-temperature gap predictions obtained from gaps of orbital eigenvalues within a hybrid functional framework. We present applications that validate the theory and demonstrate its consequences.

### [175] [Spectral phase transitions and trainability in neural network learning dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28486)
*Chanju Park,Dario Bocchi,Francesco D'Amico,Biagio Lucini,Gert Aarts*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出神经网络训练可视为初始随机矩阵系综的随机演化，随机梯度下降（SGD）更新重塑谱分布并放大信号，诱导Baik-Ben Arous-Péché（BBP）相变——孤立特征值从随机体分布中脱离——从而为高维学习动力学中的表征形成提供动力学框架。在线性教师-学生模型中可解析求解谱演化并获得由学习率和初始权重方差调控的可训练性相图，该形式化可推广至非线性和随机设定。数值模拟支持训练中谱对齐的稳健涌现，表明谱分析可为随机学习动力学提供统一视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经网络权重矩阵谱中低维结构的涌现是训练后模型的常见经验特征，但其在学习过程中的动力学起源仍是一个开放问题。本文旨在揭示这一现象背后的动力学机制。

Method: 将神经网络训练形式化为初始随机矩阵系综的随机演化，由SGD更新驱动；在可解线性教师-学生模型中解析分析谱演化，并扩展至非线性与随机设定；通过数值模拟验证。

Result: 训练过程中发生BBP相变，孤立特征值从随机体分布中脱离；在线性模型中获得了由学习率和初始权重方差调控的可训练性相图；数值模拟显示谱对齐在训练中稳健涌现。

Conclusion: 谱分析可为随机学习动力学提供统一视角，将可训练性、优化超参数、谱相变与神经网络中的表征学习联系起来。

Abstract: The emergence of low-dimensional structures in the spectra of neural network weight matrices is a common empirical feature of trained models, but the dynamical origin of this phenomenon during learning remains an open problem. We formulate neural network training as the stochastic evolution of an initially random matrix ensemble, driven by stochastic gradient descent (SGD) updates that reshape the spectral bulk while amplifying signal strength. This induces a Baik-Ben Arous-Péché (BBP) transition during training, where isolated eigenvalues detach from the random bulk distribution, providing a dynamical framework for representation formation in high-dimensional learning dynamics. We demonstrate this in a solvable linear teacher-student model, where spectral evolution is analytically tractable and a phase diagram of trainability governed by the step size (or learning rate) and initial weight variance is obtained, and subsequently extend our formalism beyond the linear regime to nonlinear and stochastic settings. Numerical simulations in realistic settings support this picture, showing robust emergence of spectral alignment during training. Our results suggest that spectral analysis may provide a unified perspective of stochastic learning dynamics, linking trainability, optimisation hyperparameters, spectral phase transitions, and representation learning in neural networks.

### [176] [Geometric Approach to Zero-Memory Quantum Dot Reservoir Computing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29320)
*Bongsu Kim,Oscar Lee,Sangjun Jeon,Kun Woo Kim*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出在无记忆系统中通过计算时空权衡，利用空间自由度替代时间记忆来外在构造记忆能力，并通过数值模拟验证了无记忆量子点系统在混沌预测等任务上的高性能表现，同时揭示了外延记忆形成的拓扑稳定机制——希尔伯特空间中的滞回环。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物理储层计算（physical reservoir computing）依赖系统的内在记忆容量（memory capacity），这限制了候选物理系统的范围。本文旨在将记忆能力与材料固有属性解耦，在原本无记忆的系统中通过外在方式构造记忆，从而拓展量子神经形态计算（quantum neuromorphic computing）的候选系统。

Method: 利用计算时空权衡（computational space-time tradeoff），采用多维输入节点（multidimensional input nodes）作为空间记忆轴，替代时间记忆。通过广义量子点（generalized quantum dot）的离散能级提供强非线性，并耦合这种内在非线性与外在构造的记忆，进行数值模拟验证。

Result: 无记忆量子储层在混沌Mackey-Glass未来预测和非线性变换任务上均实现了高性能。通过对量子态轨迹几何的分析，发现外在记忆在量子希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）中构建了滞回环（hysteresis loop），当系统状态演化与输入信号频率同步时，该环具有拓扑稳定性（topologically stable）。

Conclusion: 该工作将储层计算与材料特定的记忆属性解耦，显著拓展了量子神经形态计算候选系统的范围，为在无记忆物理平台上实现高效计算提供了新路径。

Abstract: Physical reservoir computing offers an energy-efficient alternative to conventional neural networks, where the intrinsic memory capacity in the physical system plays a central role. We demonstrate that memory capacity can be engineered extrinsically in memoryless systems by exploiting the computational space-time tradeoff, substituting temporal memory with spatial degrees of freedom. Our approach utilizes multidimensional input nodes to function as a spatial memory axis, thereby removing the dependency on intrinsic history-dependent dynamics in the reservoir. We validate this framework through numerical simulations of a generalized quantum dot, whose discrete energy levels provide strong nonlinearity crucial for reservoir computing as well. By coupling this inherent nonlinearity with our extrinsic memory, we show that memoryless quantum reservoir can achieve high performance on both chaotic Mackey-Glass future prediction and nonlinear transformation tasks. Furthermore, by analyzing the geometry of the quantum state trajectories, we identify the physical mechanism underlying this memory emergence: extrinsic memory constructs a hysteresis loop within the quantum Hilbert space, and this loop becomes topologically stable when the evolution of the system state synchronizes with the input signal's frequency. Our work decouples reservoir computing from material-specific memory properties, significantly expanding the range of candidate systems for quantum neuromorphic computing.

</details>

### [177] [Dark energy from neutrino interactions in Unimodular Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28488)
*Alejandro Gil-Ocaranza,Josue De-Santiago,Mauricio Lopez-Hernandez,Jorge L. Cervantes-Cota*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: No AI summary available.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: No AI summary available.

Method: No AI summary available.

Result: No AI summary available.

Conclusion: No AI summary available.

Abstract: We investigate a dark energy scenario generated by neutrino interactions mediated by a light scalar field, in which finite-temperature corrections induce an effective neutrino mass that evolves with the thermal history of the Universe. Within the framework of Unimodular Gravity, these interactions give rise to a non-conservation current, leading to dynamical dark energy. We study one- and two-neutrino realizations of the model. In the one-neutrino case, the dark energy density evolves monotonically, whereas in the two-neutrino scenario it can reach a maximum at intermediate redshifts before decreasing at late times. Using late time cosmological datasets, we constrain the effective interaction strength for lightest-neutrino masses in the range $0.05 \,{\rm meV}\le m_1 \le 1 \,{\rm meV}$. We find preferred interaction scales of order $G_s\sim10^{12} \, {\rm eV}^{-2}$ with a significance of $2 σ$, with the inferred coupling decreasing as the assumed neutrino mass increases. Assuming neutrino couplings of order unity, this $G_s$ value corresponds to an ultralight mediator with mass $m_φ\sim10^{-6} \, {\rm eV}$. We further assess the impact of Planck distance-prior, finding a noticeable reduction in parameter degeneracies and a reconstructed dark energy evolution closer to that of a cosmological constant. Our results show that neutrino interactions can generate both monotonic and non-monotonic dark energy evolutions while remaining compatible with current cosmological observations. The inferred interaction strengths remain consistent with non-zero values for part of the explored neutrino-mass range, supporting neutrino-induced dark energy dynamics as a viable phenomenological extension of $Λ$CDM at the background level.

### [178] [Reheating matters: Starobinsky inflation in light of joint CMB+BAO results and gravitational-wave forecasts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28502)
*Gláuber C. Dorsch,Lucas P. C. Leão,Lucas M. B. Alves,Luiz C. A. Miranda,Beatriz M. D. Sena*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了Starobinsky暴胀后若再加热由刚性流体主导时，原初引力波谱会变蓝。作者在三种场景下分析发现，当前CMB+BAO数据允许的1σ区域已被大爆炸核合成（BBN）约束排除，而2σ区域中相当部分的蓝倾效应足以被未来干涉仪（如LISA、DECIGO等）探测到，使这些场景具有可检验性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究指出，若暴胀后再加热（reheating）由状态方程$p>ρ/3$的刚性流体（stiff fluid）主导，则Starobinsky暴胀的标量谱指数（scalar spectral index）预测可与Atacama宇宙学望远镜（ACT）和南极望远镜（SPT）的联合CMB+BAO数据相符。但这一刚性时期会使原初引力波（primordial gravitational-wave, GW）谱变蓝（blue-tilting），因此需要评估该效应是否已被观测数据排除或可被未来实验检验。

Method: 作者考虑了三种再加热场景：(i) 纯刚性流体主导的再加热；(ii) 先由类物质流体（matter-like fluid，对应于暴涨子在二次势阱底部振荡）主导，后接刚性时期；(iii) 先由辐射主导（radiation-dominated）而非物质主导，后接刚性时期。基于这些场景计算原初引力波谱的蓝倾程度，并与当前宇宙学观测约束及未来探测器灵敏度进行对比。

Result: 在所有三种场景中，近期CMB+BAO数据允许的1σ置信区间已被大爆炸核合成（Big Bang Nucleosynthesis, BBN）对辐射含量的约束所排除。在剩余的2σ区域中，相当一部分参数空间的蓝倾效应足够强，使得原初引力波谱可被未来干涉仪如爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope）、LISA、DECIGO和BBO探测到。

Conclusion: Starobinsky暴胀中由刚性流体主导的再加热场景虽能改善标量谱指数与数据的符合程度，但由此导致的原初引力波蓝倾效应已受到BBN约束的强烈限制；同时，这些场景可通过未来引力波干涉仪进行检验，从而获得可观测的预测。

Abstract: It has been noted in the literature that, if post-inflationary reheating is dominated by a stiff fluid with equation of state (EoS) $p>ρ/3$, then the predictions of Starobinsky inflation for the scalar spectral index could be made to agree with measurements from the combined CMB+BAO datasets performed by the Atacama Cosmology Telescope (ACT) and the South Pole Telescope (SPT) collaborations. However, a side-effect of such a stiff epoch is the blue-tilting of the primordial gravitational-wave (GW) spectrum. In this work, we explore the observational consequences of this blue-tilting in three scenarios: (i) a purely stiff-dominated reheating, (ii) a more realistic case where reheating is first dominated by a matter-like fluid (corresponding to inflaton oscillations around the bottom of a quadratic potential well) later followed by a stiff epoch, and (iii) a case analogous to the previous one, but with an earlier radiation-dominated instead of matter-dominated epoch. We show that in all cases the $1σ$ region allowed by recent CMB+BAO data is already excluded by constraints on the amount of radiation present during Big Bang Nucleosynthesis (BBN). Moreover, in a considerable fraction of the remaining $2σ$ region we find that the blue-tilting would be severe enough to make the primordial spectrum detectable in future interferometers such as Einstein Telescope, LISA, DECIGO, and BBO, thus rendering these scenarios testable by these experiments.

</details>


### [179] [Estimating Cosmological Parameters from Localized Fast Radio Bursts: A Method for Removing Milky Way Dispersion-Measure Contributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29761)
*Yuchen Zhang,Yang Liu,Hongwei Yu,Puxun Wu*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出一种利用同一天空区域内的定位快速射电暴（localized FRBs）的色散量差值（DM differences）来消除银河系贡献的方法，从而改进基于FRB的宇宙学推断。通过模拟样本验证了方法的可靠性，并应用于实际数据，获得了与常规处理方法不同的宇宙学参数约束，凸显了银河系色散量系统误差在FRB宇宙学中的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 快速射电暴（FRBs）正成为有力的宇宙学探针，但基于色散量（DM）的宇宙学推断受限于银河系贡献（包括星际介质和银晕）的不确定性。现有方法需要采用特定的银河系电子密度模型或对银晕色散量做先验假设，这些不确定性限制了FRB宇宙学推断的精度。

Method: 提出一种差分色散量方法（differential DM method），利用同一天空区域内多个定位FRB的色散量差值（DM differences）来直接消除银河系贡献，无需依赖任何特定的银河系电子密度模型或银晕色散量的先验假设。

Result: 使用模拟FRB样本验证了该方法能够成功恢复基准宇宙学参数。将方法应用于当前已定位的FRB实际数据后，获得了对参数Γ ≡ Ω_b H_0 f_d的约束，其结果与采用常规银河系贡献处理方法推断的结果存在差异。

Conclusion: 该差异凸显了银河系色散量系统误差（Milky Way DM systematics）在FRB宇宙学中的重要性，并表明差分色散量方法在未来的大样本定位FRB数据中具有重要应用潜力。

Abstract: Fast radio bursts (FRBs) are emerging as powerful probes for cosmology. However, cosmological inference based on FRB dispersion measures (DMs) is limited by uncertainties in the Milky Way contribution, including those from the Galactic interstellar medium and the Galactic halo. In this Letter, we propose a method that eliminates the Milky Way contribution by using DM differences between localized FRBs within the same sky region. The method removes the need to adopt a specific Galactic electron-density model or a prior assumption for the Galactic halo DM. We validate the reliability of the method using mock FRB samples and show that it successfully recovers the fiducial cosmological parameter. Applying the method to current localized FRB data, we obtain a constraint on $Γ\equiv Ω_b H_0 f_{\rm d}$ that differs from that inferred using the conventional treatment of the Milky Way contribution. This difference highlights the importance of Milky Way DM systematics in FRB cosmology and demonstrates the potential of differential DM methods for future large samples of localized FRBs.

### [180] [Superhorizon curvature perturbations in hybrid inflation revisited](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29796)
*Shi Pi,Anxianyi Xiong*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文基于δN形式化（δN formalism）重新审视了多场暴胀（multi-field inflation）中的宇宙学扰动，并应用于混合暴胀（hybrid inflation）模型。研究发现，由瀑布场（waterfall field）的速失稳（tachyonic instability）驱动的增长中的等曲率扰动（isocurvature perturbation）可显著增强曲率扰动（curvature perturbation），产生具有特征性k³红外增长和对数非高斯性（logarithmic non-Gaussianity）的功率谱，其增强效应可同时解释原初黑洞暗物质（primordial black hole dark matter）和LISA、Taiji、TianQin可探测的随机引力波背景（stochastic gravitational wave background）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有单场暴胀模型（如超慢滚（ultra-slow-roll））对曲率扰动增强的解释存在局限，多场暴胀模型中沿暴胀轨迹横向方向（transverse direction）的几何效应尚未被充分纳入δN形式化的分析框架，亟需建立更完整的理论描述。

Method: 将δN形式化扩展至暴胀轨迹的横向方向，明确计入最终超曲面（final hypersurface）的几何效应；将该框架应用于混合暴胀模型，分析瀑布场速失稳引起的等曲率扰动增长及其对曲率扰动的反馈。

Result: 曲率扰动的增强发生在场空间（field space）轨迹转向过程中，该机制在定性上不同于单场暴胀的非吸引子解（non-attractor solution）。增强后的功率谱具有宽峰结构，红外端呈k³增长，紫外端谱指数（spectral tilt）唯一确定对数非高斯性的非线性参数f_NL。在混合暴胀中，f_NL的符号由瀑布场几何固定且恒正，从而普遍增强原初黑洞的形成。

Conclusion: 增强后的曲率扰动可同时解释原初黑洞暗物质以及LISA、Taiji、TianQin可探测的随机引力波背景，为多场暴胀模型与观测之间的联系提供了新的理论途径。

Abstract: We revisit cosmological perturbations in multi-field inflation using the $δN$ formalism. By extending the analysis to directions transverse to the inflationary trajectory, we explicitly account for the geometry of the final hypersurface. Applying this framework to hybrid inflation, we identify an enhancement mechanism of the curvature perturbation driven by the growing isocurvature perturbation due to the tachyonic instability of the waterfall field. This amplification occurs during the trajectory's turn in field space, a process qualitatively distinct from the non-attractor solution in single-field inflation models such as ultra-slow-roll. The resulting power spectrum features a broad peak with a characteristic $k^3$ infrared growth and a ultraviolet spectral tilt that uniquely determines the nonlinear parameter $f_\mathrm{NL}$ of a logarithmic non-Gaussianity, all of which are primarily governed by the waterfall dynamics. We found that in hybrid inflation, the sign of $f_{\rm NL}$ is fixed by tachyonic waterfall geometry and is always positive, leading to a generic enhancement of primordial black hole formation. The enhanced curvature perturbation can simultaneously account for primordial black hole dark matter and a stochastic gravitational wave background detectable by LISA, Taiji, and TianQin.

</details>


### [181] [Compaction function in stochastic inflation: a \texttt{FOREST} of type I and II primordial black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30087)
*Chiara Animali,Pierre Auclair,Baptiste Blachier,Eemeli Tomberg,Vincent Vennin*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文展示了如何在随机暴胀（stochastic inflation）框架下，通过求解随机二叉树上的场动力学来计算压实函数（compaction function），并将其应用于原初黑洞（primordial black hole, PBH）形成研究。研究发现，在经典极限下PBH质量函数分布狭窄、II型涨落被压制；而在量子和近临界（近永恒暴胀）区间，质量分布跨越多个数量级、丰度增强且II型涨落数量超过I型，云中云（cloud-in-cloud）效应也变得显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机暴胀框架中原初黑洞形成的研究需要一种能够准确计算压实函数并区分I型和II型涨落的方法，而现有方法在此方面存在不足。

Method: 通过将随机场动力学离散化到随机二叉树上，求解压实函数；该函数直接关联给定节点兄弟分支与子分支的体积比。结构分析还通过判断扰动面积半径是否随径向坐标单调增加，来区分I型和II型涨落。

Result: 在经典极限（量子扩散亚主导）下，PBH质量函数分布狭窄，II型涨落相对于I型被强烈压制。在量子和近临界（永恒暴胀附近）区间，PBH质量分布覆盖多个数量级，整体丰度显著增强，II型涨落数量超过I型。

Conclusion: 当随机效应显著时，云中云效应不可忽略，意味着需要更深入地理解II型涨落的演化和坍缩过程，才能获得稳健的PBH理论预测。

Abstract: We show how to compute the compaction function within stochastic inflation, by solving the random field dynamics on stochastic binary trees. In this framework, the compaction function is directly related to the ratio of the volumes emerging from the sibling and child branches of a given node. This construction also determines whether or not the areal radius of a perturbation increases monotonically with the radial coordinate, thereby distinguishing between type-I and type-II fluctuations. As an application, we investigate primordial black hole (PBH) formation in a single-field toy model with a constant potential slope, using stochastic-tree realizations generated with the public code \texttt{FOREST}. In the classical regime, where quantum diffusion is subdominant, the PBH mass function is narrowly distributed and type-II fluctuations are strongly suppressed relative to type I. By contrast, in the quantum and near-critical (i.e. close to eternal inflation) regimes, the PBH mass distribution spans several orders of magnitude, the overall PBH abundance is enhanced, and type-II fluctuations outnumber type I. In that case cloud-in-cloud effects are also important, highlighting the need for a better understanding of the evolution and collapse of type-II fluctuations in order to obtain robust PBH predictions when stochastic effects are significant.

</details>


### [182] [Rapid Hubble constant inference from GW170817 using GPU-accelerated nested sampling: prior sensitivity and the limits of post-hoc reweighting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30504)
*Ming Han Yang,Metha Prathaban,David Yallup,Will Handley*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文利用GPU加速的嵌套采样管道，重新计算了GW170817在四种不同距离先验下的哈勃常数（$H_0$）后验分布，发现后验重加权（post-hoc reweighting）方法无法准确复现直接在目标先验下采样得到的后验结果，尤其是在高尾端概率上存在显著偏差，并揭示了体先验（volumetric prior）忽略了一个双峰结构中的高$H_0$分支，这是重加权失效的机制根源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检查GW170817亮 sirens（bright siren）测量哈勃常数（Hubble constant）时，通过后验重加权（post-hoc reweighting）将体先验（volumetric prior）切换为均匀-in-$d_L$ 先验的做法是否可靠。

Method: 使用GPU原生异质嵌套采样管道（heterodyned nested sampling pipeline），在单块A100 GPU上约13分钟内完成完整$n_{\rm live}=5000$的采样分析，在四种先验变体下重新计算GW170817的$H_0$后验分布，并采用定向模式隔离运行（mode-isolated runs）研究双峰结构。

Result: 直接采样时，从体先验切换到均匀-in-$d_L$先验使高尾概率$P(H_0>120\,\mathrm{km/s/Mpc})$从0.017升至0.159，加权中位数$H_0$从77.6升至87.6 km/s/Mpc，而分箱MAP（binned MAP）保持在70.5 km/s/Mpc；后验重加权仅恢复尾端$P=0.041$，约为直接采样偏移的17%。三种先验变体的嵌套抽样证据（nested sampling evidence）差异$Δ\ln Z\lesssim 1.8$，表明数据对距离先验偏好微弱。

Conclusion: 后验重加权存在覆盖失效（coverage failure），无法替代完整样本的先验敏感性重跑。建议将全样本先验敏感性重跑作为亮siren宇宙学的默认稳健性工具（robustness tool），以取代后验重加权方法。

Abstract: The bright-siren measurement of the Hubble constant from GW170817 (Abbott et al. 2017) assumes that switching from a volumetric to a uniform-in-$d_L$ luminosity-distance prior can be implemented by post-hoc reweighting of the baseline samples, rather than by re-running the inference under the target prior. Using a GPU-native heterodyned nested sampling pipeline that completes the full $n_{\rm live}=5000$ analysis in about 13 min on a single A100, we recompute the GW170817 $H_0$ posterior under four prior variants for the modern aligned-spin tidal waveform IMRPhenomXAS_NRTidalv3. Switching from the volumetric to a uniform-in-$d_L$ distance prior raises the high-tail probability $P(H_0>120\,\mathrm{km/s/Mpc})$ from 0.017 to 0.159 when imposed during sampling and shifts the weighted-median $H_0$ from 77.6 to 87.6 km/s/Mpc, while the binned MAP stays at 70.5 km/s/Mpc: both the tail and the bulk move under a change of prior that leaves the mode in place. Post-hoc reweighting of the baseline samples to the same target prior recovers only $P=0.041$ in the tail, approximately 17% of the directly sampled shift. The three prior variants that carry an independent nested sampling evidence agree to $Δ\ln Z\lesssim 1.8$, so the data show at most a weak preference among the distance priors; the tail and bulk shifts are therefore properties of the prior, not a data update. Targeted mode-isolated runs reveal a $(d_L,ι)$ bimodality whose high-$H_0$, low-$d_L$ branch (Mode B; $|\ln\mathcal{B}_{\rm B/A}|<1$) the volumetric prior assigns negligible mass: this is the mechanism behind the reweighting deficit. The reweighted posterior has a lower effective sample size than the baseline, independently flagging the coverage failure. The runtime budget makes full-sample prior-sensitivity reruns the default robustness tool for bright-siren cosmology, replacing post-hoc reweighting.

</details>


### [183] [Primordial Black Holes in a Radiation-Dominated Universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30641)
*Thomas W. Baumgarte,Katy Clough,Mary Gerhardinger,John T. Giblin,Amanda Miller*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: No AI summary available.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: No AI summary available.

Method: No AI summary available.

Result: No AI summary available.

Conclusion: No AI summary available.

Abstract: Primordial fluctuations frozen out during inflation re-enter the cosmological horizon and can collapse, leading to the formation of primordial black holes. We perform simulations of the direct collapse of over-dense regions re-entering the horizon during a radiation-dominated epoch, using full 3+1 general relativistic simulations with the BSSN formalism. Building on previous studies, we impose periodic boundary conditions and allow the matter content of the Universe to self-consistently drive its dynamics. We analyze the evolution of over-densities in both the collapse and dispersal regimes and find a threshold, $0.77<δ_c<0.83$, above which over-densities collapse and form primordial black holes. Our findings are consistent with previous analytic predictions as well as numerical studies that use different formalisms and computational approaches, and hence provide independent validation of those results.

</details>

### [184] [Improving Muon-Scattering Material Identification via Coarse Momentum Encoding and Unsupervised Domain Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30028)
*Yuxin Bao,Zhao Zhang,Pei Yu,Liangwen Chen,Weibo He,Yu Zhang,Yuhong Yu,Xueheng Zhang,Lei Yang,Zhiyu Sun*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种粗动量感知域自适应（CMADA）方法，结合粗动量分箱与无监督域自适应，在不依赖高精度动量测量的情况下实现宇宙射线μ子散射材料的精确识别，显著提升了同域和跨域识别准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙射线μ子散射在检测核材料等高密度违禁品方面具有潜力，但实际部署面临挑战。主要困难在于材料特性与μ子动量之间的耦合：宽泛的自然动量分布影响散射角，阻碍了明确的材料识别。

Method: 提出粗动量感知域自适应（Coarse Momentum-Aware Domain Adaptation, CMADA）方法，采用粗动量分箱（coarse momentum binning）结合无监督域自适应（unsupervised domain adaptation）学习可迁移的散射表示；此外，提出基于重复采样平均的精确审核模式（precision review mode）以进一步提升识别性能。

Result: 在同域识别中，无动量信息时准确率为62.15%，采用5分箱动量信息后提升至89.52%，精确审核模式下进一步达到93.37%。在跨域识别中，无监督域自适应框架将准确率从源域仅基线（source-only baseline）的71.71%提升至89.00%，且无需目标域标签。

Conclusion: CMADA方法通过粗动量分箱与无监督域自适应，有效解决了μ子动量未知导致的材料识别困难，在不依赖高精度动量测量和标签数据的前提下显著提升了识别准确率。

Abstract: Cosmic-ray muon scattering has shown considerable potential for detecting nuclear materials and other dense contraband, but practical deployment remains challenging. A major difficulty arises from the coupling between material properties and muon momentum, since the broad natural momentum distribution influences the scattering angle and prevents unambiguous material identification. In this work, we propose a Coarse Momentum-Aware Domain Adaptation (CMADA) method to enable precise identification of materials. Instead of relying on high-precision momentum measurements, the proposed framework adopts coarse momentum binning combined with unsupervised domain adaptation to learn transferable scattering representations. In addition, a precision review mode based on averaging repeated samplings was proposed to further enhances identification performance. The coarse momentum binning strategy improves same-domain identification accuracy from 62.15% without momentum information to 89.52% with 5-bin momentum information, and further to 93.37% (precision review mode). Furthermore, the proposed unsupervised domain adaptation framework improves the cross-domain identification accuracy from 71.71% for the source-only baseline to 89.00% without requiring target domain labels.

</details>


### [185] [Test of a partly instrumented highly compact and granular electromagnetic calorimeter in an electron beam of 1 to 6 GeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30181)
*Adrián Irles*

Main category: physics.ins-det

Method: 采用硅-钨（silicon-tungsten）结构：钨吸收板与薄硅垫传感器（silicon pad sensor）结合；基本有源单元为紧凑硅夹层（Compact Silicon Sandwich, CSIS），集成了硅垫传感器、信号路由、高压分配和机械支撑；模块组装在专用的硅探测器集成基础设施中完成。

Result: 部分装备的原型探测器在1–6 GeV电子束下进行了测试，给出了2025年束流测试活动的首次结果，包括最小电离粒子（minimum-ionizing particle, MIP）校准以及展示高粒度探测器中簇射发展（shower development）的初步事例显示（event displays）。

Conclusion: 这些结果是向验证该技术适用于LUXE实验和未来对撞机实验迈出的重要一步。

Abstract: Highly compact and finely segmented silicon-tungsten electromagnetic calorimeters are being developed within the FCAL collaboration for applications in the LUXE experiment at DESY and future electron-positron collider facilities. These detectors combine tungsten absorber plates with thin silicon pad sensors, providing a small effective Molière radius and high spatial granularity, which are essential for resolving nearby electromagnetic showers in high-occupancy environments.
  The fundamental active unit of this calorimeter concept is the Compact Silicon Sandwich (CSIS), integrating a silicon pad sensor together with signal routing, high-voltage distribution and mechanical support in a highly compact structure. The assembly of these CSIS modules is performed within a dedicated infrastructure for silicon detector integration.
  A partially instrumented prototype of such a calorimeter has been tested in an electron beam with energies between 1 and 6~GeV. First results from the 2025 test beam campaign are presented, including minimum-ionizing particle calibration and preliminary event displays illustrating the shower development in the highly granular detector. These results constitute an important step towards the validation of this technology for LUXE and future collider experiments.

### [186] [Detector-aware target definitions for full-event particle reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30485)
*Katharina Schäuble,Alessandro Brusamolino,Dolores Garcia,Jan Kieseler*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种探测器感知的目标定义方法（detector-aware target definition），通过基于单元能量共享的击点合并算法（hit-based merging algorithm）构建与探测器空间分辨率相匹配的训练标签，从而消除基于机器学习（ML）的粒子重建中的训练歧义，提升模型在动量响应与分辨率上的性能，并增强其对事件拓扑变化的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于机器学习的粒子重建方法虽然表现良好，但其训练目标未考虑探测器几何与分辨率（detector geometry and resolution），导致训练歧义（training ambiguities），引入对样本先验（sample priors）的依赖，并降低模型在事件拓扑（event topology）变化下的鲁棒性。

Method: 论文在基于GEANT4的通用探测器模拟框架下，定义了探测器感知目标（detector-aware targets），通过对量热器簇射（calorimeter showers）实施基于单元能量共享（cell-wise energy sharing）的击点合并算法，将探测器空间分辨率纳入标签构建过程；同时提出粒子流感知变体（Particle-Flow-aware variant），以保持带电粒子的一致性。

Result: 采用固定图神经网络（GNN）重建模型，使用合并目标在训练类似样本上提升了物理性能。更重要的是，在粒子成分和拓扑不同的独立样本上，采用粒子流感知合并目标（PF-aware merged targets）训练的模型展现出更优的动量响应（momentum response）与分辨率（resolution）。

Conclusion: 去除实验上不可分辨的目标结构（experimentally non-resolvable target structure）不仅能提升重建性能，还能增强模型对依赖于过程的事件拓扑变化（process-dependent variations in event topology）的鲁棒性。

Abstract: Hit-level ML-based particle reconstruction methods have recently shown promising results. However, the reconstruction models are currently provided with targets that are unaware of the detector geometry and its resolution, resulting in training ambiguities. This can introduce a dependence on sample priors and reduce robustness under changes in event topology. We study the effect of a detector-aware target definition in the context of end-to-end Particle Flow reconstruction using a generic GEANT4-based detector simulation. We introduce the concept of detector-aware targets built from calorimeter showers with a hit-based merging algorithm based on cell-wise energy sharing that takes into account the spatial resolution of the detector. This includes a Particle-Flow-aware variant that preserves charged-particle consistency. Using a fixed GNN-based reconstruction model, we show that merged targets improve physics performance on a training-like sample. More importantly, models evaluated on an independent sample with different particle composition and topology show improved momentum response and resolution when trained with PF-aware merged targets. Our results show that removing experimentally non-resolvable target structure enhances not only reconstruction performance, but also improves model robustness against process-dependent variations in event topology.
