### [187] [A Path-Space Formulation of Prediction in World Models: From a Single Action to Prediction, Planning, and Irreversibility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28751)
*Gunn Kim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出AI世界模型（world model）中预测的路径空间（path-space）表述，认为世界模型隐式定义的是未来轨迹的概率测度（probability measure）而非单步条件分布序列。在该框架下，预测、规划和不确定性统一于一个作用量泛函（action functional）；实验发现注意力不对称性（attention asymmetry）与数据不可逆性成正比，对称化注意力会抑制熵产生（entropy production）并选择性损害长程不可逆预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有世界模型通常将预测建模为单步条件分布（one-step conditional distribution）的序列，缺乏对轨迹整体概率结构的形式化描述。本文旨在建立一种路径空间表述，将预测、规划和不确定性统一在同一数学框架下，并探索不可逆性（irreversibility）在世界模型中的角色。

Method: 提出路径空间表述，认为世界模型隐式定义未来轨迹的概率测度；在潜动力学（latent dynamics）具有有效马尔可夫描述（effective Markovian description）的局域条件下，该路径测度取昂萨格-马赫卢普（Onsager-Machlup）形式。进一步将潜动力学分解为可逆（reversible）与不可逆（irreversible）分量，从模型滚动（rollouts）中引入可操作的熵产生度量，并在可控小规模注意力（attention）模型上进行实验验证。

Result: 在可控小规模注意力模型中，注意力不对称性在训练过程中被习得，且其程度与数据的不可逆性成正比。对称化已习得的注意力会抑制熵产生，并选择性降低对不可逆动力学的长程预测（long-horizon prediction）质量，同时保留弛豫预测（relaxational prediction）能力。

Conclusion: 不可逆性可作为预测性世界模型（predictive world model）的一种计算资源（computational resource）。更根本地，预测的基本对象应理解为未来路径上的分布，而非未来状态上的分布。

Abstract: We propose a path-space formulation of prediction in AI world models. Rather than sequences of one-step conditional distributions, we argue that a world model implicitly defines a probability measure over future trajectories. In the local regime where latent dynamics admit an effective Markovian description, this path measure takes the Onsager-Machlup form. Within this framework, prediction (most probable trajectory), planning (constrained optimization), and uncertainty (fluctuations) emerge as operations on a single action functional. We decompose the latent dynamics into reversible and irreversible components and introduce operational measures of entropy production from model rollouts. In controlled small-scale attention-based models, we find that attention asymmetry is acquired during training in proportion to the irreversibility of the data. Symmetrizing the learned attention suppresses entropy production and selectively degrades long-horizon prediction of irreversible dynamics while preserving relaxational prediction. These results suggest that irreversibility may serve as a computational resource for predictive world models. More generally, the fundamental predictive object is a distribution over future paths rather than states.

</details>


### [188] [MALOQ: Massively Accelerated Learning of Operators for Quantum Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28911)
*Manasa Kaniselvan,Alexander Maeder,Denghui Lu,Alexandros Nikolaos Ziogas,Mathieu Luisier*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出MALOQ框架，基于SO(2)-等变神经网络架构，用于大规模预测密度泛函理论（DFT）哈密顿量/密度矩阵，显著降低计算成本，支持从数个到10万原子的系统，并在超级计算机上实现可扩展训练与推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器学习算子模型虽能以较低计算成本预测DFT哈密顿量/密度矩阵，从而将电子结构计算扩展到以往不可行的尺度，但现有框架在处理大规模系统、大基组和多元素种类时仍面临效率与可扩展性瓶颈。

Method: MALOQ采用最先进的SO(2)-等变（SO(2)-equivariant）骨干架构，设计了用于处理高秩哈密顿量矩阵数据的定制数据预处理内核（custom data-processing kernels），并实现了原子图的可扩展边级分布式策略（edge-wise distribution）。

Result: 在现有最大分子哈密顿量数据集上训练时，MALOQ相比分子级分布式框架（molecule-wise-distributed framework）将每个训练周期（epoch）的时间降低超过30%，并支持任意大小的材料图推理。在Alps超级计算机上，针对3000–12000原子规模实现了可扩展训练（多达192块GPU）与推理（多达256块GPU）。

Conclusion: MALOQ通过SO(2)-等变架构与边级分布式策略，有效提升了大规模DFT矩阵预测的计算效率与可扩展性，为量子输运等电子结构应用提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Machine-learned (ML) operator models can be trained to predict density functional theory (DFT) Hamiltonian/density matrices at significantly reduced computational cost, thus extending electronic-structure calculations to previously unfeasible scales. Here, we introduce MALOQ (Massively Accelerated Learning of Operators for Quantum Transport), an application built to train on and predict electronic-structure matrices for systems made of few to 100k atoms, described by large basis sets, and covering a wide range of atomic elements. Based on a state-of-the-art, SO(2)-equivariant backbone architecture, MALOQ provides (i) custom data-processing kernels to handle high-rank Hamiltonian matrix data and (ii) a scalable edge-wise distribution of atomic graph(s). Trained on the largest molecular Hamiltonian datasets available today, it reduces time-per-epoch by over 30% compared to a molecule-wise-distributed framework, and enables inference on material graphs of arbitrary size. We demonstrate scalable training and inference for 3,000-12,000 atoms on the Alps supercomputer, up to 192 GPUs and 256 GPUs, respectively.

</details>


### [189] [On Surrogate Modeling of Static Response of AM Short-Fiber Thermoplastics Using Graph Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28996)
*Pharindra Pathak,Vipin Kumar,Trenton M. Ricks,Suhasini Gururaja,Siddhartha Srivastava*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出一种数据驱动的代理框架（surrogate framework），结合图神经网络（GNN）与长短期记忆网络（LSTM），对短纤维热塑性复合材料（SFT）的微观力学行为进行高效预测，精度接近高保真有限元（FE）模拟（R²≈0.98），计算成本降低超过两个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 短纤维热塑性复合材料（short-fiber thermoplastic composites）的力学响应受纤维取向、空间聚集和制造诱导孔隙等介观尺度（mesoscale）因素控制，具有显著空间变异性。传统介观有限元（finite element, FE）模型虽能解析该异质性，但对真实三维微结构的计算成本过高，难以工程应用。

Method: 基于微计算机断层扫描（micro-computed tomography）数据重建微结构，离散为Voronoi细胞以表征纤维相互作用邻域。每个细胞通过含基体损伤的非线性FE模拟进行均质化（homogenization），所得应力-应变曲线用于训练混合图神经网络-长短期记忆（Graph Neural Network-Long Short Memory, GNN-LSTM）架构，该架构同时编码微结构拓扑与历史依赖的力学演化。

Result: 代理模型对未见微结构的刚度与应力-应变行为预测精度R²≈0.98，计算成本相比高保真FE模拟降低超过两个数量级。结合实验标定的损伤定律发现，纤维取向、聚集和孔隙率共同决定局部有效刚度。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了一条物理信息驱动（physics-informed）、数据高效（data-efficient）的路径，可用于识别力学薄弱微结构区域，并加速短纤维热塑性复合材料（SFT）构件数字孪生（digital-twin）的开发。

Abstract: Short-fiber thermoplastic (SFT) composites are increasingly employed in lightweight aerospace and automotive structures owing to their favorable strength-to-weight ratio, high production rates, and recyclability. Unlike continuous-fiber systems, the mechanical response of SFTs is governed by mesoscale interactions among fiber orientation, spatial clustering, and manufacturing-induced porosity. These features exhibit significant spatial variability in manufactured components and influence stiffness, damage initiation, and nonlinear deformation. Although mesoscale finite element (FE) models can resolve such heterogeneity, their application to realistic three-dimensional microstructures remains computationally intractable.
  A data-driven surrogate framework is proposed to predict the mechanical behavior of additively manufactured, compression-molded (AM-CM) SFTs. Microstructures reconstructed from micro-computed tomography data were discretized into Voronoi-based cells representing distinct fiber-interaction neighborhoods. Each cell was homogenized via nonlinear FE simulations incorporating matrix damage, and the resulting stress-strain responses trained a hybrid Graph Neural Network-Long Short-Term Memory (GNN-LSTM) architecture encoding microstructural topology and history-dependent mechanical evolution.
  The surrogate accurately predicts stiffness and stress-strain behavior of unseen microstructures, achieving $R^2\approx 0.98$ relative to high-fidelity FE simulations with over two orders-of-magnitude reduction in computational cost. Coupling the framework with experimentally calibrated damage laws demonstrates that fiber orientation, clustering, and porosity collectively govern local effective stiffness. The approach provides a physics-informed, data-efficient pathway to identify mechanically weak microstructural cells and accelerate digital-twin development for SFT components.

</details>


### [190] [Interpretable Inverse Design of Metal-Organic Frameworks with Large Language Model Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29459)
*Kyungmin Nam,Seunghee Han,Jihan Kim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出LLM4MOF框架，利用大语言模型（language model）智能体在无需针对每个目标单独训练模型的情况下，通过可解释的假设驱动循环，在金属有机框架（MOF）的反向设计（inverse design）中高效搜索高性能结构，并在吸附、分离和电子结构等六项任务中优于随机搜索和遗传算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金属有机框架（metal-organic frameworks, MOFs）的反向设计面临组合空间巨大（combinatorially vast）、属性标签获取昂贵（expensive property labels）以及大多数机器学习模型无法揭示结构成功原因等挑战。现有方法缺乏对设计背后化学原理的可解释性（interpretability）。

Method: LLM4MOF采用闭环框架（closed-loop framework），包含两个语言模型智能体：一个提出关于金属节点、连接子（linker）、孔隙几何结构（pore geometry）和功能化学（functional chemistry）的可解释设计假设，另一个将其转化为约束条件以选择候选MOF。每个假设通过四条诊断束（diagnostic beams）测试，每条束应用假设的不同子集，从而揭示几何、化学或金属选择对性能的影响。整个过程在10轮自主迭代中完成，无需为每个目标训练单独的模型。

Result: 在六项吸附（adsorption）、分离（separation）和电子结构（electronic-structure）任务中，LLM4MOF在仅400次属性评估内将搜索集中于高性能结构。该框架还能从头设计（de novo）新的MOF，并在实时模拟中验证，根据所请求的条件调整几何结构。其性能优于随机搜索（random search）和遗传算法（genetic algorithm），每次运行成本约为1美元。

Conclusion: LLM4MOF证明，语言模型智能体能够运行可解释的、基于模拟（simulation-grounded）的反向设计，而无需针对每个目标训练模型，为MOF材料设计提供了一种高效且可解释的新范式。

Abstract: Inverse design of metal-organic frameworks (MOFs) requires searching a combinatorially vast space where property labels are expensive and most machine-learning models reveal little about why a structure succeeds. We introduce LLM4MOF, a closed-loop framework in which language-model agents reason about chemistry, build candidate MOFs, and test them in simulation, refining hypotheses over ten autonomous iterations. One agent proposes interpretable design hypotheses over metal nodes, linkers, pore geometry, and functional chemistry, and a second translates them into constraints that select candidate MOFs, each made of a metal node, organic linker, and matching topology. Each hypothesis is tested through four diagnostic beams that apply different subsets of its constraints, so comparing them shows whether geometry, chemistry, or metal choice drives performance. Even when blind to the global property landscape of databases, LLM4MOF concentrates its search on top-performing structures across six adsorption, separation, and electronic-structure tasks within 400 property evaluations. The same loop also generates new MOFs de novo and validates them in live simulation, where it adapts the geometry to each requested condition, outperforming random search and a genetic algorithm at roughly $1 per campaign. LLM4MOF shows that language-model agents can run interpretable, simulation-grounded inverse design without training a model per objective.

</details>


### [191] [STEMGym: Benchmarking Sequential Decision-Making under Dose Budgets in Autonomous Electron Microscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29592)
*Can Polat,Erchin Serpedin,Mustafa Kurban,Hasan Kurban*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过STEMGym基准测试发现，在扫描透射电子显微镜（STEM）的自主成像中，决定剂量效率的主导因素是分析感知管线（analyst/perception pipeline），而非导航策略（navigator）。任务专用CNN配合简单光栅扫描即可显著提升DEC-AUC，而贝叶斯或自适应导航方法并无统计显著增益，生产级视觉-语言模型（vision-language models）也远不如任务专用CNN。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主科学成像（autonomous scientific imaging）的主流假设是更智能的导航（如贝叶斯、强化学习等）是提升样本效率的关键。本研究旨在检验该假设，探究在STEM这一每次测量都会施加电子剂量的原子级成像模态中，真正决定剂量效率的因素是什么。

Method: 作者构建了STEMGym，一个基于OpenAI Gymnasium的开源基准测试平台，包含15个物理模拟的STEM场景，覆盖5种材料、3个难度等级和4种表征任务。采用剂量效率曲线面积（Dose-Efficiency Curve area, DEC-AUC）作为统一标量指标，在33种智能体配置下，比较不同导航策略与感知管线对剂量效率的影响。

Result: 训练好的CNN分析器配合朴素光栅扫描，DEC-AUC比无CNN的光栅基线提升了5.5倍（0.287 vs. 0.052）；而将光栅替换为贝叶斯或自适应有限状态机导航后，未观察到统计显著的进一步增益。生产级视觉-语言模型在晶体缺陷分析任务上比任务专用CNN表现差约13倍。

Conclusion: STEMGym通过在同一剂量预算下解耦感知、导航与规划，重新界定了机器学习在自主电子显微镜中应投入的方向，即感知管线比导航策略更值得关注，并提供了验证这一结论的测量基础设施。

Abstract: A central premise of autonomous scientific imaging is that smarter navigation, whether Bayesian, RL-based, or otherwise adaptive, is the principal lever for sample-efficient acquisition. We present evidence to the contrary in scanning transmission electron microscopy (STEM), an atomic-resolution imaging modality whose every measurement deposits damaging electron dose. We introduce STEMGym, an open-source Gymnasium benchmark of 15 physics-simulated STEM worlds spanning five materials, three difficulty levels, and four characterisation tasks, scored by the Dose-Efficiency Curve area (DEC-AUC), a single scalar capturing the information-vs-dose Pareto frontier. Across 33 agent configurations under realistic dose budgets, the dominant determinant of dose efficiency is the analyst (perception) pipeline, not the navigator: pairing a trained CNN analyst with naïve raster scanning raises DEC-AUC by 5.5x over a CNN-free raster baseline (0.287 vs.\ 0.052), while substituting Bayesian or adaptive finite-state-machine navigation for raster yields no statistically significant further gain. Production-tier vision-language models further underperform task-specific CNNs by {\sim}13x on crystallographic defect analysis. By decoupling perception, navigation, and planning under a unified dose budget, STEMGym reframes where ML effort should be invested in autonomous electron microscopy and provides the measurement infrastructure to test it.

</details>


### [192] [I-BBS: Coordinate-Free Inference of Latent Sub-Manifolds Using Random Distance Matrix Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29675)
*Igor Halperin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 论文提出I-BBS方法，仅从高维距离矩阵中识别低维潜流形（latent sub-manifold）的几何结构，通过两种生成噪声模型混合潜信号与离流形成分，利用噪声下依然稳定的整数特征（非Perron多重态的重数及其收缩规律）恢复潜几何，在合成球面S¹、S²、S³上比连续谱斜率更鲁棒，且可盲测恢复流形与噪声模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Bogomolny、Bohigas与Schmit（BBS）发现，从光滑d维流形上采样N个点构造的成对距离矩阵（pairwise distance matrix）的谱中蕴含底层几何结构的特征。但该方法在面对高维嵌入空间中噪声混合潜信号与离流形成分时，无法逐个特征值解读潜几何，因此需要一种坐标无关（coordinate-free）且抗噪声的推理方法。

Method: 提出I-BBS（Inference-BBS）方法，不依赖高维向量空间，仅从距离矩阵出发识别低维潜子流形。将环境嵌入（ambient embedding）建模为两类生成噪声——基于模型（model-based）与无模型（model-free），噪声使潜信号与离流形成分混合导致特征值集体重组。从噪声中提取两个整数稳定的签名（integer-stable signatures）：顶部非Perron多重态（non-Perron multiplet）的重数（multiplicity）确定维度d，以及该多重态位置随噪声增长而收缩的无参数规律（parameter-free law）。

Result: 在合成球面S¹、S²、S³上，整数签名在噪声下远优于连续谱斜率（continuous spectral slope）的稳定性；盲测（blind test）可仅从单一距离矩阵同时恢复流形结构与噪声模型。该方法应用于神经网络表征及动态训练机制的结果在两篇配套论文中展开。

Conclusion: I-BBS提供了一种坐标无关、仅依赖距离矩阵的潜流形几何推断框架，通过整数稳定签名有效抵抗噪声干扰，在合成几何上验证了方法的鲁棒性与可识别性，并具备向机器学习表征等实际场景拓展的潜力。

Abstract: Bogomolny, Bohigas and Schmit (BBS) found that the spectrum of the pairwise distance matrix on N points sampled from a smooth d-dimensional manifold encodes a signature of the underlying geometry. We develop I-BBS (Inference-BBS), a coordinate-free method that identifies a low-dimensional latent sub-manifold embedded in a high-dimensional ambient distance matrix alone, without accessing an ambient high-dimensional vector space. It therefore applies even when that space is only partly observable or undefined. We model the ambient embedding by two classes of generative noise, model-based and model-free. The noise mixes the latent signal with off-manifold components, so the eigenvalues reorganise collectively and the latent geometry cannot be read off eigenvalue by eigenvalue. We recover it instead from two integer-stable signatures that survive the noise: the multiplicity of the top non-Perron multiplet, which fixes $d$, and a parameter-free law for how the multiplet positions shrink as the noise grows. On synthetic spheres $S^1$, $S^2$ and $S^3$ these integer signatures are far more stable under noise than the continuous spectral slope, and a blind test recovers both the manifold and the noise model from a single distance matrix. Applications to neural-network representations and to the dynamic training regime are developed in two companion papers.

</details>


### [193] [Atompack: A Storage and Distribution Layer for Read-Heavy Atomistic ML Training Datasets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29975)
*Ali Ramlaoui,Daniel T. Speckhard,Sagar Pal,Fragkiskos D. Malliaros,Alexandre Duval,Victor Schmidt*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出 Atompack——一种面向原子机器学习数据集的追加式存储格式与分发层，通过高效追加记录、提交不可变索引和内存映射读取路径，在训练场景下实现比 HDF5、LMDB、ASE 等基线快 96 倍的乱序读取速度并减小约 79% 的工件体积。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数据格式（如 HDF5、LMDB、ASE）主要针对交互式科学策展（interactive scientific curation）设计，适应可变记录和临时检查，但无法高效支持机器学习训练中大规模不可变快照的重复读取、乱序混洗和跨集群分发。Atompack 旨在填补这一空白。

Method: Atompack 采用追加式存储（append-oriented storage），在数据集构建时高效追加完整分子记录，之后提交一个不可变索引（immutable index）并发布只读工件。服务读取时通过内存映射（memory-mapped）路径直接提供记录，无需字段分块或对象重建，专为训练流水线中随机化顺序消耗完整分子记录的工作负载优化。

Result: 在代表性 64 原子工作负载上，与 ASE LMDB 相比，Atompack 在乱序训练风格读取上快 96 倍，同时生成的工件大小减小约 79%。实验还对比了顺序读取、共享文件系统行为、写入吞吐量等指标。

Conclusion: Atompack 证明，面向完整分子记录提供服务（而非字段分块或重建对象）能够显著提升训练吞吐量，同时保持工件足够紧凑以适用于公共分发。该格式瞄准的是机器学习训练与科学策藏两种工作负载之间的差异。

Abstract: Atomistic machine learning datasets are increasingly used for training: large immutable snapshots are read repeatedly, shuffled across epochs, staged across clusters' storage systems, and republished as reusable scientific artifacts. This workload differs from interactive scientific curation, where mutable records and ad hoc inspection are often more important than random indexed throughput. We present Atompack, an append-oriented storage format and distribution layer designed around a simple workload: training pipelines usually consume complete molecular records, while the order of records is randomized by the learning algorithm. Atompack appends records efficiently during dataset construction, then commits an immutable index and serves records through a memory-mapped read path optimized for training. We compare Atompack with HDF5, LMDB, and ASE baselines representing array stores, key-value records, serialized records, and object-oriented databases. The benchmarks measure sequential reads, shuffled reads, shared-filesystem behavior, write throughput, and artifact size. On a representative 64-atom workload, Atompack is 96x faster than ASE LMDB on shuffled training-style reads while producing artifacts about 79\% smaller. The results indicate that serving complete molecule records, rather than field chunks or reconstructed objects, improves shuffled training throughput while keeping artifacts compact enough for public distribution.

</details>

TL;DR: 本文提出纳米技术分子优化（NMO）基准套件，用量子模拟替代代理评分函数，对生成式分子设计模型提出严格结构约束与崎岖适应度景观要求；发现先进方法反而表现劣于简单方法，并开发了新基线方法，在物理性质上超越现有最优水平，揭示未知结构基序。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: NMO基准套件用量子模拟（quantum simulation）替换代理评分函数（proxy oracles），并引入严格协议，优先考虑科学实用性而非排行榜导向的过拟合。作者设计了基于物理的NMO任务，施加硬结构约束（hard structural constraints）和崎岖适应度景观（rugged fitness landscapes）。作为基线，提出了一种新方法，包含用于建模结构约束的新型分子表示和消除制药数据集偏差的领域无关预训练策略（domain-agnostic pretraining strategy）。

Result: 实验结果表明，先进的分子优化方法在NMO任务上反而不如更简单的方法。作者提出的新基线方法在物理性质上超越了当前最优（state-of-the-art）水平，并揭示了此前未知的结构基序（structural motifs）。

Conclusion: NMO基准为机器学习社区提供了严格的测试平台，同时可作为纳米技术研究的发现引擎。实验结果证明，机器学习能够推动真正的科学发现，为纳米技术领域提供了新的见解。

Abstract: Generative molecular design is shaped by simple proxy benchmarks for drug-like properties and models pretrained on large pharmaceutical datasets. This combination yields strong benchmark metrics but limits transferability to domains structurally distinct from drug discovery. To overcome this limitation and drive discovery toward real, scientifically grounded targets, we introduce the Nanotechnology Molecular Optimization (NMO) Benchmark, which bridges machine learning (ML) and quantum materials science. NMO acts simultaneously as a rigorous testbed for the ML community and a discovery engine for nanotechnology research. The suite replaces proxy oracles with quantum simulations and introduces strict protocols that prioritize scientific utility over leaderboard-oriented overfitting. The physics-based NMO tasks impose hard structural constraints and rugged fitness landscapes, posing fundamentally new requirements on generative models. Notably, advanced molecular optimization methods underperform much simpler approaches on the NMO tasks. We develop a new baseline method identifying the critical components to solve the NMO tasks, including a novel representation for modeling structural constraints and a domain-agnostic pretraining strategy to eliminate pharmaceutical dataset bias. Our results surpass state-of-the-art physical properties and reveal previously unknown structural motifs, offering new insights for the nanotechnology community and demonstrating that ML can drive genuine scientific discovery.

### [195] [Scalar Representations of Neural Network Training Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30384)
*Pedro Jiménez-González,Miguel C. Soriano,Lucas Lacasa*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出将神经网络训练轨迹视为时间网络（temporal network），并应用标量嵌入（scalar embedding）方法将其降至一维。实验表明，该低维表示保留了原始高维参数空间的主要动力学特征，包括对初始条件的敏感性、最大李雅普诺夫指数（Lyapunov exponent）的重建，以及渐近训练状态的统计特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经网络训练过程在高维损失景观（loss landscape）中演化，但大量可训练参数使得直接分析其动力学非常困难。因此，需要一种方法将高维训练轨迹简化为低维表示，以便于研究和可视化优化过程的动态特性。

Method: 将神经网络训练轨迹建模为时间网络，并采用针对时间网络的标量嵌入策略，将其降至一维标量时间序列。使用在MNIST分类任务上训练的多层感知机（multilayer perceptron）进行验证。

Result: 标量嵌入保留了原始参数空间的主要动力学特征，包括对特定学习率区间内初始条件敏感性的再现，以及网络最大李雅普诺夫指数的准确重建。基于嵌入轨迹定义的类李雅普诺夫时间（Lyapunov time）捕捉了原始高维系统中相近轨迹之间的典型去相关时间。渐近状态的间距分布经重标度后在不同初始条件下呈现一致的偏态对数正态分布（skew lognormal distribution）。

Conclusion: 标量低维嵌入为研究和可视化神经网络优化轨迹的动力学特性提供了一种有效的框架。

Abstract: Training in artificial neural networks can be viewed as a trajectory evolving through a high-dimensional loss landscape. However, the large number of trainable parameters makes the direct analysis of these dynamics challenging. In this work, we treat such training trajectories as temporal networks and apply recently proposed strategies for the scalar embedding of temporal networks. We investigate whether such a scalar embedding provides a meaningful low-dimensional representation of neural network training dynamics. Using a multilayer perceptron trained on the MNIST classification task, we show that the embedding preserves the main dynamical features observed in the original parameter space, including the emergence of sensitivity to initial conditions for specific learning rate regimes and an accurate reconstruction of the network's maximum Lyapunov exponent. We then use the embedded scalar trajectory to define a characteristic time, analogous to a Lyapunov time, after which the exponential separation between initially close embedded trajectories saturates. This characteristic time captures the typical decorrelation time between initially close network trajectories in the original high-dimensional system. Finally, we investigate the statistical organization of asymptotic training states through a spacing observable defined in the embedded space. We find that the distributions of rescaled asymptotic spacings collapse onto a common form across initial conditions and are compatible with a skew lognormal distribution. Altogether, our results suggest that scalar low-dimensional embeddings provide a useful framework for studying and visualizing the dynamical properties of neural network optimization trajectories.

</details>

### [196] [Detector-Output Instability near the Kesten-Stigum Boundary: Separating Hard Readout, Relaxation, and Fixed-Point Dispersion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30346)
*Faruk Alpay,Baris Basaran*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 本文研究社区检测（community detection）算法的多解输出分布，通过三种配对可观测量（硬划分变化信息、残差门控不动点变化信息、信念传播边际场的无截断Jensen-Shannon距离）系统分解Kesten-Stigum相变边界附近的检测器行为，定量刻画了信噪比、极化截断、读出不稳定性与残差门控的分离效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 社区检测算法通常只返回单次划分，但不同初始化或数据扰动常产生多个合理输出，这种多解性的定量刻画缺乏系统方法。

Method: 提出三种配对可观测量：硬划分变化信息（hard-partition variation of information, VI）、残差门控不动点VI（residual-gated fixed-point VI）、信念传播边际场的无截断Jensen-Shannon距离（cutoff-free Jensen-Shannon distance between belief-propagation marginal fields）。在对称稀疏随机块模型（symmetric sparse stochastic block model, SBM）上，对信念传播在非信息不动点附近线性化，结合高重数自举审计（high-replication bootstrap audit）和真实网络（政治博客图、六个SNAP图）上的无标签Bethe-Hessian模量边际检验进行验证。

Result: 硬VI最大值在可检测侧呈现有限大小、依赖读出的检测曲线，典型信噪比snr^⋆ ≃ 1.05–1.10；极化截断从0.001移至0.1使snr^⋆在1.047–1.128间漂移。非平凡读出激活服从snr_50(τ)-1 = 0.0086 + 0.522τ。长时间预算残差门控可分离读出与临界慢化：snr=1.05和1.10时硬VI分别为1.49和1.58比特但门控子集VI为零，snr=1.15–1.30时几乎所有运行通过门控且VI从1.31降至1.24比特。N=100000高重数审计不支持零渐近幂律，发现小平台snr^⋆-1 ≃ 0.024。真实网络上无标签测量保持有效，异质网络在强边子采样后仍保留零假设显著结构。

Conclusion: 在Kesten-Stigum边界附近实现了检测器输出的三部分分解（硬读出、松弛动力学、不动点场离散），为社区检测多解性的定量理解提供了系统框架。

Abstract: Community-detection algorithms usually return a single partition, even when independent initializations or small data perturbations yield several plausible outputs. We probe this output distribution through three paired observables: hard-partition variation of information (VI), a residual-gated fixed-point VI, and a cutoff-free Jensen-Shannon distance between belief-propagation (BP) marginal fields. For the symmetric sparse stochastic block model, linearizing BP around the uninformative fixed point gives the Kesten-Stigum onset at $\mathrm{snr}=(c_{\rm in}-c_{\rm out})/(q\sqrt{c})=1$. The hard VI maximum is instead a finite-size, readout-dependent detector curve on the detectable side, typically $\mathrm{snr}^\star \simeq 1.05\text{-}1.10$; moving the polarization cutoff from 0.001 to 0.1 shifts it across 1.047-1.128. The nontrivial-readout activation obeys $\mathrm{snr}_{50}(τ)-1 = 0.0086 + 0.522\,τ$ ($R^2=0.996$). Long-budget residual gating separates readout and critical slowing from fixed-point dispersion: at $\mathrm{snr}=1.05$ and 1.10 the hard VI is 1.49 and 1.58 bits but the gated subsets have zero VI, whereas from 1.15 to 1.30 nearly all runs pass the gate and retain VI 1.31 down to 1.24 bits. A high-replication audit through $N=100000$ disfavors a zero-asymptote power law and finds a small plateau $\mathrm{snr}^\star-1 \simeq 0.024$ (graph-bootstrap 90% interval [0.0227, 0.0316]). On real networks, a label-free Bethe-Hessian modularity margin with a Chung-Lu null gate is run on political blogs and six SNAP graphs: the measurement stays label-free, while heterogeneous networks can retain null-significant structure even after strong edge subsampling. The result is a detector-output decomposition near the Kesten-Stigum boundary, reporting hard readout, relaxation dynamics, and fixed-point-field dispersion separately.

</details>

### [197] [Monotonic Impurity Entropy beyond Unitarity: the $\mathscr{PT}-$Symmetric Quantum Impurity Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28495)
*Pradip Kattel,Abay Zhakenov,Natan Andrei*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文研究了一个 $\mathscr{PT}$ 对称的量子杂质模型（quantum impurity model），通过可积格点实现和贝特拟设（Bethe Ansatz）方法求解，发现在库仑屏蔽（Kondo-screened）区域中，尽管边界相互作用是非酉的，杂质熵仍从紫外（UV）的 $\ln 4$ 单调下降到红外（IR）的 $0$，超越了 $g$ 定理的标准假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子杂质模型在酉系统中对库仑屏蔽、边界临界性和杂质熵的研究已较为成熟，但在非厄米多体体系中的行为尚缺乏探索。本文旨在填补这一空白，研究 $\mathscr{PT}$ 对称非厄米边界相互作用对这些现象的影响。

Method: 采用可积格点实现，结合 $\mathscr{PT}$ 对称边界杂质，通过贝特拟设（Bethe Ansatz）求解，并与有限温矩阵乘积态（matrix-product-state）计算进行交叉验证，从而提取杂质对自由能和熵的贡献。

Result: 在库仑屏蔽区域，谱保持完全实值，杂质被多体库仑云屏蔽；杂质熵从紫外（ultraviolet）的 $\ln 4$ 单调递减到红外（infrared）的 $0$。这一单调流在非酉边界相互作用下仍然成立。

Conclusion: 该发现表明，即使在非厄米且超出 $g$ 定理（$g$-theorem）标准假设的体系中，熵的单调递减行为依然存在，为理解非厄米多体系统中的边界物理提供了新视角。

Abstract: Quantum impurity models provide a paradigmatic setting for studying Kondo screening, boundary criticality, and impurity entropies. While these phenomena are well understood in unitary systems, their fate in non-Hermitian many-body settings remains largely unexplored. We study a $\mathscr{PT}$-symmetric quantum impurity model consisting of a unitary $SU(2)_1$ Wess--Zumino--Witten bulk coupled to two impurity spins through complex-conjugate boundary Kondo interactions. Using an integrable lattice realization with $\mathscr{PT}$-symmetric boundary impurities, solved by the Bethe Ansatz and benchmarked against finite-temperature matrix-product-state calculations, we determine the impurity contribution to the free energy and entropy. In the Kondo-screened regime, where the spectrum remains entirely real and the impurities are screened by many-body Kondo clouds, we find that the impurity entropy decreases monotonically from $\ln 4$ in the ultraviolet to $0$ in the infrared. This monotonic flow persists despite the nonunitary nature of the boundary interaction, which places the system beyond the standard assumptions of the $g$-theorem.

### [198] [Vortex-enhanced photovoltaic current in disordered topological materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28509)
*Pavlo Sukhachov,Penghao Zhu,Ella Banyas,Liang Z. Tan,A. Alexandradinata*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文揭示无序拓扑材料中，实空间晶体缺陷与动量空间波函数奇异性（光学偶极矩阵元相位的涡旋结构）协同增强体光伏电流。该光学涡旋性（optical vorticity）由非平凡陈数（Chern number）保证，通过增强电子-杂质斜散射（skew scattering）产生弹道光伏电流，其频率指数和张量约束对拓扑材料类、缺陷对称类及光偏振敏感，并在多类拓扑体系中得到具体验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索无序拓扑材料中晶体缺陷与波函数拓扑奇异性之间的相互作用如何影响并增强体光伏电流（bulk photovoltaic current），并揭示其背后的物理机制与可观测特征。

Method: 从理论上论证了光学偶极矩阵元（optical dipole matrix element）的相位在动量空间中具有涡旋结构（vortex structure），即光学涡旋性（optical vorticity），该结构存在于所有陈数（Chern number）非平凡的拓扑材料中，并驱动电子-杂质斜散射（skew scattering）产生弹道光伏电流（ballistic photovoltaic current）。通过多折叠费米子（multifold fermions）、三维m阶外尔半金属（Weyl semimetals）及二维n阶狄拉克体系（Dirac systems，包括n层菱方石墨烯、过渡金属二硫化物和拓扑表面态）等案例进行了具体分析。

Result: 弹道光伏电流对拓扑材料类、晶体缺陷对称类及光偏振三类因素（a-c）敏感，表现为两种可观测特征：(1) 拓扑半金属中光伏电流的频率指数 $\propto ω^{\text{exponent}}$ 依赖于（a-c）；(2) 体光伏张量的约束条件依赖于（a-c），且仅能通过时间反演不变（time-reversal-invariant）拓扑材料中涌现的磁对称性（magnetic symmetries）来解释。

Conclusion: 为结合频率调谐光电导测量、缺陷表征与缺陷工程的三管齐下实验方案提供了理论指导，建立了一条通过缺陷工程调控拓扑材料光伏响应的可行路径。

Abstract: In disordered topological materials, real-space crystalline defects interplay with momentum-space wave function singularities to \textit{enhance} the bulk photovoltaic current. What's singular is the interband Berry phase, or equivalently the phase of the \textit{optical} dipole matrix element, which has a \textit{vortex} structure in momentum space. Such \textit{optical vorticity} is guaranteed to exist in all topological materials associated with nontrivial Chern numbers. These vortices enhance electron-impurity skew scattering, which manifests as a ballistic photovoltaic current that is sensitive to (a) the topological material class, (b) the symmetry class of crystalline defects, and (c) the light polarization. This sensitivity manifests in two ways: firstly, by (a-c)-dependent frequency exponents for the photovoltaic current $\propto ω^{\text{exponent}}$ in topological semimetals, with $ω$ the frequency of the light source. Secondly, by (a-c)-dependent constraints of the bulk photovoltaic tensor, which are explainable only by emergent, \textit{magnetic} symmetries of \textit{time-reversal-invariant} topological materials. These ideas are concretized by case studies on multifold fermions, 3D $m$-order Weyl semimetals and 2D $n$-order Dirac systems, which include $n$-layer rhombohedral graphene, transition metal dichalcogenides, and topological surface states. Theoretical guidance is provided for a tri-pronged experimental program that combines frequency-tuned photoconductivity measurements, defect characterization and defect engineering.

</details>


### [199] [Mixed-spin Heisenberg ladders in a magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28521)

Method: 采用密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group, DMRG）数值方法与线性自旋波（linear spin-wave）解析近似，通过变化 $J_\perp$ 和 $h$ 的扫描分析，并结合有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）方法研究横向自旋关联函数（transverse spin correlation functions）以确定临界点。

Conclusion: 交替混合自旋海森堡梯子的相行为受链间耦合 $J_\perp$ 和磁场 $h$ 共同调控，1/3 磁化平台的存在与否取决于 $J_\perp$ 的符号与大小，且该平台通过 Kosterlitz-Thouless 相变闭合，验证了数值方法与解析方法在描述该体系临界行为上的一致性。

Abstract: In this work, we study alternating mixed-spin $(s,S)$ Heisenberg ladders in the magnetic field $h$ using density matrix renormalization group and linear spin-wave calculations. The $h$ \textit{versus} interchain coupling $J_\perp$ phase diagram for the $(1/2,1)$ case is investigated in detail. { In particular, we demonstrate the compatibility between the critical line estimates and magnetic ordering by analyzing chains with variable values of $J_\perp$ and of $h$ along the chain, $J_\perp$ and $h$ scans, and considering the usual case of chains with uniform couplings}. The magnetization plateau at 1/3 of saturation magnetization, 1/3 - plateau, is observed for $J_\perp>0$ and in a limited range for $J_\perp<0$. The critical Kosterlitz-Thouless transition point, where the 1/3 - plateau closes, is identified through a finite-size analysis of the transverse spin correlation functions.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 测量了UNi₄B在不同磁场方向下的霍尔电阻率（Hall resistivity），包括面内场下的ρ_{yz} (H∥x, I∥z)和ρ_{zx} (H∥y, I∥x)以及面外场下的ρ_{yx} (H∥z, I∥x)，并采用常规霍尔效应的经验关系式对数据进行分析，结合对称性论证和已有磁结构信息进行磁空间群的约束。

Conclusion: 提出Cm'或Pm'磁对称性（取决于非磁母空间群）与霍尔电阻率、中子衍射和磁电效应测量结果一致，从而为UNi₄B的磁结构提供了新的对称性约束。

Abstract: The zero-field and applied-field Hall effects in noncollinear antiferromagnets provide evidence for topological states of matter and are tied to materials' magnetic symmetry. For UNi$_4$B, the antiferromagnetic state with $T_\mathrm{N}=20$ K at zero and low magnetic field is debated due to recent magnetoelectric measurements and theory work calling into question the proposed toroidal arrangement of magnetic dipole moments. For a magnetic field applied within the plane of uranium magnetic moments, the field-dependent Hall resistivity of UNi$_4$B shows a curved response for $ρ_{yz}$ ($H{\parallel}x$, $I{\parallel}z$) and $ρ_{zx}$ ($H{\parallel}y$, $I{\parallel}x$) up to $\sim$8 T at 2 K, while an out-of-plane field results in linear behavior of $ρ_{yx}$ ($H{\parallel}z$, $I{\parallel}x$) up to 16 T. Analysis using conventional empirical relationships for the Hall effect indicate that an intrinsic effect from momentum-space Berry curvature contributes significantly to the curved transverse resistivity. Moreover, a finite zero-field Hall effect emerges at the onset of magnetic order for $ρ_{yz}$ and $ρ_{zx}$, further supporting an intrinsic origin of the Hall response. Symmetry arguments for a finite Berry curvature, an observable magnetoelectric effect, and reported magnetic structures suggest that the previously proposed magnetic space groups for the zero-field magnetic structure cannot account for the observed finite zero-field effect for two Hall orientations. Instead, we propose that $Cm'$ or $Pm'$ magnetic symmetry, depending on the parent nonmagnetic space group, is consistent with Hall resistivity, neutron diffraction, and magnetoelectric effect measurements.

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了费米子拓扑序特有的反常结构，拓展了Kitaev十六重方式的费米子对应，并为通过高维SPT边界实现这些拓扑序提供了系统框架与格点构造。

Abstract: Fermionic topological orders can host 't Hooft anomalies with no bosonic counterpart. We identify a new sixteen-fold family of (2+1)D fermionic topological orders, forming a fermionic analogue of Kitaev's sixteen-fold way. This family is distinguished by the mod 16 't Hooft anomaly of a $\mathbb{Z}_2$ one-form symmetry, generated in each theory by a single nontrivial $\mathbb{Z}_2$ anyon. This intrinsically fermionic anomaly permits anyon spins that are forbidden in bosonic phases; the simplest new example is an Abelian fermionic topological order containing a single $\mathbb{Z}_2$ Abelian anyon of spin 1/8. Each theory can be realized as the gapped boundary of a (3+1)D fermionic symmetry-protected topological (SPT) phase protected by the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ one-form symmetry, which acquires a $\mathbb{Z}_{16}$ classification once the spacetime spin structure is twisted by the one-form symmetry. We realize these phases microscopically via lattice models built from Walker-Wang models coupled to local fermions.

Abstract: Strong correlations and ferromagnetic Hund's coupling lead to diverse electronic phenomena in transition-metal oxides that sensitively depend on the $d$-orbital electron filling. Fullerides, their $p$-electron counterparts, exhibit effective antiferromagnetic Hund's coupling in a different energy range. At half-filling ($n=3$, three electrons in triply degenerate orbitals), both $d-$ and $p$-electron systems are Mott insulators due to strong correlations and Hund's coupling. Away from half-filling, in single-electron/hole ($n=1,5$) $d$-orbital systems, Hund's coupling opposes the correlations, reducing the Mott gap and allowing survival of metallicity. Here we report a single-hole multiorbital correlated $p$-electron system, orthorhombic-structured Yb$_2$CsC$_{60}$ comprising pentavalent C$_{60}^{5-}$ anions, which also exhibits a robust metallic state with no Mott transition, just like in the metastable single-electron cubic-structured CsC$_{60}$. We assert that particle-hole symmetry holds well in ($n=1,5$) fullerides and that their $p$-electron-derived states are analogous to those in $d$-orbital solids, providing impetus for further study of these correlated systems.

### [203] [Nonequilibrium electron-phonon dynamics with high momentum resolution: Thermalization bottlenecks and the effects of phonon dispersion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28855)
*Maksymilian Środa,Philipp Werner*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用基于量子-张量-列车（quantics-tensor-train, QTT）的非平衡格林函数（nonequilibrium Green's function, NEGF）框架，对具有任意声子色散的大尺度晶格进行动量分辨的非平衡电子-声子动力学模拟，揭示了超越传统声子窗口瓶颈效应的复杂弛豫瓶颈层级结构。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用QTT-NEGF框架，利用量子-张量-列车（quantics-tensor-train）对双时格林函数进行高内存效率表示，在高达256×256格点规模的晶格上实现具有完整电子-声子反馈的动量分辨模拟。

Result: 揭示了扩展声子窗口瓶颈效应的弛豫瓶颈层级：对于光学声子，确认了主声子能量窗口并发现一个缩减窗口；识别出声子热化中的独立瓶颈，源于动量依赖的粒子-空穴连续谱耦合。对于声学声子，声子能量窗口呈现显著的动量依赖性，缩减窗口不对称，低动量声子模式存在持续瓶颈。谱的高动量与频率分辨率进一步揭示了声子弛豫与电荷响应之间的直接对应关系。

Abstract: The nonequilibrium electron-phonon interplay is central to thermalization of solids, yet the microscopic picture of transient states and relaxation pathways remains incomplete. Previous nonequilibrium Green's function (NEGF) studies were restricted to local phonons and local self-energy approximations, leaving momentum-dependent dynamics largely unexplored. In this work, we demonstrate the power of the recently developed quantics-tensor-train (QTT) NEGF framework through large-scale lattice simulations with arbitrary phonon dispersions. QTTs provide a memory-efficient representation of two-time Green's functions, enabling momentum-resolved simulations with full electron-phonon feedback on lattices up to 256x256 sites. Comparing optical and acoustic phonon models, we reveal a hierarchy of relaxation bottlenecks that extends the well-known phonon-window bottleneck effect. For optical phonons, we confirm the main phonon-energy window and uncover a reduced window separating momentum-space regions of excess and deficit electronic population. We also identify a separate bottleneck in phonon thermalization, rooted in the momentum-dependent coupling to the particle-hole continuum. For acoustic phonons, the phonon-energy window acquires pronounced momentum dependence dictated by simultaneous energy-momentum conservation. The reduced window becomes asymmetric; directional scattering between Brillouin-zone regions creates a persistent bottleneck for low-momentum phonon modes. The high momentum and frequency resolution of our spectra further reveals a direct correspondence between phonon relaxation and charge response. Our results establish QTT-NEGF simulations as a scalable and controlled framework for quantitative nonequilibrium electron-phonon dynamics, overcoming previous lattice-size and propagation-time limitations and providing accurate reference data for time-resolved spectroscopies.

### [204] [Unusual upper critical field in UTe2 revealed by magnetotransport measurements up to 42 T](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28904)
*Macha Méplan,Ilya Sheikin,Pierre Pugnat,Romain Barbier,François Debray,Cédric Grandclément,Steffen Krämer,Yuriy Krupko,Frédéric Molinié,Kévin Paillot,Robert Pankow,Rolf Pfister,Luc Ronayette,Benjamin Vincent,Charles Simon,Midori Amano Patino,Gérard Lapertot,Georg Knebel,Dai Aoki*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过高磁场（最高42 T）下的磁电阻测量，研究了重费米子超导体UTe2在磁场沿(bc)平面不同角度时的超导相行为。研究发现，SC3相首次出现在偏离b轴20°方向，在更大角度下其起始点低于反铁磁转变场Hm，但零电阻态仅在Hm以上达到。此外，21°和24°方向SC3相的温度稳定性不同，并在c轴附近观测到Shubnikov de Haas振荡。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对高质量UTe2单晶在静磁场（最高42 T）下沿(bc)平面施加不同角度的磁场，在0.35 K低温下进行磁电阻测量，构建场-角相图（field-angle phase diagram）。

Result: SC3相首次在偏离b轴20°处出现；在更大角度下，SC3相起始点（以电阻率最大值定义）低于Hm，但零电阻态在所有研究角度下仅在Hm以上达到。21°处SC3相随温度升高迅速被抑制，而24°处其鲁棒性更强，可持续至约1 K。在c轴附近观测到Shubnikov de Haas振荡，其频率与先前结果一致。

Conclusion: SC3相可能并非完全局限于Hm以上的自旋极化态，因为其在较大角度下起始于更低的磁场，但零电阻条件仍要求系统进入自旋极化区域。不同角度下SC3相的温度稳定性差异表明该相的微观机制具有角度依赖性。

Abstract: The heavy-fermion superconductor UTe2 is unique in that, at ambient pressure, it exhibits three distinct superconducting phases, two of which are induced by magnetic field. When the field is applied along the crystallographic b axis in the orthorhombic structure, the field-induced phase SC2 develops above approximately 20 T and persists up to the metamagnetic transition at Hm about 34 T. When the magnetic field is tilted towards the c axis, another superconducting phase, SC3, emerges at very high fields above about 40 T over a certain angular range. The origin of this exotic phase remains under debate. One of the key open questions regarding the origin of SC3 is whether it is confined to the spin-polarized state above Hm, or whether it already develops at lower fields. Here, we report magnetoresistance measurements performed on a high-quality single crystal of UTe2 in static magnetic fields up to 42 T applied in the (bc) plane at temperatures down to 0.35 K. At this temperature, we find that the SC3 phase first appears at an angle of 20 deg from the b axis. At larger angles, the onset of the SC3 phase, defined by a maximum in resistivity, occurs below Hm. However, zero resistivity is reached only above Hm throughout the entire angular range investigated. These results are summarized in the resulting field-angle phase diagram. Furthermore, we find that at 21 deg the SC3 phase is rapidly suppressed with increasing temperature, whereas at 24 deg it becomes considerably more robust and persists up to about 1 K. Finally, we observe Shubnikov de Haas (SdH) oscillations in the vicinity of the c axis. The observed oscillation frequencies are in good agreement with our previous results. The field dependence of the strongest SdH frequency and of the effective mass is discussed.

Abstract: The kagome metal ScV$_6$Sn$_6$ has attracted attention as a platform for exploring the interplay between charge density wave (CDW) order and symmetry-breaking phenomena, including a recently reported intermediate phase and a low-field Hall anomaly that has been attributed to an anomalous Hall effect (AHE). We resolve a sequence of closely spaced transitions in the immediate vicinity of $T_{CDW}$ that emerges above a sharp threshold of RRR $\approx 4$, and demonstrate through elastoresistivity that the intermediate phase breaks the three-fold rotational symmetry of the parent lattice. These results refine the symmetry-breaking landscape of ScV$_6$Sn$_6$ and establish systematic mobility tuning as a diagnostic for disentangling an intrinsic AHE from multi-band Hall contributions in kagome CDW systems.

### [206] [Winding-Sector Transitions and Thermodynamic Incommensurability in Helical Valence Bond Phase under Tilted Boundary Conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29242)

<details>

Method: 采用投影量子蒙特卡洛（projector quantum Monte Carlo）模拟方法；引入 45° 倾斜周期性边界条件（tilted periodic boundary condition）以消除中间相；定义畴壁密度（domain wall density）量化螺旋价键相的空间调制，并进行热力学极限外推（thermodynamic extrapolations）。

Conclusion: 螺旋价键相是热力学极限下具有长程键-键序（long-range bond-bond order）的真正二维非公度相；扇区跃迁并非本征相变，而是由边界公度性（boundary commensurability）施加的有限尺寸效应。

Abstract: We investigate the ground states of the $S = 1/2$ staircase $J$-$Q_3$ model in the maximally anisotropic limit by employing projector quantum Monte Carlo simulations. To overcome boundary-induced finite-size ambiguities inherent in the study of spatially modulated structures, we implement a $45^{\circ}$ tilted periodic boundary condition that eliminates intermediate phases and provides direct access to winding-sector transitions of the system. By defining a domain wall density to quantify the spatial modulation of the helical valence bond phase, we perform thermodynamic extrapolations and demonstrate that both the domain wall density and the characteristic wavevector evolve continuously with the coupling ratio, exhibiting no commensurate lock-in behavior. Our results establish that the helical valence bond phase is a genuine two-dimensional incommensurate phase with long-range bond-bond order in the thermodynamic limit, clarifying that winding-sector transitions are finite-size effects enforced by boundary commensurability. Furthermore, we determine the phase transition point between columnar valence bond solid phase and helical valence bond phase to be $g_c = 0.046(2)$.

Method: 通过求解泊松-薛定谔方程（Poisson-Schrödinger equations）对实验器件中的有限层厚进行建模，得到垂直方向的电子波函数；结合从实验提取的无序能量，估算弱无序最低朗道能级（lowest Landau level）中的电荷能隙（charge gap）与迁移率能隙（mobility gap）。

The finite layer thickness is modeled by solving the Poisson-Schrödinger equations for the experimental devices, yielding the electron wave functions in the perpendicular direction. Using these and the disorder energy extracted from the experiment, we estimate the charge gap and the mobility gap at $ν=1/3$ in the weakly disordered lowest Landau level. Remarkably, both gaps show good quantitative agreement with the activation gap measured from the experiment in narrow quantum wells. Our results also indicate the potential need of incorporating higher subbands to make accurate theoretical predictions of the energy gap in wide quantum wells.

### [208] [What Does the Single-Particle Spectrum Imply on the Pairing Nature and Pairing Mechanism in La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29470)
*Yu-Bo Liu,Zhi-Yan Shao,Zhiming Pan,Chen Lu,Fan Yang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过分析沿布里渊区（Brillouin zone, BZ）对角线的配对能隙（pairing gap）行为，区分了双层镍氧化物La₃Ni₂O₇中的多种配对机制。对称性分析表明，轨道杂化（orbital hybridization）沿BZ对角线消失，使得基于d_{z²}轨道杂化驱动的配对机制必然在α/β-pocket上产生能隙节点（gap nodes），与实验观测的全能隙（full gap）矛盾；而基于Hund耦合（Hund's rule）的d_{x²-y²}轨道主导配对机制则给出全能隙，与角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）和扫描隧道显微镜（STM）结果一致。弱耦合（weak-coupling）理论同样产生节点或近节点，与实验不符，从而确立了Hund耦合驱动的配对机制为最主要机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双层镍氧化物La₃Ni₂O₇的超导配对机制（pairing mechanism）仍存在激烈争论。现有的强耦合（strong-coupling）理论分为层内d波配对和层间s波配对两类，后者又进一步分为d_{z²}轨道杂化驱动和d_{x²-y²}轨道Hund耦合驱动两种机制。实验（ARPES和STM）一致揭示了无节点的全能隙（nodeless full pairing gap），支持s波配对，但具体轨道起源尚不明确，亟需理论辨明。

Method: 采用对称性分析（symmetry analysis）考察布里渊区（Brillouin zone, BZ）对角线上的配对能隙行为；结合随机相位近似（random-phase-approximation, RPA）进行弱耦合计算，对比理论预言与ARPES和STM实验观测结果。

Result: 对称性分析表明，轨道杂化沿BZ对角线消失，因此γ-pocket上的能隙反映d_{z²}轨道配对强度，α/β-pocket上的能隙反映d_{x²-y²}轨道配对强度。d_{z²}轨道杂化驱动机制必然在α/β-pocket沿BZ对角线产生能隙节点，与ARPES的全能隙结果和STM的U形dI/dV曲线矛盾。Hund耦合驱动的d_{x²-y²}轨道主导机制则给出全能隙，与实验吻合。弱耦合RPA计算同样倾向于d_{z²}轨道主导配对，沿BZ对角线在α/β-pocket上产生节点或近节点，与实验冲突。

Conclusion: 本文的分析明确了d_{x²-y²}轨道在配对中的主导作用，并确立了Hund耦合（Hund's rule）驱动的配对机制为La₃Ni₂O₇中最相关的配对机制。

Abstract: The pairing mechanism of the bilayer nickelates La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ remains a hotly-debated open question. Existing strong-coupling theories are divided into class favoring intralayer d-wave pairing and that favoring interlayer s-wave pairing, with the latter further divided into $d_{z^2}$ orbital dominated mechanism driven by orbital hybridization and $d_{x^2-y^2}$ orbital dominated mechanism driven by Hund's rule. Recent angle-resolved-photoemission-spectrum (ARPES) and scanning-tunneling-microscope (STM) combinedly reveal a nodeless full pairing gap with low anisotropy, supporting the s-wave pairing. Here we propose that the pairing gap along the Brillouin zone (BZ) diagonal can serve as a useful probe of pairing mechanism. Symmetry analysis suggests that orbital hybridization vanishes along the BZ diagonal, rendering that the pairing gaps on the $γ$- and $α/β$- pockets reflect the $d_{z^2}$- and $d_{x^2-y^2}$- orbital pairing strength respectively. Under the $d_{z^2}$ orbital dominated pairing mechanism driven by orbital hybridization, gap nodes are inevitable on the $α$- and $β$- pockets along the BZ diagonal, which conflicts with the full gap revealed by ARPES and the U-shaped dI/dV curve observed by STM. The Hund's rule driven pairing mechanism instead leads to a full pairing gap, which well fits the ARPES and STM results. Furthermore, through a random-phase-approximation based calculation, we show that the weak-coupling theory, which tends to yield a $d_{z^2}$-orbital dominated pairing, also leads to nodes or near-nodes on the $α$- and $β$- pockets along the BZ diagonal, conflicting with experiments. This analysis clarifies the dominant role of $d_{x^2-y^2}$ orbital in the pairing and establishes the Hund's rule driven pairing mechanism as the most relevant one in La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$.

*Lauro B. Braz,Steffen Bötzel,Frank Lechermann,Igor Plokhikh,Rustem Khasanov,Luis G. G. V. Dias da Silva,Ilya M. Eremin*

Conclusion: 建立了La₃Ni₂O₇中有序态的层次结构，提供了环境压力相与超导高压相之间的关键联系；在已有实验文献背景下讨论结果，并提出了进一步实验检验建议以阐明自旋密度波/密度波（SDW/DW）态的起源。

Abstract: The low-pressure phase diagram of La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ provides an important reference for understanding its pressure-induced high-temperature superconductivity. While the spin-density-wave transition at $T_{\text{SDW}}\approx150$ K is increasingly well established, the origin of the second density-wave transition at $T_{\text{DW}}\approx130$ K has remained unresolved. Here, we perform unrestricted Hartree-Fock calculations to investigate the potential origin of the second transition. {Within the orthorhombic phase, the degeneracy between possible ordering wavevectors at $\boldsymbol{Q}_{Y}=(0,π)$ and at $\boldsymbol{Q}_{X}=(π,0)$ is lifted and the electronic system} develops a double-stripe spin-density wave with ordering vector $\boldsymbol{Q}_{Y}=(0,π)$. We identify that the pure double stripe spin state is unstable in La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ towards a commensurate charge-density wave instability, which favors a spin-modulated double stripe order with intertwined charge and spin instabilities and establish the hierarchy of ordered states in La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$, providing an important link between its ambient-pressure and superconducting high-pressure phases. We further discuss our results in the context of available experimental literature and propose further experimental tests to elucidate the origin of the SDW/DW states in this system.

### [210] [Trimers in the Extended Hubbard Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30176)

Method: 采用密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group, DMRG）计算，估计相分离线（phase separation, PS）和交叉线（crossover lines）。

Abstract: The Lieb theorem is a cornerstone of quantum magnetism theory in condensed matter. In this work, we investigate the instability of the Lieb insulating ferrimagnetic phase in the extended Hubbard model on a trimer chain at half-filling, with one electron per site, under increasing the nearest-neighbor Coulomb coupling $V$. Our results show that despite a noticeable increase in doublon density with $V$, the ferrimagnetic insulating phase remains robust up to the phase separation (PS) line, which is observed at $V \gtrsim U/4$, where $U$ is the local Coulomb repulsion. Above the PS line, one of the coexisting phases is primarily populated by doublons on one of the two sublattices of the chain. This phase coexists with a metallic, unsaturated ferromagnetic phase for $U \gtrsim t$, and with a singlet phase for $U \lesssim t$, where $t$ is the intra-trimer hopping amplitude. ### [211] [NQS-Agent: Health-Aware Agentic Hyperparameter Optimization for Neural-Network Quantum States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30464)
*Jia-Qi Wang,Xiao-Qi Han,Ze-Feng Gao,Rong-Qiang He,Zhong-Yi Lu*

Conclusion: 评估 NQS 结果时应考虑优化轨迹的稳定性和恢复历史。健康感知 HPO 提供了一种可复现的调优协议，其意义超越了仅选择单次最低能量计算的传统做法。

Abstract: Neural-network quantum states (NQS) provide expressive variational representations for strongly correlated quantum many-body systems, but their practical accuracy depends sensitively on architecture-level hyperparameters and optimization schedules. Here we develop NQS-Agent, an implemented open-source software framework for health-aware hyperparameter optimization (HPO) in NQS calculations. Its workflow monitors energy trajectories, detects destructive optimization events, stops unstable calculations, modifies the learning-rate schedule, resumes optimization from safe checkpoints, and ranks candidates with an anomaly-aware score. We demonstrate the approach on a residual convolutional NQS for the square-lattice Heisenberg $J_1$-$J_2$ model, using architectures with parameter counts comparable to aCNN, a convolutional NQS architecture used here as a reference. The results show that NQS-Agent improves over the reported human-tuned aCNN baseline for the aCNN reference architecture and identifies a structurally distinct wide-and-shallow competitive candidate within the parameter-count-matched residual-CNN search space. These results show that the stability and recovery history of an optimization trajectory should be considered when assessing an NQS result. Health-aware HPO therefore provides a reproducible tuning protocol that goes beyond selecting a single lowest-energy calculation.

*Wojciech Niedziółka,Jacek Wojtkiewicz*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究利用相互作用费米子基态能量的密度展开公式，检验了哈伯德模型在五种受挫晶格（包括面心立方晶格）上的基态铁磁有序问题。结果表明，在受挫晶格上，即使在中等甚至低密度下，大多数模型确实展现出铁磁基态，这支持了晶格结构是哈伯德模型出现铁磁性的关键因素的猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 凝聚态物理和数学物理中长期悬而未决的问题之一是，证明某些哈伯德模型（Hubbard model）的基态能够呈现铁磁有序（ferromagnetic ordering）。已有猜想认为晶格结构是关键因素：在简单立方晶格上不太可能出现铁磁有序，但在受挫晶格（frustrated lattices）上，即使磁矩载体密度较低，铁磁性也可能自然产生。本研究旨在对这一问题进行检验。

Method: 采用Lieb、Seiringer和Solovej在连续情形下严格证明、Giuliani在简单立方晶格上验证的相互作用费米子基态能量公式，作为“密度展开”（density expansion）的首项。假设该展开同样适用于某些其他晶格，将其应用于五种受挫晶格，其中包括面心立方晶格（face-centered cubic lattice）。

Result: 大多数在受挫晶格上建立的模型，在中等甚至低密度下确实具有铁磁基态。虽然该方法不能被视为基态铁磁性的严格证明，但结果强烈表明铁磁性的存在。在某些情况下，铁磁性出现在低密度区域，这为未来证明密度展开收敛性并严格证明“丰富铁磁性”（wealthy ferromagnetism）提供了希望。

Conclusion: 研究结果支持了晶格受挫结构是哈伯德模型出现铁磁有序的关键因素的猜想。尽管采用的密度展开方法并非严格证明，但所得证据已足够有力。低密度区域出现铁磁性的发现，为后续开展严格的数学证明指明了可能方向。

Abstract: One of the long-standing and only partially solved problems of theoretical condensed matter physics and mathematical physics is to demonstrate that ground states of some of the versions of the Hubbard model can exhibit a ferromagnetic ordering. It has long been speculated that the opportunity crucial for the occurrence of ferromagnetism is the structure of the lattice on which the Hubbard model is formulated \cite{TasakiMB}. As a consequence, while on simple cubic lattices no ferromagnetic ordering seems to be possible, it can naturally arise, even for low densities of magnetic moment carriers, on so-called frustrated lattices.
  We investigate the problem of ground state ferromagnetic ordering with the use of the formula for ground-state energy of interacting fermions as the first term of `density expansion', proven rigorously by Lieb, Seiringer and Solovej \cite{fermi exact} in continuum and by Giuliani \cite{hub exact} for the simple cubic lattice. Assuming that analogous expansion holds also for certain another lattices we apply this formula to five frustrated lattices -- among them to the face-centered cubic one. The hypothesis is confirmed: most of examined models formulated on frustrated lattices do indeed have ferromagnetic ground states already for densities being moderate or even low. Although the approach adopted cannot be treated as a rigorous proof that the ground state is ferromagnetic, the results obtained here strongly indicate that it can be the case. Moreover, as in some cases FM occurs at low densities, one can hope that it would be possible to prove convergence of the density expansion and prove rigorously the occurrence of `wealthy ferromagnetism' in these cases.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.other'></div>

# cond-mat.other [[Back]](#toc)

### [213] [Electromagnetic response of two interacting topological insulator spheres in external fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28982)
*J. Cornejo Gómez,M. Ibarra-Meneses,L. Medel Onofre,A. Martín-Ruiz*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文研究了嵌入电介质中的两个球形拓扑绝缘体在均匀外电场下的静态电磁响应。通过分片常数轴子场（axion field）描述带隙表面态，利用双球坐标系对静电场问题进行了零阶精确求解，并在精细结构常数（fine-structure constant）的一阶导出场论中计算了磁电耦合（magnetoelectric coupling）诱导的响应，给出了诱导矢量势与磁场的闭合级数表示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然单个球形拓扑绝缘体（topological insulator）的电磁响应已有研究，但多个球体之间的相互作用特别是磁电耦合（magnetoelectric coupling）诱导的磁静力学（magnetostatics）效应尚缺乏严格解析处理。作者旨在建立一个可解析控制的框架，以描述耦合球状磁电系统（magnetoelectric systems）中的相互作用诱导磁静力学。

Method: 采用分片常数轴子场（piecewise constant axion field）描述球界面上的能隙表面态，将问题归约为各向同性磁电介质（isotropic magnetoelectric media）的静电问题。使用双球坐标系（bispherical coordinates）对外电场平行与垂直于球心连线的两种取向进行零阶静电场的精确求解，模式展开由三项递推关系（three-term recurrence relations）确定，并通过微扰方法在球体不重叠条件下求解。磁电耦合诱导的响应在有效耦合强度（effective coupling strength）的一阶导场中计算。

Result: 诱导源（induced sources）纯为界面性质，在平行与垂直两种几何构型下产生截然不同的磁静场（magnetostatic field）分布。获得了诱导矢量势（vector potential）与磁场的闭合级数表示，该表示由零阶静电系数（zeroth-order electrostatic coefficients）表达。

Conclusion: 本文为耦合球状磁电系统提供了可解析控制的磁静力学描述，揭示了界面磁电耦合在不同几何取向下诱导的不同磁场构型。该形式框架同样适用于更一般的各向同性磁电介质，具有良好的推广性。

Abstract: We study the static electromagnetic response of two spherical topological insulators embedded in a dielectric medium and subjected to a uniform external electric field. The gapped surface states are described by a piecewise constant axion field, which induces a topological magnetoelectric coupling localized at the spherical interfaces. {More generally, the same formalism applies to isotropic magnetoelectric media characterized by an effective scalar magnetoelectric response.} The electrostatic problem is solved at zeroth order using bispherical coordinates, allowing for an exact treatment of both parallel and perpendicular orientations of the external field relative to the center-to-center axis. The resulting mode expansions are determined by three-term recurrence relations, which are solved perturbatively for nonoverlapping spheres. The { magnetoelectric}-induced response is then computed to leading order in the fine-structure constant {(or, more generally, in the effective coupling strength)}. The induced sources are purely interfacial and generate distinct magnetostatic field configurations in the parallel and perpendicular geometries. Closed-form series representations for the induced vector potential and magnetic field are obtained in terms of the zeroth-order electrostatic coefficients. These results provide an analytically controlled description of {interaction-induced magnetostatics in coupled spherical magnetoelectric systems}.

</details>

### [214] [Lagrangian correspondences of nonabelian Hodge type and shifted twistor structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30637)
*Jacob Kryczka,Yuuji Tanaka,Shing-Tung Yau*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文在导出几何（derived geometry）框架下，将经典非阿贝尔霍奇理论（nonabelian Hodge theory）推广到完美复形（perfect complexes）模空间上，建立了平坦与Higgs完美复形的拉格朗日对应（Lagrangian correspondence），并证明了具有λ-联络的完美复形模叠（moduli stack）上的超凯勒（hyperkähler）型导出扭量结构（derived twistor structure），特别地，在光滑射影代数曲面上给出了Kapustin–Witten方程模空间的(-2)-移位预处理结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受Kapustin–Witten理论的启发，作者希望在更一般的完美复形框架下（特别关注曲面情形），建立经典非阿贝尔霍奇理论中Dolbeault与de Rham模空间之间的对应，并进一步研究其导出扭量结构。

Method: 利用Pantev–Toën–Vaquié–Vezzosi（PTVV）建立的移位辛几何（shifted symplectic geometry）理论，构造平坦与Higgs完美复形导出叠（derived stacks）之间的拉格朗日对应；结合AKSZ/PTVV递推（transgression）、拉格朗日交截（Lagrangian intersection）及（超凯勒）辛约化（symplectic reduction）定理，并在导出Riemann–Hilbert对应的相容性框架下分析移位预处理结构与辛形式的关系。

Result: 证明了光滑射影代数簇X上的解析Deligne–Hitchin–Simpson模叠具有一个次数为2(1−dim X)的移位预处理结构（shifted pretwistor structure）；特别地，光滑紧合复代数曲面上Kapustin–Witten方程模空间（模规范等价）展现出(−2)-移位的（预）处理结构作为ℙ¹_C上的族。

Conclusion: 该结果将经典非阿贝尔霍奇理论的导出几何推广到更广泛的完美复形模空间情形，建立了与移位辛结构相容的导出处理结构，并证实了长期预期的关于Deligne–Hitchin–Simpson模叠具有规范移位预处理结构的结论。

Abstract: Classical nonabelian Hodge theory identifies Dolbeault and de Rham moduli spaces by providing a real-analytic isomorphism. In this paper, motivated by the Kapustin--Witten theory, we study this correspondence in the more general framework of perfect complexes on proper varieties, paying special attention to the surface case. We establish a Lagrangian correspondence which relates the shifted symplectic geometries by Pantev--Toën--Vaquié--Vezzosi (PTVV) between the derived stacks of flat and Higgs perfect complexes.Furthermore, we investigate the existence of the derived twistor structure of hyperkähler type on the moduli stack of perfect complexes endowed with $λ$-connections by Deligne--Hitchin--Simpson. We establish a version of the AKSZ/PTVV transgression, Lagrangian intersection, and (hyperkähler) symplectic reduction theorems in this context. Moreover, we prove that the derived Riemann--Hilbert correspondence of Porta and Holstein--Porta, which states an equivalence of derived analytic stacks of perfect complexes on $X_{\mathrm{Betti}}$ and $X_{\mathrm{DR}}$, is compatible with the natural shifted--symplectic structures. We then study the relation between the shifted (pre-)twistor structures and the shifted symplectic forms on the fibers, and prove that the analytic Deligne--Hitchin--Simpson moduli stack on a smooth projective variety $X$ has a canonical $2(1-\dim X)$ shifted pretwistor structure over $\mathbb{P}^1_{\mathbb{C}}$, a result which has been anticipated for some time. In particular, the moduli stack of solutions to the Kapustin--Witten equations modulo gauge equivalence on a smooth proper complex algebraic surface exibits a $(-2)$-shifted (pre)twistor structure as a family over $\mathbb{P}^1_{\mathbb{C}}$.

</details>

### [215] [The topological susceptibility slope $χ^\prime$ in the large-$N$ limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29885)
*Claudio Bonanno*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文首次在非微扰（non-perturbative）框架下，利用格点规范理论（lattice gauge theory）在大$N$极限下确定了杨-米尔斯拓扑磁化率斜率（topological susceptibility slope）$χ^\prime$。该工作基于一种避免拓扑冻结（topological freezing）的新算法和一种可靠的格点计算方法，其结果对于通过Shore-Veneziano公式描述深度非弹性散射（deep inelastic scattering）中的质子自旋具有重要意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑磁化率斜率$χ^\prime$是拓扑荷密度两点关联函数动量展开中的$\mathcal{O}(p^2)$项，对强相互作用的理论和唯象学具有重要含义。此前在大$N$极限和精细格点上的计算受限于拓扑冻结问题，缺乏非微扰的格点测定。

Method: 基于一种避免大$N$精细格点上拓扑冻结现象的新型算法，以及一种能够在格点上可靠计算$χ^\prime$的新方法。

Result: 成功给出了大$N$极限下杨-米尔斯拓扑磁化率斜率$χ^\prime$的首个非微扰格点测定值。

Conclusion: 该计算结果为通过Shore-Veneziano公式描述深度非弹性散射实验中质子自旋的结构提供了相关理论依据。

Abstract: This paper presents the first non-perturbative lattice determination of the Yang--Mills topological susceptibility slope $χ^\prime$ in the large-$N$ limit. This quantity represents the $\mathcal{O}(p^2)$ term of the momentum expansion of the topological charge density two-point correlator, and has important theoretical and phenomenological implications for strong interactions. This calculation is based on a novel algorithm that avoids topological freezing at large $N$ on fine lattices, and on a novel method to reliably compute $χ^\prime$ on the lattice. The results of this study are relevant for the description of the proton spin in deep inelastic scattering experiments via the Shore--Veneziano formula.

### [216] [Quark and hybrid stars with renormalization group improvement of NNLO perturbative QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29576)
*Loïc Fernandez,Jean-Loïc Kneur,Marcus Benghi Pinto,Constança Providência,Claudia Ratti,Tulio E. Restrepo*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本工作将重整化群优化微扰论（renormalization-group-optimized perturbation theory, RGOPT）框架下的NNLO微扰QCD压强推广至β平衡与电荷中性条件，获得了致密夸克物质的状态方程（EoS），并给出了适用于N_f=2+1大质量夸克的紧凑拟合公式。基于该EoS，研究描述了纯夸克星和含夸克核的混合星，发现纯夸克星在X=3.08–3.58时与天文观测相容，而混合星在X≈2–2.98时可稳定存在并与大质量脉冲星PSR J0740+6620的质量观测一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前工作已在RGOPT框架下对冷密对称物质（cold dense symmetric matter）的NNLO微扰QCD压强进行了重求和，所得压强对重整化标度（renormalization scale）的敏感性低于标准NNLO微扰QCD结果。本文旨在将该方法推广至更接近真实中子星环境的β平衡（β-equilibrium）与电荷中性（charge neutrality）条件，从而获得更实际的状态方程。

Method: 在RGOPT框架下，对包含任意夸克质量的冷密物质在β平衡与电荷中性条件下的NNLO微扰QCD压强进行计算；提供了针对N_f=2+1大质量夸克的紧凑“口袋”拟合公式（pocket fitting formula），并给出不同重整化标度参数X（X≡Λ μ_B/3）下的EoS。基于该EoS，分别构建纯夸克星（pure quark star）与含夸克核的混合星（hybrid star with quark core），其中混合星采用三种基于相对论平均场（relativistic mean-field）描述的强子模型，以覆盖软与硬的状态方程。

Result: 纯夸克星在X=3.08–3.58范围内与天体观测相容；若将GW190814的低质量天体视为中子星，则需更大的X值（4.10）。混合星方面，在X≈2–2.60–2.98范围内可获得与大质量脉冲星PSR J0740+6620质量相容的稳定结构，其中最大标度对应半径5–8 km的大型夸克核，最小标度则对应星体中心的小型夸克核。

Conclusion: RGOPT框架下的微扰QCD状态方程可在适当的重整化标度参数取值下描述纯夸克星与混合星，并满足现有天文观测约束（如大质量脉冲星与引力波事件GW190814）。研究表明，不同X取值可导致夸克核大小显著变化，为未来通过多信使观测区分致密星内部组分提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Recently, the NNLO perturbative QCD pressure of cold and dense symmetric matter, with arbitrary quark masses, has been resummed within the renormalization-group-optimized perturbation theory (RGOPT) framework. By being imbued with renormalization group properties, the resulting pressure is less sensitive to renormalization scale ($Λ\equiv X μ_B/3$) variations than the NNLO perturbative QCD pressure. Here, we extend this by considering $β$-equilibrium and charge neutrality to evaluate the corresponding equation of state (EoS). We provide a compact ``pocket" fitting formula for the EoS for $N_f=2+1$ massive quarks at different renormalization scale parameter ($X$) values. We describe pure quark stars as well as hybrid stars with quark-cores. Pure quark stars compatible with astrophysical observations were obtained with $X=3.08-3.58$, whereas a larger value (4.10) is needed if the low mass object of the observation GW190814 represents a neutron star. Hybrid stars were built considering three representative hadron models based on a relativistic mean-field description, and chosen to produce soft and stiff EoSs. Stable hybrid stars with masses compatible with the massive pulsar PSR J0740+6620 were obtained considering $X$ of the order of 2 to 2.60-2.98, the largest scale giving rise to hybrid stars with a large quark core with a radius of 5 to 8 km, and the smallest to a small quark core at the center of the star.

</details>


### [217] [Nonequilibrium Andreev transport at the QGP-2SC interface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30521)
*Tingyu Zhang,Honoka Hoshino,Hiroyuki Tajima,Motoi Tachibana,Mariusz Sadzikowski*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文基于Schwinger-Keldysh框架和相对论隧穿模型，研究了夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）与两味色超导（2SC）夸克物质界面上的非平衡Andreev反射，发现该反射出现在隧穿强度的四阶，其行为与超导材料中的Andreev反射类似，并提出了致密物质界面强关联输运的场论路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动机在于探索致密星内部非平衡动力学中，QGP与2SC夸克物质界面处的强关联输运机制，特别是非平衡Andreev反射这一尚未被充分研究的量子过程。

Method: 采用Schwinger-Keldysh框架（非平衡量子场论）结合相对论隧穿模型（relativistic tunneling model），在化学势偏置下计算具有动量分辨的隧穿电流。

Result: Andreev反射出现在隧穿强度的四阶：QGP中的入射夸克转化为反射空穴（hole），同时一个库珀对（Cooper pair）注入2SC凝聚体中；当化学势偏置接近能隙（gap）时反射增强，超能隙区（supergap region）则被抑制，与超导材料行为类似。

Conclusion: 该公式为描述致密物质界面上的强关联非平衡输运提供了场论途径，对理解致密星（compact star）中的非平衡动力学具有潜在意义。

Abstract: We discuss a nonequilibrium Andreev reflection at an interface between quark-gluon plasma (QGP) and two-flavor color superconducting (2SC) quark matter. Based on the Schwinger-Keldysh framework and a relativistic tunneling model, we evaluate the momentum-resolved tunneling current generated by a chemical-potential bias between the QGP and 2SC phases. We find that the Andreev reflection appears as at the fourth order of the tunneling strength, in which an incident quark in QGP is converted into a reflected hole, while a Cooper pair is injected into the 2SC condensate. We show that the Andreev reflection is enhanced when the bias becomes comparable to the gap and is suppressed in the supergap region, which is similar to that in superconducting materials. The present formulation provides a field-theoretical pathway to strongly-correlated transport across dense-matter interfaces relevant to nonequilibrium dynamics in compact stars.

</details>

### [218] [Neural posterior estimation of Galactic Binary signals for the LISA mission](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29039)
*Tanguy Delmond,Natalia Korsakova,Thomas Oberlin,Sylvain Marsat,Antoine Basset,Nicolas Dobigeon*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文探索使用基于模拟的推断（simulation-based inference）方法，通过条件归一化流（conditional normalizing flow）作为神经后验估计器，对LISA任务中的银河系双星（galactic binaries）进行高效参数估计，无需显式计算似然，并能扩展到多个重叠源的分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LISA任务中银河系双星信号在时域和频域上高度重叠，传统贝叶斯推断方法（如马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛采样，Markov Chain Monte Carlo sampling）因问题的高维度和复杂的似然面（likelihood landscape）难以扩展，亟需一种可扩展的参数估计替代方案。

Method: 采用基于模拟的推断（simulation-based inference）框架，使用条件归一化流（conditional normalizing flow）构建神经后验估计器（neural posterior estimator）。模型通过专用模拟框架生成样本进行训练，无需任何似然计算；训练完成后可在无需显式似然评估的情况下，每秒生成数千个后验样本。

Result: 在窄频带单源场景下取得了有效结果，随后扩展到更宽频率范围。作为概念验证，进一步展示了两个重叠源这一更具挑战性的场景下的可行性。

Conclusion: 基于似然无关的推断（likelihood-free inference）方法有望成为分析LISA银河系双星时传统马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛采样的可扩展替代方案。

Abstract: ESA's LISA mission will open a new window onto the gravitational-wave sky by detecting signals from a wide variety of sources in the millihertz frequency band. Among these, galactic binaries are expected to be the most numerous sources observable by LISA. Their analysis and parameter estimation represent a significant challenge, as the signals are expected to strongly overlap in both the time and frequency domains. Conventional Bayesian inference approaches, such as Markov Chain Monte Carlo sampling, are difficult to scale to this setting due to the high dimensionality of the problem and the complicated likelihood landscape which can hinder convergence. In this work, we explore simulation-based inference as a means to perform efficient parameter estimation for single galactic binaries, with a potential extension to the analysis of multiple overlapping sources. Our approach relies on a conditional normalizing flow acting as a neural posterior estimator. The model is trained using samples generated according to a dedicated simulation framework that does not require any likelihood computation. Once trained, the neural posterior estimator enables the generation of thousands of posterior samples per second, again without explicit likelihood evaluation. We first present results for a single source in a narrow frequency band, and then extend the analysis to wider frequency ranges. As a proof of concept, we further investigate the more challenging case of two overlapping sources. These results demonstrate the potential of likelihood-free inference as a scalable alternative to conventional Markov chain Monte Carlo sampling for the analysis of LISA galactic binaries.

</details>


### [219] [A Covariance-Aware Framework for Spatially Resolved Exoplanet Biosignature Inference with the Solar Gravitational Lens](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29138)
*Slava G. Turyshev*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出一种协方差感知的太阳引力透镜（Solar Gravitational Lens, SGL）框架，通过时间标记的斯托克斯光谱立方体（Stokes spectral cube）重建系外行星图像与光谱，并对其在宜居性（habitability）和可能生物活动评估中的可行性、性能与信息增益进行了系统计算与分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估系外行星上可能存在生命需要空间、光谱、时间及环境背景信息，而非仅仅检测单一分子或表面特征；现有盘积分（disk-integrated）观测无法提供此类多维度背景，亟需一种能够实现表面分辨成像与区域光谱学的新方法。

Method: 开发了一个协方差感知的太阳引力透镜框架，数据产品为从波长相关的爱因斯坦环（Einstein-ring）测量重建的时间标记斯托克斯光谱立方体。模拟了距地球30 pc、半径与地球相当的系外行星在650 AU处以(128×128)光栅、128个同步光谱通道、R≈70的0.45–2.40 μm斯托克斯-I反射光观测；同时进行0.40–20 μm架构级计算以追踪反射与热光子、SGL增益、日冕噪声、仪器背景、通量、驻留时间及重建协方差。

Result: 受控总体审计（controlled population audit）中，结构前向模型失配保持了块排序（block ordering）：气体 > 表面 > 云/路径 > 矿物 > 校准/SGL，但将组合条件信息增益（combined conditional information gain）降至匹配模型值的0.83。重建协方差括号（reconstruction-covariance bracket）将(8×8)区域共加（regional coadd）增益从7.77降至3.00，意味着6.7倍的驻留时间惩罚（dwell penalty）。

Conclusion: 成像与低分辨率制图是更早期的目标，而全区域光谱学需要同步采集、亚ppm有效日冕校准、实测重建协方差及分支特定辐射度量验证。太阳引力透镜为表面分辨制图、区域光谱学、热气候诊断及共定位测试提供了独特而强大的路径，可提供超越盘积分前驱观测的空间、光谱、时间及环境背景，从而强化对宜居性和可能生物活动的评估。

Abstract: Assessing possible life on an exoplanet requires spatial, spectral, temporal, and environmental context rather than a threshold detection of one molecule or surface feature. We develop a covariance-aware Solar Gravitational Lens (SGL) framework in which the data product is a time-tagged Stokes spectral cube reconstructed from wavelength-dependent Einstein-ring measurements. The demonstrated calculation is a 0.45-2.40 um Stokes-I reflected-light simulation of an Earth-radius planet at 30 pc, observed from 650 AU with a (128 x 128) raster, 128 simultaneous spectral channels, and $R\simeq70$. A separate 0.40-20 um architecture-level calculation tracks reflected and thermal planet photons, SGL gain, solar-corona noise, instrumental backgrounds, throughput, dwell time, and reconstruction covariance. In the controlled population audit, structural forward-model mismatch preserves the block ordering gas > surface > cloud/path > mineral > calibration/SGL while reducing the combined conditional information gain to 0.83 of the matched-model value. A reconstruction-covariance bracket reduces an (8 x 8) regional coadd gain from 7.77 to 3.00, implying a 6.7-fold dwell penalty. The feasibility results are design scalings, not a mission verdict: imaging and low-resolution mapping are earlier objectives, whereas full regional spectroscopy requires simultaneous acquisition, sub-ppm effective coronal calibration, measured reconstruction covariance, and branch-specific radiometric validation. We show that the SGL offers a uniquely powerful path to surface-resolved mapping, regional spectroscopy, thermal-climate diagnostics, and co-location tests, providing spatial, spectral, temporal, and environmental context that could strengthen assessments of habitability and possible biological activity beyond disk-integrated precursor observations.

</details>
