# gr-qc [[Back]](#toc)

### [220] [Quantum corrections to symmetron fifth forces for planar sources](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28423)
*Peter Millington,Michael Udemba*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文对有限厚度平面源附近对称子（symmetron）第五力的量子修正进行了半解析计算，发现与经典预言相比，第五力在源的一个康普顿波长（Compton wavelength）内被抑制约10%，在更远处则被增强。该空间轮廓变化对当前及未来的力定律实验和几何优化具有重要参考价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在屏蔽标量-张量引力理论（screened scalar-tensor theories of gravity）中，对称子第五力的经典行为已有较多研究，但其量子修正效应尚缺乏系统分析。本文旨在通过半解析方法计算量子修正对第五力空间轮廓的影响，为实验检验和数值模拟提供基准。

Method: 采用半解析方法（semi-analytic calculation），对具有非零厚度（nonzero thickness）的平面源周围的对称子第五力进行量子修正（quantum corrections）计算。

Result: 在源的一个康普顿波长范围内，第五力的量子修正导致其相比经典预言被抑制约10%；在更远距离处，第五力则被增强。在CANNEX等实验相关的参数区域中，这种抑制效应达到了可观测量级。

Conclusion: 第五力空间轮廓的变化可能对当前及近未来的地面和天体物理力定律测试（tests of force laws）产生影响，并对原子干涉仪（atom interferometers）等实验几何构型的优化具有启示意义。该工作为未来量子修正第五力的数值研究提供了关键基准。

Abstract: We provide a semi-analytic calculation of the first quantum corrections to the symmetron fifth force around a planar source with nonzero thickness. We find a suppression of the fifth force compared with the classical prediction within a Compton wavelength of the source, which is of order 10% in the parameter region relevant to experiments like CANNEX, while the fifth force is enhanced at larger distances from the source. The resulting change in the spatial profile of the fifth force may be relevant to current and near future terrestrial and astrophysical tests of force laws, and has implications for the optimisation of experimental geometries, including atom interferometers. This work provides a key benchmark for future numerical studies of quantum-corrected fifth forces in screened scalar-tensor theories of gravity.

</details>


### [221] [Reverse Isoperimetric Conjecture as a Noether-Charge Stability Theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28427)
*Naman Kumar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明了反等周猜想（reverse isoperimetric conjecture）——即固定热力学体积下Schwarzschild–AdS黑洞熵最大——实质上是一个边界完备化的Noether荷稳定性定理。通过将体部的Hollands–Wald正则能与约束渐近荷Hessian结合，得到了可容许定容分量上的熵凹性，并将已知反例重新解释为紧致性、正性或刚性条件的失效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反等周猜想是黑洞热力学中的一个核心几何不等式，但其成立条件和物理机制尚不清晰。本文旨在揭示该猜想的深层变分结构，将其纳入更一般的Noether荷稳定性框架，并解释已知反例的根源。

Method: 论文识别出体部Hollands–Wald正则能（canonical energy）并非完整的熵Hessian——沿精确平稳黑洞族它为零，缺失的曲率由约束渐近荷Hessian（constrained asymptotic charge Hessian）补足。将这一边界项与体部正则能正性结合，推导出熵在可容许定容分量上的凹性，并利用零能刚性（zero-energy rigidity）确定等号成立情形。

Result: 定理再现了Einstein引力中的面积-体积不等式，并自然推广到高阶导数理论中的Wald熵。已知违反反等周猜想的案例可被重新解释为紧致性（compactness）、正性（positivity）或刚性（rigidity）条件的失败，而非变分机制本身的问题。

Conclusion: 反等周猜想是边界完备化的Noether荷稳定性定理在固定体积下的具体形式。这一变分框架统一了已知结果，厘清了猜想成立的先决条件，并为未来在更一般引力理论中分析黑洞熵极值问题提供了理论基础。

Abstract: The reverse isoperimetric conjecture asserts that, at fixed thermodynamic volume, Schwarzschild--AdS black holes maximize entropy. We prove that this statement is the fixed-volume form of a boundary-completed Noether-charge stability theorem. The essential observation is that the bulk Hollands--Wald canonical energy is not the full entropy Hessian: along exact stationary black-hole families it vanishes, and the missing curvature is supplied by a constrained asymptotic charge Hessian. Combining this boundary term with bulk canonical-energy positivity gives entropy concavity on admissible fixed-volume components, while zero-energy rigidity determines the equality sector. The theorem reproduces the Einstein-gravity area-volume inequality and extends naturally to Wald entropy in higher-derivative theories. Known violations are thereby reinterpreted as failures of compactness, positivity, or rigidity rather than failures of the variational mechanism.

</details>


### [222] [Thermodynamic Geometry, Heat Engines, and Topology of Sharma--Mittal ModMax-dRGT Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28468)
*Hassan Hassanabadi,Abdullah Guvendi,Dhruba Jyoti Gogoi,Semra Gurtas Dogan,Farokhnaz Hosseinifar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了ModMax非线性电动力学与dRGT-like有质量引力耦合下的带电AdS黑洞的热力学结构，引入Sharma–Mittal熵修正，分析了Weinhold几何、矩形热机效率以及修正温度和自由能的拓扑性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索ModMax非线性电动力学与dRGT-like有质量引力理论中黑洞的热力学与几何性质，特别是熵修正（Sharma–Mittal熵）对微观相互作用、热机效率以及拓扑相变的影响。

Method: 采用Weinhold度量（Weinhold metric）在由视界半径和电荷张成的参数空间中分析热力学几何；构造扩展相空间中的矩形黑洞热机（rectangular black hole heat engine）推导效率解析表达式；对修正温度和广义自由能进行拓扑分析（topological analysis），研究拓扑荷（topological charge）。

Result: 热力学Ricci标量（Ricci scalar）的曲率奇点标示了极端边界和热力学度量的退化；ModMax参数和有质量引力耦合通过焓基转换影响热机效率，Sharma–Mittal参数通过修正黑洞温度改变Carnot界；拓扑分析揭示了常规和新颖临界点及其守恒拓扑荷。

Conclusion: ModMax参数和有质量引力耦合对黑洞热力学几何、热机效率和拓扑结构具有显著调控作用，Sharma–Mittal熵修正进一步丰富了黑洞的相变和临界行为。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic structure of charged AdS black holes in ModMax nonlinear electrodynamics coupled to dRGT-like massive gravity, incorporating Sharma--Mittal entropy corrections. The thermodynamic geometry is analyzed using the Weinhold metric in the parameter space spanned by the horizon radius and electric charge. The resulting thermodynamic Ricci scalar characterizes effective microscopic interactions, with curvature singularities signaling extremal boundaries and degeneracies of the thermodynamic metric. We further construct a rectangular black hole heat engine in the extended phase space and derive an exact expression for its efficiency, demonstrating how the ModMax parameter and massive-gravity couplings influence the enthalpy-based conversion of heat into work, while the Sharma--Mittal parameters modify the Carnot bound through corrections to the black-hole temperature. Finally, a topological analysis of the corrected temperature and generalized free energy reveals both conventional and novel critical points, and the associated conserved topological charge is investigated.

</details>


### [223] [Non-perturbative, background independent canonical quantum gravity in Fock representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28788)
*Thomas Thiemann*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文表明，在非微扰正则量子引力框架内，存在背景独立的Fock型表示。这种Fock真空的激发必然纠缠物质与几何，且Fock量子引力（FQG）的希尔伯特空间是可分的，这有利于将Wheeler-DeWitt约束实现为稠密定义的二次型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义相对论的量子场论需要非微扰（non-perturbative）表述，且经典广义相对论的背景独立性（background independence）为相应量子场论的希尔伯特空间表示提供了物理选取准则。论文旨在探索是否存在满足背景独立性的Fock型表示。

Method: 采用约束量子化方法（constraint quantisation method），并引入合适的物质场（matter fields）与几何场（geometry field）共存。通过比较Fock量子引力（Fock quantum gravity, FQG）与圈量子引力（Loop quantum gravity, LQG）的希尔伯特空间结构来展开分析。

Result: 成功构造了背景独立的Fock型表示，其中Fock真空的激发必然纠缠物质与几何。FQG的希尔伯特空间是可分的（separable），这与LQG的不可分希尔伯特空间形成鲜明对比。

Conclusion: Fock量子引力因其可分的希尔伯特空间，在将Wheeler-DeWitt约束（Hamiltonian constraint）实现为稠密定义的二次型（densely defined quadratic form）方面具有显著优势，为非微扰正则量子引力提供了不同于圈量子引力的新途径。

Abstract: It is commonly believed that a quantum field theory of General Relativity requires a non-perturbative formulation. In addition, the background independence of classical General Relativity supplies a physical selection criterion for suitable Hilbert space representations of the corresponding quantum field theory.
  In this contribution we show that there exist background independent representations of Fock type within the manifestly non-perturbative, canonical approach to quantum gravity. Mandatory for their existence is the presence of suitable matter fields next to the geometry field. In particular, the excitations of the corresponding Fock vacuum necessarily entangles matter and geometry.
  In this article we use the constraint quantisation method. We compare the resulting Fock incarnation of background independent, non-perturbative canonical quantum gravity with the well known Loop quantum gravity incarnation. One of the most important differences is that the Fock quantum gravity (FQG) Hilbert space, in contrast to the Loop quantum gravity (LQG) Hilbert space, is separable. This has many advantages when attempting to implement the Hamiltonian constraint, also known as Wheeler-DeWitt constraint, as a densely defined quadratic form.

</details>


### [224] [Quadrupole and quadratic-in-spin effects in quasicircular, spinning, asymmetric binaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28937)
*Mostafizur Rahman,Misbah Shahzadi,Adam Pound,Josh Mathews*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在自引力（self-force）理论的多尺度波形生成框架下，计算了非对称质量比双星系统在准环形旋进（quasicircular inspiral）过程中，小质量伴星绕Kerr黑洞运动时的完全相对论有限尺寸效应，包括二次自旋项、自旋诱发四极矩项和潮汐诱发四极矩项对能流通量的贡献，并给出了第六后牛顿阶（post-Newtonian order）的解析展开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 下一代引力波探测器（next-generation gravitational-wave detectors）需要大幅改进当前的理论波形模型（waveform models），尤其是非对称质量比双星（asymmetric-mass binaries）的情形。现有模型在该参数空间下精度不足，亟需纳入更完整的相对论有限尺寸效应（finite-size effects）。

Method: 在自引力理论（self-force theory）的多尺度波形生成框架下，推导小质量比极限下准圆形旋进过程中的能流通量（fluxes of energy）。计算涵盖二次自旋项（quadratic-in-secondary-spin terms）、自旋诱发四极矩项（spin-induced quadrupole terms）和潮汐诱发四极矩项（tidally induced quadrupole terms）。结果以Chebyshev网格上的完整数值数据集和第六后牛顿阶（sixth PN order）的解析展开两种形式呈现。

Result: 获得了包括二次自旋项、自旋诱发四极矩项和潮汐诱发四极矩项在内的能流通量完全相对论计算结果，并提供完整的数值数据集和至第六后牛顿阶的解析展开表达式。

Conclusion: 该结果可与文中推导的能量平衡律（energy-balance law）结合，用于构建适用于恒星绕黑洞运动的非对称双星系统的自洽波形模型，也可推广改进其他跨所有质量比的波形模型族。

Abstract: Next-generation gravitational-wave detectors will require significant improvements in current theoretical waveform models, particularly in the case of asymmetric-mass binaries. Here we provide one such improvement by calculating fully relativistic finite-size effects for small mass ratios -- primarily, fluxes of energy -- including quadratic-in-secondary-spin terms, spin-induced quadrupole terms, and tidally induced quadrupole terms, for quasicircular inspirals of a small companion into a Kerr black hole. We formulate these calculations within a multiscale waveform-generation framework in self-force theory, which could be used, with an energy-balance law we derive, to develop self-contained waveform models for asymmetric binaries involving stars orbiting black holes. Our results could additionally be used to improve other families of waveform models across all mass ratios. We present results both as complete numerical data sets on a Chebyshev grid and as analytical post-Newtonian expansions (to sixth PN order relative to the leading term in each contribution to the flux).

</details>


### [225] [Vacuum stability in Geometric Trinity of Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28956)
*Vincenzo Branchina,Salvatore Capozziello,Filippo Contino,Carmen Ferrara*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 论文研究了广义相对论（GR）的两种经典等价表述——**TEGR** 和 **STEGR** 中的亚稳态真空衰变问题，发现隧穿指数（tunneling exponent）在三种表述下保持一致，表明经典等价性可延伸至量子层面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究表明引力对真空衰变率计算有显著影响，因此有必要检验广义相对论的不同经典等价表述（TEGR 和 STEGR）是否在量子层面也保持等价性。真空稳定性分析为此提供了一个灵敏的检验平台。

Method: 论文在 TEGR（teleparallel equivalent of GR）和 STEGR（symmetric teleparallel equivalent of GR）框架下计算了亚稳态（假）真空的衰变率，并与广义相对论（GR）中的结果进行对比。

Result: 分析表明，在 TEGR 和 STEGR 中计算得到的真空衰变隧穿指数与 GR 中的对应结果完全一致。

Conclusion: 该结果提供了一个非平凡的例子，证明不同表述的引力理论之间的等价性不仅限于经典动力学，而是可以延伸到量子层面——至少在真空衰变这一特定问题上成立。

Abstract: The decay of a metastable (false) vacuum plays a crucial role in constraining Standard Model and beyond the Standard Model physics. In particular, it has been shown that gravity can have a significant impact on the calculation of the decay rate. In this context, it is natural to ask whether different but classically equivalent formulations of gravity lead to the same physical predictions. The aim of this paper is to analyze vacuum decay in teleparallel and symmetric teleparallel equivalent formulations of General Relativity (GR), namely TEGR and STEGR. Although these theories describe the same classical dynamics, it is of paramount importance to understand whether this equivalence persists also at the quantum level. In this respect, the analysis of vacuum stability may provide a particularly sensitive testing ground. The central question is whether the decay rate of a false vacuum computed within TEGR or STEGR coincides with the corresponding result obtained in GR. Our analysis shows that the tunneling exponent remains unchanged, offering a non-trivial example in which the equivalence between different formulations of gravity extends beyond classical dynamics.

</details>


### [226] [Quasi-normal modes as probes of black hole reentrant phase transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29101)
*M. Kord Zangeneh,S. Abdollahi,D. Afshar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了弱非线性带电反德西特（anti-de Sitter）黑洞中热力学相变与准正则模（quasi-normal modes, QNMs）动力学行为之间的相互作用，首次利用QNMs作为动力学探针识别了重入型大-小-大（中间）相变中的零级和一级相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究非线性带电反德西特黑洞在热力学相变过程中的动力学响应，尤其是准正则模（QNMs）能否作为相变的动力学探针。

Method: 在非扩展相空间（non-extended phase space）中识别重入型（reentrant）大-小-大（中间）相变；采用打靶法（shooting method）求解无质量标量场的克莱因-戈尔登方程（Klein-Gordon equation），计算各相中的QNM频率。

Result: 首次报告利用QNMs作为重入型相变（包含零级和一级相变）中热力学相变的动力学探针，发现不同相中QNMs表现出不同的行为特征。

Conclusion: QNMs可作为热力学相变的有效动力学探针，为理解非线性带电黑洞的热力学与动力学性质提供了新见解。

Abstract: We investigate the interplay between thermodynamic phase transitions and the dynamical behavior of quasi-normal modes (QNMs) in weakly nonlinear charged anti-de Sitter black holes. In a non-extended phase space, we identify a reentrant large-small-large(intermediate) phase transition for these black holes. Employing the shooting method to solve the Klein-Gordon equation for a massless scalar field, we compute QNM frequencies across these phases, revealing distinct behaviors in different phases. Specifically, to our knowledge, this is the first report of utilizing QNMs as dynamical probes of thermodynamic phases during reentrant phase transitions including zeroth and first-order transitions. These findings establish QNMs as a powerful dynamical probe for thermodynamic phase transitions, providing new insights into the thermodynamic and dynamical properties of nonlinear charged black holes as well.

### [227] [Beyond Classical Instability Limits of Anisotropic Self-gravitating Fluid Configurations in Hu-Sawicki Inspired f(R) Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29174)
*M. Yousaf,A. Rehman,M. Zeeshan Gul,Mohammed Zakarya,Nadiah Zafer Al-Shehri,Imtiaz Khan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文在 Hu-Sawicki 启发的 f(R) 引力模型框架下，研究了非静态、轴对称、自引力流体构型的动力学不稳定性，导出了包含绝热指数 Γ、能量密度、压力各向异性、度规扰动及高阶曲率修正的不稳定性条件，并证明广义相对论极限和各向同性极限可分别恢复经典结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究在修改引力理论（modified gravity）背景下，轴对称自引力系统在扰动下的动力学不稳定性（dynamical instability）如何受高阶曲率修正和物质各向异性（anisotropy）的影响，以推广经典引力坍缩理论。

Method: 采用 vorticity-free 几何假设，构建包含三主轴应力和非对角应力分量的各向异性能量-动量张量（energy-momentum tensor）；利用线性扰动方案（linear perturbation scheme）分离平衡态与含时部分，导出坍缩方程（collapse equation），并在牛顿近似（Newtonian approximation）和后牛顿近似（post-Newtonian approximation）下以绝热指数 Γ 表达不稳定性条件。

Result: 不稳定性条件表明坍缩的触发起始不仅依赖于流体的刚度（绝热指数 Γ），还依赖于背景能量密度、方向性压力各向异性（directional pressure anisotropies）、度规扰动（metric perturbations）以及 Hu-Sawicki 模型产生的高阶曲率贡献（higher-curvature contributions）。压制修改引力参数可恢复广义相对论极限，各向同性极限则恢复经典的 Chandrasekhar 阈值。

Conclusion: 曲率修正和各项异性应力能够显著改变轴对称致密系统（axially symmetric compact systems）的传统不稳定性条件，在修改引力框架下分析致密天体动力学稳定性时须考虑这些修正效应。

Abstract: In this draft, we investigate the dynamical instability of a restricted class of non-static, axially symmetric, self-gravitating fluid configurations within a Hu-Sawicki inspired f(R) gravity model. The matter source is described by an anisotropic energy-momentum tensor containing three principal stresses and an off-diagonal stress component. For the adopted vorticity free geometry, conservation equations are formulated, and a linear perturbation scheme is applied to separate the equilibrium and time-dependent sectors. This procedure yields a collapse equation that governs the evolution of the perturbed compact configuration. The associated instability conditions are then derived in terms of the adiabatic index Γ under the Newtonian and post-Newtonian approximations, whereas the resulting bounds show that the onset of instability depends not only on the stiffness of the fluid, but also on the background energy density, directional pressure anisotropies, metric perturbations, and higher-curvature contributions generated by the Hu-Sawicki model. The general relativistic limit is recovered by suppressing the modified gravity parameters, while the isotropic limit reproduces the classical Chandrasekhar threshold. These results demonstrate that curvature corrections and anisotropic stresses can appreciably modify the conventional instability conditions of axially symmetric compact systems.

</details>


### [228] [Scalar Vacuum Polarization in Loop Quantum Gravity Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29307)
*Antonino Flachi,Marco Pasini*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于圈量子引力（Loop Quantum Gravity）导出的宏观量子“克鲁斯卡尔”黑洞解，采用扩展的Anderson-Candelas-Christensen-DeWitt方法数值计算了标量场真空极化（vacuum polarization）⟨ϕ²⟩。结果表明，量子引力指数ε增强近视界极化并引发负尾部，该尾部源于背景曲率效应；对于天体物理上微小的ε，结果与经典史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）不可区分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在圈量子引力框架下已获得包含量子几何效应的宏观黑洞解，但其外部的量子活性（quantum activity）尚未被精确表征。该研究旨在通过计算量子真空极化，量化这些量子修正黑洞周围的场涨落行为。

Method: 采用扩展的Anderson-Candelas-Christensen-DeWitt方法计算量子真空极化，并在该量子修正黑洞几何外部进行了数值实现，首次得到标量真空极化⟨ϕ²⟩的数值结果。

Result: 量子引力指数ε增强了近视界区域的真空极化；在更远区域出现微小的负尾部，经无参数DeWitt-Schwinger对比确认其源于背景曲率（在里奇平坦（Ricci-flat）的史瓦西时空中不存在该效应）。该修正与ε呈线性关系，对于天体物理上微小的ε，结果在数值上与经典史瓦西黑洞无法区分。

Conclusion: 该计算为量子修正黑洞外部的量子活性提供了一致性检验，表明场涨落追踪局域曲率且在外域无反常增长，从而验证了圈量子引力黑洞解的物理合理性。

Abstract: A quantum macroscopic ``Kruskal'' black hole solution that incorporates quantum geometry effects has been derived in Loop Quantum Gravity as the counterpart to the classical Schwarzschild solution with a distinct imprint outside the event horizon, even at scales much larger than the Planck length. This resulting black hole quantum geometry is supported by an effective energy density of quantum origin, outside the horizon, which prevents asymptotic flatness at large distances and confines massive particles to finite radii, thereby preventing their escape to infinity. In this work we adapt to these solutions the extended Anderson-Candelas-Christensen-DeWitt approach to compute the quantum vacuum polarization in order to provide an accurate measure of the quantum activity around these black holes. We carry out a numerical implementation of the formalism and present, to our knowledge for the first time, the scalar vacuum polarization $\langleφ^2\rangle$ exterior to this quantum-corrected geometry. We find that the quantum-gravity exponent $ε$ enhances the near-horizon polarization and induces, farther out, a small negative tail that we identify -- through a parameter-free DeWitt--Schwinger comparison -- with the field's response to the nonzero curvature of the background (absent for Ricci-flat Schwarzschild). The correction scales linearly with $ε$, the parameter tracking the quantum gravitational corrections, so that for astrophysically realistic (i.e., tiny) $ε$, the result is numerically indistinguishable from Schwarzschild. The calculation furnishes a consistency check on the quantum activity around these solutions, the fluctuations tracking the local curvature without anomalous growth in the exterior.

</details>


### [229] [Self-force on a static scalar charge in traversable wormholes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29401)
*Jerome P. Mecca,Ian Vega*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过模和正则化（mode-sum regularization），系统分析了Konoplya-Zhidenko虫洞中静态标量自力的行为，发现自力方向不唯一且衰减速率依赖于虫洞参数(p,q)，在某些极限下可趋近Ellis虫洞中的标量自力行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 带电粒子所受自力（self-force）对弯曲时空的整体结构敏感，可作为探测局部曲率之外几何性质的工具。本文旨在通过计算静态标量自力，探究虫洞几何参数对其行为的影响。

Method: 采用Konoplya和Zhidenko提出的两参数球对称虫洞族（属于更广泛的Morris-Thorne可穿越虫洞类），利用模和正则化方法计算了点电荷上的静态标量自力，分析了其随形状指数q（控制喉部几何）和红移参数p（决定红移函数与潮汐强度）的依赖关系。

Result: 自力通常不是单向的：它随着与喉部径向距离的变化而改变符号，最多可出现两次过零点，具体取决于参数(p,q)。当p足够大时，自力的衰减速率可慢于孤立天体时空典型的~r^{-3}行为；更强的扩张（更负的q）导致更快的衰减。在p→∞且q→-∞的联合极限下，渐近衰减趋近于Ellis虫洞中的静态标量自力。

Conclusion: 虫洞参数(p,q)系统地调控了自力的方向与远距离衰减行为，且自力可作为区分不同虫洞几何的有效探针。

Abstract: The self-force acting on a charged particle is sensitive to the global structure of curved spacetime and can serve as a probe of geometry beyond local curvature. We compute the static scalar self-force on a point charge in the two-parameter family of spherically symmetric wormholes introduced by Konoplya and Zhidenko, members of the broader Morris-Thorne class of traversable wormholes. Using mode-sum regularization, we analyze its dependence on the shape exponent $q$, which controls the throat geometry, and the redshift parameter $p$, which determines the redshift function and tidal strength. We find that the self-force is generally not unidirectional: it can change sign with radial distance from the throat, with up to two distinct zero crossings depending on $(p,q)$. We provide a systematic characterization of how both the direction and large-distance falloff depend on the wormhole parameters. For sufficiently large $p$, the force can decay at a slower rate than the canonical $\sim r^{-3}$ behavior typical of isolated-body spacetimes, with stronger flaring (more negative $q$) leading to more rapid decay. In the combined limit $p \to \infty$ and $q \to -\infty$, the asymptotic falloff approaches that of the static scalar self-force in the Ellis wormhole.

### [230] [Gravitational lensing by extremal rotating black holes in the strong deflection limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29418)
*Fabiano Feleppa,Valerio Bozza,Welmoed Marit de Graaf*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文针对极端旋转黑洞（extremal rotating black holes）提出了一种新的强偏折极限展开（strong deflection limit expansion），用以描述当顺行临界光子轨道（prograde critical photon orbit）与退化视界（degenerate horizon）重合时偏折角（deflection angle）的非对数发散行为，并推广到准赤道运动以计算高阶像的放大率和焦散点位置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统强偏折极限（strong-deflection limit）在球对称和慢速旋转黑洞场景下能准确描述偏折角的对数发散（logarithmic divergence），但当顺行临界光子轨道与极端旋转黑洞的退化视界重合时，该近似失效。因此需要发展新的展开方法以正确描述该情形下的引力透镜效应。

Method: 提出一种适用于一般类极端旋转黑洞的强偏折极限新展开，表明偏折角在原有对数发散之外还表现出更强的幂律发散（power-law divergence）。高阶像的准确描述需保留展开中的附加项。先考虑赤道面上的顺行引力透镜（prograde gravitational lensing），再推广到准赤道运动（quasi-equatorial motion），以此计算高阶像的放大率（magnification）和焦散点（caustic points）位置。

Result: 发现当临界光子轨道与退化视界重合时，偏折角同时包含对数发散和更强的幂律发散。通过准赤道运动分析，可计算高阶像的放大率和焦散点位置。该框架可具体应用于Kerr、Kerr-Newman和Kerr-Sen等度规。

Conclusion: 该新强偏折极限展开能够有效描述极端旋转黑洞在临界光子轨道退化情形下的引力透镜行为，且可推广到多种已知的极端旋转黑洞度规中，为极端自旋黑洞的高阶像分析提供了理论基础。

Abstract: In the strong deflection regime, light rays passing close to an astrophysical black hole may remain trapped near unstable photon orbits for a long time before escaping to infinity. The traditional strong-deflection limit, which accurately describes the logarithmic divergence of the deflection angle for spherically symmetric and slowly rotating black holes, breaks down when the relevant prograde critical photon orbit coincides with the degenerate horizon of an extremal rotating black hole. We present a new strong deflection limit expansion for this horizon critical orbit, covering a general class of extremal rotating black holes. We show that the deflection angle exhibits a stronger power-law divergence in addition to the logarithmic divergence. For an adequate description of higher-order images, additional terms in the expansion must be retained. We first study prograde gravitational lensing in the equatorial plane and then extend the analysis to quasi-equatorial motion, which allows us to calculate the magnification of the higher-order images and the position of the caustic points. We finally apply the general framework to explicit examples, including the Kerr, Kerr-Newman, and Kerr-Sen metrics.

### [231] [Radial oscillations of quark stars in light of current astrophysical constraints: A comparative study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29510)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有观测证据表明存在质量低于太阳质量的致密天体（如HESS J1731--347），传统强子中子星模型难以完全解释这类亚太阳质量构型，因此需要探索奇异夸克星（strange quark star）作为替代方案。同时，通过计算径向振荡频率并对比多信使约束，可为下一代引力波探测提供区分夸克星与中子星的星震学判据。

Method: 采用三种物态方程：色味锁定（color flavor locked, CFL）相、相互作用夸克物质模型（interacting quark matter model）以及线性因果物态方程（linear (causal) equation of state）。通过数值求解Tolman–Oppenheimer–Volkoff（TOV）方程和径向微扰方程，构建平衡态恒星序列，并计算三种代表性质量（0.77、1.40、2.00太阳质量）的振荡谱。分析诊断包括质量-半径曲线和径向模式本征频率及其大频率间隔。

Result: 三种物态方程均给出超过2太阳质量的最大质量，典型半径在10-12 km，满足当前观测约束。基频模式频率范围在4-7 kHz，不同模型的大频率间隔存在差异。所有模型均能容纳HESS J1731--347的亚太阳质量构型。

Conclusion: 自束缚夸克物质模型（self-bound quark matter）可以自然解释HESS J1731--347的低质量致密天体，巩固了奇异夸克星解释的可行性。4-7 kHz的振荡频率处于当前及下一代引力波探测器（gravitational-wave observatories）的探测频段，可作为区分奇异夸克星与强子中子星的后并合星震学信号（asteroseismic signatures）。

Abstract: We investigate the structural and oscillatory properties of isotropic strange quark stars within General Relativity, focusing on three physically motivated equations of state: the color flavor locked (CFL) phase, an interacting quark matter model, and a linear (causal) equation of state. By numerically solving the Tolman Oppenheimer Volkoff and radial perturbation equations, we construct equilibrium stellar sequences and compute oscillation spectra across three representative masses (0.77, 1.40, and 2.00 solar masses). Our analysis is focused on two diagnostics: (i) mass to radius profiles and (ii) radial mode eigenfrequencies with large frequency separations. We compare theoretical predictions against multimessenger constraints from NICER X ray timing of key pulsars, the massive pulsars at two solar masses, and the low mass compact object in HESS J1731--347. All three equations of state yield maximum masses exceeding 2 solar masses with canonical mass radii of (10--12) km, satisfying current observational bounds. Fundamental mode frequencies span (4--7) kHz, with asymptotic large separations differing among the models. These elevated frequencies lie within the detection band of current and next generation gravitational-wave observatories, offering potential asteroseismic signatures for distinguishing strange quark stars from hadronic neutron stars in post merger emission. Our results demonstrate that self bound quark matter naturally accommodates the sub solar mass configuration of HESS J1731--347, reinforcing the viability of strange quark star interpretations.

### [233] [Saturation Equations of State in Critical Gravitational Collapse: The Primordial Black Hole Threshold](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29590)
*Benaoumeur Bakhti*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究引力临界坍缩中，物质状态方程（equation of state）的压力硬化（pressure stiffening）效应如何改变原初黑洞（primordial black hole, PBH）的形成阈值和标度律。采用单占据格子气的封闭形式状态方程进行广义相对论球对称坍缩模拟，发现非线性压力反馈使PBH形成阈值相对于辐射流体提高约0.5%，但临界质量标度指数（critical mass-scaling exponent）保持不变（γ≈0.357），表明该效应在近临界区仅为轻微扰动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力临界坍缩的阈值与标度律对物质状态方程高度敏感。现有PBH研究普遍假设辐射流体（radiation fluid），但真实致密物质在接近最大密度时会出现压力硬化（pressure stiffening）这一普遍特征，其对PBH形成的影响尚不明确。

Method: 采用单占据格子气（single-occupancy lattice gas）的封闭形式状态方程 p = -T ln(1-ρ)，该方程具有密度依赖的声速和饱和密度。基于广义相对论（general relativity）球对称坍缩模拟，在因果性（causality）约束有效的参数区域内，比较该状态方程与辐射流体的临界行为差异。

Result: 压力硬化使PBH形成阈值较辐射流体提高0.50±0.02%；临界质量标度指数γ=0.357±0.001，与辐射流体值在数值精度内一致。该一致性源于格子气状态方程在低密度区域趋近辐射流体，在近临界区域仅为轻微扰动，而非反映指数的普适性。

Conclusion: 饱和诱导的硬化效应能够稳定引力坍缩并改变PBH形成阈值；研究建立了一种线性响应框架（linear-response framework），可用于评估更真实状态方程对原初黑洞形成的影响。

Abstract: The threshold and scaling laws of gravitational critical collapse depend sensitively on the matter equation of state. We investigate how these quantities are modified by a generic feature of dense matter that is absent from the radiation fluid commonly assumed in primordial black hole (PBH) studies: pressure stiffening as a maximum density is approached. As an analytically tractable proxy, we adopt the closed-form equation of state of a single-occupancy lattice gas, \(p=-T\ln(1-ρ)\), which exhibits a density-dependent sound speed and a saturation density. Using general-relativistic simulations of spherically symmetric collapse, we show that this nonlinear pressure feedback increases the PBH formation threshold by \(0.50\pm0.02\%\) relative to the radiation equation of state within the causal regime of the model. At the same time, the critical mass-scaling exponent remains \(γ=0.357\pm0.001\), consistent with the radiation-fluid value to within our numerical precision. This agreement reflects the fact that the lattice equation of state approaches the radiation fluid at low density and remains only a mild perturbation over the near-critical regime, rather than indicating a universal critical exponent. Our results provide a proof of principle that saturation-induced stiffening can stabilize gravitational collapse and shift the PBH threshold, while introducing a linear-response framework for assessing the impact of more realistic equations of state on primordial black hole formation.

### [234] [Quasibound states of a charged Dirac field around regular black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29704)
*Shao-Jun Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了阿勇-贝阿托-加西亚（ABG）规则黑洞背景下有质量带电狄拉克场的准束缚态，发现在超辐射放大缺失的情况下，规则带电几何结构会修改费米子能谱：ABG与Reissner-Nordström（RN）黑洞共享主导的类氢实频，但阻尼速率差异显著，ABG内势垒可降低视界通量，使某些模式寿命更长；在所探索参数范围内，狄拉克准束缚模均为阻尼模式，未出现狄拉克超辐射不稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨规则黑洞（regular black hole）背景中带电狄拉克场（Dirac field）的准束缚态（quasibound state）特性，特别是规则带电几何结构如何在没有超辐射放大（superradiant amplification）的情况下改变费米子谱（fermionic spectrum）。

Method: 推导了分离的狄拉克方程（separated Dirac equations），施加准束缚边界条件（quasibound boundary conditions），得到远场束缚条件$Mμ^2-qQω_R>0$及其弱束缚同号极限$Mμ>qQ$；在频域计算复频率，并通过时域演化（time-domain evolution）进行验证。

Result: ABG与RN黑洞具有相同的牛顿势和库仑势尾部，因此共享主导的类氢实频（hydrogenic real-frequency spectrum）；差异主要体现在次领头阶移位和阻尼率上。ABG内势垒可降低视界通量，使某些模式的寿命显著长于RN对应模式。在所探索参数范围内，所有狄拉克准束缚模均为阻尼模式。

Conclusion: 规则带电几何结构可以改变费米子云的寿命，但不会产生狄拉克超辐射不稳定性（Dirac superradiant instability）。

Abstract: We study quasibound states of a massive charged Dirac field on the Ayón-Beato--García (ABG) regular black-hole background and determine how a charged regular geometry modifies the fermionic spectrum in the absence of superradiant amplification. We derive the separated Dirac equations, impose quasibound boundary conditions, and obtain the far-field trapping condition $Mμ^2-qQω_R>0$, whose weak-binding, same-sign limit is $Mμ>qQ$. The complex frequencies are computed in the frequency domain and checked against time-domain evolutions. Because ABG and Reissner--Nordström (RN) black holes have the same Newtonian and Coulomb tails, they share the leading hydrogenic real-frequency spectrum. Their differences appear in subleading shifts and, more prominently, in the damping rates. The ABG inner barrier can reduce the horizon flux, making some modes much longer lived than their RN counterparts. Within the explored parameter range, the Dirac quasibound modes remain damped: the regular charged geometry changes the lifetime of the fermionic cloud but does not produce a Dirac superradiant instability.

</details>


### [235] [Optical Appearances of Accreting Ellis-Bronnikov Wormholes Observed from Both Sides of Throats](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29780)
*Yu-Hao Cui,Kai Lin,Sen Guo,Yu Liang,Tong Liu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了Ellis-Bronnikov（EB）虫洞在光学厚和光学薄吸积条件下，从喉两侧观察的光学外观。通过求解测地线方程并采用射线追踪方法，发现当观测者与吸积盘位于喉两侧时，撞击参数与瞄准距离不相等。光学厚吸积下，参数n增大会使虫洞表观尺寸增大但亮度降低；光学薄吸积下，图像呈现内外反转特征。模拟结果表明，小n的EB虫洞可在一定程度上模拟事件视界望远镜（EHT）图像，而大n虫洞或观测者位于R⁻侧的情况可被排除。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索虫洞作为一种潜在可观测的天体物理对象，其光学特征与黑洞图像的区分性，尤其是Ellis-Bronnikov虫洞在两种吸积模式下的视觉表现，为未来观测识别虫洞提供理论依据。

Method: 通过求解测地线方程（geodesic equation）推导光子撞击参数（impact parameter）与瞄准距离（aiming distance）之间的关系；采用射线追踪方法（ray-tracing method）模拟虫洞在不同吸积条件下的光学图像。

Result: 光学厚吸积下，参数n增大使虫洞表观尺寸增大、亮度降低；光学薄吸积下，图像呈现类似内外反转的特征，且直接图像不会遮挡高阶像（higher-order images），使更靠近事件视界（event horizon）的辐射可到达观测者。当观测者位于R⁺侧时，小n的EB虫洞可部分模拟EHT图像；大n虫洞或观测者位于R⁻侧的情况可被排除。

Conclusion: Ellis-Bronnikov虫洞的光学外观强烈依赖于参数n及观测者位置，部分参数空间下的虫洞图像与EHT观测结果存在相似性，但特定条件（大n或观测者位于R⁻侧）下的虫洞模型可被观测排除。

Abstract: This study investigates the optical appearance of the Ellis-Bronnikov wormhole as viewed from both sides of its throat, under conditions of optically thick and thin accretion. By solving the geodesic equation, we derive the relationship between the impact parameter and the aiming distance of photons, and found that if the observer and the accretion disk are located on both sides of the throat, these two quantities are not equal. The optical image of the wormhole observed from the other side of the throat is obtained through the ray-tracing method. For optically thick accretion, increases in the parameter $n$ lead to an increase in the apparent size of the wormhole but a decrease in its brightness. For optically thin accretion, the image is similar to the internal and external inversion of the image observed from the other side. Furthermore, for optically thin accretion flows, the direct image does not block the emission from higher-order images, allowing radiation emitted from regions much closer to the event horizon to reach the observer. Our simulation results show that when the observer is on the $\mathcal{R}^+$ side, EB wormholes with small $n$ can mimic the images taken by the EHT to some extent, while wormholes with large $n$ or with the observer on the $\mathcal{R}^-$ side can be ruled out.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用HKLWH度规框架，分析虫洞的能量特征；在洛伦兹加速（Lorentz-boosted）参考系中研究$\gamma$对潮汐力（tidal forces）的影响；引入基于Tangherlini菲涅尔系数（Fresnel coefficients）的概率同一性（probabilistic identity）概念，考察不同位置外部观测者的识别差异。

Result: 观测结果依赖于观测者的位置；即使在$\gamma\neq 0$的条件下，仍存在非零概率将HKLWH虫洞识别为黑洞。

Conclusion: HKLWH虫洞的观测身份具有概率性特征，不同位置的观测者可能得出不同的识别结论，这一发现挑战了传统的虫洞-黑洞二分法。

Abstract: The Harko, Kovács, and Lobo wormhole (HKLWH) metric contains two free parameters: one is the wormhole throat $r_{0}$, and the other is a dimensionless deviation parameter $γ$ with values $0<γ<1$, the latter ensuring the needed violation of the null energy condition at the throat. In this paper, we study the energetics of the HKLWH and the influence of $γ$ on the tidal forces in the Lorentz-boosted frame. Finally, we apply\ a new concept, namely, the probabilistic identity of the object observed by different external observers in terms of the Fresnel coefficients derived by Tangherlini. The intriguing result is that observations can differ depending on the location of the observer, i.e., there is a nonzero probability that the HKLWH will be identified as a black hole even when $γ\neq 0$.

### [237] [Gravitational time advancement effect in Bumblebee gravity for Earth bound systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29819)

TL;DR: 本文基于洛伦兹对称性破缺（LSB）的Bumblebee引力理论，将引力时间提前（负时间延迟）效应推广至旋转黑洞情形，推导至第三后牛顿（PPN）阶。通过在月地及卫星-地球信号传播配置中的应用，发现存在临界径向距离使Shapiro延迟为零并转为提前，并给出了LSB修正的时域上界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用近期提出的旋转Bumblebee黑洞解，将Shapiro时间延迟形式推广至第三后牛顿（post-Newtonian, PPN）阶。以地球-月球和地球-卫星两种信号传播构型为实例，基于Bumblebee参数 ℓ 在第二PPN阶（∝aM 和 M²）计算时间提前效应。

Conclusion: LSB修正源自无质量Bumblebee时空的锥形几何（conical geometry）。时间提前效应在现有实验约束下虽极为微小，但仍具理论意义，且文中简要讨论了该效应的直接实验探测可行性。

Abstract: This paper is a novel application of the new effect of gravitational time advancement or \textit{negative} time delay, first predicted for static black holes (spin $a=0$), that can be regarded as complementary to the well known effect of positive Shapiro time delay. We shall extend the Shapiro time delay formalism up to third PPN order using the recently proposed spinning ($a\neq 0$) black hole solution of the Lorentz symmetry breaking (LSB) Bumblebee gravity that is believed to reveal signatures of quantum gravity at low energies. Adopting two practical examples of signal propagation along Earth-Moon and Earth-Satellite configurations, we shall calculate the influence of the Bumblebee parameter $\ell$ on time advancement using terms up to the second PPN order $\varpropto aM$ and $M^{2} $ as the Bumblebee solution is valid only upto first order in $a$. It is shown that there is a critical radial distance $r_{c}$ above the Earth, where the Shapiro delay vanishes, and beyond $r_{c}$ the delay becomes negative, i.e., time advancement begins to set in, leading to the intriguing consequence that the measured LLR distance to Moon or any Satellite becomes \textit{less} than the zeroth order Euclidean distance. It is shown that the LSB correction arises from the conical geometry of the massless Bumblebee spacetime leading to upper bounds on the correction to the zeroth order Euclidean time interval as $δτ_{\text{LSB}}^{\text{Eucl}}<0.8\times 10^{-4}$ (ns) and to time advancement as $Δτ_{\text{LSB}}^{\text{adv}}<-4.5\times 10^{-13}$ (ns), both estimates based on the bound on $\ell $ corresponding to the Cassini spacecraft experiment. We shall also briefly touch upon the feasibility of direct experimental detection of the advancement effect.

Abstract: We consider a black hole solution embedded in a mass varying dark matter halo and study scalarization induced by dark matter. This study provides a novel connection between dark matter phenomenology and scalarization around a black hole.

### [239] [Photon Motion and Shadows of Rotating Black Holes with Nonlinear Electromagnetic and Anisotropic Matter Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29881)
*Mou Xu,Jianbo Lu,Yu Liu,Shumin Wu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用哈密顿-雅可比（Hamilton-Jacobi）形式体系研究了非线性电磁场和各向异性物质场对旋转黑洞（BH）的光子运动、阴影结构及能量发射率的影响，发现各向异性物质场参数对光子区域和阴影尺寸的影响显著强于非线性电磁场参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究非线性电磁场和各向异性物质场如何影响旋转黑洞的光子运动、阴影结构及能量发射率，以期加深对相关观测特征的理论理解。

Method: 采用哈密顿-雅可比（Hamilton-Jacobi）形式体系导出光子运动方程，分析光子区域的分布与稳定性；利用天球坐标（celestial coordinates）构建黑洞阴影，并通过反向光线追迹（backward ray tracing）获得阴影图像。

Result: 各向异性物质场参数对事件视界外不稳定光子区域的尺寸和形状影响显著大于非线性电磁场参数；$K$减小使不稳定光子区域扩大并变得扁平。阴影半径和面积随$K$减小而显著减小，随各向异性物质状态参数$ω$增大而明显增大；降低$K$或增加磁荷$Q$会抑制能量发射率峰值，$ω$的影响则较温和。

Conclusion: 各向异性物质场对旋转黑洞阴影尺寸的影响强于对阴影形状的影响，相关结果可为理解非线性电磁场和各向异性物质场对旋转黑洞阴影及观测特征的贡献提供理论参考。

Abstract: This paper investigates the effects of the nonlinear electromagnetic field and the anisotropic matter field on photon motion, shadow structures, and the energy emission rate of a rotating black hole (BH). Using the Hamilton-Jacobi formalism, we derive the photon motion equations and analyze the distribution and stability of photon regions. The results show that the anisotropic matter field parameters affect the size and shape of the photon region outside the event horizon more significantly than the nonlinear electromagnetic field parameter. As the anisotropic matter field parameter $K$ decreases, the unstable photon region outside the BH gradually expands and becomes increasingly flattened. Furthermore, we construct the BH shadow in terms of the celestial coordinates and obtain the corresponding shadow images by backward ray tracing. Several shadow observables, including the shadow radius, distortion parameter, shadow area, and oblateness, are also analyzed. The results indicate that the anisotropic matter field affects the shadow size more strongly than the shadow shape. Specifically, the shadow radius and area both decrease significantly as the parameter $K$ decreases, but increase markedly as the anisotropic matter state parameter $ω$ increases. In addition, we analyze the energy emission rate of the BH and find that decreasing $K$ or increasing magnetic charge $Q$ suppresses its peak value, while the influence of $ω$ remains comparatively mild. These results provide a useful reference for understanding the effects of nonlinear electromagnetic and anisotropic matter fields on rotating BH shadows and related observational signatures.

### [241] [Black holes with regular scalar hair in Brans-Dicke gravity via the Herglotz variational principle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30091)
*Marek Wazny*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 在赫尔格洛茨变分原理（Herglotz variational principle, HVP）框架下重新表述了布兰斯-迪克理论（Brans-Dicke theory），在参数ω₀=0且势能V(φ)=0的条件下得到了一个带有标量毛发（scalar hair）的精确黑洞解，从而提供了一种规避标量-张量理论中标准无毛定理（no-hair theorems）的新机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的布兰斯-迪克理论中存在"无毛定理"的限制，即静态黑洞无法携带非平凡的标量场配置。该研究试图通过引入赫尔格洛茨变分原理来重新表述该理论，以寻求规避无毛定理的新型黑洞解。

Method: 将布兰斯-迪克理论在赫尔格洛茨变分原理下进行重新表述，并在ω₀=0与V(φ)=0的特定条件下求解黑洞解。同时基于弱场极限（weak-field limit）的启发，选择了特定的赫尔格洛茨函数η(r)=η₀(r-2M)^k/r^{k+2}，其中η₀为具有长度量纲的常数。

Result: 得到了一个严格为正的标量场分布，对应一个隐身的史瓦西解（stealth Schwarzschild solution），且该解无需固定原本任意的赫尔格洛茨函数η(r)。所选择的η(r)形式使得标量场构型在黑洞视界（horizon）处保持正则。

Conclusion: 赫尔格洛茨变分原理为标量-张量理论中规避标准无毛定理提供了一种新的机制。

Abstract: Brans-Dicke theory is reformulated within the Herglotz variational principle (HVP), and an exact black hole solution with scalar hair is obtained for $ω_{0}=0$ and vanishing potential $V(φ)=0$. The scalar profile is strictly positive and the resulting stealth Schwarzschild solution arises without fixing the otherwise arbitrary Herglotz function $η(r)$. Motivated by the weak-field limit, the explicit choice $η(r)=η_{0}(r-2M)^k/r^{k+2}$, with $η_0$ a constant of dimension length, produces a scalar field configuration remaining regular at the black hole horizon. Consequently, the HVP provides a new mechanism for evading standard no-hair theorems in scalar-tensor theories.

### [242] [Wave Optics Effects from Gravitational Wave Propagation Through Dark Matter Halos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30149)
*Annamalai P. Shanmugaraj,Roland Haas,Erik Schnetter,Sofie Marie Koksbang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过数值演化完整爱因斯坦方程（Einstein equations），研究了线性化平面引力波（gravitational waves, GWs）在穿过静态球对称天体结构（如高斯、NFW、Burkert势）时的波光学效应（wave optics effects），发现GW传播不仅依赖于透镜质量，还强烈依赖于引力势分布，且GW在强/弱引力下均不沿零测地线（null geodesics）传播；与标量波近似相比，中心势内差异为量级一，穿过结构后降至百分之几。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在几何光学近似（geometric optics approximation）失效的情形下，引力波通过与其波长尺度相近的结构时会产生波光学效应。为探究弯曲时空背景中此类效应的具体表现，需要超越几何光学近似，对线性化引力波在静态球对称天体结构中的传播进行数值研究。

Method: 采用数值演化包含全部10个分量的完整爱因斯坦方程，针对高斯（Gaussian）、NFW和Burkert引力势，在弱引力与强引力两种场景下模拟线性化平面引力波的传播；对NFW和Burkert势采用简化形式。通过将引力波波长设定为小于结构的史瓦西半径（Schwarzschild radius）来隔离衍射（diffraction）效应。

Result: 散射不仅依赖于透镜质量，还强烈依赖于引力势分布；引力波在通过高斯密度结构时，无论强引力还是弱引力下均不沿零测地线传播；在强引力情形下，Burkert势会使平面波的凸性（convexity）在离开结构时翻转；与线性化标量波（linearized scalar wave）预测对比，中心势内差异为量级一，穿过结构后差异降至仅百分之几。

Conclusion: 虽然这些效应较小，但未来的引力波探测器和脉冲星计时阵列（Pulsar Timing Arrays, PTAs）可能对这些信号敏感，从而有望用于约束暗物质尖峰（dark matter spikes）或晕（halos）的结构。

Abstract: Gravitational wave (GW) propagation is usually studied under the geometric optics approximation. But when GWs propagate through structures of sizes similar to their wavelength, this approximation breaks down. Going beyond the geometric optics approximation allows us to explore the wave optics effects in curved background that appear in such cases. In this work, we present a scheme for numerically evolving linearised plane GWs through stationary, spherical astrophysical structures in both weak and strong gravity regimes. Our simulations evolve the full Einstein equations (with all 10 components) for Gaussian, NFW and Burkert potentials, although in simplified form for the two latter. Our simulations show that the scattering of the GWs depends not only on the mass of the lens but also strongly on the gravitational potential distribution of the lens. We isolate the effects of diffraction by setting the wavelength of GW to be less than the Schwarzschild radius of the structure. Among our most important results, we find that the GWs do not propagate along null geodesics when propagating through the Gaussian density, neither in the strong nor weak gravity setting. We also find that for the Burkert potential, the convexity of the plane wave is flipped when leaving the structure, in the strong gravity case.
  We compare our results with the linearized scalar wave predictions and find that the difference between these and the exact GW modes are of order one when the wave is inside the central potential. However, the difference reduces to only a few percent when the wave has passed through the structure. Although these effects are small, future GW detectors and Pulsar Timing Arrays (PTAs) could be sensitive to these signals which could thus potentially help in constraining the structure of dark matter spikes or halos.

</details>


### [243] [Orbital, Shadow, and Thin-Disk Signatures of a Regular Black Hole with Gravitational Self-Energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30195)
*Erdinç Ulaş Saka*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了由非局域引力自能（gravitational self-energy）贡献产生的正则黑洞（regular black hole）的测地线运动（geodesic motion）、阴影观测量（shadow observables）和薄盘吸积（thin-disk accretion）特性。随着自能尺度增大，光子环（photon ring）和ISCO外移，阴影面积在极端情形下增大约2.7倍，薄盘吸积峰高降至Schwarzschild情形的约61%，形成一套自洽的光学、轨道与吸积特征信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨非局域引力自能正则化对黑洞可观测量的影响，识别该正则化方案在光学、轨道和吸积过程中的特征信号。

Method: 计算了光子环、临界碰撞参数（critical impact parameter）、表观阴影半径（apparent shadow radius）、零Lyapunov指数（null Lyapunov exponent）、最内稳定圆轨道（innermost stable circular orbit, ISCO）、轨道频率以及Novikov-Thorne流量分布。

Result: 自能尺度增大时，光子环与ISCO向外移动，光子环频率与不稳定性指数下降。近极端基准下，视界归一化的阴影面积增大约2.7倍，而按ADM质量归一化的阴影半径减小。ISCO束缚效率（binding efficiency）小幅增长；零力矩薄盘吸积流量峰向外移动，在趋近残余态时峰高降至Schwarzschild情形的约61%。

Conclusion: 上述趋势构成了引力自能正则化（gravitational-self-energy regularization）产生的一组相干的光学、轨道与吸积特征信号。

Abstract: We investigate geodesic motion, shadow observables and thin-disk accretion for the regular black hole generated by a non-local gravitational self-energy contribution. The geometry is controlled by a zero-point length and can be followed smoothly from the Schwarzschild limit to a cold extremal remnant. We compute the photon ring, critical impact parameter, apparent shadow radius, null Lyapunov exponent, innermost stable circular orbit, orbital frequencies and Novikov-Thorne flux profile. As the self-energy scale grows, both the photon ring and the ISCO move outward, while the photon-ring frequency and instability exponent decrease. The horizon-normalized shadow area increases by about a factor of 2.7 for the near-extremal benchmark, although the same shadow radius decreases when normalized by the ADM mass. The ISCO binding efficiency grows modestly, whereas the zero-torque thin-disk flux peak moves outward and falls to about 61% of the Schwarzschild peak as the solution approaches the remnant regime. These trends identify a coherent set of optical, orbital and accretion signatures of the gravitational-self-energy regularization.

### [244] [Comment on the "New Rotating Black Hole in Electromagnetic Fields: Cosmological Horizon without Cosmological Constant''](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30426)
*Hryhorii Ovcharenko*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过代数分析和显式坐标变换，证明[L. Ma, H. Lü, arXiv:2606.23782]中声称的新时空实际上属于一类特殊的带电荷的Kundt型电真空时空（electrovacuum Kundt spacetimes of type D），并非真正的新时空。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者旨在指出[L. Ma, H. Lü]声称的新时空背景实际上并非全新构造，而是属于已知的特殊时空类别，并希望通过分析该背景的结构，促进对更一般时空类别的理解，如由加速电荷产生的类克尔（Kerr-like）黑洞。

Method: 首先分析该时空的代数性质（algebraic properties），然后通过寻找显式坐标变换（explicit coordinate transformations），将其归入已知的带电荷Kundt型电真空时空类别。

Result: 证明该所谓的新时空背景属于带有电或磁荷（electric or magnetic charge）的D型Kundt电真空时空（electrovacuum Kundt spacetimes of type D），并非真正的新时空。

Conclusion: 该背景并非新时空，而是已知时空类的一个特例；对这一背景的分析有助于更好地理解更一般的时空类别结构，例如由加速电或磁荷产生的类克尔黑洞。

Abstract: In this comment we discuss some properties of the novel spacetime, recently found in [L. Ma, H. Lü, arXiv:2606.23782]. In particular, we draw attention to the background of this solution that the authors claim to be a new spacetime. We show that this is not the case because this background belongs to the special class of electrovacuum Kundt spacetimes of type D with either electric or magnetic charge. We show this by first analyzing the algebraic properties of this spacetime, and then by finding the explicit coordinate transformations. We hope that this analysis of the background allows for a better understanding of the structure of the general class of this type, namely as the Kerr-like black holes in the background generated by an accelerating electric or magnetic charge.

### [245] [The Role of the Volume in Black Hole Thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30507)
*William Ballik*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过定义与Killing矢量相关联的守恒量 \(H^I_\chi\)，阐释了为何Kerr-anti-de Sitter黑洞的能量 \(E\)（与渐近非旋转系关联）满足热力学第一定律，而能量 \(F\)（与渐近旋转系关联）则否，并解释了“热力学体积” \(V_{th}\) 与“几何体积” \(V_{geo}\)（等于向量体积 \(V_C\)）分别出现在不同Smarr关系中的原因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究表明，Kerr-anti-de Sitter黑洞的能量 \(E\) 满足热力学第一定律，而另一种能量 \(F\) 则不满足；同时，与 \(F\) 关联的Smarr关系中自然出现几何体积 \(V_{geo}\)（等于 \(V_C\)），而非与 \(E\) 关联的关系。本文旨在解释为何必须使用 \(E\) 而非 \(F\) 才能获得有效的第一定律，以及为何 \(V_C\) 更自然地出现在 \(F\) 对应的Smarr关系中。

Method: 本文借鉴Barnich和Compère的方法，定义了一个与Killing矢量 \(\chi\) 相关联的守恒量 \(H^I_\chi\)。能量 \(E\) 和 \(F\) 分别由 \(H^I_\xi\) 和 \(H^I_\beta\) 给出，其中 \(\xi\) 是渐近超曲面正交的Killing矢量，\(\beta\) 正比于主共形Killing-Yano张量 \(\boldsymbol{h}\) 的散度。通过分析第一定律成立的条件，即要求 \(\chi^a\) 和背景反德西特（anti-de Sitter）度规的分量保持不变，本文检验了 \(\xi^a\) 和 \(\beta^a\) 是否满足该条件。

Result: 本文发现，第一定律成立的条件要求Killing矢量 \(\chi^a\) 和背景反德西特（anti-de Sitter）度规的分量均保持不变；该条件对 \(\xi^a\) 成立，但对 \(\beta^a\) 不成立，从而解释了为何能量 \(E\) 满足第一定律而 \(F\) 不满足。此外，由于与主共形Killing-Yano张量 \(\boldsymbol{h}\) 相关的简化，\(V_C\) 出现在与 \(\beta\) 关联的Smarr关系中。

Conclusion: 本文通过守恒量 \(H^I_\chi\) 的形式体系，系统解释了Kerr-anti-de Sitter黑洞热力学中 \(E\) 与 \(F\) 在满足第一定律方面的差异，以及 \(V_C\) 在Smarr关系中的出现机制，从而调和了已有文献中看似矛盾的结果。

Abstract: Gibbons et al. [arXiv:hep-th/0408217] found the energy $E$ of Kerr--anti-de Sitter black holes by integrating the first law of black hole thermodynamics. They found that $E$ corresponds to the Ashtekar--Magnon--Das (AMD) energy associated with an asymptotically nonrotating frame, whereas the AMD ``energy'' which I will call $F$ associated with an asymptotically rotating frame does not satisfy the first law. In Cvetič et al. [arXiv:1012.2888], the first law was extended by interpreting $E$ as an enthalpy and $Λ$ as being proportional to a pressure. The term conjugate to the pressure was then interpreted as the ``thermodynamic volume'' $V_{th}$. Associated with the first law (with varying pressure) is a Smarr relation for $E$. The Smarr relation for $F$ also exists, and the term conjugate to the pressure in that Smarr relation is the ``geometric volume'' $V_{geo}$, shown in [arXiv:1310.1935] to be equal to the vector volume $V_C$ of the black hole.
  To address why it is necessary to use $E$ rather than $F$ to have a viable first law but $V_C$ appears naturally in the Smarr relation associated with $F$ rather than $E$, I adapt Barnich and Compère [arXiv:gr-qc/0412029], by defining a conserved quantity $H^I_χ$ associated with Killing vector $χ$. $E$ and $F$ are given by $H^I_ξ$ and $H^I_β$ respectively where $ξ$ is asymptotically hypersurface-orthogonal and $β$ is proportional to the divergence of the Principal Conformal Killing--Yano tensor $\boldsymbol{h}$. I show that the first law will be satisfied by $H^I_χ$ if both $χ^a$ and the background anti-de Sitter metric have unvarying components, which holds for $ξ^a$ but not $β^a$, explaining why the first law works for $E$ but not $F$. I show that $V_C$ appears in the $β$-associated Smarr relation due to simplifications related to $\boldsymbol{h}$.

</details>


### [246] [Evaluating the Fourier Approximation in Pulsar Timing Array Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30536)
*Yongqi Zhang,Hayden Scholz,Ken D. Olum,Lucas Steinberger,Gabriella Agazie,Akash Anumarlapudi,Anne M. Archibald,Zaven Arzoumanian,Paul T. Baker,Paul R. Brook,H. Thankful Cromartie,Kathryn Crowter,Megan E. DeCesar,Paul B. Demorest,Timothy Dolch,Justin A. Ellis,Elizabeth C. Ferrara,William Fiore,Emmanuel Fonseca,Gabriel E. Freedman,Nate Garver-Daniels,Peter A. Gentile,Joseph Glaser,Deborah C. Good,Jeffrey S. Hazboun,Ross J. Jennings,Megan L. Jones,David L. Kaplan,Matthew Kerr,Michael T. Lam,Duncan R. Lorimer,Jing Luo,Ryan S. Lynch,Alexander McEwen,Maura A. McLaughlin,Natasha McMann,Bradley W. Meyers,Cherry Ng,David J. Nice,Timothy T. Pennucci,Benetge B. P. Perera,Nihan S. Pol,Henri A. Radovan,Scott M. Ransom,Paul S. Ray,Ann Schmiedekamp,Carl Schmiedekamp,Brent J. Shapiro-Albert,Ingrid H. Stairs,Kevin Stovall,Abhimanyu Susobhanan,Joseph K. Swiggum,Stephen R. Taylor,Michele Vallisneri,Rutger van Haasteren,Haley M. Wahl*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了脉冲星计时阵列（pulsar timing arrays）中常用的傅里叶近似似然（Fourier approximation likelihood）与精确似然之间的差异，发现对于幂律谱（power-law spectra），近似似然平均比精确似然高约一倍；但在关键的无相关模型与Hellings-Downs相关模型的比较中，由于修正对称，模型对比结果基本不受影响；参数估计方面两种方法差异很小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 脉冲星计时阵列在分析随机引力波背景（gravitational wave background）时，为了降低计算复杂度，通常采用傅里叶近似（Fourier approximation）来计算贝叶斯似然（Bayesian likelihood）。这种近似将信号视为观测时间内的傅里叶模式之和，而真实信号并非周期性的。该近似引入的误差及其对科学结论的影响尚不明确，因此需要系统地量化该近似与精确结果之间的差异。

Method: 采用NANOGrav 15年数据集，对比傅里叶近似的似然与精确似然（或使用更密集频率作为精确结果的代理）之间的差异。对于幂律谱（power-law PSD）计算边际似然（marginal likelihood）和参数估计，并评估近似在不同模型比较场景下的影响。

Result: 对于幂律谱（power-law PSD），傅里叶近似的边际似然平均约为精确似然的两倍，可能导致模型比较中因子的误差。但在无相关模型与Hellings-Downs相关模型的对比中，两种模型受到相似的修正，因此模型比较结果基本不受影响。参数估计方面，两种方法的结果差异很小。对于具有尖锐特征（sharper features）的谱，近似误差可能更大。

Conclusion: 傅里叶近似在脉冲星计时阵列分析中引入系统性似然偏差，但在关键的引力波背景相关模型比较中影响有限；参数估计的稳健性较好。研究提示对于具有尖锐谱特征的信号，需谨慎使用该近似。

Abstract: Pulsar timing arrays search for stochastic processes such as gravitational waves by comparing pulse time of arrival data for millisecond pulsars to expectations from a background with a given power spectral density (PSD). To make the analysis computationally tractable, the Bayesian likelihood is usually computed using an approximation in which the signal is taken to be a sum of Fourier modes appropriate to the total time of observation, even though the true signal is not periodic. We study the difference between likelihoods computed with this Fourier approximation method for power law spectra and those computed exactly (or using more-closely spaced frequencies as a proxy for the exact result) in the NANOGrav 15-year dataset. We find that the true marginal likelihoods for power-law PSDs are on average about half as large as the likelihoods computed using the Fourier approximation. This could lead to an error of a factor of two in model comparison. However, in the important comparison of uncorrelated vs. Hellings-Downs correlated models, a very similar correction appears in both, so the model comparison is essentially unaffected. We also compare parameter estimation results for power law PSDs, finding little difference between the methods. We briefly discuss spectra with sharper features, for which the approximation could be much worse.

</details>


### [247] [Efficient Eccentric Effective-One-Body Dynamics via Near-Identity Averaging Transformations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30594)
*Philip Lynch,Alessandra Buonanno,Aldo Gamboa,Maarten van de Meent*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过将非自旋偏心有效一体（eccentric effective-one-body, EOB）运动方程改写为轨道根数（osculating orbital elements）并应用近恒等平均变换（near-identity averaging transformations），消除了吸气过程中的快速轨道时间尺度振荡，将吸气动力学计算成本降低了最多两个数量级，总波形生成速度提升1.5–8倍，并在大范围参数空间验证了精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 下一代引力波探测器（如LISA、爱因斯坦望远镜和宇宙探索者）需要精确且高效的长时程偏心双黑洞信号模型，但偏心有效一体模型在解析低质量和大质量比系统的快速振荡轨道动力学时计算成本过高，构成主要瓶颈。

Method: 将非自旋偏心有效一体运动方程改写为轨道根数形式，随后应用近恒等平均变换，逐阶抑制快速轨道时间尺度振荡（每阶抑制因子为轨道时间尺度与辐射反作用时间尺度之比）。在辐射反作用时间尺度上演化平均后的动力学，最后映射回完整有效一体动力学以完成最终过渡到并合（plunge）。

Result: 吸气动力学计算成本降低最多两个数量级，消除了长波形生成的主要瓶颈；总波形生成速度提升1.5–8倍。将平均过程推进到次次领头阶（next-to-next-to-leading-order）可精确建模可比质量双星，失配度（mismatch）≤ 8.05×10⁻⁵。

Conclusion: 近恒等平均变换为高效生成偏心有效一体吸气波形提供了一条实用路径，并为进一步扩展到低偏心率和自旋波形模型奠定了基础。

Abstract: Next-generation gravitational-wave detectors, such as LISA, the Einstein Telescope, and Cosmic Explorer, will require accurate and efficient models of long-lived black-hole binary signals, including those with significant eccentricity. A challenge for eccentric effective-one-body models is the cost of resolving rapidly oscillating orbital dynamics over the inspiral, particularly for low mass and large mass-ratio systems. We address this by recasting the nonspinning eccentric effective-one-body equations of motion in terms of osculating orbital elements and then applying near-identity averaging transformations to eliminate the fast orbital-timescale structure during the inspiral. Each order in this procedure suppresses the oscillatory behavior by one factor of the ratio of orbital to radiation-reaction timescales. The resulting averaged dynamics are evolved on the radiation-reaction timescale and then the system is mapped back to the full EOB dynamics for the final transition to plunge. This reduces the cost of the inspiral dynamics by up to two orders of magnitude, eliminating this as the primary bottleneck for long waveforms. The overall waveform-generation speed-up spans $1.5 - 8 \times$, motivating the development of more efficient waveform generation methods. We also validate the accuracy of the method by comparing waveforms generated from the averaged and full effective-one-body dynamics across a broad region of parameter space for moderate to large eccentricities. Carrying out this averaging procedure to next-to-next-to-leading-order is needed to accurately model comparable-mass binaries, yielding mismatches $\leq 8.05 \times 10^{-5}$. These results establish near-identity averaging as a practical route to efficient eccentric effective-one-body inspirals, and provide a foundation for further extensions to low-eccentricity and spinning waveform models.

</details>

### [248] [Flow-polarity decoupling and universal mobility enhancement in dense bacterial active fluids with mesoscale order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29410)
*Yuhao Wang,Premkumar Leishangthem,Yiming Ding,Xinliang Xu,Yilin Wu*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本研究通过同时成像细胞体、鞭毛和流场，揭示了稠密三维细菌活性流体中极性-流场解耦（flow-polarity decoupling）的微观动力学机制：细菌极性在介观尺度流场中随机分布，但自生溶剂流场却呈现介观有序；实验发现细菌相对于局部溶剂流场普遍向上游运动，且自平流速度受流控常数增强；数值模拟表明，传统力偶极子假设（force-dipole assumption）因流场梯度和近场水动力相互作用而失效，导致活性力方向与极性解耦。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 活性流体（active fluids）中微生物个体的运动及其与自生介观尺度溶剂流（self-generated mesoscale solvent flows）的相互作用是理解活性流体涌现特性的关键，但微观动力学机制尚不清晰。

Method: 对稠密三维细菌活性流体中的细胞体、鞭毛和流场进行同步成像实验，并结合全水动力相互作用（full hydrodynamic interactions）的数值模拟进行分析。

Result: 发现细胞极性在介观流场区域内随机分布，但溶剂流场呈现介观有序；细胞相对于局部溶剂流场主要向上游运动，自平流速度（self-advection speed）被一个流控常数（flow-controlled constant）普遍增强；传统力偶极子假设在流场梯度和近场水动力相互作用下失效，总活性力方向与极性不再一致。

Conclusion: 近场水动力相互作用（near-field hydrodynamic interactions）作为一种新型的、依赖构型的活性力，深刻影响稠密细菌悬浮液的自组织和输运行为，为理解稠密极性活性流体的集体行为提供了基础性知识。

Abstract: Active fluids consisting of living cells or synthetic microswimmers display rich emergent behavior and nonequilibrium mechanical properties, which not only shed light on various biological processes but also inform the engineering of autonomous fluidics and self-driven materials. The individual behavior of microswimmers and their interaction with self-generated mesoscale solvent flows underlie the emergent properties of active fluids. Here we studied the microscopic dynamics in dense 3D bacterial active fluids by simultaneous imaging of cell body, flagella, and flow field. A surprising finding is that the polarity of cells was randomly distributed in mesoscale flow regimes, and yet the system displays mesoscale order in the self-generated solvent flows. Despite the apparent flow-polarity decoupling, the motion of cells relative to local solvent flows predominantly navigated upstream, with the self-advection speed universally enhanced by a flow-controlled constant. Numerical modeling with full hydrodynamic interactions reveals that the observed flow-polarity decoupling arises from the breakdown of the commonly held force-dipole assumption for anisotropic microswimmers: in the presence of flow gradient and near-field hydrodynamic interactions, the direction of total active forcing exerted by a swimming bacterium to the surrounding fluid no longer aligns with its polarity. The simulations suggest that near-field interactions serve as a new type of emergent, configuration-dependent active forcing, which profoundly impact self-organization and transport in dense bacterial suspensions. Taken together, our work establishes fundamental knowledge for faithfully understanding the collective behavior of dense polar active fluids.

</details>


### [249] [Entropic Time, Psychophysics, and Deformed Neural Dynamics: A Unified Physical Theory for Human Time Perception](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29427)
*José Weberszpil,Oscar Sotolongo-Costa*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一个统一的物理理论，论证人类主观时间感知并非追踪几何坐标时间 $t$，而是源于宏观物理熵产生驱动的局部度规突变。通过建立“非广延三元组”（Nonextensive Troika）——将相空间分形维数 $D$、共形导数阶 $\alpha$ 与 Tsallis 非广延参数 $q$ 关联为封闭代数三重组——消除了独立的现象学拟合常数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模型依赖独立的现象学拟合常数，缺乏从第一性原理（first principles）出发的统一物理框架来解释主观时间感知的时间膨胀（例如在迷幻状态下的 REBUS 模型）和时间压缩（例如认知老化过程中的时间感知变化）。

Method: 通过建立“非广延三元组”（Nonextensive Troika），即相空间分形维数 $D$、共形导数阶 $\alpha$ 与 Tsallis 非广延参数 $q$ 三者构成的封闭代数三重组，证明局部时间度规固有地按 $t^\alpha$ 标度，推导共形算子（conformable operator）为必要的动力学结果，并从等概率单分形 Tsallis 熵 $S_q$ 导出 $q$ 指数。

Result: 该结构封闭性在变形漏积分放电框架（deformed leaky integrate-and-fire framework）内统一了异常神经耗散输运，并解析地预测了宏观心理物理响应转变，为迷幻状态下的时间膨胀（REBUS 模型）和认知老化中的时间压缩提供了清晰的热力学基础。

Conclusion: 人类主观时间感知不追踪几何坐标时间 $t$，而是由宏观物理熵产生的局部度规突变所决定；非广延三元组为这一机制提供了自洽的理论基础。

Abstract: We present a unified physical theory demonstrating that human subjective time perception does not track geometric coordinate time $t$, but instead emerges from a local metric mutation driven by macroscopic physical entropy production. By establishing the Nonextensive Troika -- a closed, mutually dependent algebraic triplet linking the phase-space fractal dimension $D$, the conformable derivative order $α$, and the Tsallis nonextensive parameter $q$ -- we eliminate independent phenomenological fitting constants. We prove that the local time metric inherently scales as $t^α$, deriving the conformable operator as a necessary kinetic consequence. Furthermore, we derive the $q$-index from the equiprobable monofractal Tsallis entropy $S_q$. This structural closure unifies anomalous neural dissipative transport within a deformed leaky integrate-and-fire framework and analytically predicts macroscopic psychophysical response transitions, providing a clear thermodynamic basis for time dilation in psychedelic states (the REBUS model) and temporal compression during cognitive aging.

</details>

### [250] [Anisotropic Mixed Fractional Landau Inequalities for Rotating Compressible Flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28388)
*Rômulo Damasclin Chaves dos Santos,Delvonei Alves de Andrade*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文针对高马赫数下旋转可压缩流体（rotating compressible fluids）建立了各向异性混合分数阶Landau不等式（anisotropic mixed fractional Landau inequalities）的严格理论，引入旋转分数阶Sobolev空间（rotating fractional Sobolev spaces），并利用旋转Littlewood–Paley分解等工具证明了显式依赖于马赫数、旋转速率和各向异性向量的最优不等式，最终将其应用于神经算子（neural operators）的稳定性与逼近率分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高马赫数旋转可压缩流动在工程与地球物理中广泛存在，但其数学分析工具尚不完善，尤其是缺乏统一处理各向异性（anisotropy）、分数阶耗散（fractional dissipation）与旋转效应（Coriolis和离心力）的理论框架。

Method: 引入了旋转分数阶Sobolev空间 $\mathcal{W}^{ν,p}_{α,Ω}(\mathbb{R}^k)$，用于编码方向性缩放、分数阶耗散与旋转效应；发展了一种旋转Littlewood–Paley分解（rotating Littlewood–Paley decomposition），并建立了带有旋转修正的各向异性极大估计（anisotropic maximal estimates with rotational corrections）以及Coriolis项的交换子估计（commutator estimates）。

Result: 证明了含马赫数、旋转速率$|Ω|$和各向异性向量$α$显式依赖的尖锐分数阶Landau不等式；作为应用，给出了神经算子逼近旋转可压缩流的稳定性界，并得到了最优逼近率 $N^{-ν/d_{α,Ω}}$，其中有效各向异性-旋转维数（effective anisotropic–rotational dimension）为 $d_{α,Ω}=\sum_iα_i^{-1}+κ|Ω|^{2/ν}$。

Conclusion: 该理论为分析高马赫旋转流动提供了数学基础，并为设计物理信息驱动的神经架构（physically informed neural architectures）提供了理论指导。

Abstract: We develop a rigorous theory of anisotropic mixed fractional Landau inequalities for rotating compressible fluid flows at high Mach numbers, incorporating Coriolis and centrifugal forces. We introduce rotating fractional Sobolev spaces $\mathcal{W}^{ν,p}_{α,Ω}(\mathbb{R}^k)$, which encode directional scaling, fractional dissipation and rotational effects. We prove sharp fractional Landau inequalities with explicit dependence on the Mach number, the rotation rate $|Ω|$ and the anisotropy vector $α$. Key tools are a rotating Littlewood--Paley decomposition, anisotropic maximal estimates with rotational corrections, and commutator estimates for the Coriolis term. As applications, we establish stability bounds for neural operators approximating rotating compressible flows and derive optimal approximation rates of order $N^{-ν/d_{α,Ω}}$, where $d_{α,Ω}=\sum_iα_i^{-1}+κ|Ω|^{2/ν}$ is the effective anisotropic--rotational dimension. Our results provide a mathematical foundation for analysing high--Mach rotating flows and for designing physically informed neural architectures.

### [251] [Noncommutative Anisotropic Diffusion in Hilbert Space. I. The Consistent A-Geometry, Mosco Stability, and the Weak Bridge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28964)
*E. Yu. Shchetinin,A. A. Shevchuk,S. I. Salpagarov*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文构建了可分希尔伯特空间（separable Hilbert space）中非交换各向异性扩散（noncommutative anisotropic diffusion）的分析层框架，证明了能量形式的可闭性（closability）、前向动力学的适定性、伽辽金收敛性（Galerkin convergence）以及A-对数索博列夫不等式（A-LSI）的Mosco极限稳定性等基本分析性质，并提出一个泛函分析定理保证了后向弱漂移的存在性与基本熵耗散估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有扩散模型在假设扩散算子与协方差算子可交换（即[D(x),Q]=0）时，能量形式可简化为⟨D∇u,∇v⟩；但实际应用中该交换性条件往往不成立，需要建立更一般的非交换各向异性扩散分析框架，以处理状态依赖的各向异性（state-dependent anisotropy）情形。

Method: 以参考高斯测度μ₀=N(0,Q)为基准，定义前向随机微分方程（SDE）的σ(x)=D(x)^{1/2}Q^{1/2}，引入一致能量形式Γ_A(u,v)=⟨Q^{1/2}D(x)^{1/2}∇u, Q^{1/2}D(x)^{1/2}∇v⟩；通过泛函分析方法证明了该形式的可闭性，并建立了A-一致性、均匀A-LSI及后向弱形式右端项的负能量空间可表示性等条件，推导出后向弱漂移的存在性定理。

Result: 证明了能量形式的可闭性、前向动力学的适定性、Galerkin收敛性和A-LSI在Mosco极限下的稳定性；提出了一个泛函分析定理，表明在A-一致性、均匀A-LSI和可表示性条件下后向弱漂移v=A∇Φ存在并满足基本熵耗散估计；给出了一个三维张量各向异性类、无扩散退化条件，以及在柱面子空间和紧尾类上的均匀化极限（homogenization limit）速率估计，进而得到强预解收敛和相应前向SDE的收敛性。

Conclusion: 本文第一部分奠定了非交换各向异性扩散的泛函分析基础，后续第二部分将处理统计闭包、独立各向同性基准（isotropic benchmark）以及A-自适应网络的逼近定理。

Abstract: This first part of the series builds the analytic layer of noncommutative anisotropic diffusion in a separable Hilbert space. Let $μ_0=\mathcal{N}(0,Q)$ be the reference Gaussian measure, with $Q\in L^1(\mathcal{H})$, and let $D(x)$ be a positive, state-dependent anisotropy. We do not assume that $[D(x),Q]=0$. Consequently, for the forward SDE with $σ(x)=D(x)^{1/2}Q^{1/2}$, the correct energy form is given not by the expression $\langle D\nabla u,\nabla v\rangle$ but by the consistent form $Γ_A(u,v)= \langle Q^{1/2}D(x)^{1/2}\nabla u, Q^{1/2}D(x)^{1/2}\nabla v\rangle$. We prove closability of the form, well-posedness of the forward dynamics, Galerkin convergence, stability of the $A$-LSI under a Mosco limit, the chain rule for relative entropy, and a general weak-bridge theorem. The main result of Part~I is a functional-analytic theorem: if $A$-consistency, a uniform $A$-LSI, and representability of the right-hand side of the backward weak form in the negative energy space all hold, then a backward weak drift $v=\mathsf{A}\nablaΦ$ exists and the basic entropy dissipation estimate holds. In addition, we single out a three-dimensional tensor class of anisotropies, formulate a condition for the absence of diffusion degeneracy, and obtain a rate estimate for the homogenization limit, first on cylindrical subspaces and then on compact-tail classes, which yields strong resolvent convergence and convergence of the forward SDEs. The statistical closure, an independent isotropic benchmark, and an approximation theorem for $A$-adapted networks are treated in Part~II.

</details>


### [252] [A Local--to--Global Propagation Principle for Dirichlet--to--Neumann Maps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29233)
*Thierry Daudé,Alberto Enciso,Bernard Helffer,Niky Kamran,François Nicoleau*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文建立了狄利克雷-诺伊曼映射（Dirichlet-to-Neumann maps）的三个局部到全局传播结果：第一个在一般几何框架下通过唯一延拓（unique continuation）和自伴性（self-adjointness）证明；第二个利用Jerison-Lebeau的谱唯一延拓理论将几何邻域假设替换为指数谱假设；第三个在共形扭曲乘积度规（conformally warped product metrics）的特殊情形下，结合Weyl-Titchmarsh理论与拟解析传播定理（quasi-analytic propagation theorem），显著削弱了假设条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在逆边界值问题（inverse boundary value problem）中，狄利克雷-诺伊曼映射是核心研究对象；理解其局部信息如何决定全局信息，对于电导率成像（electrical impedance tomography）等实际应用具有重要意义。

Method: 第一个结果结合唯一延拓与自伴性论证；第二个结果基于Jerison-Lebeau的谱唯一延拓理论，通过Le Rousseau-Lebeau的表述形式；第三个结果融合Weyl-Titchmarsh理论与Ganguly-Thangavelu的拟解析传播定理。

Result: 成立三个传播定理：(1) 若两个度规在连通边界分支的邻域中重合，则局部狄利克雷-诺伊曼映射的相等性可传播至全局映射；(2) 将几何邻域假设替换为全局狄利克雷-诺伊曼映射差的指数谱假设，仍可得到相同结论；(3) 在对称空间边界与共形扭曲乘积度规下，仅需共形因子满足拟解析边界接近性（quasi-analytic boundary closeness）即可。

Conclusion: 本文系统地揭示了狄利克雷-诺伊曼映射从局部到全局传播的若干充分条件，在一般流形与特殊对称空间上都给出了明确的传播机制，为逆问题唯一性理论提供了新的分析工具。

Abstract: We establish three local-to-global propagation results for Dirichlet--to--Neumann maps. First, in a general geometric setting, we show that if two smooth Riemannian metrics coincide in a collar neighborhood of a connected boundary component \(Γ\), then equality of the corresponding local Dirichlet--to--Neumann maps on a nonempty open subset of \(Γ\) propagates to equality of the associated global Dirichlet--to--Neumann maps on all of \(Γ\). The proof combines unique continuation and self-adjointness arguments.
  Our second result replaces the geometric collar assumption by an exponential spectral assumption on the difference of the corresponding global Dirichlet--to--Neumann maps. The proof relies on the spectral unique continuation theory of Jerison--Lebeau, through the formulation of Le~Rousseau--Lebeau.
  Finally, we specialize to a particular class of conformally warped product metrics. In this setting, the local Borg--Marchenko theorem identifies the exponential spectral assumption with the coincidence of the metrics in a collar neighborhood of the boundary. Assuming in addition that the boundary is a compact Riemannian symmetric space, we show that this assumption can be substantially weakened by requiring only a suitable quasi--analytic boundary closeness of the conformal factors. The proof combines Weyl--Titchmarsh theory with the quasi--analytic propagation theorem of Ganguly and Thangavelu.

</details>


### [253] [The massless Boltzmann equation in Minkowski spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30437)
*Ho Lee,Ernesto Nungesser,John Stalker,Paul Tod*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 该论文研究了闵可夫斯基时空中空间均匀的无质量玻尔兹曼方程（massless Boltzmann equation），针对硬相互作用和软相互作用两类情形分别证明了整体存在性和局部存在性，为解决无质量粒子的玻尔兹曼方程存在性问题提供了少数严格证明之一。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无质量玻尔兹曼方程在数学上存在显著的困难，尤其是软相互作用下动量零点处的奇异性（singularities at p=0）使得经典存在性理论无法直接适用。该研究受此前在宇宙学背景下关于无质量爱因斯坦-玻尔兹曼系统（massless Einstein–Boltzmann system）工作的启发，旨在填补无质量玻尔兹曼方程存在性证明的空缺。

Method: 对于硬相互作用（hard interactions），推导了针对无质量粒子的Povzner型不等式（Povzner-type inequality），以此建立解的全局时间存在性。对于软相互作用（soft interactions），引入奇异权重（singular weights）来控制动量零点处由粒子无质量性引发的奇异性，从而获得局部存在性（local existence）。

Result: 对于硬相互作用，证明了无质量玻尔兹曼方程的解在未来所有时间存在（solutions exist for all time into the future）。对于软相互作用，通过奇异权重方法获得了解的局部存在性。

Conclusion: 该工作为无质量玻尔兹曼方程的存在性理论提供了为数不多的严格证明之一，尤其针对软相互作用情形下的奇异控制问题给出了有效处理方案，有助于进一步理解无质量粒子在动力学理论（kinetic theory）中的数学结构。

Abstract: We study the spatially homogeneous, massless Boltzmann equation in Minkowski spacetime for a certain range of hard and soft interactions. For hard interactions, we derive a Povzner-type inequality for massless particles and show that solutions exist for all time into the future. For soft interactions, we employ singular weights to control singularities at $ p = 0 $, which arise from the masslessness of particles, to obtain local existence. These results, which are among rather few proofs of existence for the massless Boltzmann equation, are motivated by our earlier work on the massless Einstein--Boltzmann system in certain cosmological settings.

</details>

### [254] [What Naturalness Measures: Fine-Tuning and Informational Invariants in Cosmology and Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29660)
*Stefano Profumo*

Main category: physics.hist-ph

TL;DR: 本文论证了物理理论中“自然性（naturalness）”的传统理解混淆了表征依赖量与不变量的区别，提出自然性的客观内容在于参数到可观测量之映射的“普适类（universality class）”，它是一种不受参数化与测度约定变换影响的信息不变量（informational invariant），并通过引力与宇宙学示例予以阐明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关于自然性的讨论通常将其呈现为物理理论的客观约束条件——一个需要精细调节（fine-tuning）的模型被认为不可信。然而，这种表述将表征依赖的量与不变量混为一谈。实际上，精细调节的判断结果依赖于基本参数的选择、先验（prior）以及测度约定（measure convention），并不直接对应于世界的某一特征。因此，需要澄清自然性的客观基础究竟是什么。

Method: 本文采用概念分析与结构论证的方法。作者首先指出自然性判断的表征依赖性，继而提出替代方案：客观内容在于从参数到可观测量之映射的普适类（universality class），该普适类在容许的参数化与测度约定变换下保持不变，且独立于参数空间的任何先验。作者进一步追溯自然性判断确定性的历史渊源，从奥卡姆（Ockham）经狄拉克（Dirac）到温伯格（Weinberg），指出现代自然性继承了这一传统权威但缺乏其后续辩护。最后，作者在引力与宇宙学领域（特别是引力与粒子暗物质候选体的统一分析）中展开论证。

Result: 分析表明：精细调节追踪的是丰度映射（abundance map）的解析结构而非候选体的性质；由此得到的分类在所有测度约定下都不变，而调谐数值则不然。暗物质候选体的统一分析支持了信息结构实在论（informational structural realism）。

Conclusion: 自然性既非审美偏好也非客观概率，而是关于物理学通过表征编码观测的可区分性几何（distinguishability geometry）的陈述。本文的立场部分接受了尺度自主性（autonomy-of-scales）论述，但反对消解性解读（deflationary reading）——后者识别了借用的权威却丢弃了结构的残余。

Abstract: Naturalness is commonly presented as an objective constraint on physical theories: a model requiring fine-tuning is judged implausible. This presentation conflates a representation-dependent quantity with an invariant one. A fine-tuning verdict depends on the choice of fundamental parameters, the prior, and the measure convention, so it does not by itself fix a feature of the world. Here, I argue that what is objective is structural: the universality class of the map from parameters to observables, invariant under admissible changes of parametrization and measure convention, and independent of any prior over parameter space; it constitutes an informational invariant. On this account naturalness is neither an aesthetic preference nor an objective probability, but a statement about the distinguishability geometry of the representations through which physics encodes observation. I trace the certainty of naturalness verdicts to a tradition, from Ockham through Dirac and Weinberg, in which parsimony and beauty are taken as guides to truth; modern naturalness inherits that tradition's authority without its successive justifications. The argument is developed in the gravitational and cosmological sector, where naturalness reasoning is sharpest and its effective-field-theory grounding is weakest. A uniform analysis across gravitational and particle dark matter candidates shows that fine-tuning tracks the analytic structure of the abundance map, not the nature of the candidate; that the resulting classification is invariant across measure conventions while the tuning number is not; and that this decomposition instantiates informational structural realism. I situate the position against the autonomy-of-scales account, which the argument largely accepts, and against the deflationary reading, which identifies the borrowed authority but discards the structural residue.

</details>

### [255] [Kinetic energy from the cubic sum rule of the dynamic structure factor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30123)
*Fotios Kalkavouras,Panagiotis Tolias,Sebastian Schwalbe,Thomas Gawne,Alexander Benedix Robles,Jan Vorberger,Zhandos Moldabekov,Maximilian Böhme,Tobias Dornheim*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次探索利用动态结构因子 $S(\mathbf{q},ω)$ 的第三频率矩求和规则（third frequency moment sum rule）作为量子多体系统动能 $K$ 的替代估计方法。以均匀电子气（uniform electron gas）在温稠密物质（warm dense matter）条件下的情况为例，通过路径积分蒙特卡洛（path integral Monte Carlo）和介电形式（dielectric formalism）两种途径验证了该方法的有效性与局限性，并发现在短波长极限下常见的半经典近似会导致动能 $K$ 出现波数依赖的错误结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的动能估计方法在量子多体系统中存在局限性，亟需发展新的替代途径；同时，温稠密物质条件下的均匀电子气是一个具有挑战性的模型系统，可用于检验新方法的有效性。

Method: 分别通过两条路径提取动能 $K$：一是利用准精确的 \emph{ab initio} 路径积分蒙特卡洛（path integral Monte Carlo）结果，基于虚时密度-密度关联函数 $F(\mathbf{q},τ)$ 提取 $K$；二是通过近似的介电形式（dielectric formalism）结果，基于动态结构因子 $S(\mathbf{q},ω)$ 提取 $K$。

Result: 从路径积分蒙特卡洛结果提取的 $K$ 与热力学微分途径（thermodynamic differentiation route）的结果表现出极好的自洽性（self-consistency）；而从介电形式结果提取的 $K$ 则显示出波数依赖性，且常见半经典近似在短波长极限下给出了不正确的结果。

Conclusion: 该研究结果对多种应用具有广泛意义，包括含时密度泛函理论（time-dependent density functional theory）、介电形式方案、温稠密物质模型，以及为无模型访问完整电子状态方程（equation of state）的专用 X 射线汤姆孙散射（x-ray Thomson scattering）实验设计提供指导。

Abstract: The third frequency moment sum rule of the dynamic structure factor $S(\mathbf{q},ω)$ is explored for the first time as an alternative estimator of the kinetic energy $K$ of quantum many-body systems. As a practical example, the uniform electron gas at warm dense matter conditions is considered. First, $K$ is extracted from quasi-exact \emph{ab initio} path integral Monte Carlo results for the imaginary-time density--density correlation function $F(\mathbf{q},τ)$ and the expected excellent self-consistency with the thermodynamic differentiation route is confirmed. Second, $K$ is extracted from approximate dielectric formalism results for $S(\mathbf{q},ω)$ and it is observed that common semi-classical approximations lead to a wave-number dependent $K$ with an incorrect short-wavelength limit. Our results are expected to be of broad interest for a great variety of applications, including time-dependent density functional theory, dielectric formalism schemes and warm dense matter models, as well as for the design of dedicated x-ray Thomson scattering experiments with the potential to provide model-free access to the full electronic equation of state.

</details>
