### [256] [Factorizable Normalizing Flows for parameter-dependent density morphing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30489)
*Davide Valsecchi,Mauro Donegà,Rainer Wallny*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出可分解归一化流（Factorizable Normalizing Flows, FNFs），通过将参数依赖的密度分解为固定参考流与因子化多项式变换的组合，实现对连续参数形变的高效建模，避免了对组合参数空间进行指数级采样的需求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准归一化流（normalizing flows）擅长建模单一固定密度，但在高能物理等科学问题中，需处理密度随多个连续参数（如物理效应强度、校准常数、系统不确定度源）的形变。为每个参数组合单独学习一个流会面临组合爆炸，计算上不可行。

Method: FNF 将参数依赖密度表示为：一个固定、高保真的参考流（reference flow），复合一个关于参数的多项式可学习变换，且该变换对参数进行因子化分解（factorized over parameters）。每个参数的影响在仅变化该参数的样本中单独学习，推理时通过求和恢复多参数联合响应，无需采样组合参数空间。可选交互项（interaction terms）可捕捉多个参数同时强变化时的残余相关性。

Result: 在一个施加了两种可解释联合形变（interpretable deformations）的受控问题上，FNF 学习到的变换能够复现真实形变，达到最优似然（optimal likelihood）。模型具有可解释性（interpretable），参数规模与参数数量呈线性关系，且似然保持可计算（tractable）。

Conclusion: FNF 为需要连续密度形变（continuous density morphing）的推理工作流提供了一种通用工具，可直接推动高能物理中下一代无分箱似然拟合（unbinned likelihood fits）的发展。

Abstract: Normalizing Flows excel at modeling a single fixed density, yet many problems across the sciences, such as high energy physics, instead require modeling how that density deforms as a function of continuous parameters: the strength of a physical effect, a calibration constant, or a source of systematic uncertainty. Learning a separate flow for every parameter configuration quickly becomes intractable, since the number of joint settings grows exponentially with the number of parameters. We introduce Factorizable Normalizing Flows (FNFs), which represent the parameter-dependent density as a fixed, high-fidelity flow for a reference configuration composed with a learnable transformation that is polynomial in the parameters and factorized over them. This structure has a practical consequence: each parameter's effect is learned in isolation, from samples in which that parameter alone is varied. The combined response of many parameters is then recovered by summation at inference, without ever sampling their combinatorially large joint space. On a controlled problem with two interpretable deformations applied jointly to the data, the learned transformation reproduces the true deformations and matches the optimal likelihood, while optional interaction terms capture residual correlations when several parameters vary strongly at once. The resulting model is interpretable, scales linearly with the number of parameters, and keeps the likelihood tractable. This provides a general tool for any inference workflow requiring continuous density morphing, and directly enables the next generation of unbinned likelihood fits in high energy physics.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.mes-hall'></div>

# cond-mat.mes-hall [[Back]](#toc)

### [257] [The Position Space Chern Number: A Topological Index for Chiral Magnetic Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28549)
*Zachariah Addison*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文引入了一个新的拓扑指标——位置空间陈数（position space Chern number, C_R），用于对绝缘手性磁性系统的拓扑结构进行分类。该指标与传统的动量空间陈数（C_K）不同，其非零值保证动量空间中局域势垒边缘存在拓扑保护能隙内态。通过陈-西蒙斯有效场论揭示了位置空间陈绝缘体中横向力算符之间的拓扑量子化关联。研究展示了在斯格明子（skyrmion）磁相系统中C_R为非零，并阐明了该指标如何推广经典斯格明子绕数（skyrmion winding number）的概念。最后，讨论了动量和位置空间拓扑之间的竞争，并指出同时具有C_R≠0与C_K≠0的系统存在明显障碍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 绝缘手性磁性系统的拓扑分类尚不完整；现有的动量空间陈数（C_K）无法捕捉位置空间中的拓扑结构。本文旨在引入一个能直接刻画位置空间拓扑的新指标。

Method: 定义位置空间陈数（C_R）作为拓扑分类指标；采用陈-西蒙斯有效场论（Chern-Simons effective field theory）描述位置空间陈绝缘体；通过分析横向力算符的关联揭示拓扑量子化特征；在斯格明子磁相系统中验证C_R的存在性，并将其与经典斯格明子绕数进行对比。

Result: C_R的非零值保证动量空间局域势垒边缘存在拓扑保护的能隙内态；陈-西蒙斯场论揭示了描述动量空间中量子流流动的横向力算符之间存在拓扑量子化关联；在斯格明子磁相系统中确认了C_R的非零性；发现动量空间拓扑（C_K）与位置空间拓扑（C_R）之间存在竞争，且二者同时非零的系统存在明显的实现障碍。

Conclusion: 位置空间陈数（C_R）为手性磁性绝缘体引入了新的拓扑分类维度，补充了传统动量空间拓扑理论。该指标与斯格明子绕数的一般化关系表明，位置空间拓扑在磁性材料中具有物理可实现性。动量和位置空间两种拓扑之间的不相容性为进一步研究拓扑相（topological phases）之间的竞争与共存提供了方向。

Abstract: This paper introduces an index that categorizes the topology of insulating chiral magnetic systems. The position space Chern number, $C_R$ is distinct from its momentum space counterpart, $C_K$. A nonzero index guarantees the existence of topologically protected in-gap states that localize on the edge of local potential barriers in momentum space. The Chern-Simons effective field theory describing position space Chern insulators reveals a topologically quantized correlation between transverse force operators that describe the flow of quanta in momentum space. We demonstrate the existence of nonzero $C_R$ in systems hosting skyrmion magnetic phases and show how the index generalizes the classical concept of a skyrmion winding number. Lastly we investigate the competition between momentum space and position space topologies, and highlight an apparent obstruction to having systems with both $C_R \neq 0$ and $C_K \neq 0$.

</details>


### [258] [TetMaG-Guided Design and Operando Electron Holography Validation of Current-Induced Domain-Wall Motion in 3D Curved and Cornered Fe Nanobridges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28576)
*Sameh Okasha,Shriyar Tariq,Attila Kákay,Ryan Yang,Gregor Hlawacek,Akhil G. Nair,Rafal Dunin-Borkowski*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究结合TetMaG微磁模拟、聚焦电子束诱导沉积（FEBID）和离轴电子全息术，系统研究了三维磁性纳米桥中曲率和拐角几何结构对畴壁（domain-wall, DW）行为的影响，并通过实验验证了模拟预测，揭示了几何结构在调控三维磁行为中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维磁性纳米结构为突破平面系统限制、控制畴壁构型提供了新机遇，但实现可靠的三维磁性器件需要精确理解几何依赖的畴壁行为并获取定量实验验证。

Method: 采用TetMaG微磁模拟（micromagnetic simulation）预测不同几何结构下的磁性行为；通过聚焦电子束诱导沉积（focused electron beam induced deposition, FEBID）制备高保真三维纳米桥结构；利用离轴电子全息术（off-axis electron holography）对磁化构型进行定量实验表征。

Result: 拐角纳米桥作为优先钉扎位点（pinning sites），稳定局域磁构型并实现邻近钉扎位置间的受控切换；弯曲纳米桥则促进渐进的磁化旋转，降低钉扎并实现更平滑的畴壁运动。电子全息术测量得到的磁感应图与模拟磁化构型高度吻合，提供了直接实验验证。Operando电流偏置实验进一步揭示了电流驱动下的畴壁运动，包括在拐角结构中尾对尾畴壁（tail-to-tail DW）向头对头畴壁（head-to-tail configuration）的位移。

Conclusion: 曲率和拐角几何结构在三维磁性纳米桥中表现出截然不同的畴壁特性，几何因素是调控三维磁行为的关键因素，研究结果为三维磁性器件的设计与优化提供了理论和实验基础。

Abstract: Three-dimensional (3D) magnetic nanostructures offer new opportunities for controlling domain-wall (DW) configurations beyond the limitations of planar systems, providing promising architectures. However, the realization of reliable 3D magnetic devices requires precise control of geometry-dependent DW behaviour and quantitative experimental validation of the resulting magnetic states. Here, we combine TetMaG micromagnetic simulations, focused electron beam induced deposition (FEBID), and off-axis electron holography to investigate the influence of curvature and corner geometries on DW behaviour in 3D magnetic nanobridges. TetMaG simulations predict fundamentally different magnetic properties for curved and cornered geometries. Cornered nanobridges act as preferential DW pinning sites, stabilizing localized magnetic configurations and enabling controlled switching between neighbouring pinning positions. While curved nanobridges promote gradual magnetization rotation, reduced pinning, and smoother DW motion. These optimized geometries were fabricated with high structural fidelity using FEBID and subsequently characterized by quantitative electron holography. Electron holography measurements revealed magnetic induction maps that matched the simulated magnetization configurations, providing direct experimental validation of the TetMaG predictions. Curved and cornered geometries exhibited distinct DW characteristics governed by their local structural features, demonstrating the critical role of geometry in tailoring magnetic behaviour in 3D systems. Operando current-biasing experiments further revealed current-induced DW motion, including the displacement of a tail-to-tail DW into a head-to-tail configuration within corner structures.

</details>


### [259] [Voltage-tunable Josephson Junctions on Germanium Quantum Wells with in-situ Aluminum Contacts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28585)
*Joshua P. Thompson,Jason T. Dong,Bernardo Langa,Chomani K. Gaspe,Riss Card,Brycelynn Bailey,Shiva Davari,Bethany E. Matthews,Matthew J. Olszta,Silas Hoffman,Thomas M. Hazard,Kyle Serniak,Hugh O. H. Churchill,Kasra Sardashti,Christopher J. K. Richardson*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出一种深台面刻蚀（deep mesa etch）工艺，通过将外延材料除 VT-JJ 器件外全部去除，并在低损耗浮区硅衬底上用分子束外延（MBE）生长锗量子阱（Germanium quantum well）并原位沉积铝触点，实现电压可调约瑟夫森结（VT-JJ）与低微波损耗电路元件的集成。优化后的工艺使侧壁倾斜度足以连续沉积金属，制备的约瑟夫森结展现出栅极可调的超电流，最大临界电流超过 100 nA，临界电流-正常电阻乘积为 8.63 μV，为 VT-JJ 在量子电路中的集成提供了可行路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电压可调约瑟夫森结（voltage-tunable Josephson junctions, VT-JJs）是超导量子电子学中的新兴元件，有望扩展传统电路设计的功能。尽管 VT-JJs 与晶圆级半导体工艺高度兼容，但由于未解决的半导体微波损耗问题，其集成到量子电路中仍面临挑战。

Method: 采用深台面刻蚀工艺（deep mesa etch process），将除 VT-JJ 器件外的外延材料全部去除，使得电路元件可直接放置于低损耗衬底上。在浮区硅（float zone silicon）衬底上用分子束外延（Molecular Beam Epitaxy, MBE）生长锗量子阱（Germanium quantum well），并原位沉积铝触点，形成无氧化物的超导体-半导体界面。优化深台面刻蚀工艺，使侧壁形成足够倾斜的锥度（sidewall taper），实现从衬底到台面顶部连续的金属沉积，用于静电栅极电极和互连。

Result: 制备的约瑟夫森结表现出栅极可调的超电流（gate-tunable supercurrents），最大临界电流超过 100 nA，临界电流-正常电阻乘积（critical-current normal-resistance product）为 8.63 μV。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，该工艺为将电压可调超导电路元件（voltage-tunable superconducting circuit elements）与量子电子学基本构件（如耦合器和量子比特）的改进集成提供了一条可行路径。

Abstract: Voltage-tunable Josephson junctions (VT-JJs) are an emerging element in superconducting quantum electronics with potential to expand the functionality of conventional designs. While VT-JJs are largely compatible with wafer-scale semiconductor processing, their integration into quantum circuits remains a challenge due to unmitigated semiconductor microwave loss. Here, a deep mesa etch process, wherein the epitaxial material is removed except the VT-JJ device, will facilitate the integration of VT-JJs with low-microwave-loss circuit elements by allowing these circuit elements to be placed directly on a low-loss substrate. A Germanium quantum well is grown by Molecular Beam Epitaxy (MBE) on a float zone silicon substrate with in-situ deposited aluminum contacts. This combination allows the formation of an oxide-free superconductor-semiconductor interface. The deep mesa etch process is optimized to produce a sidewall taper sufficient for continuous metal deposition from the substrate to the top of the mesa for electrostatic gate electrodes and interconnects. The fabricated Josephson junctions demonstrate gate-tunable supercurrents with a maximum critical current over 100 nA and critical-current normal-resistance product of $8.63~μV$. These results demonstrate a pathway toward improved integration of voltage-tunable superconducting circuit elements with quantum electronic building blocks such as couplers and qubits.

</details>


### [260] [Graphene as a Tunable Nonradiative Bath for Moiré Excitons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28591)
*Katsunori Wakabayashi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种描述二维激子（尤其莫尔局域激子）非辐射能量转移到附近石墨烯层的最小理论模型。基于费米黄金规则，将转移速率写为激子近场光谱与石墨烯长波电子损失函数的重叠，并乘以激子形状因子。在点偶极极限下，该框架复现了能量转移的z⁻⁴定律；考虑莫尔激子的有限空间展宽后，高动量成分在z≲lX时被过滤，使得转移速率可作为激子局域化的探针。将石墨烯视为栅极可调库，Pauli阻塞模型预测当2|μF|接近ħω时带间电子-空穴激发被强烈抑制，部分恢复PL强度与寿命。全随机相位近似验证了模型在相关距离范围内的准确性（误差几%以内）。石墨烯栅极因此不仅是被动静电元件，而是可调二维电子库，其长波响应可通过激子PL淬灭被探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解并调控二维激子（尤其莫尔局域激子）向石墨烯的非辐射能量转移机制，探索利用光致发光（photoluminescence, PL）淬灭作为激子局域化探针的可能性，并揭示石墨烯栅极在过渡金属硫族化合物（transition-metal dichalcogenide, TMD）/六方氮化硼（hexagonal boron nitride, hBN）/石墨烯异质结构中的主动光学角色。

Method: 从费米黄金规则（Fermi's golden rule）出发，将非辐射能量转移速率表示为激子近场光谱与石墨烯长波电子损失函数（electronic loss function）的重叠积分，并引入激子形状因子（form factor）。采用高斯形状因子描述莫尔激子的有限空间展宽，构建Pauli阻塞（Pauli-blocking）模型处理石墨烯的栅极可调性，并与全随机相位近似（random-phase approximation, RPA）损失函数进行对比验证。

Result: 点偶极极限下复现了能量转移的Γ∝z⁻⁴标度律。考虑有限激子局域长度lX后，高动量近场成分在间距z≲lX时被过滤，使转移速率及PL淬灭可反映激子局域化程度。Pauli阻塞模型显示，当2|μF|接近ħω时带间电子-空穴激发被强烈抑制，导致PL强度和寿命部分恢复。全RPA验证表明，在相关距离范围内、代表性近红外激子参数下，最小模型误差在几%以内。

Conclusion: 石墨烯栅极在TMD/hBN/石墨烯异质结构中并非仅作为被动静电元件，而是充当一个栅极可调的二维电子库（tunable 2D electronic reservoir），其长波电子响应可通过激子PL淬灭实验被间接探测。激子的PL淬灭行为可作为激子局域长度的灵敏探针。

Abstract: A minimal theory for the nonradiative transfer of energy from a two-dimensional (2D) exciton -- especially a moiré-localized exciton -- to a nearby graphene layer is presented. Starting from Fermi's golden rule, the transfer rate is written as the overlap between the exciton near-field spectrum and the long-wavelength electronic loss function of graphene, weighted by an exciton form factor. In the point-dipole limit the framework reproduces the established $\GET\propto z^{-4}$ law for energy transfer to graphene. Including the finite spatial extent of a moiré exciton through a Gaussian form factor with localization length $\lX$, we show that high-momentum components of the near field are filtered out for $z\lesssim\lX$, so that the transfer rate -- and hence the photoluminescence (PL) quenching -- can serve as a probe of exciton localization. Treating graphene as a gate-tunable bath, a Pauli-blocking model predicts that interband electron-hole excitations are strongly suppressed once $2|\muF|$ approaches $\hbarω$, partially restoring PL intensity and lifetime. Benchmarking against the full random-phase-approximation loss function of doped graphene confirms the minimal model to within a few percent over the relevant distance range for representative near-infrared exciton parameters. We map the resulting PL observables over experimentally relevant ranges of spacer thickness, localization length, emission energy, and Fermi level, and identify when graphene-induced quenching dominates the optical response of transition-metal dichalcogenide/hexagonal boron nitride/graphene heterostructures. A graphene gate thus acts not as a passive electrostatic element but as a tunable 2D electronic reservoir whose long-wavelength response can be probed through exciton PL quenching.

</details>


### [261] [Direct observation of interfacial exchange coupling in a magnetic tunnel junction through spin-polarized quasiparticle interference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28686)
*Xu Wang,Chenxi Wang,Ying Yang,Yining Hu,Qingle Zhang,Chen Chen,Donglai Feng,Tong Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究利用自旋极化扫描隧道显微镜（spin-polarized scanning tunneling microscopy, SP-STM）和准粒子干涉技术，直接观察了Fe涂层针尖与Cr(001)表面构成的磁性隧道结中的界面交换耦合（interfacial exchange coupling），发现铁磁针尖可在Cr(001)的自旋极化表面态中诱导高达10 meV的能量偏移，且该偏移对针尖-表面距离和自旋排列高度敏感，证明了扩展的二维表面态能够跨异质结介导强交换耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 界面交换耦合（interfacial exchange coupling）在磁性异质结（magnetic heterostructures）中对于实现自旋三重态超导、量子反常霍尔效应（quantum anomalous Hall effect, QAHE）等新颖现象至关重要，然而该耦合的微观表征在技术上极具挑战，亟需直接的实验观测手段。

Method: 采用自旋极化扫描隧道显微镜（SP-STM）和准粒子干涉（quasiparticle interference）技术，以Fe涂层针尖与Cr(001)表面构成磁性隧道结（magnetic tunnel junction），直接观测界面交换耦合效应。

Result: 铁磁Fe针尖在Cr(001)的自旋极化表面态中诱导了高达10 meV的显著能量偏移；该能量偏移对针尖与表面之间的距离以及Fe针尖与Cr表面之间的自旋排列（spin-alignment）高度敏感，且可通过外加磁场切换自旋排列方向。

Conclusion: 扩展的二维表面态（extended 2D surface states）能够在异质结中作为媒介，实现强交换耦合，从而在局域尺度上调控由界面交换相互作用诱导的物理现象。

Abstract: Interfacial exchange coupling plays a critical role in enabling novel phenomena in magnetic heterostructures, such as spin triplet superconductivity, quantum anomalous Hall effect (QAHE), and advanced spintronic functionalities. While microscopic characterization of this coupling is essential for elucidating the underlying mechanism, it remains technically challenging. Here, using spin-polarized scanning tunneling microscopy (SP-STM) and quasiparticle interference, we directly observed interfacial exchange coupling in a magnetic tunnel junction formed by an Fe coated tip and a Cr(001) surface. We found the ferromagnetic tip induces significant energy shift (up to 10 meV) in the spin-polarized surface state of Cr(001). This shift is highly sensitive to the tip-surface distance and the spin-alignment between Fe tip and Cr surface, which can be switched by external magnetic field. Our results demonstrate that extended 2D surface states can mediate strong exchange coupling across a heterojunction, enabling local control of interfacial exchange interaction induced phenomena.

</details>


### [262] [Multi-level π-junction in a proximitized Ge/SiGe quantum dot probed by an on-chip superconducting microwave resonator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28762)
*Luigi Ruggiero,Vera Jo Weibel,Pauline Drexler,Carlo Ciaccia,Christian Olsen,Dominique Bougeard,Christian Schönenberger,Andrea Hofmann*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过片上微波测量，研究了锗/硅锗异质结构中由邻近效应量子点形成的多能级π结。实验结合直流输运与微波技术，揭示了多能级π结在栅压依赖性和微波响应中的定性特征，包括尖锐或平滑的相变及其电感和耗散特性，从而将锗基平台确立为研究超导/半导体杂化物理的可行系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多能级约瑟夫森输运（multilevel Josephson transport）此前主要见于碳纳米管等极端洁净系统，而基于锗（germanium）的量子点平台是否能够实现并观测到类似的多能级π结行为尚不明确。

Method: 在锗/硅锗异质结构中制备邻近效应量子点（proximitized quantum dot），当多个量子点轨道同时贡献超导输运时，利用片上微波测量（on-chip microwave measurements）结合直流输运（DC transport）技术，研究多能级π结的栅压依赖性和微波响应。

Result: 观测到多能级π结在栅压变化中呈现尖锐或平滑的相变（phase transitions），并具有不同的电感（inductive）和耗散（dissipative）信号特征。这表明在锗基系统中成功实现了多能级约瑟夫森输运。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了邻近效应锗（proximitized Ge）作为研究超导/半导体杂化物理（hybrid superconductor/semiconductor physics）的平台，并展示了栅极定义超导量子器件与高质量片上微波谐振器（on-chip microwave resonators）的集成可能性。

Abstract: Using on-chip microwave measurements, we investigate multilevel $π$-junctions formed by proximitized quantum dot (QD) in a germanium (Ge)/silicon-germanium (SiGe) heterostructure. In the multilevel regime, where several QD orbitals contribute simultaneously to superconducting transport, the Josephson ground state is no longer determined solely by the occupation of a single orbital. By combining DC transport and microwave techniques, we identify the qualitative signatures of multilevel $π$-junctions in both their gate-voltage dependence and microwave response. In particular, we observe combinations phase transitions that are sharp or smooth in gate voltage and which exhibit distinct inductive and dissipative signatures. Such multilevel Josephson transport has previously been observed primarily in exceptionally clean systems such as carbon nanotubes. Our results establish proximitized Ge as a platform for investigating hybrid superconductor/semiconductor physics and demonstrate the integration of gate-defined superconducting quantum devices with high-quality on-chip microwave resonators.

</details>


### [263] [Inter-band coherence effects in disordered crystals: beyond the non-crossing approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28809)
*Zhanning Wang,James H. Cullen,Roberto Raimondi,Dimitrie Culcer*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文发展了一种适用于布洛赫电子（Bloch electrons）在均匀直流电场驱动下的量子动理学理论（quantum kinetic theory），通过将非平衡密度矩阵（nonequilibrium density-matrix）形式论扩展到超越非交叉近似（non-crossing approximation）的阶数，系统包含了杂质散射到四阶的贡献，并应用于二维大质量狄拉克费米子模型，获得了包括交叉杂质过程对反常霍尔电导（anomalous Hall conductivity）的修正在内的解析结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准非交叉近似无法捕捉与内禀能带几何响应（如反常霍尔效应及相关自旋、轨道和谷输运）竞争的名义上为零阶于无序强度（zeroth order in disorder strength）的稳态项，因此需要更高级的理论框架来一致地处理这些贡献。

Method: 在长度规范（length gauge）下采用高斯白噪声无序模型，将杂质散射展开到杂质势的四阶；通过杂质诱导的密度矩阵涨落的迭代求解，在扣除不连通杂质配对后得到一个连通的 V⁴ 碰撞积分，避免了重复计数；由此产生的项分为自能修正、梯型顶点重整化（ladder-type vertex renormalization）和交叉量子干涉（crossed quantum-interference）贡献。

Result: 在二维大质量狄拉克费米子模型中，获得了玻恩近似下单粒子寿命、输运弛豫时间和纵向电导率的解析表达式；评估了包含交叉杂质过程的反常霍尔电导，发现这些过程产生一个与内禀贝里曲率（Berry curvature）项共存的、阶数为 τ⁰ 的外禀贡献；在该模型的高斯白噪声无序下，Ψ 型贡献被抵消而 X 型项保持有限。

Conclusion: 该形式论为将能带几何（band geometry）和交叉无序修正纳入多带输运提供了一致路径，可推广至自旋、赝自旋、轨道和谷现象的研究。

Abstract: We develop a quantum kinetic theory for Bloch electrons driven by a uniform dc electric field, extending the nonequilibrium density-matrix formalism beyond the non-crossing approximation. This extension is required to capture steady-state terms that are nominally zeroth order in disorder strength and compete with intrinsic band-geometric responses, as in anomalous Hall and related spin, orbital, and valley transport. Working in the length gauge with Gaussian white-noise disorder, we include impurity scattering to fourth order in the disorder potential. An iterative solution for the impurity-induced density-matrix fluctuations yields a connected $V^4$ collision integral after subtracting disconnected impurity pairings, thereby avoiding double counting. The resulting terms separate into self-energy corrections, ladder-type vertex renormalization, and crossed quantum-interference contributions. We clarify the correspondence between this density-matrix kinetic equation and the Keldysh formalism, and decompose the response into Fermi-surface and Fermi-sea components. As an application, we study the two-dimensional massive Dirac fermion model. We obtain analytical expressions for the single-particle lifetime, transport relaxation time, and longitudinal conductivity at the Born level, and then evaluate the anomalous Hall conductivity including crossed impurity processes. These processes generate an extrinsic contribution of order $τ^0$ that coexists with the intrinsic Berry-curvature term; for Gaussian white-noise disorder in this model, the $Ψ$-type contribution cancels while the $X$-type term remains finite. The formalism provides a consistent route for incorporating band geometry and crossed-disorder corrections into multiband transport, with applications to spin, pseudospin, orbital, and valley phenomena.

</details>


### [264] [Topological phase and its effective tuning in a ladder lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28816)
*Qi-Bo Zeng*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个由SSH链（具有交错跃迁振幅的一维晶格）与均匀跃迁的一维紧束缚晶格构成的双腿梯子模型（two-leg ladder model）。通过调节腿间耦合强度，即使SSH链处于平庸（trivial）区域，系统中也能涌现出具有零能边缘模（zero-energy edge modes）的非平庸拓扑相（topologically nontrivial phase）。相比单条SSH链，梯子模型中参数空间的非平庸区域显著扩大。该拓扑相位由量子化的贝里相位（Berry phase）刻画，边界可通过解析方法确定。进一步分析拓扑零模的分布发现，非平庸区域可依据能谱中的能隙闭合点划分为两个子区域，分别对应边缘模分布在不同腿上的情形。这些结果表明，通过在平庸晶格上的调控可有效调节拓扑相位与边缘模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索由一条SSH链（具有交错跃迁）与一条均匀跃迁的普通紧束缚链构成的双腿梯子系统中，是否会出现新的拓扑非平庸相，以及如何通过平庸晶格的调控来诱导或扩展拓扑相位。

Method: 构建两腿梯子模型，其中一条腿为SSH晶格（交错最近邻跃迁振幅），另一条腿为均匀跃迁的一维紧束缚晶格；系统性地改变腿间耦合强度，结合数值与解析方法（能谱分析、贝里相位计算、解析推导相边界）研究拓扑相变。

Result: 发现即使SSH腿处于平庸区域，通过调节腿间耦合也能诱导出具有零能边缘模的拓扑非平庸相；非平庸区域在参数空间中相比单条SSH链显著扩大；非平庸区域还可依据能谱中的能隙闭合点进一步分为两个子区域，分别对应边缘模分布在SSH腿或普通腿上。

Conclusion: 在梯子晶格中可通过调控平庸晶格来有效调节拓扑相位与边缘模，揭示了梯子结构中涌现非平庸拓扑的新机制，为研究拓扑相提供了一种新平台。

Abstract: We study a two-leg ladder model consists of a one-dimensional (1D) Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) lattice with staggered nearest-neighboring hopping amplitudes and a normal 1D tight-binding lattice with uniform hopping. By varying the strength of inter-leg coupling, we find that topologically nontrivial phase with zero-energy edge modes will emerge, even when the SSH leg is in the trivial regime. Compared with the single SSH model, the nontrivial region in the parameter space is significantly expanded in the ladder. The topological phase is characterized by quantized Berry phase, and the phase boundaries are determined analytically. We also analyze the distributions of topological zero modes in the ladder, and find that the nontrivial regime can be further divided into two regions, which are separated by a gap closing point in the energy spectrum and correspond to the cases with edge modes residing in different legs. These results indicate that the topological phase and edge modes can be effectively tuned through the manipulations in the trivial lattice. Our work unveils the emergence of nontrivial topology in the ladder lattices and provides a new platform for studying topological phases.

### [265] [Interplay of Electrode Coupling Engineering, Quasiperiodicity, and Magnetic Flux in Quantum Transport through a Su-Schrieffer-Heeger Ring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28846)
*Sridhar,Souvik Roy,Malay Bandyopadhyay*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了通过设计电极-耦合（electrode-coupling）构型可以根本性地重塑准周期量子系统中的相干输运现象。基于非平衡格林函数（nonequilibrium Green's function）理论，系统分析了带有磁通（magnetic flux）的准周期Su-Schrieffer-Heeger环在对称和非对称多位点（multi-site）耦合下的电荷、热输运及电流涨落。研究发现多位点引线耦合将增强输运的区域延伸至拓扑相（topological phase）深处，非对称源-漏耦合诱导出无序辅助导电相，磁通则通过干涉机制与无序效应产生双重影响，并驱动最优输运窗口随无序强度迁移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为准周期量子系统中的最优输运发生在均匀跃迁极限（homogeneous-hopping limit）附近，但电极-耦合构型对相干输运的调控机制尚不清晰。本研究旨在揭示多位点耦合、非对称源-漏连接以及磁通调控如何从根本上重塑准周期量子系统中的输运行为，从而为理性设计非平衡输运提供新范式。

Method: 采用非平衡格林函数（nonequilibrium Green's function）理论，对一个被磁通穿透的准周期Su-Schrieffer-Heeger环（quasiperiodic Su-Schrieffer-Heeger ring）进行了系统分析。研究了对称与非对称多位点储层-耦合（multi-site reservoir coupling）构型下的电荷输运、热输运以及电流涨落（current fluctuations）。

Result: 多位点引线耦合将增强输运区域从均匀跃迁极限附近扩展至拓扑相（topological phase）深处；非对称源-漏耦合（asymmetric source-drain coupling）诱导出无序辅助导电相（disorder-assisted conducting phase），其中准周期调制增强了而非抑制了电荷与能量输运；磁通（magnetic flux）同时激活了干涉介导的额外传输通道并抑制了无序诱导的重入导电区（re-entrant conducting regime）；随无序强度增大，最优输运窗口从拓扑区（topological regime）向平凡跳跃区（trivial-hopping regime）迁移。

Conclusion: 耦合工程（coupling engineering）可作为调控准周期材料中非平衡输运的有力范式，通过调控无序（disorder）、拓扑（topology）和量子干涉（quantum interference）之间的相互作用，可以精确调节量子器件中的输运特性。

Abstract: We reveal that engineering electrode-coupling configurations can fundamentally reshape coherent transport phenomena in quasiperiodic quantum systems. Leveraging nonequilibrium Green's function theory, we systematically analyze charge and heat transport, as well as current fluctuations, in a magnetic-flux-threaded quasiperiodic Su-Schrieffer-Heeger ring with both symmetric and asymmetric multi-site reservoir couplings. Contrary to the conventional expectation that optimal transport is achieved near the homogeneous-hopping limit, our results reveal that multi-site lead coupling fundamentally reshapes the transport landscape, extending the regime of enhanced transport deep into the topological phase. Strikingly, asymmetric source-drain coupling induces a disorder-assisted conducting phase where quasiperiodic modulation enhances, rather than suppresses, charge and energy transport. Magnetic flux exerts a dual influence: it activates additional interference-mediated transmission channels that amplify transport while simultaneously suppressing the disorder-induced re-entrant conducting regime. Furthermore, we uncover a flux-driven migration of the optimal transport window with increasing disorder strength, shifting from the topological regime toward the trivial-hopping regime. This behavior highlights the intricate interplay among quasiperiodicity, dimerization, magnetic-flux-induced quantum interference, and the geometry of the system-reservoir coupling. Collectively, our findings position coupling engineering as a powerful paradigm for the rational control of nonequilibrium transport in quasiperiodic materials and chart a route toward quantum device configurations in which transport characteristics can be precisely tuned via the interplay of disorder, topology, and quantum interference.

### [266] [Coherent and Incoherent Interfacial Spin Transport: Quantum-to-Classical Crossover in Spin Superfluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28877)
*A. R. Moura,L. S. L. Barbosa*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究通过自洽谐波近似（SCHA）结合微观线性响应理论，分析了NM/FMI/NM三明治异质结构中界面自旋输运的热力学性质，揭示了自旋混合电导（$g_{\uparrow\downarrow}$）可分解为相干凝聚组分（$g_{\mathrm{cond}}$）和涨落驱动组分（$g_{\mathrm{fluct}}$），并指出了$S=1/2$极端量子极限下的相干温度行为及低温$T^2$标度律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解量子多体涨落与宏观自旋超流体（spin superfluid）动力学之间的桥梁，为量子自旋电子学（quantum spintronics）器件中长程相干输运的优化提供基础物理原理。

Method: 采用自洽谐波近似（self-consistent harmonic approximation, SCHA）结合微观线性响应（linear response）理论，对由各向异性量子XXZ模型描述的FMI层进行界面自旋混合电导的解析计算。

Result: 自旋混合电导可分解为由自旋超流体的宏观相位驱动的相干凝聚组分（$g_{\mathrm{cond}}$）和由随机热磁振子（stochastic thermal magnons）中介的非相干涨落驱动组分（$g_{\mathrm{fluct}}$）。在$S=1/2$极端量子极限下，$g_{\mathrm{cond}}$急剧下降并在有限相干温度$T_{\mathrm{coh}}$处消失；$g_{\mathrm{fluct}}$在$T=0$时消失，低温下呈现$T^2$二次标度律，并随宏观磁化强度增强而受到$1/S$振幅压制。

Conclusion: 该微观理论桥接了量子多体涨落与宏观自旋超流体水力学（spin-superfluid hydrodynamics），为设计实现长程相干输运的量子自旋电子学器件奠定了清晰的基础原理。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamics of interfacial spin transport within a normal metal/ferromagnetic insulator/normal metal ($\mathrm{NM/FMI/NM}$) trilayer heterostructure, where the central magnetic layer is described by the anisotropic quantum XXZ model. By employing the self-consistent harmonic approximation (SCHA) combined with a microscopic linear response formulation, we evaluate the interfacial spin-mixing conductance $g_{\uparrow\downarrow}$ across all spin regimes. We demonstrate that $g_{\uparrow\downarrow}$ uniquely decomposes into a coherent condensed component ($g_{\mathrm{cond}}$), driven by the macroscopic phase of the spin superfluid, and an incoherent fluctuation-driven term ($g_{\mathrm{fluct}}$) mediated by stochastic thermal magnons. Crucially, in the extreme quantum limit of $S = 1/2$, $g_{\mathrm{cond}}$ drops steeply and vanishes at a finite coherence temperature $T_{\mathrm{coh}}$. Conversely, the fluctuation-driven term $g_{\mathrm{fluct}}$ vanishes at $T = 0$, exhibits a characteristic $T^2$ quadratic scaling at low temperatures, and undergoes a systematic $1/S$ amplitude suppression as the macroscopic magnetization becomes robust. Our microscopic insights bridge the gap between quantum many-body fluctuations and macroscopic spin-superfluid hydrodynamics, providing clear foundational principles for optimizing long-range coherent transport in quantum spintronic devices.

Recently, for quasi two-dimensional, flat $\textrm{MoS}_2$ flakes, the use of semimetals has led to a breakthrough, making transparent and Ohmic contacts possible. ### [269] [Synchronic scattering and geometric dephasing in microwave-induced resistance oscillations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28977)
*Jesus Iñarrea*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

Method: 构建量子输运模型，将瞬态散射率与驱动相干态的速度直接关联；引入非线性几何退相（非线性几何退相，$\exp(-A/R_c)$）机制，当振荡位移幅度$A$接近回旋半径$R_c$时触发。

Conclusion: 该模型为MIRO提供了一种完全相干的非平衡输运描述，统一解释了直流产生与振幅饱和的微观机制。

Abstract: We present a novel quantum transport model for microwave-induced resistance oscillations (MIRO) where we prove that the instantaneous scattering rate is directly modulated by the velocity of the driven coherent state. This interaction peaks exactly at $ωt = 2nπ$, where the wave packets sweep through the impurity landscape at maximum speed, breaking time-reversal symmetry to generate a net direct current. Additionally, we introduce a dephasing architecture to explain amplitude saturation: a non-linear geometric dephasing ($\exp(-A/R_c)$) triggered when the displacement amplitude $A$ of the oscillating coherent state,
  approaches the cyclotron radius $R_{c}$. This perfectly captures the linear-to-sublinear power crossover at high intensities, offering a fully coherent description of non-equilibrium transport.

Abstract: Cooperative emission is a collective quantum optical process that requires macroscopic phase coherence among coupled emitters. This study addresses this question through power-dependent steady-state PL and time-resolved PL decay measurements. In particular, neither superlinear intensity scaling nor power-dependent emission delay was observed, indicating the absence of cooperative-radiation signatures. This can be understood from two disorder-related aspects. Temperature-dependent spectroscopy reveals pronounced inhomogeneous broadening and low-temperature dark-exciton participation, pointing to intra-domain static disorder and exciton-state mixing. Conclusion: 该工作建立了一种将局域谱学测量与有效多体哈密顿量（many-body Hamiltonian）桥接起来的通用策略，为从实验数据直接提取空间非均匀微观相互作用提供了系统化途径。

Abstract: Inferring microscopic Hamiltonians from experimental data is a central challenge in quantum materials and quantum simulation. In low-dimensional spin systems, exchange interactions are often assumed to be spatially uniform, despite structural and environmental inhomogeneities that can locally modify the coupling. Here, we leverage a local, length-independent machine learning methodology to reconstruct spatially modulated exchange interactions directly from inelastic scanning tunneling spectroscopy maps. We demonstrate this approach with nanographene spin chains, identifying both near-uniform and inhomogeneous regimes across the synthesized magnets. The reconstructed models quantitatively reproduce the experimental spectra and recover the correct scaling of the excitation gap with system size. ### [272] [Emergent energy scales in magnonic systems with relative motion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29316)
*Daigo Oue*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出并阐述了相对运动在相互作用系统中产生涌现能量尺度（emergent energy scale）的机制，以磁振子系统（magnonic systems）为平台，展示了由此驱动的非平衡输运现象和参量不稳定性（parametric instabilities），并将其与量子摩擦（quantum friction）、切伦科夫辐射（Cherenkov emission）和泽尔多维奇超辐射（Zeldovich superradiance）等物理现象联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示相对运动如何在不引入传统驱动（如温度梯度或化学势差）的情况下，在相互作用系统中产生新的能量尺度，并为非平衡现象提供统一的理解框架。

Method: 以磁振子系统作为具体平台，结合微扰理论（perturbative regime）和临界速度以上的参量不稳定性分析，讨论了多普勒频率（Doppler frequency）作为非平衡偏置（nonequilibrium bias）的作用，以及涌现能量尺度对磁振子对（magnon pair）产生的共振驱动效应。

Result: 在微扰框架下，相对运动产生的多普勒频率可驱动磁振子流，即使不存在温度梯度或化学势差；当相对速度超过某一临界阈值时，涌现能量尺度大到足以共振产生磁振子对，导致微扰描述失效、磁振子真空失稳，从而引发强化的输运和非平衡动力学。

Conclusion: 涌现能量尺度为理解相对运动量子系统中的输运现象和不稳定性提供了一个统一的框架，并可推广至量子摩擦、切伦科夫辐射和泽尔多维奇超辐射等相关物理现象。

Abstract: Relative motion between interacting systems can generate emergent energy scales that are absent in isolated systems. While uniform motion can be eliminated by a Galilean transformation, relative motion between interacting systems generally cannot. In the presence of characteristic spatial structures, relative motion gives rise to a Doppler frequency scale determined by the characteristic wavevector of the excitation and the relative velocity of the system. This emergent scale provides a fundamental mechanism for driving nonequilibrium phenomena in moving systems. In particular, the emergent energy scale is determined by how the relative motion probes the spatial structure of the relevant excitation. In this tutorial, we illustrate these ideas using magnonic systems as a concrete platform. We first discuss motion-induced magnon transport between relatively moving ferromagnets, in which the Doppler frequency serves as an effective nonequilibrium bias in the perturbative regime. This mechanism produces magnon currents even in the absence of conventional driving forces such as temperature gradients or chemical potential differences. We then introduce motion-induced parametric instabilities. When the emergent scale becomes sufficiently large to resonantly create magnon pairs, the perturbative description breaks down, and the magnonic vacuum becomes unstable. Above a critical velocity threshold, spontaneous magnon-pair creation emerges, resulting in strongly enhanced transport and nonequilibrium dynamics. Connections to related phenomena, including quantum friction, Cherenkov emission, and Zeldovich superradiance, are also highlighted. The concept of an emergent energy scale provides a unifying framework for understanding transport phenomena and instabilities in quantum systems with relative motion.

*Akito Daido*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文为非相互作用电子体系推导出一个局域轨道磁化（local orbital magnetization）的量子力学公式，该公式通过巨势的局域磁通响应（local-flux response）确定，在二维中唯一确定，在三维中则对应纵向量度（longitudinal ambiguity）下的一个自然代表。粗粒化（coarse graining）后得到的局域标记（local marker）可生成至三阶导数的电流，其位点位置矩（site-position moment）等于有限大小体系的轨道磁四极矩（orbital magnetic quadrupole moment），并通过Haldane模型加以验证。

Method: 通过考虑巨势（grand potential）对局域磁通（local-flux）的响应，为无相互作用电子（non-interacting electrons）推导出局域轨道磁化的量子力学公式；在二维中该公式由局域磁通响应唯一确定，在三维中则从纵向量度中选出自然代表。进一步通过粗粒化得到可生成电流的局域标记，并计算其与轨道磁四极矩的关系。

Result: 局域磁通响应在二维中唯一确定了局域轨道磁化公式，在三维中给出了纵向量度下的自然代表。粗粒化后的局域标记能生成至三阶导数阶的电流，且其位点位置矩等于有限大小体系的轨道磁四极矩。通过Haldane模型对所得结果进行了验证。

Conclusion: 本文填补了局域轨道磁化量子力学公式的空白，建立了其与平衡电流密度、体轨道磁化理论以及轨道磁四极矩之间的自洽联系，为相关凝聚态物理计算提供了理论工具。

Abstract: Local orbital magnetization is the field whose rotation generates the equilibrium current density. Unlike spin magnetization, a quantum-mechanical local formula consistent with both this current relation and the modern theory of bulk orbital magnetization has been missing. In this work, we derive a quantum-mechanical formula for the local orbital magnetization for non-interacting electrons by considering local-flux response of the grand potential. The local-flux response fixes the formula uniquely in two dimensions, whereas in three dimensions it selects a natural representative within a longitudinal ambiguity. Furthermore, coarse graining yields a natural local marker that generates the current to third-derivative order, and its site-position moment equals the orbital magnetic quadrupole moment of finite-size systems. Result: STM/STS凭借原子级空间分辨率与高能量灵敏度，成功将量子相位转换为实空间可解析的局域观测量。相位分辨的STM成像为拓扑物态、对称性破缺模式及强电子关联提供了严格约束条件。

Abstract: The quantum geometric phase intrinsically dictates the geometry, topology, and many-body correlations of electronic wave functions. While quantum geometric phases are conventionally inferred through momentum-space probes or macroscopic transport measurements, their direct visualization and quantification in real space have historically been restricted by the spatial averaging of bulk techniques. Scanning tunneling microscopy and spectroscopy (STM/STS) circumvent this limitation, leveraging atomic-scale spatial resolution and high energy sensitivity to resolve local electronic phase profiles directly. This review highlights recent progress across four representative methodologies: probing the Aharonov-Bohm (AB) geometric phase via nanoscale real space interferometry; extracting the Berry phase from defect-induced quasiparticle interference and wavefront dislocations; reconstructing the complex phase structure in symmetric systems, such as magic-angle graphene, using order parameter decomposition; and mapping the phase textures and topological defects of pair density wave (PDW) and charge density wave (CDW) in unconventional superconductors utilizing the numerical 2D lock-in technique. Together, these developments show how quantum phases can be translated onto real space and locally resolvable observables. Phase-resolved STM imaging provides stringent constraints on topological states of matter, symmetry-breaking patterns, and strong electronic correlations, outlining a robust framework for in situ phase engineering in quantum materials.

### [275] [Length--Velocity Gauge Equivalence of Quantum Geometric Nonlinear Conductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29663)
*Shakeel Ahmad,Fei Xue*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过发展规范一致的密度矩阵理论，解决了内禀二阶非线性直流响应中不同规范（长度规范与速度规范）在绝热直流极限下看似结果不一致的歧义，证明了两者等价，并揭示了非线性响应本质上是费米面上的量子几何贡献，而非费米海项。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非线性输运已成为探测超越贝里曲率（Berry curvature）线性响应的量子几何（quantum geometry）的灵敏探针，但内禀二阶直流响应的不同量子与半经典表述在静态极限、费米海（Fermi sea）与费米面（Fermi surface）贡献的分配上存在明显歧义。

Method: 发展了一种规范一致的密度矩阵理论（density-matrix theory），分别在长度规范（length gauge，电场通过位置算符耦合）和速度规范（velocity gauge，电场通过矢势引入）下推导内禀非线性电导率，并统一采用相同的推迟延拓（retarded continuation）并纳入所有含场顶点。

Result: 两规范在绝热直流响应上等价；表观上的费米海项在完整表达式中抵消，剩余贡献为费米面上的量子几何项，由能带归一化的量子度量（band-normalized quantum metric）决定；完全带隙绝缘体在绝热清洁极限下无残余直流非线性霍尔电流；耗散欧姆部分需更仔细地处理弛豫与杂质散射。

Conclusion: 建立了长度规范与速度规范在量子几何非线性响应中的等价性，为利用非线性输运探测磁性量子几何（尤其是PT对称反铁磁体）提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Nonlinear transport has emerged as a sensitive probe of quantum geometry beyond the Berry-curvature physics of linear response. However, the intrinsic second-order dc response remains conceptually subtle: different quantum and semiclassical formulations can appear to give different static limits, with different assignments of Fermi sea and Fermi surface contributions. Here we resolve this ambiguity by developing a gauge-consistent density-matrix theory of intrinsic nonlinear conductivity in both the length gauge, where the electric field couples through the position operator, and the velocity gauge, where it enters through the vector potential. We show that the two gauges give the same adiabatic dc response when the same retarded continuation is used for all external frequencies and when the velocity gauge current includes all field-dependent vertices. The apparent Fermi sea terms cancel in the full expression, leaving a Fermi surface quantum geometric contribution determined by the band-normalized quantum metric. This result implies that a fully gapped insulator has no residual dc nonlinear Hall current in the adiabatic clean limit. The reactive part of the Fermi surface term agrees with the original semiclassical Berry-connection-polarizability response, while the dissipative Ohmic sector requires a more careful treatment of relaxation and impurity scattering. Our work establishes the length-velocity gauge equivalence for quantum geometric nonlinear response and provides a foundation for using nonlinear transport to probe magnetic quantum geometry, especially in PT-symmetric antiferromagnets.

Abstract: Graphene-based Sierpiński fractals host a zero-energy chiral mode and spin-1 Dirac dispersions within the nearest-neighbor tight-binding model. However, the presence of complex next-nearest neighbor hopping arising from the local flux and the staggered Semenoff mass terms, modeled within the Haldane Hamiltonian, breaks the time-reversal and spatial inversion symmetries, respectively, and makes these flat bands dispersive. Moreover, they introduce rich topological phases in this class of systems that can be characterized by Chern numbers up to $\pm 3$, i.e., beyond the conventional honeycomb lattice.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一种基于圆二色性（circular dichroism）的光谱探针方案，利用手性度量敏感驱动（chiral metric-sensitive drives），即旋转的四极“鞍点”（quadrupolar "saddle"）扰动，来有效调制度量并耦合到面积保持形变（area-preserving deformations）的生成元。

Result: 所得二色性信号可直接测量霍尔黏度；频率分辨光谱可将其与其他激发过程分离；局域化表述进一步提供了适用于连续体系和晶格体系的空间分辨标记。

Abstract: Hall viscosity characterizes the geometric response of a quantum Hall droplet to deformations of the underlying metric, yet it has remained difficult to measure directly. We propose a spectroscopic probe based on circular dichroism, using chiral metric-sensitive drives -- implemented as rotating quadrupolar ("saddle") perturbations -- that effectively modulate the metric and couple to the generators of area-preserving deformations. The resulting dichroic signal directly measures the Hall viscosity, while frequency-resolved spectroscopy disentangles it from other excitations. A local formulation further enables spatially resolved markers of Hall viscosity applicable to both continuum and lattice systems. Our results open a direct route to measuring Hall viscosity in quantum-engineered platforms such as cold atoms in optical lattices.

### [278] [Perfect elliptic dichroism: Probing the metric of anisotropic quantum Hall droplets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30052)
*Bruno Mera,Alberto Nardin,Anaïs Defossez,Baptiste Bermond,Tomoki Ozawa,Nathan Goldman*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出利用椭圆二色性探针来探测量子霍尔液滴的内在几何结构，揭示了“完美椭圆二色性”现象，并将其推广到理想Chern能带和晶格体系（如Harper-Hofstadter模型），为观测量子霍尔相中的几何重整化效应提供了光谱学途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过设计一个二色性探针（dichroic probe）的偏振几何结构，引入并识别了“完美椭圆二色性”（perfect elliptic dichroism）的响应区间，在该区间内系统只对特定手性（chirality）的椭圆偏振驱动产生响应。该方法被推广到理想Chern能带（ideal Chern bands）和Harper-Hofstadter模型等晶格实现中。

Result: 完美椭圆二色性可直接作为量子霍尔液滴内在度量的诊断工具。在理想Chern能带中，占据态的全纯性（holomorphicity）导致某一手性的吸收率严格为零，而另一手性呈现量子化响应。在晶格实现中，有限晶格间距修正破坏了连续介质度规描述，产生重整化的涌现朗道轨道度规（emergent Landau-orbit metric），完美二色性对应的探针椭圆率随之发生偏移。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了量子霍尔相丰富的几何结构，并为在量子工程化平台（quantum-engineered platforms）中观测这些效应提供了具体的光谱学实验途径。

Abstract: Understanding the geometry of quantum Hall systems is a central challenge in modern condensed matter physics. We introduce a framework for probing the geometric structure of quantum Hall droplets by engineering the geometry of a dichroic probe and identifying the onset of "perfect elliptic dichroism", a regime in which the system responds exclusively to an elliptically polarized drive of a given chirality. This phenomenon provides a direct diagnostic of the droplet's intrinsic metric, and we show that it extends naturally to ideal Chern bands, where holomorphicity of the occupied states guarantees the vanishing of one chiral absorption rate with a quantized response for the other. In lattice realizations, such as the Harper-Hofstadter model, finite lattice-spacing corrections break the exact continuum metric description and give rise to a renormalized, emergent Landau-orbit metric; the probe ellipticity at which perfect dichroism is achieved then shifts accordingly, offering a direct spectroscopic window onto this lattice-induced geometric renormalization. Our results illuminate the rich geometric structure of quantum Hall phases and offer concrete pathways for observing these effects in quantum-engineered platforms.

### [279] [Anomalous Duffing mechanics of a suspended carbon nanotube quantum dot at ultrastrong coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30099)

Motivation: 悬浮单壁碳纳米管量子点（suspended single-wall carbon nanotube quantum dot）在低温下既可作为原型量子点，又可作为高品质因数机械谐振器，且单电子隧穿可实现超强电子-振动耦合（ultrastrong electron-vibron coupling regime）。本研究旨在定量探究此类器件的Duffing响应参数及其与库仑阻塞振荡（Coulomb blockade oscillation）之间的关系。

Method: 对悬浮单壁碳纳米管量子点器件进行低温测量，定量分析其Duffing响应参数，并考察该参数随单电子隧穿区（single-electron tunneling region）的变化行为。

Result: 在单电子隧穿区域的边缘，观察到Duffing参数局部增大，对应硬化弹簧（stiffening spring）行为。该效应的幅度及近似标度关系与单电子隧穿现象相符，但后者原本应导致软化弹簧（softening spring）行为。

Conclusion: 实验观测到的硬化弹簧效应与基于单电子隧穿的理论预期（软化弹簧）相矛盾，文中讨论了这一令人困惑的结果的可能成因。

Abstract: At cryogenic temperatures, suspended single-wall carbon nanotube quantum dots act both as prototypical quantum dots as well as high-quality factor mechanical resonators. Single-electron tunneling enables reaching an ultrastrong electron-vibron coupling regime, where the coupling parameter exceeds the vibration frequency. Due to the high quality factors, a strongly nonlinear Duffing response is easily reached. Here, we quantitatively study the Duffing response parameters of such a device and their relation to Coulomb blockade oscillation. At the edges of single-electron tunneling regions, a local increase of the Duffing parameter corresponding to a stiffening spring is observed. Size and approximate scaling of the effect agree with single-electron tunneling phenomena, which however should lead to softening spring behaviour. Possible causes of these puzzling results are discussed.

### [280] [Rolling Two-Dimensional Collinear Magnets into Chiral Nanotubes with $p$-Wave Magnetism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30214)
*Zhejunyu Jin,Robin R. Neumann,Rodrigo Jaeschke-Ubiergo,Jairo Sinova,Alexander Mook*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出，将二维共线磁性材料（铁磁体、反铁磁体、交变磁体）卷曲成纳米管，可产生由曲率、手性和磁序控制的丰富自旋对称性景观；其中，具有径向或切向共面自旋织构的手性纳米管无论其共线母相如何，均能实现p波磁性，并预测其非相对论性Edelstein响应比常规自旋-轨道驱动的电荷-自旋转换高一个数量级以上。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过将二维共线磁体——铁磁体（ferromagnet）、反铁磁体（antiferromagnet）和交变磁体（altermagnet）——卷曲成纳米管，系统研究了曲率、手性和磁序对自旋对称性的调控作用。

Result: 手性纳米管中，只要存在径向或切向共面自旋织构（coplanar spin texture），无论其共线母相是什么，都能实现p波磁性。该奇宇称自旋对称性同时体现在电子谱和磁振子谱（magnonic spectra）中，表现为反对称的p波自旋劈裂。预测的非相对论性Edelstein响应比常规自旋-轨道驱动机制高出一个数量级以上。

Conclusion: 结果表明，磁性纳米管可作为工程化非常规p波磁性的通用平台，并且其巨大的非相对论性Edelstein响应为高效自旋转换提供了全新路径。

Abstract: $p$-wave magnets are noncollinear compensated magnetic systems that exhibit nonrelativistic antisymmetric spin splitting in momentum space. Their odd-parity spin symmetry enables unconventional spintronic functionalities, including highly efficient charge-to-spin conversion via the Edelstein effect. An outstanding question is whether such magnetic phases can emerge from simple and broadly accessible magnetic building blocks rather than from intrinsically noncollinear magnetic orders. Here, we show that rolling two-dimensional collinear magnets -- ferromagnets, antiferromagnets, and altermagnets -- into nanotubes generates a rich spin-symmetry landscape controlled by curvature, chirality, and magnetic order. Remarkably, chiral nanotubes hosting radial or tangential coplanar spin textures generically realize $p$-wave magnetism irrespective of the underlying collinear parent phase. The emergent odd-parity spin symmetry manifests itself in both electronic and magnonic spectra through antisymmetric $p$-wave spin splitting. Our results establish magnetic nanotubes as a versatile platform for engineering unconventional $p$-wave magnetism and predict a nonrelativistic Edelstein response that exceeds conventional spin-orbit-driven charge-to-spin conversion by more than an order of magnitude.

### [281] [Topological control of third-harmonic generation in a mesoscopic quantum ring with spiral dislocation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30245)
*Carlos Magno O. Pereira,Denise Assafrão,Edilberto O. Silva*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了含螺旋位错（spiral dislocation）的二维介观量子环（mesoscopic quantum ring）的非线性光学响应，重点聚焦于三次谐波产生（third-harmonic generation, THG）。通过引入曲率自由但由扭转（torsion）变形的有效度规，结合弯曲空间中的最小耦合（minimal coupling）形式、径向环约束和垂直磁场，导出了有效径向薛定谔问题并得到了束缚态，进而利用电偶极近似（electric-dipole approximation）计算了非线性极化率。结果表明轴向对称性保持偶极选择定则 Δm=±1，从而抑制了二次谐波产生（second-harmonic generation），但允许三次谐波产生通过多步跃迁链实现。此外，论文通过三种互补分析（去相位控制的谱分辨率、三维瀑布谱、通道分辨的THG振幅分解）进一步验证了螺旋位错作为调控介观环形纳米结构非线性光学活性的稳健几何调控手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索拓扑缺陷（topological defect）——尤其是螺旋位错——对介观量子环非线性光学特性（特别是三次谐波产生）的影响，旨在揭示几何变形能否成为调控非线性光学响应的有效工具。

Method: 采用曲率自由但存在扭转的螺旋位错模型描述空间变形；结合弯曲空间中的最小耦合形式、径向环约束和外加垂直磁场，构建有效径向薛定谔问题并计算束缚态；在电偶极近似下评估非线性极化率。

Result: 轴向对称性使得偶极选择定则 Δm=±1 得以保持，因此二次谐波产生被禁止，而三次谐波产生可通过多步跃迁链实现；去相位控制分析、三维瀑布谱以及通道分辨的THG振幅分解进一步证实了螺旋位错的调控作用。

Conclusion: 螺旋位错可作为调控介观环形纳米结构非线性光学活性的稳健几何调控手段（robust geometric knob）。

Abstract: We investigate the nonlinear optical response of a two-dimensional mesoscopic quantum ring subjected to a spiral dislocation, with emphasis on third-harmonic generation (THG). The topological defect is modeled through a torsion-induced deformation of space, which modifies the effective metric without introducing curvature. By combining the minimal-coupling prescription in curved space with a radial ring confinement and a perpendicular magnetic field, we derive the effective radial Schrödinger problem, obtain the bound states, and evaluate the nonlinear susceptibilities within the electric-dipole approximation. We show that the axial symmetry of the topologically deformed ring preserves the dipole selection rule $Δm=\pm 1$ and therefore suppresses second-harmonic generation, while THG remains allowed through multistep transition chains. The study is further expanded through three complementary analyses that can be implemented without changing the Hamiltonian: a dephasing-controlled study of spectral resolution, three-dimensional waterfall spectra showing the dependence on $β$ and $B$, and a channel-resolved decomposition of the THG amplitude. Together, these results establish the spiral dislocation as a robust geometric knob for tuning nonlinear optical activity in mesoscopic ring-shaped nanostructures.

*Tsuyoshi Yamamoto,Manuel Houzet*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用张量网络（tensor-network）方法计算稳态热流，能够处理强关联（strongly correlated）区域；在弱耦合（weak-coupling）和非相干隧穿（incoherent-tunneling）等极限区域与解析公式进行基准验证；在红外不动点附近应用微扰理论（perturbation theory）推导整流比的解析形式。

Result: 识别出一个标度区域：系统从温度高于近藤温度（Kondo temperature）的紫外（ultraviolet）区域流向温度低于近藤温度的红外（infrared）区域；发现红外不动点附近的整流比（rectification ratio）遵循普适幂律（universal power law），数值结果与解析预测吻合良好。

Conclusion: 研究结果为理解耗散诱导的多体物理如何影响热输运提供了基础性认识，揭示了量子二能级系统热整流的普适标度行为。

Abstract: We study heat rectification through a quantum two-level system asymmetrically coupled to two thermal baths, as described by the Ohmic spin-boson model. We evaluate the steady-state heat current using a tensor-network approach, which enables us to access the strongly correlated regime, and benchmark the results against analytical formulas in several limiting regimes, including the weak-coupling and incoherent-tunneling regimes. We identify a scaling regime where the studied system flows from an ultraviolet regime, at temperatures larger than the Kondo temperature, to an infrared regime, at temperatures lower than the Kondo temperature. By applying perturbation theory near the infrared fixed point, we find that the rectification ratio follows a universal power law. Our numerical results agree well with this analytical prediction. Our results provide a fundamental understanding of how dissipation-induced many-body physics affects heat transport.

We find that the TRS breaking modifies the density of states and localisation/delocalisation property of the eigenstates which in turn affect the transport characteristics. Moreover, we find that the impact of the TRS breaking is not identical for the long-range Kitaev chain and its short-range counterpart. Therefore, noticeable differences in the transport properties can be observed due to the interplay between the TRS breaking and the range of interaction.

This process provides a practical route for preparing high-quality platelet suspensions for levitated nanoparticle experiments and other applications requiring suspensions of two-dimensional nanostructures.

</details>

# math.DG [[Back]](#toc)

### [286] [Conformal boundary rigidity from null geodesic travel times](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28689)
*Gabriel Paternain,Eric Woolgar*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 该论文研究渐近反德西特时空（asymptotically anti-de Sitter spacetimes）中一种新型正质量定理（positive mass theorem）的刚性情形（rigidity case），探讨若从彭罗斯共形无穷远（Penrose conformal infinity）出发的所有零测地线（null geodesics）在对跖点（antipodal point）重新聚焦，该时空是否共形于反德西特空间（anti-de Sitter space）。论文在零能量条件（null energy condition）或静态（static）情形下给出简单证明，并利用磁测地线理论（magnetic geodesics）处理全局平稳（globally stationary）情形，同时讨论了渐近平直时空（asymptotically flat spacetimes）中的类似问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前的正质量定理未依赖传统能量条件，但尚不明确其是否具有刚性情形（rigidity case），即是否可以从某种聚焦条件唯一确定时空的共形结构。

Method: 论文在渐近AdS时空中，所有从共形无穷远出发并返回该处的零测地线若都在对跖点重新聚焦，则通过三种情形论证该时空共形于AdS空间：满足零能量条件（null energy condition）的情形、静态（static）情形，以及利用磁测地线（magnetic geodesics）理论处理全局平稳（globally stationary）情形。

Result: 在上述三种情形下，若所有从共形无穷远一点出发的零测地线在对跖点重新聚焦，则时空共形于反德西特空间（anti-de Sitter space）。

Conclusion: 渐近AdS时空中的新型正质量定理具有刚性情形，且可通过不同条件（零能量条件、静态性或全局平稳性）证明；类似结论在渐近平直时空（asymptotically flat spacetimes）中也有对应讨论。

Abstract: The gravitational field of a distant, isolated system is manifested by the conformally invariant Weyl tensor. Thus the conformal structure far from the system encodes the system's gravitational mass. It also encodes the causal structure, thereby linking it to the mass. For asymptotically anti-de Sitter (AdS) spacetimes, this link led to a novel positive mass theorem of Page, Surya, and the second author \cite{PSW} which did not rely on any traditional energy condition. Here we ask whether that theorem has a rigidity case. Specifically, we consider all null geodesics in an asymptotically AdS spacetime that depart from the Penrose conformal infinity, travel through spacetime, and return to conformal infinity. If all such geodesics from a given point refocus at an antipodal point at infinity, is the spacetime conformal to anti-de Sitter space? It is easy to answer the question if the asymptotically AdS spacetime either (i) obeys the null energy condition or (ii) is static, and we give simple proofs in those cases. We also answer the question in the case of globally stationary, asymptotically AdS spacetimes, by applying the theory of magnetic geodesics on the Riemannian manifold-with-boundary obtained by quotienting by the stationary Killing vector field. The question has an analogue for asymptotically flat spacetimes, which we also discuss.

</details>


### [287] [Differential Invariants of Carrollian Spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30274)
*Boris Kruglikov,Eivind Schneider,Wijnand Steneker*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文从屏幕丛（screen bundle）的几何结构出发，计算了Carroll时空（Carrollian spacetimes）的不变量，并生成了其完整微分不变量代数；在jet空间框架下计算了Hilbert函数与Poincaré函数以揭示这些不变量的计数规律；最后计算了Spencer上同调（Spencer cohomology），揭示了内在挠率（intrinsic torsion）与内在曲率（intrinsic curvature）等基本不变量，并讨论了Carroll时空的对称性规模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Carroll时空在物理中具有特殊相关性（尤其在三维情形），但其几何不变量的系统构造与计数规律尚不完善，需要从微分不变量代数与Spencer上同调等角度进行系统性分析，以服务于等价问题（equivalence problem）与对称性分析（symmetry analysis）。

Method: 从屏幕丛的几何结构出发推导Carroll时空的不变量；对一般Carroll结构，生成整个微分不变量代数（微分不变量代数），重点分析物理上具有特殊重要性的三维情形；在jet空间（jet-spaces）框架下计算Hilbert函数与Poincaré函数，以量化各阶不变量的数目；最后计算Spencer上同调，提取内在挠率与内在曲率等基本不变量。

Result: 得到了Carroll时空的微分不变量代数及其生成方式；给出了三维Carroll情形的详细结果；计算了Hilbert函数与Poincaré函数，揭示了各阶不变量的计数规律；通过Spencer上同调计算，区分了内在挠率与内在曲率等基本不变量，并据此分析了Carroll时空的对称性规模。

Conclusion: 该工作为Carroll时空的几何不变量提供了系统完整的构造与计数框架，三维情形具有特殊物理意义；Spencer上同调方法有效刻画了基本不变量结构，为等价问题与对称性分析奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: We compute invariants of Carrollian spacetimes, deriving them from the geometry of the screen bundle. For generic Carrollian structures we specify how to generate the entire algebra of differential invariants, with emphasis on dimension 3, which has special physical relevance. Then, in the framework of jet-spaces, we compute the numerology behind these invariants: the Hilbert and Poincaré functions that govern their numbers according to order. Finally, we compute the Spencer cohomology behind the Carrollian geometry that, in particular, contains the spaces of intrinsic torsion and intrinsic curvature, which are fundamental invariants, important in the equivalence problem and symmetry analysis. Thus, we also discuss symmetry sizes of Carrollian spacetimes.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在通过测量e⁺e⁻→π⁺π⁻D_s⁺D_s⁻过程的Born截面，探寻可能存在的类粲偶素共振态，以加深对粲物理及强子谱的理解。

Method: 利用BESIII探测器在BEPCII储存环采集的8.5 fb⁻¹ e⁺e⁻对撞数据，质心能量范围覆盖4.42至4.95 GeV。对e⁺e⁻→π⁺π⁻D_s⁺D_s⁻过程进行事例重建与信号提取，并基于D_s⁺D_s⁻不变质量谱搜索中间类粲偶素共振结构。

Result: 在各能量点下，未观测到显著的信号，以90%置信水平确定了e⁺e⁻→π⁺π⁻D_s⁺D_s⁻的Born截面上限。D_s⁺D_s⁻不变质量谱分析中，当前统计量下未发现显著的类粲偶素共振结构。

Conclusion: 在当前统计精度下，e⁺e⁻→π⁺D_s⁺D_s⁻过程截面及D_s⁺D_s⁻质量谱中均未观测到显著信号或共振结构，表明该过程的产生截面较低，或需更大统计量的数据以进一步搜寻可能的类粲偶素态。

Abstract: Based on $8.5~{\rm fb}^{-1}$ of $e^+e^-$ collision data collected at center-of-mass energies between 4.42 and 4.95 GeV with the BESIII detector at the BEPCII storage ring, we investigate the process $e^+e^-\to π^+π^-D_s^+D_s^-$. With no significant signal observed, upper limits on the Born cross sections of $e^+e^-\to π^+π^-D_s^+D_s^-$ at each energy value are determined at the 90% confidence level. Additionally, a search for intermediate charmonium-like resonances is performed in the $M(D_s^+D_s^-)$ invariant-mass spectrum, but no significant resonant structures are observed with the current statistics.

</details>


### [289] [Influence of the KK graviton decay into hh on the triple Higgs measurement at LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29922)
*Alain Le Yaouanc,François Richard*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于先前在380 GeV和700 GeV处发现的两个KK引力子候选者，依据Randall-Sundrum（RS）模型预测在1000 GeV和1300 GeV处应出现额外共振；ATLAS在寻找三希格斯耦合（triple Higgs coupling）时发现的超出与该预测一致，暗示可通过RUN3数据确认KK引力子共振系列的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有证据表明在380 GeV和700 GeV处存在两个KK引力子候选事件。依据Randall-Sundrum（RS）模型的理论解释，应在1000 GeV和1300 GeV处出现另外两个共振态。最近ATLAS在对三希格斯耦合（triple Higgs coupling）的搜索中，在这些质量区域观测到了与预测相符的超出，因此有必要系统分析这些超出及其对RS模型的验证意义。

Method: 采用Randall-Sundrum（RS）理论框架进行解释，利用ATLAS合作组在寻找三希格斯耦合过程中报告的质量区域超出数据，并参考对衰变至ZZ/WW的重共振（heavy resonances）的半轻子（semi-leptonic）和全强子（fully hadronic）衰变模式的搜索，以及来自精密测量（precision measurements）的间接证据。

Result: 在1000 GeV和1300 GeV质量区域的局部截面（local cross sections）明显超出标准模型预言，即便在kl取较大值时也是如此。该超出出现在低本底区域，尽管统计显著性仍处于边缘水平（marginally significant），但有望通过RUN3数据获得更好的发现前景。

Conclusion: 该结果可解释三希格斯耦合（kl）测量中观测到的超出，并确认可在大型强子对撞机（LHC）上观测到一系列KK引力子共振。此外，在半轻子和全强子衰变模式的重共振搜索以及精密测量中也存在支持RS模型的间接证据。

Abstract: Evidence for two KK graviton candidates has been previously reported at 380 GeV and 700 GeV. Following a Randall Sundrum interpretation, two extra resonances should appear at 1000 GeV and 1300 GeV. Recently ATLAS, in its search for triple Higgs coupling, has reported an excess in that mass region in conformity with this prediction. Local cross sections are therefore clearly in excess of the standard predictions even for large values of kl. While still marginally significant, this effect appears in a mass region with low background which allows to expect good prospects of discovery with RUN3 data. Such a result could therefore allow to interpret an excess in the measurement of kl and confirm the existence of a series of KK graviton resonances observable at LHC. Other opportunities seem to appear in searches for heavy resonances decaying into ZZ/WW in semi-leptonic and fully hadronic modes. Indirect evidences for the RS model coming from precision measurements are also presented.

</details>


### [290] [Tracking performance study of the LHCb UP Detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29927)
*Yisheng Fu,Jianchun Wang,Xuhao Yuan*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文介绍了LHCb UP探测器（基于MAPS的像素追踪器）的布局设计及其独立径迹重建算法，结果表明该算法在LHCb Upgrade II中可实现接近98%的重建效率，同时鬼迹率低于4%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为LHCb Upgrade II阶段的高亮度环境设计一种基于单片有源像素传感器（MAPS，Monolithic Active Pixel Sensor）的UP探测器布局，并开发其独立径迹（standalone track）重建算法，以应对未来高亮度对撞实验中的实时径迹重建挑战。

Method: 设计了由四个探测平面组成的MAPS基像素追踪器布局，并开发了专用的UP径迹重建算法（dedicated UP tracking algorithms）用于独立径迹重建。

Result: 独立径迹重建效率接近98%，同时鬼迹率（ghost rate）保持在4%以下，表明算法在保持高纯度（high purity）的同时实现了高效重建。

Conclusion: UP独立径迹能够为全局LHCb重建提供高质量的输入，并为未来高亮度径迹重建和实时重建挑战提供可行的解决方案。

Abstract: This work presents the layout design of the LHCb UP detector, a MAPS-based pixel tracker composed of four detection planes, and several approaches for its standalone track reconstruction. The dedicated UP tracking algorithms demonstrates that efficient standalone reconstruction can be achieved for LHCb Upgrade II with high purity, reaching efficiencies close to $98\%$ while maintaining a ghost rate below $4\%$. These results indicate that UP standalone tracks can provide high-quality inputs for global LHCb reconstruction and offer a viable solution for future high-luminosity tracking and real-time reconstruction challenges.

</details>

### [291] [Search for Diffuse Supernova Neutrino Background in the Full KamLAND Dataset with Neural-Network-Based Event Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29381)
*D. Chernyak,T. Eda,M. Eizuka,R. Endo,A. Gando,Y. Gando,T. Hachiya,F. Haneishi,K. Hata,T. Hirai,K. Hosokawa,K. Ichimura,H. Ikeda,K. Inoue,K. Ishidoshiro,Y. Kamei,N. Kawada,Y. Kishimoto,M. Koga,K. Mikami,H. Miyake,K. Mizukoshi,D. Morita,K. Nakamura,R. Nakamura,J. Nakane,Y. Nakano,N. Obata,Y. Ota,K. Saito,I. Sakaki,I. Shimizu,J. Shirai,A. Suzuki,K. Tachibana,A. Takeuchi,K. Tamae,H. Watanabe,Z. Xu,S. Yoshida,S. Umehara,K. Fushimi,K. Kotera,Y. Urano,S. Kurosawa,H. Ozaki,B. E. Berger,B. K. Fujikawa,J. G. Learned,J. Maricic,Z. Li,L. A. Winslow,Y. Efremenko,H. J. Karwowski,D. M. Markoff,W. Tornow,S. Dell'Oro,T. O'Donnell,J. A. Detwiler,S. Enomoto,M. P. Decowski,K. M. Weerman,C. Grant,O. Penek,H. Song,A. Li*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文利用KamLAND探测器搜索弥散超新星中微子背景（DSNB），基于液闪探测器9.02–9.42千吨·年的曝光量和新型深度神经网络（deep neural network, DNN）事件分类技术，在8.3–30.8 MeV能区观测到7个候选事件。结果与仅含背景的预期（16.2±9.4个事件）一致，未发现显著DSNB信号，从而设定了90%置信度下的DSNB通量上限（38–43 cm⁻² s⁻¹）以及模型无关的电子反中微子通量上限，并在13.3 MeV以下能区获得部分最强约束。此外，该工作展示了神经网络事件分类在液闪探测器中抑制中子相关背景的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探测弥散超新星中微子背景（DSNB）是理解宇宙超新星历史和中微子天文学的重要课题；由于DSNB信号极其微弱且被大量背景事件淹没，亟需发展高效背景抑制方法以提高探测灵敏度。

Method: 利用KamLAND液闪探测器，通过逆β衰变（inverse beta decay）探测电子反中微子，能量范围为8.3–30.8 MeV；采用基于深度神经网络（deep neural network, DNN）的新事件分类技术来区分信号与背景；曝光量分别为9.02千吨·年（8.3–9.3 MeV）和9.42千吨·年（9.3–30.8 MeV）。

Result: 观测到7个候选事件，与仅含背景的预期值16.2±9.4个事件（含神经网络选择的系统不确定度）一致；能谱和径向分布的谱分析未发现显著DSNB信号；在90%置信度下设定DSNB通量上限为38–43 cm⁻² s⁻¹（依赖DSNB模型），并给出模型无关的电子反中微子通量上限，在13.3 MeV以下能区获得部分最强约束。

Conclusion: 未检测到DSNB信号，所设通量上限对DSNB模型和电子反中微子通量给出了当前最严格约束之一；同时，基于神经网络的事件分类被证明是液闪中微子探测器中抑制中子相关背景的有效方法。

Abstract: We report a search for the diffuse supernova neutrino background (DSNB) with the KamLAND detector, targeting electron antineutrinos via inverse beta decay in the neutrino energy range of 8.3 to 30.8 MeV. Using liquid-scintillator exposures of 9.02 kton-year for 8.3 to 9.3 MeV and 9.42 kton-year for 9.3 to 30.8 MeV, we observe seven candidate events after applying a new deep-neural-network-based event classification technique. This result is consistent with the background-only expectation of 16.2 plus or minus 9.4 events, including systematic uncertainties associated with the neural-network selection. A spectral analysis of the energy and radial distributions finds no significant excess attributable to the DSNB. We therefore set 90 percent confidence-level upper limits on the DSNB flux of 38 to 43 per square centimeter per second, depending on the assumed DSNB model. We also derive model-independent 90 percent confidence-level upper limits on the electron-antineutrino flux, obtaining some of the most stringent constraints below 13.3 MeV. Beyond the DSNB search itself, this work demonstrates neural-network-based event classification as a promising approach for suppressing neutron-associated backgrounds in liquid-scintillator neutrino detectors.

</details>


### [292] [Modelling the delayed shock-breakout emission following jet-launching binary neutron star mergers via relativistic MHD simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29515)
*Matteo Pais,Riccardo Ciolfi,Andrea Pavan*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本研究利用相对论性磁流体动力学（relativistic MHD）模拟，探讨双中子星合并（binary neutron star merger）产生的喷流激波突破抛射物（shock breakout, SBO）所引发的电磁信号，发现引力波-电磁信号时间延迟（GW-EM delay）对视向角（viewing angle）和抛射物不透明度（opacity）依赖较弱，可作为约束喷流模型的稳健诊断工具；与GRB 170817A对比表明，显著受阻喷流（substantially choked jet）模型与观测最为吻合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双中子星合并中，当相对论性喷流驱动的激波突破合并抛射物时，会产生电磁信号。该激波突破信号相对引力波信号的时间延迟，是探测喷流发射及早期传播物理条件的有力手段。本文旨在系统研究SBO发射及其对应的GW-EM延迟，并考察其对视向角和抛射物不透明度的依赖性。

Method: 研究基于先前双中子星合并模拟的最终状态，直接导入后合并环境，开展相对论性MHD模拟。作者引入特定程序，忠实重建早期动力学抛射物直至其自然前沿。模拟在三维（3D）中推进至0.6秒，随后施加轴对称假设并采用更高分辨率继续演化。通过变化喷流发射时间和光度，识别出从早期突破到扩展受阻喷流的三种代表性模型。对于每种情况，追踪喷流驱动的前向激波直至光球层，计算角度依赖的波尔光度学SBO光度，并考虑非径向光子传播、相对论性多普勒频移以及光传播时间效应。研究还考察了相差10倍的两个不透明度值。

Result: 研究发现，GW-EM延迟对视向角和抛射物不透明度的依赖性均较弱，表明该延迟可作为约束喷流模型的稳健诊断量。与GRB 170817A对比后，显著受阻喷流模型在峰值波尔光度、GW-EM延迟以及信号持续时间方面均与观测最为接近。

Conclusion: GW-EM时间延迟是一个稳健的诊断量，可用于区分不同的喷流传播模型。显著受阻喷流模型最符合GRB 170817A的观测特征。

Abstract: In binary neutron star (BNS) mergers launching a relativistic jet, an electromagnetic (EM) signal is produced when the jet-driven shock breaks out of the merger ejecta. The observed time delay of this shock-breakout (SBO) emission with respect to the gravitational-wave (GW) signal from the merger provides a powerful probe of the physical conditions governing jet launching and early-time jet propagation. Considering different models of jet propagation in realistic post-merger environments, we investigate the SBO emission and corresponding GW-EM delay that would be observed depending on the viewing angle and the assumed ejecta opacity. We perform relativistic MHD simulations of jets propagating through a post-merger environment directly imported from the outcome of a previous BNS merger simulation. We also introduce a specific procedure to faithfully reconstruct the early dynamical ejecta up to their natural front. The evolution is followed in 3D up to 0.6 s and then continued imposing axisymmetry and higher resolution. Varying jet launching time and luminosity, we identify three representative models spanning regimes from early breakout to extended jet choking. For each case, we track the jet-driven forward shock up to the photosphere and compute the angle-dependent bolometric SBO luminosity, assuming full conversion of the thermal energy within the shocked material into radiation, and taking into account non-radial photon propagation, relativistic Doppler shifts, and light-travel-time effects. We consider two opacity values spanning a factor of 10. We find that the GW-EM delay depends weakly on both viewing angle and ejecta opacity, making it a robust diagnostic for constraining models. Comparing with GRB 170817A, the model resulting in a substantially choked jet provides the most plausible peak bolometric luminosity and the closest match to the observed GW-EM delay and signal duration.

</details>


### [293] [General Relativistic Shock Wave Solutions with Black Hole Formation: The Singular Isothermal Sphere Case](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29607)
*Chien-Ting J. Chen,Michael J. Cai,Fabio Pacucci*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究在广义相对论框架下推导了奇异等温球（SIS）塌缩为黑洞时的自相似激波解，发现激波速度可达光速的约40%，中心吸积率比光滑膨胀波解压低约5–7倍，而激波释放的能量可达包裹静质量的约10%，为直接塌缩黑洞形成提供了分析性能量预算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: JWST在红移z≳6处揭示的大量超大质量黑洞（SMBH）和估计质量M_•>10^10M_⊙的类星体表明，早期宇宙中需要高效的生长路径。奇异等温球（singular isothermal sphere, SIS）在广义相对论下的光滑塌缩已有解析解，但塌缩中必然伴随的激波（shock wave）尚未被处理。

Method: 将Cai & Shu (2005)的框架扩展到非连续流，推导了等温流体的广义相对论跃变条件（jump conditions）；利用零速面（zero-velocity surface）的坐标匹配技术，将史瓦西（Schwarzschild）描述与共动自相似（comoving self-similar）描述唯一地连接起来。

Result: 获得了丰富的激波族，激波传播速度最高可达光速的约40%；中心吸积率仅由内部塌落决定，比光滑膨胀波解压低约5–7倍；激波释放的能量达到包裹静质量（rest mass）的约10%，接近史瓦西吸积辐射效率5.7%的两倍。

Conclusion: 这些结果为直接塌缩黑洞形成提供了分析性能量预算，对超大质量黑洞种子（SMBH seed）的组装、高红移黑洞周围的稠密茧（dense cocoon）、JWST新发现的小红点（Little Red Dots）以及伽马射线暴（gamma-ray burst）等相对论瞬变现象具有重要意义。

Abstract: The rapid emergence at $z\gtrsim 6$ of ubiquitous populations of supermassive black holes (SMBHs) revealed by JWST and of quasars with estimated masses $M_\bullet > 10^{10} M_\odot$ demands efficient pathways for early growth. The smooth collapse of a singular isothermal sphere (SIS) has been solved analytically in full general relativity, but the shock waves that inevitably accompany such collapse have not. Here, we derive general-relativistic self-similar shock-wave solutions for the collapse of an SIS to a black hole, extending the framework of Cai \& Shu (2005) to discontinuous flows. We obtain the general relativistic jump conditions for an isothermal fluid and show that they connect interior collapse solutions to exterior envelopes that may be static, expanding, or collapsing, yielding a rich family of shocks propagating at up to $\sim$40\% the speed of light; the available exterior types narrow with increasing sound speed. A coordinate-matching technique that uses the zero-velocity surface uniquely bridges the Schwarzschild and comoving self-similar descriptions, completing the characterization of the growing black hole. The central accretion rate is set by the interior collapse alone and is suppressed by a factor of $\sim$5--7 relative to the smooth expansion-wave solution, while the energy released at the shock reaches $\sim$10\% of the enclosed rest mass -- nearly twice the 5.7\% radiative efficiency of Schwarzschild accretion. These results provide an analytical energy budget for direct-collapse black hole formation, with implications for SMBH seed assembly, the dense cocoons around nascent high-redshift black holes, the recently discovered JWST's Little Red Dots, and relativistic transients such as gamma-ray bursts.

</details>


### [294] [Joint population and strong-lensing inference for resolved gravitational-wave events probes the black-hole merger rate beyond the peak of star formation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30144)
*Matthew Mould*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文通过同时推断引力波事件的强透镜（strong lensing）状态、放大率以及并合种群参数，对LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA目录中的双黑洞并合事件进行分析。结果显示所有事件的后验透镜概率均不超过1%，种群约束与未检测到强透镜的假设一致；但相比标准分析，并合率峰值的红移不确定性降低了约10%，高红移率上限改善了一个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波在传播过程中可能被不同尺度的中间势场透镜化，强透镜效应若未被考虑，会导致距离被低估、质量被高估，从而偏倚天体物理结论。因此，需要一种能够同时处理透镜检测、放大率估计和种群建模的分析方法，以消除这种系统偏差。

Method: 使用参数化（parametric）和非参数化（nonparametric）两种种群模型，并结合两种透镜光学深度（lensing optical depth）模型，对LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA双黑洞并合目录进行联合推断，同时估计每个事件的强透镜状态、放大率（若被透镜）及背后的并合种群分布。

Result: 所有事件的后验透镜概率均不超过1%，因此种群约束与假设未检测到强透镜或透镜从未发生的分析结果一致。然而，相比标准分析，并合率峰值的红移不确定性降低了约10%，高红移率上限改善了一个数量级。这些结果是首次仅利用已解析事件，在目前地基引力波探测器通常不灵敏的红移范围（恒星形成峰附近及更远处）获得约束。

Conclusion: 尽管透镜检测结果不显著，但联合分析方法在种群参数约束上带来了有限但实际的改进，特别是在高红移区域。这标志着首次使用已解析的引力波事件在恒星形成峰值红移附近获得约束，展示了同时处理透镜与种群建模的潜力。

Abstract: Gravitational waves can be lensed by intervening potentials of various scales. Strong lensing leads to underestimated distances and overestimated masses, biasing astrophysical results if not accounted for. I present a novel analysis of the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA catalog of binary black-hole mergers, simultaneously inferring (1) whether or not each event is strongly lensed, (2) their magnifications if so, and (3) the underlying merger population, using both parametric and nonparametric population models as well as two models for the lensing optical depth. Posterior lensing probabilities do not exceed 1% for any event, so population constraints are consistent with those assuming nondetection of strong lensing or that lensing never occurs. This includes multiple subpopulations over black-hole mass and a component with high aligned spins. Compared to standard analyses, however, there are reductions of order 10% in uncertainty on the redshift at which the merger rate peaks and an order of magnitude in high-redshift rate upper limits. Though modest, these are the first constraints using only resolved events at redshifts where current ground-based gravitational-wave detectors are usually insensitive, at and beyond the peak of star formation.

</details>
